**Searchable Electronic Edition of the _Śrāddhakāṇḍa_ of the _Smṛticandrikā_ by Devaṇabhaṭṭa**, transcribed, edited, formatted, and color-coded by Patrick Olivelle, is licensed under a [Creative Commons Attribution 4.0 International License](https://creativecommons.org/licenses/by-sa/4.0/).

_Last updated: December 2020_

Patrick Olivelle ([jpo@austin.utexas.edu](mailto:jpo@austin.utexas.edu))

University of Texas at Austin



**śrāddhakāṇḍa**

uktam āhnike nityaśrāddham | adhunā tatprasaṅgāc chrāddhaprakaraṇam ārabhyate | tatrādau śrāddhamahimā | tatra sumantuḥ |

	śrāddhāt parataraṃ nānyac chreyaskaram udāhṛtam |

	tasmāt sarvaprayatnena śrāddhaṃ kuryād vicakṣaṇaḥ ||

devalo 'pi |

	arogaḥ prakṛtisthaś ca cirāyuḥ putrapautravān |

	arthavān arthakāmī ca śrāddhakāmo bhaved iha ||

	paratra ca parāṃ tuṣṭiṃ lokāṃś ca vividhān śubhān |

	śrāddhakṛt samavāpnoti yaśaś ca vipulaṃ naraḥ ||

yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	āyuḥ prajāṃ dhanaṃ vidyāṃ svargaṃ mokṣaṃ sukhāni ca |

	prayacchanti tathā rājyaṃ prītā nṝṇāṃ pitāmahāḥ ||

yamo 'pi |

	ye yajanti pitṝn devān brāhmaṇān sahutāśanān |

	sarvabhūtāntarātmānaṃ viṣṇum eva yajanti te ||

	āyuḥ putrān yaśaḥ svargaṃ kīrtiṃ puṣṭiṃ balam śriyam |

	paśūn sukhaṃ dhanaṃ dhānyaṃ prāpnuyāt pitṛpūjanāt ||

mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe 'pi |

	pitā pitāmahaś caiva tathaiva prapitāmahaḥ |

	piṇḍasaṃbandhino hy ete vijñeyāḥ puruṣās trayaḥ ||

	lepasaṃbandhinas tv anye pitāmahapitāmahāt |

	prabhṛty uktās trayas teṣāṃ yajamānaś ca saptamaḥ ||

	tathānye pūrvajāḥ svarge ye cānye narakaukasaḥ |

	ye ca tiryaktvam āpannā ye ca bhūtādisaṃsthitāḥ ||

	tāṃt sarvān yajamāno vai śrāddhaṃ kurvan yathāvidhi |

	samāpyāyayate vastsa yena yena śṛṇuṣva tat ||

	annaprakiraṇaṃ yat tu manuṣyaiḥ kriyate bhuvi |

	tena tuṣṭim upāyānti ye piśācatvam āgatāḥ ||

	yad ambu snānavastrotthaṃ bhūmau patati putraka |

	tena ye marutāṃ prāptās teṣāṃ tṛptiḥ prajāyate ||

	yās tu gandhāmbukaṇikāḥ patanti dharaṇītale |

	tābhir āpyayanaṃ teṣāṃ ye devatvaṃ kule gatāḥ ||

	uddhṛteṣu tu piṇḍeṣu yāś cātra kaṇikā bhuvi |

	tābhir āpyāyanaṃ teṣāṃ ye tiryaktvaṃ kule gatāḥ ||

	ye cādantāḥ kule bālāḥ kriyāyogyā hy asaṃskṛtāḥ |

	vipannās te tu vikirasaṃmārjanajalāśinaḥ ||

	bhuktvā cācamatāṃ yac ca jalaṃ yac cāṅghrisecane |

	brāhmaṇānāṃ tathaivānte tena tṛptiṃ prayānti vai ||

	tenānekakule tatra tat tad yonyantaraṃ gatāḥ |

	prayānty apyāyanaṃ vatsa samyak śrāddhakriyāvatām ||

bṛhaspatir api |

	ya evaṃ vetti matimāṃs tasya śrāddhaphalaṃ bhavet |

	upadeṣṭānumantā ca loke tulyaphalau smṛtau ||

	imaṃ śrāddhavidhiṃ puṇyaṃ kuryād vāpi paṭhet tu yaḥ |

	sarvakāmaiḥ sa badhnāti hy amṛtatvaṃ ca vindati ||

tathākaraṇe 'pi doṣas tenaiva darśitaḥ |

	na tatra vīrā jāyante nārogā na śatāyuṣaḥ |

	na ca śreyo 'dhigacchanti yatra śrāddhaṃ vivarjitam ||

ādityapurāṇe 'pi |

	na santi pitaraś ceti kṛtvā manasi yo naraḥ |

	śrāddhaṃ na kurute tatra tasya raktaṃ pibanti te ||

tathā dhanāśuddhāv api doṣo mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe darśitaḥ |

	anyāyopārjitair dravyair yac chrāddhaṃ kriyate naraiḥ |

	tṛpyanti tena caṇḍālāḥ pulkasādyāś ca yonayaḥ || iti ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ śrāddhamahimā**

**atha śrāddhabhedāḥ**

tatra viśvāmitraḥ |

	nityaṃ naimittikaṃ kāmyaṃ vṛddhiśrāddhaṃ sapiṇḍanam |

	pārvaṇaṃ ceti vijñeyaṃ gauṣṭhyaṃ śuddhyartham aṣṭamam ||

	karmāṅgaṃ navamaṃ proktaṃ daivikaṃ daśamaṃ smṛtam |

	yātrāsv ekādaśaṃ proktaṃ puṣṭyarthaṃ dvādaśaṃ smṛtam ||

tatra nityanaimittikayor lakṣaṇaṃ pāraskareṇoktam |

	ahany ahani yac chrāddhaṃ tan nityam iti kīrtitam |

	vaiśvadevavihīnaṃ tu aśakto 'py udakena tu ||

	ekoddiṣṭaṃ tu yac chrāddhaṃ tan naimittikam ucyate |

	tad apy adaivaṃ kartavyam ayugmān āśayed dvijān || iti |

kāmyādīnāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ vṛddhavasiṣṭhenoktam |

	abhipretārthasiddhyarthaṃ kāmyaṃ pārvaṇavat smṛtam |

	putrajanmavivāhādau vṛddhiśrāddham udāhṛtam ||

	navānītārghyapātraṃ ca piṇḍaś ca parikīryate |

	pitṛpātreṣu piṇḍeṣu sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ tu tat ||

	pratiparva bhaved yasmāt procyate pārvaṇaṃ tu tat |

	goṣṭhyāṃ yat kriyate śrāddhaṃ goṣṭhīśrāddaṃ tad ucyate |

	bahūnāṃ viduṣāṃ prāptau sukhārthaṃ pitṛtṛptaye || iti |

śuddhyarthasya lakṣaṇaṃ pracetasoktam |

	kriyate śuddhaye yat tu brāhmaṇānāṃ tu bhojanam |

	śuddhyartham iti tat proktaṃ śrāddhaṃ pārvaṇavat kṛtam ||

karmāṅgādīnāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ pāraskareṇoktam |

	niṣekakāle some ca sīmantonnayane tathā |

	jñeyaṃ puṃsavane śrāddhaṃ karmāṅgaṃ vidhivat kṛtam ||

	devān uddiśya kriyate yat tad daivikam ucyate |

	tan nityaśrāddhavat kuryād dvādaśyādiṣu yatnataḥ ||

	gacchan deśāntaraṃ yad dhi śrāddhaṃ kuryāt tu sarpiṣā |

	tad yātrārtham iti proktaṃ praveśe ca na saṃśayaḥ || iti |

atra karmāṅgavacanam akaraṇe karmavaiguṇyajñāpanārtham | sarpiṣā sarpiḥ pradhānakenety arthaḥ | anyathā kevalena tṛpter aśakyatvāt ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ śrāddhabhedāḥ **

**atha śrāddhādhikārinirṇayaḥ**

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	pramītasya pituḥ putraiḥ śrāddhaṃ deyaṃ prayatnataḥ |

	jñātibandhusuhṛcchiṣyaṛtvigbhṛtyapurohitaiḥ || iti |

putrābhāva iti śeṣaḥ | pitur grahaṇaṃ mātur api pradarśanārtham | ata eva sumantuḥ |

	mātuḥ pituḥ prakurvīta saṃsthitasyaurasaḥ sutaḥ || iti |

etad anupanītenāpi kāryam | tad āha sumantuḥ |

	śrāddhaṃ kuryād avaśyaṃ tu pramītapitṛko hi yaḥ |

	vratastho vāvratastho vā eka eva bhaved yadi ||

avratastho 'nupanītaḥ | ata eva vṛddhamanuḥ |

	kuryād anupanīto 'pi śrāddham eko hi yaḥ sutaḥ |

	pitṛyajñāhutiṃ pāṇau juhuyād brāhmaṇasya saḥ || iti |

atra veśeṣam āha vyāghraḥ |

	kṛtacaulas tu kurvīta udakaṃ piṇḍam eva ca |

	svadhākāraṃ prayuñjīta vedoccāraṃ na kārayet ||

mātāpitor iti śeṣaḥ | smṛtyantare 'pi |

	kṛtacūḍo 'nupetas tu pitroḥ śrāddhaṃ samācaret |

	udāharet svadhākāraṃ na tu vedākṣarāṇy asau || iti |

vedākṣarāṇy api prayoktavyānīty āha |

	na hy asmin yujyate karma kiṃcid ā mauñjibandhanāt |

	nābhivyāhārayed brahma svadhāninayanād ṛte || iti |

evaṃ cātra vikalpo draṣṭavyaḥ | putrābhāve tu śaṅkhoktam |

	pituḥ putreṇa kartavyāḥ piṇḍadanodakakriyāḥ |

	putrābhāve tu patnī syāt patnyabhāve tu sodaraḥ || iti |

putragrahaṇenātra mukhyā gauṇāś ca gṛhyante,

	piṇḍado 'ṃśaharaś caiṣāṃ pūrvābhāve paraḥ paraḥ |

iti yājñavalkyasmaraṇāt | ato dvividhaputrābhāve "putrābhāve tu patnī syāt" it vacanārthaḥ | tad api pautrābhāvaviṣayam,

	pautro 'tha putrikāputraḥ svargaprāptikarāv ubhau |

	rakthe ca piṇḍadāne ca samau tau parikīrtitau || 

iti bṛhaspatinā gauṇaputrasāmānyābhidhānāt | na caivaṃ piṇḍadāne putrapautrayor vikalpaḥ syād iti śaṅkanīyam,

	putreṣu vidyamānexu nānyo vai kārayet svadhām |

iti ṛśyaśṛṅgasmaraṇāt,

	naitat pautreṇa kartavyaṃ putravāṃś cet pitāmahaḥ |

iti kātyāyanasmaraṇāt | putrābhāve tu patnī syād ity etad yajñapatnyā dāyaharatvāt tadviṣayam | anyathā tu yo dāyaharaḥ sa eva dadyāt | ata eva viṣṇvāpastambau: "yaś cārtharahaḥ sa piṇḍadāyī, putraḥ pitṛvittābhāve piṇḍaṃ dadyāt" iti | ata eva yājñavalkyenāpi,

	piṇḍado 'ṃśaharaś caiṣāṃ pūrvābhāve paraḥ paraḥ |

iti piṇḍadatvāṃśaharatvayor aikādikaraṇyam uktam | evaṃ sodare 'pi draṣṭavyam | evaṃ ca yad uktaṃ manunā,

	bhrātṝṇām ekajātānāṃ ekaś cet putravān bhavet |

	sarve te tena putreṇa putriṇo manur abravīt || 

iti, tatra putragrahaṇaṃ grāmasya tāta itivat praśaṃsārtham ity avagantavyam | anyathā "patnī duhitaraḥ" ityādy asamañjasaṃ syāt | anenaivābhiprāyeṇa gautamo 'pi: "putrābhāve 'sya bāndhavāḥ sapiṇḍāḥ mātṛsapiṇḍāḥ śiṣyāś ca dadyuḥ | tadabhāve ṛtvigācāryau" iti | mātṛsapiṇḍā mātulādayaḥ | sapiṇḍābhāve samānodakāḥ piṇḍaṃ dadyuḥ | tathā ca mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe |

	putrābhāve sapiṇḍās tu tadabhāve tu sodakāḥ |

	mātuḥ sapiṇḍā ye vā syur ye vā mātuś ca sodakāḥ ||

	kuryur enaṃ vidhiṃ samyag aputrasya sutāḥ smṛtāḥ |

	kuryān mātāmahāyaivaṃ putrikātanayas tathā ||

	sarvābhāve striyaḥ kuryuḥ svabhartṝṇām amantrakam |

	tadabhāve ca nṛpatiḥ kārayet svakuṭumbinām ||

	tajjātīyaiḥ naraiḥ samyag dāhādyāḥ sakalāḥ kriyāḥ |

	sarveṣām eva varṇānāṃ bāndhavo nṛpatir yataḥ ||

śrīviṣṇupurāṇe parāśaro 'pi |

	putraḥ pautraḥ prapautro vā tadvad vā bhrātṛsantatiḥ |

	sapiṇḍasantatir vāpi kriyārhā nṛpa jāyate ||

	teṣām abhāve sarveṣāṃ samanodakasantatiḥ |

	mātṛpakṣasya piṇḍena saṃbaddhā ye jalena vā ||

	kuladvaye 'pi cotsannaiḥ strībhiḥ karyāḥ kriyā nṛpa |

	tatsaṅghātagatair vāpi kāryā pretasya vai kriyāḥ ||

	utsannabandhurikthānāṃ kārayed avanīpatiḥ || iti |

ukteṣu putrādiṣu kasyakasmin karmaṇy adhikāra ity āśaṅkya sa evāha |

	pūrvāḥ kriyā madhyamāś ca tathā caivottarāḥ kriyāḥ |

	triprakārāḥ kriyā hy etās tāsāṃ bhedān śṛṇuṣva me ||

	ādyāhād dvādaśāhāc ca madhye yāḥ syuḥ kriyā matāḥ |

	tāḥ pūrvā madhyamā māsi māsy ekoddiṣṭasaṃjñikāḥ ||

	prete pitṛtvam āpanne sapiṇḍīkaraṇād anu |

	kriyante yāḥ kriyāḥ patnyāḥ procyante tā nṛpottarāḥ ||

	pitṛmātṛsapiṇḍais tu samānasalilais tathā |

	tatsaṅghātagataiś caiva rājñā vā dhanahāriṇaḥ ||

	pūrvāḥ kriyāś ca kartavyāḥ putrādyaiś cottarāḥ kriyāḥ |

	dauhitrair vā nṛpaśreṣṭha kāryās tattanayais tathā || iti |

sapiṇḍādyair avanipatyantaiḥ pūrvāḥ kriyāḥ madhyamāś ca kartavyāḥ | putrādyair eva bhrātṛsantatyantarair dauhitrādyaiś cottarāḥ kriyāḥ kartavyā na sapiṇḍādyair avanipatyantair ity arthaḥ | dauhitre tu bhaviṣyatpurāṇokto viśeṣaḥ |

	yathā vratastho 'pi sutaḥ pituḥ kuryāt kriyāṃ nṛpa |

	udakādyā mahābāho dauhitro 'pi tathārhati || iti |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca putrābhāve tu patnī syād ity etat "sarvābhāve striyaḥ kuryuḥ svabhartṝṇām amantrakam" iti purāṇavacanena virudhyate | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span>, "putrābhāve tu patnī syāt" ity etad brāhmādivivāhoḍhādiviṣayam, tasyā yajñānvitatvena tatraiva patnīśabdaprayogāt | itaratra tu,

	krayakrītā tu yā nārī na sā patnī vidhīyate |

	na sā daive na sā pitrye dāsīṃ tāṃ kavayo viduḥ ||

iti patnītvābhāvāt svabhartṝṇām amantrakam iti purāṇavacanaṃ tadviṣayam | yad vā, "putrābhāve tu patnī syāt" ity etad brahmavādinīviṣayam, tasyā adhyayanasadbhāvena mantrayogitvāt | purāṇavacanaṃ tv adhyayanavihīnasadyovadhvabhiprāyam ity anusaṃdheyam | yad atra yuktaṃ tad grāhyam | patnyāṃ tu viśeṣam āha vṛddhamanuḥ |

	aputrā śayanaṃ bhartuḥ palayantī vrate sthitā |

	patnī dadyāt tu tatpiṇḍaṃ kṛtsnam aṃśaṃ labheta ca || iti |

śayanaṃ pālayantī susaṃyatety arthaḥ | viṣṇur api |

	śvaśrvādīnāṃ tathā piṇḍaṃ patnī dadyāt susaṃyatā || iti |

yat tu kātyāyanenoktam,

	putraḥ śiṣyo 'tha vā patnī pitā bhrātātha vā guruḥ |

	strīhārī dhanahārī ca kuryuḥ piṇḍodakakriyām ||

iti, yad api vṛddhaśātātapena,

	mātulo bhāgineyasya svastrīyo mātulasya ca |

	śvaśurasya guroś caiva sakhyur mātāmahasya ca ||

	eteṣāṃ caiva bhāryāṇāṃ svasur mātuḥ pitus tathā |

	śrāddam āmaṃ tu kartavyam iti vedavidāṃ sthitiḥ ||

iti, atrāpi śrīviṣṇupurāṇavacanānusāreṇa vyavasthā veditavyā | yat tu kātyāyanenoktam,

	aputrāyāṃ patir dadyāt saputrāyāṃ tu na kvacit |

	na putrasya pitā kuryān nānujasya tathāgrajaḥ ||

iti, tat snehavihīnapitrādiviṣayam | ata eva bodhāyanaḥ |

	pitrā śrāddhaṃ na kartavyaṃ putrāṇāṃ tu kathaṃcana |

	bhrātrā naiva ca kartavyaṃ bhrātṝṇāṃ ca kanīyasām ||

	api snehena kuryātāṃ sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ vinā |

	gayāyāṃ tu viseṣeṇa jyāyān api samācaret || iti |

atra dhanahāritvādinimittābhāve 'pi kṛte 'bhyudaya ity āha vṛddhaśātātapaḥ |

	pituḥ śrāddhaṃ tu kartavyaṃ sarveṣāṃ varṇaliṅginām |

	evaṃ kuryān naraḥ samyaṅ mahatīṃ śriyam āpnuyāt || iti |

liṅgina āśramiṇaḥ | etac ca savarṇābhiprāyeṇa, anyathā doṣaśravaṇāt | tathā ca marīciḥ |

	brāhmaṇo hy asavarṇasya yaḥ karoty aurdhvadaihikam |

	tadvarṇatvam asau yāti iha loke paratra ca ||

pāraskaro 'pi |

	na brāhmaṇena kartavyaṃ śūdrasya tv aurdhvadaihikam |

	śūdreṇa vā brāhmaṇasya vinā pāraśavāt kvacit ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ śrāddhādhikārinirṇayaḥ**

**atha mātāmahaśrāddhādhikārinirṇayaḥ**

tatra pulastyaḥ:

	mātuḥ pitaram ārabhya trayo mātāmahāḥ smṛtāḥ |

	teṣāṃ tu pitṛvac chrāddhaṃ kuryur duhitṛsūnavaḥ ||

pitṛvac chrāddhaṃ pārvaṇam ity arthaḥ | tac ca śrāddham āvaśyakam | ata eva vyāsaḥ |

	pitṝn mātāmahāṃś caiva dvijaḥ śrāddhen tarpayet |

	anṛṇaś ca pitṝṇāṃ tu brahmalokaṃ sa gacchati ||

purāṇe 'pi |

	kṛtvā tu paitṛkaṃ śrāddhaṃ pitṛprabhṛtiṣu triṣu |

	kuryān mātāmahānāṃ ca tathaivānṛṇyakāraṇāt || iti |

ānṛṇyagrahaṇaṃ nityatvajñāpanārtham | ata evākaraṇe doṣa purāṇe darśitaḥ |

	pārvaṇaṃ kurute yas tu kevalaṃ pitṛhetukam |

	mātāmahyaṃ na kurute pitṛhā sa prajāyate ||

	pitaro yatra pūjyante tatra mātāmahā dhruvam |

	aviśeṣeṇa kartavyaṃ viśeṣān narakaṃ vrajet || iti |

yatra yasmin karmaṇi pitaraḥ pūjyante tatrāviśeṣeṇa mātāmahā api pūjyā ity arthaḥ | anena sarvasminn api pitṛśrāddhe mātāmahaśrāddham api kāryam ity uktaṃ bhavati | atra keṣucid apavādam āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	karṣūsamanvitaṃ muktvā tadādyaṃ śrāddhaṣoḍaśam |

	pratyābdikaṃ ca śeṣeṣu piṇḍāḥ syuḥ ṣaḍ iti sthitiḥ || iti |

karṣūsamanvitaṃ sapiṇḍīkaraṇaśrāddham | ṣoḍaśagrahaṇam ekoddiṣṭopalakṣaṇārtham | evaṃ ca yan mātāmahaśrāddhaṃ pitṛśrāddheṣu vihitaṃ tatraiva doṣānṛṇyayor abhidhānāt tad eva sarvadauhitrasādhāraṇam | yaḥ punar dhanahārī dauhitraḥ sa navaśrāddhādy api kuryād eva, "yo yata ādadīta sa tasmai śrāddhaṃ kuryāt" iti smaraṇāt | anenaivābhiprāyeṇa skando 'pi |

	śrāddhaṃ mātāmahānāṃ tu avaśyaṃ dhanahāriṇā |

	dauhitreṇārthaniṣkṛtyai kartavyaṃ vidhivat sadā || iti |

yo dhanahārī dauhitraḥ tenāvaśyaṃ navaśrāddhādyaurdhavadaihikaṃ kāryam ity arthaḥ | tatropapattim āha sa eva |

	malam etan manuṣyāṇāṃ draviṇaṃ yat prakīrtitam |

	tad gṛhṇan malam ādatte durbhedaṃ jñāninām api ||

	ṛṣibhis tasya nirdiṣṭā niṣkṛtiḥ pāvanī parā |

	ā dehapatanāt kuryāt tasya piṇḍodakakriyām || iti |

<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca,

	kuryān mātāmahaśrāddhaṃ niyamāt putrikāsutaḥ |

	ubhayor api saṃbaddhaḥ kuryāt sa ubhayor api ||

iti yamena putrikāputra eva niyamagrahaṇād anyatra niyamo na gṛhyate | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span>, vacanārthāparijñānāt | asyārthaḥ: dvividho hi putrikāputraḥ, eko mātāmahena saṃbaddhaḥ aparaḥ pitṛmātāmahābhyām iti | tatra prathamo mātāmahaśrāddhaṃ niyamena kuryāt pitṛśrāddham icchayā, ya ubhayasaṃbaddhaḥ sa ubhayor apīti | ato nānena niyamo 'vagamyate | yad api manunoktam,

	dauhitro hy akhilaṃ riktham aputrasya pitur haret |

	sa eva dadyāt dvau piṇḍau pitre mātāmahāya ca ||

iti, tad api yo dhanahārī dauhitraḥ sa eva pitṛmātāmahayor navaśrāddhādyaurdhvadaihikaṃ kuryāt, netara ity evaṃparaṃ na punar itarasya śrāddhamātraniṣedhārtham, pūrvoktānṛṇyādipratipādakavacanavirodhāt | evaṃ ca yat kaiścid uktaṃ dhanahāriputrikāputrayor mātāmahaśrāddham āvaśyakaṃ nānyasyeti, tat pūrvoktavacanādarśananibandhanam ity upekṣaṇīyam | putrikāputraśrāddhe viśeṣam āha manuḥ |

	mātuḥ prathamataḥ piṇḍaṃ nirvapet putrikāsutaḥ |

	dvitīyaṃ tu pitus tasyās tṛtīyaṃ tu pituḥ pituḥ || iti |

dvyāmuṣyāyaṇe tu putrikāputre uśanasokto viśeṣaḥ |

	mātāmahyaṃ tu mātrādi paitṛkaṃ pitṛpūrvakam |

	mātṛtaḥ pitṛto yasmād adhikāro 'sti dharmataḥ || iti |

kṣetraje tu dvyāmuṣyāyaṇe devaloktam |

	dvyāmuṣyāyaṇakā dadyuḥ dvābhyāṃ piṇḍodake pṛthak | iti |

dvābhyāṃ pitṛmātṛvargābhyām ity arthaḥ | atra kramaviśeṣam āha marīciḥ |

	sagotro vānyagotro vā yo bhaved vidhinā sutaḥ |

	piṇḍaṃ śrāddhavidhānaṃ ca kṣetriṇe prāg vinirvapet ||

	bījine tu tataḥ paścāt kṣetrī jīvati cet kvacit |

	bījine dadyur ādau tu mṛte paścāt pradīyate || iti |

kṣetriṇa iti śeṣaḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ mātāmahaśrāddhādikārinirṇayaḥ **

**atha jīvapitṛkaśrāddhanirṇayaḥ**

tatra kātyāyanaḥ |

	sapituḥ pitṛkṛtyeṣu adhikāro na vidyate |

	na jīvantam atikramya kiṃcid dadyād iti śrutiḥ || iti |

pitṛkṛtyeṣu śrāddheṣu pitāmahādisaṃbandheṣv ity arthaḥ | atra keṣucid apavādo maitrāyaṇīyapariśiṣṭe darśitaḥ |

	udvāhe putrajanane pitryeṣṭyāṃ saumike makhe |

	tīrthe brāhmaṇa āyāte ṣaḍ ete jīvataḥ pituḥ || iti |

jīvataḥ pituḥ putrasya ṣaḍ ete śrāddhakālā ity arthaḥ | pitryeṣṭyāṃ cāturmāsyeṣu, saumike makhe somayāgādau puroḍāśāt piṇḍadāne ca | etat sāgikābhiprāyam | ata eva sumantuḥ |

	na jīvapitṛkaḥ kuryāc chrāddham agnim ṛte dvijaḥ (?) |

	yebhya eva pitā dadyāt tebhyaḥ kurvīta sāgnikaḥ ||

	pitāmaho 'py evam eva kuryāj jīvati sāgnikaḥ |

	sāgniko 'pi na kurvīta jīvati prapitāmahe || iti |

prapitāmahagrahaṇaṃ pitṛpitāmahopetaprapitāmahapradarśanārtham | ata eva viṣṇuḥ: "pitari pitāmahe prapitāmahe ca (?) jīvati naiva dadyāt" iti | pitari pitāmahe ca jīvati kathaṃ kāryam ity apekṣite sa evāha: "pitari jīvati yaḥ śrāddhaṃ kuryāt sa yeṣāṃ pitā kuryāt teṣāṃ kuryāt pitari pitāmahe ca yeṣāṃ pitāmahaḥ" iti | tathā pitādiṣu (?) triṣu dvayor ekasya vā maraṇe 'pi tenaivoktam: "yasya pitā pretaḥ syāt sa pitre piṇḍaṃ nidhāya pitāmahāt paraṃ dvābhyāṃ dadyāt | yasya pitāmahaḥ pretaḥ syāt tasmai piṇḍaṃ nidhāya prapitāmahāt paraṃ dvābhyāṃ dadyāt | yasya pitāmahaprapitamahau ca pretau syāyāṃ yasya pitā prapitāmahaś ca pretau syātāṃ sa pitre piṇḍaṃ nidhāya pitāmahāt paraṃ dvābhyāṃ dadyāt" iti | bhaviṣyatpurāṇe pitari jīvati dvayor eva śrāddham uktam |

	jīvamāne na deyaṃ syād yasmād bharatasattama |

	tasmāj jīvapitā kuryād dvābhyām eva na saṃśayaḥ || iti |

manus tu triṣu yo jivati tam eva śrāddhe bhojayed ity āha |

	dhriyamāṇe tu pitari pūrveṣām eva nirvapet |

	vipravad bhāvitaṃ śrāddhe svakaṃ pitaram āśayet ||

	pitā yasya tu vṛttaḥ syāj jīved vāpi pitāmahaḥ |

	pitus tu nāma saṃkīrtya kīrtayet prapitāmaham ||

	pitāmaho vā tac chrāddhaṃ bhuñjītety abravīn manuḥ || iti |

pūreveṣāṃ pitāmahādīnām | nigamo 'pi: "yo jīvati pitṝṇāṃ taṃ bhojayet pitṛsthāna ity eke, jīvatām ajīvatāṃ vā deyam eveti hiraṇyaketuḥ" iti | evaṃ piṇḍapitṛyajñe 'pi draṣṭavyam | ata eva yājñavalkyaḥ |

	homataḥ pitṛyajñasya jīvet pitari jīvataḥ |

	pitaraṃ bhojayitvā vā piṇḍau nirvṛṇuyāt pitā ||

	ubhau yasya vyatītau tu jīvec cet prapitāmahaḥ |

	piṇḍau nirvṛṇuyāt pūrvau bhojayet prapitāmaham || iti |

yamas tu homo 'pi pākṣika ity āha |

	pitryaṃ jīvapitur noktam agnau homo 'pi pākṣikaḥ |

	yebhyo vāpi pitā tebhyo dadyād vaitānakarmaṇi ||

	dadyāt tebhyaḥ parebhyas tu jīvec cet tritayaṃ yadi || iti |

pitryaṃ piṇḍadānam, vaitānakarmaṇi piṇḍapitṛyajña ity arthaḥ | āpastambas tu pitari jīvati na piṇḍadānaṃ nityam ity āha: "yadi jīvati pitā na dadyād ā homāt tyaktvā viramet" iti | atra yathāsvaśākhaṃ vyavasthā | bhaviṣyatpurāṇe 'pi śrāddhe pratyakṣārcanaṃ niṣiddham ity uktam |

	pratyakṣam arcanaṃ śrāddhe na yuktaṃ manur abravīt |

	piṇḍanirvāpaṇaṃ cāpi mahāpātakasaṃmitam || iti |

manur atra jñānavān, manunā tu pratyakṣārcanasyoktatvāt ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ jīvapitṛśrāddhādhikāranirṇayaḥ **

**atha śrāddhakālāḥ**

tatra yājñavalkyaḥ |

	amāvāsyāṣṭakā vṛddhiḥ kṛṣṇapakṣo 'yanadvayam |

	dravyaṃ brāhmaṇasaṃpattiḥ viṣuvat sūryasaṃkramaḥ ||

	vyatīpāto gajacchāyā grahaṇaṃ candrasūryayoḥ |

	śrāddhaṃ prati ruciś caiva śrāddhakālāḥ prakīrtitāḥ || iti |

yasyāṃ tithau sūryācandramasoḥ saṃnikarṣaḥ sāmāvāsyā | tasyāṃ tithau śrāddham āvaśyakam | tathā ca laugākṣiḥ |

	śrāddhaṃ kuryād avaśyaṃ tu pramītapitṛkaḥ svayam |

	indukṣaye māsi māsi vṛddhau pratyabdam eva ca || iti |

indukṣayo 'māvāsyā | aṣṭakā mārgaśīrṣādimāsacatuṣṭayāparapakṣāṣṭamyaḥ, "hemantaśiśirayoś caturṇām aparapakṣāṇām aṣṭamīṣv aṣṭakāḥ" iti śaunakasmaraṇāt | atrāpi śrāddham āvaśyakam,

	amāvāsyāvyatīpātapaurṇamāsyaṣṭakāsu ca |

	vidvān śrāddham akurvāṇaḥ prāyaścittiyate tu saḥ || 

iti pitāmahasmaraṇāt | vṛddhiḥ putrādiḥ | atrāpi śrāddham āvaśyakam,

	vṛddhau na tarpitā yair vai devatā gṛhamedhibhiḥ |

	tad dānam āsuraṃ sarvam āsuro vidhir eva saḥ || 

iti vṛddhaśātātapasmaraṇāt | kṛṣṇapakṣo 'parapakṣaḥ | atrāpi śrāddhaṃ nityam, "śākenāpy aparapakṣaṃ nātikramet" iti kātyāyanasmaraṇāt | atra viśeṣam āha vasiṣṭhaḥ: "aparapakṣa ūrdhvaṃ caturthyāḥ pitṛbhyo dadyāt" iti | ūrdhvaṃ caturthyāḥ pañcamīm ārabhyety arthaḥ | gautamo 'pi: "atha śrāddham amāvāsyāyāṃ pitṛbhyo dadyāt pañcamīprabhṛti vāparapakṣasya yathāśrāddhaṃ sarvasmin vā" iti | aparapakṣasya pañcamīm ārabhya pitṛbhyo dadyāt sarvasmin vāparapakṣe pratipadam ārabhyety arthaḥ | kātyāyano 'pi: "aparapakṣe śrāddhaṃ kurvītordhvaṃ caturthyā yad ahaḥ saṃpadyeta" iti | caturthyā ūrdhvaṃ yasminn ahani dravyādi saṃpadyeta tasmin vā kuryād ity arthaḥ | anenaikasminn ahanit śrāddhaṃ kuryād ity uktaṃ bhavati | uktaṃ ca gautamena: "sarvasmin vā dravyadeśabrāhmaṇasaṃnidhāne vā" iti | atra yathāsāmarthyaṃ vyavasthā | ata eva gautamaḥ: "kālaniyamaś śaktitaḥ" iti | atra sāmarthyataḥ kālaniyamo bhavatīty arthaḥ | yadaikasmin ahani tadā pṛthag eva amāvāsyāśrāddhaṃ kāryam, "amāvāsyāṣṭakā vṛddhiḥ kṛṣṇapakṣaḥ" iti pṛthagupādānāt, "aparapakṣe yad ahaḥ saṃpadyeta amāvāsyāyāṃ viśeṣeṇa" it niyamasmaraṇāt, tathā,

	na nirvapati yaḥ śrāddhaṃ pramītapitṛko dvijaḥ |

	indukṣaye māsi māsi prāyaścittīyate tu saḥ ||

iti vyāghreṇākaraṇe prāyaścittavidhānāc ca | tathā "yathā kathaṃcin nityāni kuryād indukṣayādiṣu" iti hārītena nityatvābhidhānāt | ato yat kaiścid uktam: "amāvāsyāśrāddham āparapakṣikaśrāddhena vikalpyate" iti, tad apāstam | aparapakṣe punar āpastambokto viśeṣaḥ: "māsi māsi kāryam aparapakṣasyāparāhṇaḥ śreyāṃs tathāparapakṣasya jaghanyāny ahāni" iti | jaghanyāni daśamyādīni | ata eva manuḥ |

	kṛṣṇapakṣe daśamyādau varjayitvā caturdaśīm |

	śrāddhe praśastās tithayo yathaitā na tathetarāḥ || iti |

daśamyāditithiṣu caturdaśīṃ varjayitvety arthaḥ | caturdaśī tu śastrahatānām eva | yathāha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	pratipat prabhṛti khyātā varjayitvā caturdaśīm |

	śastreṇa tu hatā ye vai tebhyas tava pradīyate || iti |

śastragrahaṇam viṣāder api pradarśanārtham | ata eva marīciḥ |

	viṣaśastraśvāpadāhitiryagbrāhmaṇaghātinām |

	caturdaśyāṃ kriyā kāryā anyeṣāṃ tu vigarhitā ||

pracetā api |

	vṛkṣārohaṇalohādyaiḥ vidujjalaviṣādibhiḥ |

	nakhidaṃṣṭriviṣannānāṃ teṣāṃ śastā caturdaśī || iti |

atra viśeṣam āha gargaḥ |

	caturdaśyāṃ tu yac chrāddhaṃ sapiṇḍīkaraṇāt param |

	ekoddiṣṭavidhānena tat kāryaṃ śastraghātine || iti |

śastraghātine yadāparapakṣikaśrāddhaṃ caturdaśyāṃ kriyate tadaikoddiṣṭavidhānena nānyathety arthaḥ | | ata eva sumantuḥ |

	ekapiṇḍīkṛtānāṃ tu pṛthaktvaṃ nopapadyate |

	sapiṇḍīkaraṇād ūrdhvam ṛte kṛṣṇacaturdaśīm || iti |

yat tu mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe,

	pratipaddhanalābhāya dvitīyā dvipadapradā |

	parārthināṃ tṛtīyā tu caturthī śatrunāśinī ||

	pañcamyāṃ śriyam āpnoti ṣaṣṭyāṃ pūjyo bhaven naraḥ |

	gāṇādhipatyaṃ saptamyām aṣṭamyām ṛddhim uttamām ||

	śriyo navamyām āpnoti daśamyāṃ pūrṇakāmatām |

	vedāṃs tathāpnuyāt sarvān ekādaśyāṃ kriyāparaḥ ||

	dvādaśyāṃ japalābhaṃ ca prāpnoti pitṛpūjakaḥ |

	prjām iṣṭāṃ paśūn medhyān svātantryaṃ buddhim uttamām ||

	dīrgham āyus tathaiśvaryaṃ kurvāṇas tu trayodaśīm |

	avāpnoti na saṃdehaḥ śrāddhaṃ śrāddhaparo naraḥ ||

	yuvānaḥ pitaro yasya mṛtāḥ śastreṇa vā hatāḥ |

	tena kāryaṃ caturdaśyāṃ teṣāṃ siddhim abhīpsatā ||

	śrāddhaṃ kurvann amāvāsyāṃ yatnena puruṣaḥ śuciḥ |

	sarvān kāmān avāpnoti svargaṃ cānantam aśnute || 

iti, tat nityatvanirākaraṇārthaṃ na, kiṃ tu kālaviśeṣāt phalaviśeṣo bhavatīty evaṃparam | ata eva āpastambaḥ: "sarveṣv evāparapakṣasyāhaḥsu kriyamāṇe pitṝn prīṇāti kartus tu kālaniyamāt phalaviśeṣaḥ" iti | prakṛtam ucyate: ayanadvayaṃ makarakarkaṭakasaṃkrāntī | atrāpi śrāddhaṃ nityam | ata eva viṣṇupurāṇe parāśaraḥ |

	upaplave candramaso raveś ca triṣv aṣṭakāsv apy ayanadvaye ca |

	pānīyam apy atra tilair vimiśraṃ dadyāt pitṛbhyaḥ prayato manuṣyaḥ ||

	śrāddhaṃ kṛtaṃ tena samāḥ sahasraṃ rahasyam etat pitaro vadanti ||

atra pānīyam apy atreti vacanād ayanaśrāddhaṃ nityam iti gamyate | jātūkarṇyo 'pi |

	grahoparāge viṣuve ca jāte pitrye maghāyām ayanadvaye ca |

	nityaṃ ca śaṅkhe ca tathaiva padme dattaṃ bhaven niṣkasahasratulyam || iti |

atra nityaṃ dattaṃ niṣkasahasratulyam ity anvayaḥ | pitrye nabhasyāparapakṣe yā maghā tasyām ity arthaḥ | śaṅkhādisvarūpamami (?) tenaivoktam |

	śaṅkhaṃ prāhur amāvāsyāṃ kṣīṇasomāṃ dvijottamāḥ |

	aṣṭakāsu bhavet padmaṃ tatra dattaṃ yathākṣayam || iti |

atha vā padmaṃ śaṅkhoktam |

	yathā viṣṭir vyatīpāto bhānuvaras tathaiva ca |

	padmakaṃ nāma tat proktam ayanāc ca caturguṇam || iti |

yat tu viṣṇunoktam: "ādityasaṃkramo viṣuvaddvayaṃ vyatīpāto janmarkṣam abhyudayaś ca,

	etāṃś ca śrāddhakālān vai kāmyān āha prajāpatiḥ |

	śrāddham eteṣu yad dattaṃ tad ānantyāya kalpate" || 

iti, tad api na nityatvanirākaraṇārtham | vacanadvayenāgnihotrādivan nityatvakāmyatvayor avirodhāt | dravyaṃ brāhmaṇasaṃpattir iti, dravyasya śrāddhārhasya brāhmaṇasya vā vakṣyamāṇasya saṃpattir lābho yasmin kāle saḥ śrāddhakāla ity arthaḥ | atrāpi śrāddham āvaśyakam | yathāha hārītaḥ |

	tīrthe dravyopapattau tu na kālam avadhārayet |

	pātraṃ ca brāhmaṇaṃ prāpya samyak chrāddaṃ vidhīyate || iti |

tīrthaṃ gaṅgdi | viṣuvat meṣe tulāyāṃ ca sūryasaṃkramaḥ | atra pulastyokto viśeṣaḥ |

	ayanadvitaye śrāddhaṃ viṣuvaddvitaye tathā |

	yugādiṣu ca sarvāsu piṇḍanirvāpaṇād ṛte || iti |

sūryasaṃkramaḥ sūryasya rāśito rāśyantaragamanam | sūryasaṃkrama ity anenaiva saṃkrāntimātrasiddhau ayane viṣuve ceti pṛthagvacanaṃ phalabhūyastvārtham | ata eva śaṅkhaḥ |

	hasticchāyāsu yad dattaṃ yad dattaṃ rāhudarśane |

	viṣuvaty ayane caiva sarvam ānantyam aśnute || iti |

vyatīpāto yogaviśeṣaḥ vṛddhamanunoktaḥ |

	śravaṇāśvidhaniṣṭhārdrānāgadaivatamastakaiḥ |

	yady amā ravivāreṇa vyatīpātaḥ sa ucyate || iti |

yady amāvāsyā ravivāreṇa śravaṇādinā ca yuktā sa vyatīpāta ity arthaḥ | nāgadaivatam āśleṣānakṣatram | mastakaṃ mṛgaśirāḥ | tatrāpi śrāddhaṃ nityam,

	amāvāsyāvyatīpātapaurṇamāsyaṣṭakāsu ca |

	vidvān śrāddham akurvāṇaḥ prāyaścittīyate tu saḥ ||

iti pitāmahasmaraṇāt | gajacchāyā hasticchāyā, tasyāṃ śrāddhaṃ dadyāt | tathā kāṭhakaśrutiḥ: "etad dhi devapitṝṇām ayanaṃ yad dhasticchāyāyāṃ śrāddhaṃ dadyāt" iti | mahābhārate 'pi: 

	ājena sarvalohena varṣāsu niyatavrataḥ |

	hasticchāyāsu vidhivat karṇavyajanavījitam || iti |

śrāddhaṃ dadyād iti śeṣaḥ | karṇavyajanavījitam ity anenaitad dhasticchāyāviṣayam ity avagamyate | manur api |

	api naḥ sa kule bhūyād yo no dadyāt trayodaśīm |

	pāyasaṃ madhusarpirbhyāṃ prākchāye kuñjarasya ca || iti |

prācī chāyā yasya deśasya sa prākchāyaḥ, tasminn ity arthaḥ | atha vā pāribhāṣikī gajacchāyā | sā ca smṛtyantare darśitā |

	yadenduḥ pitṛdaivatye haṃsaś caiva kare sthitaḥ |

	tithir vaiśravaṇī yā ca gajacchāyeti sā smṛtā || iti |

pitṛdaivatye makhāyām | haṃsaḥ sūryaḥ | karo hastanakṣatram | vaiśravaṇī trayodaśī | purāṇe 'pi |

	haṃse hastasthite yā tu makhāyuktā trayodaśī |

	tithir vaiśravaṇī nāma sā chāyā kuñjarasya tu ||

	haṃse karasthite yā tu amāvāsyā karānvitā |

	sā chāyā kuñjaracchāyā iti bodhāyono 'bravīt ||

	vanaspatigate some yā chāyā prāṅmukhī bhavet |

	gajacchāyā tu sā proktā tasyāṃ śrāddhaṃ prakalpayet || iti |

amāvāsyāyām aparāhṇ ity arthaḥ |

	saiṃhikeyo yadā sūryaṃ grasate parvasaṃdhiṣu |

	gajacchāyā tu sā proktā tasyāṃ śrāddhaṃ prakalpayet ||

saiṃhikeyo rāhuḥ | atra phalaviśeṣo vāyupurāṇe darśitaḥ |

	ghṛtena bhojayed viprān ghṛtaṃ bhūmau samutsṛjet |

	chāyāyāṃ hastinaś caiva datvā śrāddhaṃ na śocati ||

śrīviṣṇudharmottare 'pi |

	gayāyāṃ darśane rāhoḥ khaḍgamāṃsena yoginam |

	bhojayec ca kule 'smākaṃ chāyāyāṃ kuñjarasya ca ||

	ākalpikī tu sā tṛptis tenāsmākaṃ bhaviṣyati |

	dātā sarveṣu lokeṣu kāmacārī bhaviṣyati ||

	yadaitat pañcakaṃ na syād ekenāpi vayaṃ sadā |

	tṛptiṃ prāpsyāma cānantāṃ kiṃ punaḥ sarvasaṃpadā || iti |

tathā bhoktur api doṣaḥ smṛtyantare darśitaḥ |

	kṛṣṇājinapratigrāhī vikrayī vā bhavet tu yaḥ |

	gajacchāyāśrito bhuktvā na bhūyaḥ puruṣo bhavet ||

grahaṇaṃ candrasūryayor iti, grahaṇam uparāgaḥ | atrāpi śrāddhaṃ nityam | ata eva śātātapaḥ |

	sarvasvenāpi kartavyaṃ śrāddhaṃ vai rāhudarśane |

	akurvāṇas tu tac chrāddhaṃ paṅke gaur iva sīdati ||

tathātra phalaviśeṣo viṣṇunā darśitaḥ |

	rāhudarśanadattaṃ hi śrāddham ācandratārakam |

	guṇavat sarvakāmīyaṃ pitṝṇām upatiṣṭhati || iti |

ṛṣyaśṛṅgo 'pi |

	rāhugraste tu vai sūrye yas tu śrāddhaṃ prakalpayet |

	tena vai sakalā pṛthvī dattā viprasya vai kare || iti |

atra kālaniyamam āha vṛddhavasiṣṭhaḥ |

	tridaśāḥ sparśasamaye tṛpyanti pitaras tathā |

	manuṣyā madhyakāle tu mokṣakāle tu rākṣasāḥ || iti |

yat tu mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe,

	viśiṣṭabrāhmaṇaprāptau sūryendugrahaṇe 'yane |

	viṣuve ravisaṃkrāntau vyatīpāte ca putrake ||

	śrāddhārhadravyasaṃprāptau tathā duḥsvapnadarśane |

	janmarkṣagrahapīḍāsu śrāddhaṃ kurvīta cecchayā ||

iti — icchā kāmaḥ tadāpi (tad api?) śrāddhaṃ kurvītety evaṃparam, na punaḥ kāmyam eveti vaktum | ata eva kūrmapurāṇe |

	naimittikaṃ tu kartavyaṃ grahaṇe candrasūryayoḥ |

	bāndhavānāṃ ca maraṇe narakī (?) syāt tato 'nyathā ||

	kāmyāni caiva śrāddhāni śasyante grahaṇādiṣu || iti |

"śrāddhaṃ prati ruciḥ" iti: rucir icchā śrāddhaṃ prati yadā tadaiva tat kāryam ity arthaḥ | cakāro 'nyeṣām api śrāddhakālānāṃ pradarśanārthaḥ | ata eva yamaḥ |

	āṣāḍhyām api kārtikyāṃ māghyāṃ trīn pañca vā dvijān |

	tarpayet pitṛpūrvaṃ tu tasyāpy akṣayyam ucyate ||

devalo 'pi |

	tṛtīyā rohiṇīyuktā vaiśākhasya sitā tu yā |

	madhābhiḥ sahitā kṛṣṇā nabhasye tu trayodaśī ||

	tathā śatabhiṣaḥ śuktā kārtike navamī tathā |

	indukṣayagajacchāyāvaidhṛtīṣu yugādiṣu ||

	ete kālāḥ samuddiṣṭāḥ pitṝṇāṃ prītivardhanāḥ || iti |

yugādayas tu matsyapurāṇe darśitāḥ |

	vaiśākhasya tṛtīyā tu navamī kārtikasya tu |

	mādhe pañcadaśī caiva nabhasye ca trayodaśī |

	yugādayaḥ smṛtā hy etā dattasyākṣayakārakāḥ || iti |

viṣṇupurāṇe 'pi |

	vaiśākhamāsasya sitā tṛtīyā navamy asau kāritkaśuklapakṣe |

	nabhasyamāsasya ca kṛṣṇapakṣe trayodaśī pañcadaśī ca māghe ||

	pānīyam apy atra tilair vimiśraṃ dadyāt pitṛbhyaḥ prayato manuṣyaḥ |

	śrāddhaṃ kṛtaṃ tena samāḥ sahasraṃ rahasyam etat pitaro vadanti ||

atra śuklapakṣe tṛtīyā, pañcadaśī kṛṣṇapakṣe ity anvayaḥ | ata eva nāradīyapurāṇam |

	dve śukle dve ca kṛṣṇe tu yugādyāḥ kavayo viduḥ || iti |

brahmapurāṇe tu mādhasya paurṇamāsī yugādir ity uktam |

	vaiśākhaśuklapakṣasya tṛtīyāyāṃ kṛtaṃ yugam |

	kārtike śuklapakṣe ca tretā ca navame 'hani ||

	atha bhādrapade kṛṣṇe trayodaśyāṃ tu dvāparam |

	māghe ca paurṇamāsyāṃ tu ghoraṃ kaliyugaṃ tathā ||

	yugāraṃbhās tu tithayo yugādyās tena viśrutāḥ |

	sūryasya siṃhasaṃkrāntyām antaṃ kṛtayugasya tu ||

	atha vṛścikasaṃkrāntyām antaṃ tretāyugasya tu |

	jñeyo vṛṣabhasaṃkrāntyāṃ dvāparāntaś ca saṃkhyayā ||

	tathā ca kumbhasaṃkrāntyām antaḥ kaliyuge smṛtaḥ |

	yugādiṣu yugānteṣu śrāddham akṣayyam ucyate || iti |

purāṇe 'pi |

	vaiśākhasya tṛtīyā yā navamī kārtikasya tu |

	paurṇamāsī tu mādhasya nabhasye ca trayodaśī ||

	yugādayaḥ smṛtā hy etā dattasyākṣayakārakāḥ |

	tathā manvantarādau ca deyaṃ śrāddhaṃ vijānatā || iti |

atra kalpabhedena vyavastheti kecit | atra pulastyokto viśeṣaḥ |

	ayanadvitaye śrāddhaṃ viṣuvaddvitaye tathā |

	yugādiṣu ca sarveṣu piṇḍanirvāpaṇād ṛte ||

manvantarādayas tu matsyapurāṇe darśitāḥ |

	aśvayukchuklanavamī kārtike dvādaśī sitā |

	tṛtīyā caitramāsasya tathā bhādrapadasya ca |

	phālgunasya tv amāvāsyā puṣyasyaikādaśī sitā ||

	āṣāḍhasyāpi daśamī māghamāsasya saptamī |

	śrāvaṇasyāṣṭamī kṛṣṇā tathāṣāḍhī ca pūrṇimā ||

	kārtikī phālgunī caitre jyeṣṭhe pañcadaśī sitā |

	manvantarādayas tv ete  dattasyākṣayyakārakāḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ śrāddhakālāḥ**

**atha amāvāsyādvaidhanirṇayaḥ**

tatra gautamaḥ: "atha śrāddham amāvāsyāyāṃ pitṛbhyo dadyāt" iti | amāvāsyā kṛṣṇapakṣasya pañcadaśī tithiḥ | tasyāṃ śrāddhaṃ kāryam ity arthaḥ | tatra kātyāyanokto viśeṣaḥ |

	piṇḍānvahāryakaṃ śrāddhaṃ kṣīṇe rājani śasyate |

	vāsarasya tṛtīye 'ṃśe nātisaṃdhyāsamīpataḥ || iti |

piṇḍapitṛyajñāṅgabhūtānāṃ piṇḍānām anu paścād āhriyate kriyata iti piṇḍānvāhāryakaṃ śrāddham amāvāsyāyāṃ kṣīṇe rājani indau kartavyam ity arthaḥ | so 'pīndukṣayaḥ kadā bhavatīty apekṣite sa evāha |

	aṣṭamāṃśe caturdaśyāḥ kṣīṇo bhavati candramāḥ |

	amāvāsyāṣṭamāṃśe ca punaḥ kila bhaved aṇuḥ || iti |

evaṃ ca tithidvaidhe sinīvālyām eva śrāddhaṃ kāryam ity uktaṃ bhavati | uktaṃ ca vyāsena |

	dṛṣṭacandrā sinīvālī naṣṭacandrā kuhūr matā |

	sinīvālī yadā pitrye kuhūr daive tu karmaṇi ||

hārīto 'pi |

	yasyāṃ saṃdhyāgataḥ somo mṛṇālam iva dṛśyate |

	aparāhṇe kśayas tasyāṃ piṇḍānāṃ karaṇaṃ dhruvam || iti |

yasyāṃ tithau śarvaryāṃ pūrvasyāṃ diśi saṃdhyāgataḥ somaḥ sūkṣma iva dṛśyate tasyām aparāhṇe candrakṣaya iti tatraiva śrāddhaṃ kāryam ity arthaḥ | etac ca karmakālavyāpinyāṃ sinīvālyāṃ draṣṭavyam, anyathā doṣaśravaṇāt | tathā ca bodhāyanaḥ |

	madhyāhnāt parato yatra caturdaśy anuvartate |

	sinīvālī tu sā jñeyā pitṛkārye tu niṣphalā || iti | 

uktalakṣaṇā sinīvālī pitṛkārye niṣphaleti jñeyety arthaḥ | bṛhaspatir api |

	madhyāhnād yā amāvāsyā parastāt sampravartate |

	bhūtaviddhā tu sā jñeyā na sā pañcadaśī bhavet ||

madhyāhnāt parastāt karmakālam atikramety arthaḥ | anenaivābhiprāyeṇa kārṣṇājinir api |

	bhūtaviddhām amāvāsyāṃ mohād ajñānato 'pi vā |

	śrāddhakarmaṇi ye kuryus teṣām āyuḥ prahīyate || iti |

ataḥ karmakālavyāpiny eva sinīvālī grāhyety arthaḥ | ata eva vṛddhamanuḥ |

	yasyām astaṃ ravir yāti pitaras tām upāsate |

	tithiṃ tebhyo yato datto hy aparāhṇaḥ svayaṃbhuvā || iti |

yadā tv evaṃvidhā sanīvālī na labhyate tadā karmakālavyāpinī kuhūr eva grāhyety āha hārītaḥ |

	aparāhṇaḥ pitṝṇāṃ tu yāparāhṇānuyāyinī |

	sā grāhyā pitṛkāryeṣu na pūrvāstānuyāyinī ||

yā kuhūr aparāhṇānuyāyinī saiva grāhyā, na punar evaṃvidhā sinīvālīty arthaḥ | evaṃ ca tithidvaidhe yā karmakālavyāpinī saiva grāhyety uktaṃ bhavati | uktaṃ ca tenaiva |

	bhūtaviddhāpy amāvāsyā pratipanmiśritāpi vā |

	pitrye karmaṇi vidvadbhiḥ grāhyā kutupakālikā ||

bhūtaviddhā caturdaśīviddhā | smṛtyantare 'pi |

	madhyāhnavyāpinī yā tu tithiḥ pūrvā parāpi vā |

	tad ahaḥ karma kurvīta hrāsavṛddhī na kāraṇam || iti |

yadā tu tithidvaye 'pi karmakālavyāpinī na bhavati tadā bhūtaviddhaiva parigrāhyety āha bodhāyanaḥ |

	ghaṭikaikāpy amāvāsyā pratipatsu na cet tathā |

	bhūtaviddhāpi kartavyā daive pitrye ca karmaṇi || iti |

pratipatsu ghaṭikaikā karmakālasaṃbandhinī yadi na syād ity arthaḥ | ata eva jābāliḥ |

	pratipatsv apy amāvāsyā pūrvāhṇavyāpinī yadi |

	bhūtaviddhāpi sā kāryā pitrye karmaṇi sarvadā || iti |

evaṃ ca yad uktaṃ hārītena,

	pūrvāhṇe ced amāvāsyā aparāhṇe ca cet tu sā |

	pratipady api kartavyaṃ śrāddhaṃ śrāddhavido viduḥ ||

iti, yat yatra pūrvedyuś candradarśanāsaṃbhavena piṇḍapitṛyajñotkarṣaḥ, tatra pratipadi piṇḍapitṛyajñavidhānārtham, anyathā pūrvoktavacanavirodhāt | yad api tenaivoktam,

	tulāmakaramīneṣu kanyāyāṃ mithune tathā |

	bhūtaviddhāpy amāvāsyā pūjyā bhavati yatnataḥ ||

iti, etat vratopavāsādiviṣayam iti kaiścid vyākhyātam | yadā tu tithidvaye 'pi karmakālavyāpinī tadā pracetasoktam |

	sinīvālī kuhūś caiva śrutyukte śrāddhakarmaṇi |

	syāyāṃ cet te tu madhyāhne śrāddhaṃ dadyāt kathaṃ tadā ||

	tithikṣaye sinīvālī tithivṛddhau kuhūs tathā |

	sāmye 'pi ca kuhūr jñeyā vedavedāṅgavedibhiḥ ||

sāmye kṣayavṛddhyabhāve | evam aviśeṣeṇa sarveṣām api kṣaye sinīvalyām eva śrāddhaprāptau viśeṣārtham āha laugākṣiḥ |

	sinīvālī dvijaiḥ kāryā sāgnikaiḥ pitṛkarmaṇi |

	strībhiḥ śūdraiḥ kuhūḥ kāryā tathā cānagnikair dvijaiḥ || iti |

evaṃ ca kṣaye sāgnikaiḥ sinīvālyāṃ śrāddhaṃ kāryam | vṛddhau tu sarvair eva paredyuḥ kāryam ity anusaṃdheyam |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanv</span> evam api na kṣayamātre sāgnikaiḥ sanīvālī grāhyā | yatra kṣaye sinīvālyāṃ piṇḍapitṛyajñaḥ tatraiva | anyathā,

	pitṛyajñaṃ tu nirvartya vipraś candrakṣaye 'gnimān |

	piṇḍānvāhāryakaṃ śrāddhaṃ kuryān māsānumāsikam ||

iti manunā sāgnikaiḥ kṛte piṇḍapitṛyajñe śrāddavidhānāghaṭanāt | ato yatra kṣaye kuhvāṃ piṇḍapitṛyajñas tatra sāgnikair api saiva grāhyeti | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span>, dinadvaye 'pi madhyāhnavyāpitve kṣaye sinīvālyām eva candradarśanasaṃbhavena kadācid api piṇḍapitṛyajñāprāpteḥ "yad ahaś candramasaṃ na paśyanti tad ahaḥ piṇḍapitṛyajñaṃ kurvīta" ity āpastambena candrādarśana eva piṇḍapitṛyajñavidhānāt | candrādarśanaṃ ca yatra caturdaśī muhūrtatrayād arvāg eva samāpyate tatraiveti jyotiḥśāstre prasiddham | ato yatra śrāddhadine candrādarśane ca piṇḍapitṛyajñaprāptiḥ tatrāgnimān kṛtvaiva pitṛyajñaṃ śrāddhaṃ kuryād iti manunā niyamyate, na punaḥ sarvatra kṛtapiṇḍapitṛyajñasyaiva agnimataḥ śrāddhādhikāra iti pitṛyajñaśabdasya piṇḍapitṛyajñaparatvam aṅgīkṛtvoktam | paramārthatas tu pitṛyajñaśabdaḥ tarpaṇākhyapitṛyajñapara eva | tad uktaṃ matsyapurāṇe |

	pitṛyajñaṃ tu nirvartya tarpaṇākhyaṃ tu yo 'gnimān |

	piṇḍānvāhāryakaṃ kuryāc chrāddham indukṣaye sadā || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyām amāvāsyādvaidhanirṇayaḥ**

**athānyāny apy amāvāsyaviṣayāṇi kānicid vacanāni likhyante**

tatra vyāsaḥ |

	amā vai somavāreṇa ravivāreṇa saptamī |

	caturthī bhaumavāreṇa viṣuvat sadṛśaṃ phalam ||

amā amāvāsyā | śaṅkho 'pi |

	amāvāsyā tu somena saptamī bhānunā saha |

	caturthī bhūmiputreṇa somaputreṇa cāṣṭamī ||

	catasras tithayas tv etāḥ tulyāḥ syur grahaṇādibhiḥ |

	sarvam akṣayam atroktaṃ snānadānajapādikam ||

bhūmiputro maṅgalaḥ | somaputro budhaḥ | śrīviṣṇupurāṇe 'pi |

	amāvāsyā yadā maitraviśākhāsvātiyoginī |

	śrāddhe pitṛgaṇas tṛptim avāpnoty aṣṭavārṣikīm ||

maitram anūrādhā |

	amāvāsyā yadā puṣye raudra ṛkṣe punarvasau |

	dvādaśābdaṃ tadā tṛptiṃ prayānti pitaro 'rcitāḥ ||

raudram ārdrā |

	vāsavājaikapādṛkṣe pitṝṇāṃ tṛptim icchatām |

	vāruṇenāpy amāvāsyā devānām api durlabhā ||

vāsavaṃ vasudaivatyaṃ dhaniṣṭhānakṣatram | ajaikapādṛkṣaṃ pūrvabhādranakṣatram | vāruṇaṃ śatabhiṣaṅnakṣatram |

	māghāsite pañcadaśī kadācid upaiti yogaṃ yadi vāruṇena |

	ṛkṣeṇa kālaḥ sa paraḥ pitṝṇāṃ na hy alpapuṇyair upalabhyate 'sau ||

	kāle dhaniṣṭhā yadi nāma tasmin bhavet tu bhūpāla tadā pitṛbhyaḥ |

	dattaṃ jalānnaṃ pradadāti tṛptiṃ varṣāyutaṃ tat kulajair manuṣyaiḥ ||

tasmin kāle māghāsitapañcadaśyam ity arthaḥ |

	tatraiva ced bhādrapadās tu pūrvāḥ kāle tadā yat kriyate pitṛbhyaḥ |

	śrāddhaṃ parāṃ tṛptim upetya tena yugān sahasraṃ pitaraḥ svapanti ||

tatraiva tasyām eva pañcadaśyām ity arthaḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyām amāvāsyāviṣayāṇi**

**atha prasaṅgāt parvāpi nirṇīyate**

tatra gobilaḥ: "yaḥ paramo viprakarṣaḥ sūryācandramasoḥ sā paurṇamāsī, yaḥ paramaḥ saṃnikarṣaḥ sāmāvāsyā" iti | te ca dvividhe, tathā ca purāṇam |

	rākā cānumatiś caiva paurṇamāsī dvidhā smṛtā |

	sinīvālī kuhūś caiva amāvāsyā dvidhaiva tu || iti |

atrānumatiḥ sinīvālī ca caturdaśīmiśrā, rākā kuhūś ca pratipanmiśre | tathā ca śrutiḥ: "yā pūrvā paurṇamāsī sānumatiḥ, yottarā sā rākā, yā pūrvāmāvāsyā sā sinīvālī, yottarā sā kuhūḥ" iti | atra vyavasthayā karmanirṇayam āha gobhilaḥ: "pakṣāntā upavastavyāḥ pakṣādayo 'bhiyaṣṭavyāḥ" iti | pakṣāntāḥ pañcadaśya upavastavyās tāsv anvādhānādi kāryam | pakṣādayaḥ pratipadaḥ, tā abhiyaṣṭavyāḥ | tāsu hastāvanejanādy abhījyā kāryety arthaḥ | atra laugākṣiṇokto viśeṣaḥ |

	trīn aṃśān aupavastasya yāgasya caturo viduḥ |

	dvāv aṃśāv utsṛjed antyau yāge ca vrakarmaṇi ||

antyaḥ pādaḥ pañcadaśyā aupavaste 'nvādhānādau parihartavyaḥ, pakṣādeś cāntyaḥ pādaḥ yāge pariharaṇīya ity arthaḥ | kathaṃ tarhi yāge catura ity apekṣite yajñapārśvaḥ |

	pañcadaśyāḥ paraḥ pādaḥ pakṣādeḥ prathamās trayaḥ |

	kālaḥ pārvaṇayāge syād anyathā tu na vidyate ||

vṛddhaśātātapo 'pi |

	parvaṇo yaś caturtho 'ṃśa ādyāḥ pratipadas trayaḥ |

	yāgakālaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ prātar ukto manīṣibhiḥ || iti |

anena pratipaccaturthāṃśe na yaṣṭavyam ity uktaṃ bhavati | uktaṃ ca kātyāyanena |

	na yaṣṭavyaṃ caturthāṃśe yāgaiḥ pratipadaḥ kvacit |

	rakṣāṃsi tad vilumpanti śrutir eṣā sanātanī || iti |

yat tu śrutau "saṃdhau yajeta" iti, tatra saṃdher atisūkṣmatvāt tatra yāgānupapatteḥ tat samīpakālalakṣaṇāyāṃ prastutāyām aviśeṣāt saṃdhiśabdaḥ saṃnihitaparvapratipadātmakakāladvayapara ity avirodhaḥ | ata eva śrutyantaram "saṃdhim abhito yajeta" iti | parvapratipadoḥ saṃdhim abhita ubhayato yajetety arthaḥ | ato yatra parvacaturthāṃśe yāgas tatrādipratipady eva yāgasamāptiḥ, anyathā "saṃdhim abhitaḥ" iti śrutivirodhāt | uktaṃ ca gargeṇa |

	pratipady apraviṣṭāyāṃ yadā tv iṣṭiḥ samāpyate |

	punaḥ praṇīya kṛtsneṣṭiḥ kartavyā yāgavittamaiḥ || iti |

pratipadyoge tu saṃdheḥ pūrvam agnyanvādhānād ity avirodhaḥ | saṃdhiparijñāne tu smṛtyantare viśeṣo darśitaḥ |

	titheḥ parasyā ghaṭikās tu yāḥ syuḥ nyūnās tathā cābhyadhikās tu tāsām |

	ardhaṃ viyojyaṃ ca tathā prayojyaṃ hrāse ca vṛddhau prathame dine tat || iti |

parasyās titheḥ pratipado yā ghaṭikāḥ pūrvasyās titheḥ syuḥ nyūnā adhikā vā tāsām ardhaṃ pūrvasmin dine hrāse viyojyaṃ vṛddhau tu saṃyojyam ity arthaḥ | anena rākākuhvor uttare 'hani ca yat parvapratipadayoḥ ghaṭikāvṛndaṃ tadaharbhir itaṃ tad ekīkṛtya dvedhā vibhajya saṃdhiparijñānaṃ kāryam ity uktaṃ bhavati | evaṃ ca yasminn ahani parvasaṃdhis tasminn uttaredyur vā prātaḥ parvacaturthāṃśādivihitasaṃdhisaṃbhavaḥ tatraiva yāgo nānyatrety anusaṃdheyam | ata eva laugākṣiḥ |

	pūrvāhṇe vātha madhyāhne yadi parva samāpyate |

	upoṣya tatra pūrvedyuḥ tad ahar yāga iṣyate ||

	aparāhṇe 'tha vā rātrau yadi parva samāpyate |

	upoṣya tasminn ahani śvobhūte yāga iṣyate || iti |

tatraiva vihitakālasaṃbhavād iti bhāvaḥ | gṛhyakārikāpi |

	pañcadaśī pratipac ca samete ekadine mahatī yadi tasmin |

	pañcadaśī prakṛter upavāsaḥ pañcadaśīha tanur yadi yāgaḥ || iti |

samete saṃbaddhe ity arthaḥ | anenaivābhiprāyeṇa āpastambo 'pi: "yad ahaḥ purastāc candramāḥ pūrṇa utsarpet tāṃ paurṇamāsīm upavaset | śvaḥ pūriteti vā | kharvikāṃ tṛtīyāṃ vājasaneyinaḥ samāmananti | yad ahar na dṛśyate tad ahar amāvāsyā | śvo nadraṣṭāra iti vā" iti | tatra kharvikāsūtrasyārtha upariṣṭād bhaviṣyati | yad ahaḥ purastāc candramāḥ pūrṇa utsarpet yad ahar na dṛśyate iti ca sūtradvayasyāyam arthaḥ | sarvathā tāvad rākākuhvor eva candramasaḥ pūrṇatvam adarśanatvaṃ ceti jyotiḥśāstre prasiddham | tatra yasminn ahani purastāt pūrvasyāṃ diśi candramāḥ pūrṇa utsarpet udayān na dṛśyeta vā tatra yady apy aparāhṇe rātrau vā sarvasaṃdhiḥ tadā paurṇamāsīm amāvāsyāṃ vopavased iti | yadā tu pūrvāhṇe vā madhyandine vā parvasaṃdhis tadā yasyāhnaś candramāḥ pūritā pūrṇo bhavitā yasyāṃ vā nadraṣṭāro nekṣitāro bhaveyuḥ tām anumatiṃ sinīvālīṃ vopavased iti śvaḥpūritā śvo nadraṣṭāra iti veti sūtradvayasyāyam arthaḥ | uktaṃ ca bhāṣyārthasaṃgrahakāreṇa |

	aparāhṇe 'tha vā rātrau yadi parva samāpyate |

	upoṣyā tatra rākā syāt sā pūrṇotsarpilakṣaṇā ||

	pūrvāhṇe vātha madhyāne yadi parva samāpyate |

	upoṣyānumatis tatra sā śvaḥpūritalakṣaṇā ||

	aparāhṇe kṣapāyāṃ vā parvasaṃdhir bhaved yadi |

	upoṣyā tu kuhūs tatra yad ahar netilakṣaṇā ||

	pūrvāhṇe vātha madhyāhne parvasaṃdhir yadā bhavet |

	tatropoṣyā sinīvālī śvo nadraṣṭāralakṣaṇā || iti |

tatra pūrvāhṇāparāhṇaśabdābhyāṃ dvedhā vibhaktasyāhnaḥ pūrvāparabhāgau pratipādyete | madhyāhnaśabdena tu tayosaṃdhir ity anusaṃdheyam | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanv</span> atra pūrvāhṇādiśabdānāṃ tredhā vibhaktasyāhnaḥ krameṇa bhāgatrayaparatvam astu | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span>, tasmin pakṣe madhyāhnasyāvartanād upari ghaṭikāpañcakaparyantatvāt tatra saṃdhau tad ahar eva yāgaḥ prasajyeta | na ca prasajyatām iti vācyam, tatra prātaḥ parvacaturthāṃśādivihitakālāsaṃbhavena "parvaṇo yaś caturtho 'ṃśaḥ" ityādivacanavirodhāt | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> dvedhā vibhāgena yatrāvartanād upari ghaṭikāmātre parvasaṃdhiḥ tatrottaredyur eva yāga iti tatrāpi kālāsaṃbhavād vacanavirodhas tulya eva |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span>, "parvaṇo yaś caturho 'ṃśaḥ" ityādikālasya yāgānvayāvagateḥ bhavitavyaṃ tāvad yāgasya kālānvayenety upagantavyam | evaṃ ca tatrottaredyur yāge kriyamāṇe na yāgasya kālānvaya iti pūrvedyur eva yāga ity avirodhaḥ | evaṃ sarvatra draṣṭavyam | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanv</span> evaṃ tarhy aparāhṇasaṃdhāv uttaredyur yāgavidhānaṃ virudhyeta |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span>, yatrāparāhṇe parvasaṃdhāv uttaredyuḥ pratipaccaturthāṃśe yāgo na bhavati, tathāvidhāparāhṇasyaivātra grahaṇam ity avirodhaḥ | yuktaṃ caitat, anyathā hemantakāle 'tisvalpatvād ahnāṃ tatra kiṃcid ūnacaturdaśaghaṭikāmātra āvartanaṃ bhavati | tathā tatraiva tithivṛddhau kadācit ṣoḍaśanāḍiko 'pi caturthāṃśo bhavati | tatrāvartanād upari ghaṭikāmātraparvasaṃdhāv uttaredyur eva yāgaḥ prasjyeta, na caitad yuktam, tatra vihitakālāsaṃbhavān na yaṣṭavyam iti niṣedhāt pūrveduyḥ kālasaṃbhavāc ca | atroktāparāhṇaśabdasya saṃkoca eva syāt jyāyān | kiṃ ca grīṣmakāle 'hnām atidīrghatvāt tatra pādādhikaṣoṣaśaghaṭikātmake kāle āvartanaṃ bhavati | tathā tatraiva tithihrāse kadācit sārdhatrayodaśanāḍiko 'pi parvacaturthāṃśo bhavati | tatra yadā pādonāvartanena parvasaṃdhiḥ tadā pūrvāhṇa eva parvasaṃdhir iti tadahar eva yāgaḥ syāt | na caitad yuktam, tatra prātaḥ parvacaturthāṃśādivihitakālāsaṃbhavāt | asmin pakṣe tūttaredyur eva yāgaḥ, tatraiva vihitakālasaṃbhavāt | ata evoktom āpastambenāpi: "kharvikāṃ tṛtīyāṃ vājasaneyinaḥ samāmananti" iti | kharvikām alpikām iti yāvat | alpatvaṃ ca dinārdhatvābhāvāt | uktaṃ ca bhāṣyārthasaṃgrahakāreṇa |

	madhyandināt syād ahanīha yasmin prākparvaṇaḥ saṃdhir iyaṃ tṛtīyā | iti |

amāvāsyāyāṃ tu sutarām atrottaredyur eva yāgaḥ, udayāt prāg eva tasyās tatra prārambhāt | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanv</span> evaṃ tarhi pūrvāhṇasaṃdhau tadahar eva yāgavidhānaṃ virudhyeta | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span>, tasyaitadvyatiriktaviṣayāntarasaṃbhavenāvirodhāt | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> tarhi "pūrvāhṇe vātha madhyāhne" iti laugākṣivacanabalād eva vihitakālābhāve 'pi tatraiva yāgo 'stu | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span>,

	pañcadaśyāḥ paraḥ pādaḥ pakṣādeḥ prathamās trayaḥ |

	kālaḥ pārvaṇayāge syād anyathā tu na vidyate ||

iti vacanārdhāṃśoditakālavyatirekeṇa kālāntarābhāvasmaraṇāt | kiṃ ca, evaṃ sati "parvaṇo yaś caturthāṃśaḥ" ityādikālavidhāyakaśāstrāṇāṃ viṣayāsaṃbhavena vaiyarthyam eva syāt | ato yat kaiścid uktam: "aparāhṇasaṃdhāv uttaredyuḥ pratipaccaturthāṃśe 'pi yāgo na doṣāya" iti, tad apāstam | evaṃ ca yad uktaṃ kātyāyanena, 

	yajanīye 'hni somaś ced vāruṇyāṃ diśi dṛśyate |

	tatra vyāhṛtibhir hutvā daṇḍaṃ dadyād dvijātaye || 

iti, yad api smṛtyantaram,

	trimuhūrtā dvitīyā cet pratipady āparāhṇikī |

	anvādhānaṃ caturdaśyāṃ parataḥ somadarśanāt ||

iti, tat pūrvāhṇaparvasaṃdhiviṣayam ity avagantavyam | yad api vacanāntaram,

	ṣoḍaśe 'hany abhīṣṭeṣṭir madhyā pañcadaśe 'hani |

	caturdaśe jaghanyeṣṭiḥ pāpā saptadaśe 'hani ||

iti, tena saptadaśe 'hanīṣṭiṃ na kuryān nānvādadhīteti tatrānvādhānam eva niṣidhyate na yāgaḥ | tathātve tithivṛddhau viśiṣṭair ananuṣṭhānam eva syāt | ato yajanīyadinād ārabhya saptadaśe 'hny aupavasathakarma na kāryam ity avagantavyam | ata eva bodhāyanaḥ |

	yatraupavasathaṃ karma yajanīyāt trayodaśam |

	bhavet saptadaśaṃ vāpi tat prayatnena varjayet || iti |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> dinadvayasya kṣayavṛddhyoḥ saṃbhavāt trayodaśe 'hani saptadaśe 'hani vā kadācid aupavasathyaṃ karma na prāptam iti kathaṃ niṣedhaḥ |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span>, yady aprāptiḥ tarhi "nāntarkṣe na divi" itivan nityānuvāda iti sarvam anavadyam | paurṇamāsyāṃ tv āpastambokto viśeṣaḥ: "paurṇamāsyām anvādhānaparistaraṇopavāsāt sadyo vā sadyaḥkālāyāṃ sarvaṃ kriyate" iti | asyārthaḥ: sadyaḥkālāyāṃ paurṇamāsyām agnyanvādhānādīni sadyaḥ samāne 'hanit kriyante pūrvedyur vā tatra sarvaṃ brāhmaṇatarpanāntaṃ kriyate | neḍāntādikam ity uktaṃ bhāṣyārthasaṃgrahakāreṇa |

	anvāhitiś cāstaraṇopavāsāḥ pūrvedyur ete khalu paurṇamāsyām |

	āvartanāt prāg yadi parvasaṃdhiḥ sadyas tadā vā kriyate samastam || iti |

āvartanāt prāk saṅgavād ūrdhvam iti śeṣaḥ,

	saṃdhiś cet saṅgavād ūrdhvaṃ prāk paryāvartanād raveḥ |

	sā paurṇamāsī vijñeyā sadyaḥkālavidhau tithiḥ ||

iti kātyāyanasmaraṇāt | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">kecit</span> tu, "paurṇamāsyām" ityādi "sadyo vā" ity etadantam ekaṃ sūtram, aparaṃ tu "sadyaḥkālāyāṃ sarvaṃ kriyate" iti vadanti | tatra sarvasyāṃ paurṇamāsyām agnyanvādhānādi sadyaḥ pūrvedyur vā kriyata iti pūrvasūtrasyārthaḥ | dvitīyasya tu sadyaḥkālā vikṛtiḥ tasyāṃ sarvaṃ brāhmaṇatarpaṇāntaṃ kriyate neḍāntādikam iti |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">naitad yuktam</span>, aparāhṇasaṃdhau sayaḥkālapakṣe "saṃdhim abhito yajeta" iti śrutivirodhāt evaṃ prakṛtāv uktam | vikṛtau yady api "darśapūrṇamāsāv iṣṭīnāṃ prakṛtiḥ" ity anena darśapūrṇamāsikavidhyantātideśād atrāpi sa eva parvacaturthāṃśādilakṣaṇaḥ kāla iti pratibhāti | tathāpi "yadīṣṭyā yadi paśunā yadi somena yajetāmāvāsyāyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ vā yajeta" ity āpastambena vikṛtau punaḥkālavidhānāt pañcadaśyām eva yāgasamāpattiḥ, ato yatra saṃpūrnaiva pañcadaśī pratipac ca tatra pañcadaśyām eva vikṛtiṃ samāpyānantaraṃ prakṛter agnyanvādhānādi | khaṇdatithau yadā pūrvāhṇe parvasaṃdhiḥ tadā pūrvedyur upadiṣṭakālāsaṃbhavāt saṃbhave 'pi karmopakramadaśāyām asaṃbhavena sāṅgapradhānāvyāpitatvāt "sāṅgapradhānaṃ deśe kāle kartarīti nirdiśyate" ity āpastambena sāṅgasyaiva vihitakālasaṃbandhavidhānāt | uktaṃ paredyur api | prakṛteḥ pūrvoktatvāt "apūrvam ante syāt" ity āpastambenaiva vikṛteḥ pūrvaṃ prakṛtividhānāt anantaram evātideśikapratipadādyabhāgatraye 'ṅgapradhānaparyāpter vikṛtyanuṣṭhānam avagantavyam | yadā tv aparāhṇe rātrau vā parvasaṃdhiḥ tadā tadahar eva yāgaḥ, tatraivopadiṣṭakālasaṃbhavāt | etat sarvam abhisaṃdhāyoktam |

	āvartanāt prāg yadi parvasaṃdhiḥ kṛtvā tu tasmin prakṛtiṃ vikṛtyāḥ |

	tadaiva yāgaḥ parato yadi syāt tasmin vikṛtyāḥ prakṛteḥ śva eva || iti |

evaṃ paśāv api draṣṭavyam | ata eva tatrāpy uktam |

	arvāg adhno bhavati niyataḥ parvasaṃdhiḥ purastāt

	kṛtvā tasminn ahani tu paśūn sadya eva dvyahaṃ vā |

	ārabhyātha prakṛtir atha cet parvasaṃdhiḥ parastāt 

	kṛtvā tasmin prakṛtim atha tu syāt paśuḥ sadya eva || iti |

pūrvāhṇasaṃdhāv uttaredyur vihitakālāsaṃbhavāt sadya evety uktam | upadeśas tatrāpi dvyahakālatām āha | tan na yaṣṭavyam ityādivacanaviruddham ity upekṣaṇīyam eva ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ parvanirṇayaḥ**

**atha prasaṅgāt tithidvaidhanirṇayaḥ**

tatra skandapurāṇam |

	pratipatprabhṛtayaḥ sarvā udayādodayād raveḥ |

	saṃpūrṇā iti vikhyātā harivāsaravarjitāḥ || iti |

atra saṃpūrṇāsu niḥsaṃdigdham eva karmānuṣṭhānam | yatra punaḥ kṣayavṛddhibhyāṃ tithidvaividhyaṃ tatra nigamoktam |

	yugmāgniyugabhūtānāṃ ṣaṇmunyor vasurandhrayoḥ |

	rudreṇa dvādaśī yuktā caturdaśyā ca pūrṇimā ||

	pratipadāpy amāvāsyā tithyor yugmaṃ mahāphalam |

	etad vyastaṃ mahādoṣaṃ hanti puṇyaṃ purākṛtam || iti |

tatra yugmādirandhrāntyaiḥ śabdaiḥ krameṇa dvitīyādinavamyantānāṃ grahaṇam, tithyor yugmam ity abhidhānāt | rudra ekādaśī | dvitīyādipratipadantāsu krameṇa dvayor dvayos tithyoḥ parasparam eva yugmaṃ mahāphalam, na punar vyastatithyantarayugam ity arthaḥ | anenoktayugmatithisaptake pūrvā tithiḥ uttaraviddhā grāhyā | uttarā tu pūrvaviddhety uktaṃ bhavati | tṛtīyādivad daśamītrayodaśyāv api pūrvaviddhe | tathā ca paiṭhīnasiḥ |

	pañcamī saptamī caiva daśamī ca trayodaśī |

	pratipannavamī caiva kartavyā saṃmukhā tithiḥ || iti |

saṃmukhā pūrvaviddhety arthaḥ,

	saṃmukhā nāma sāyāhnavyāpinī dṛśyate yadā | 

iti skandapurāṇe darśanāt | yat tu nigamavākye tṛtīyāpaurṇamāsyoḥ pūrvaviddhatvam uktam, tat vrataviśeṣābhiprāyam | ata eva brahmakaivarte |

	rambhākhyāṃ varjayitvā tu tṛtīyāṃ dvijasattama |

	anyeṣu sarvakāryeṣu gaṇayuktā praśasyate ||

	bhūtaviddhā na kartavyā amā pūrṇā kadācana |

	varjayitvā muniśreṣṭha sāvitrīvratam uttamam || iti |

rambhākhyāṃ tṛtīyāṃ rambhātṛtīyākhyaṃ vratam ity arthaḥ | gaṇayuktā caturthīyuktā amā amāvāsyā | evaṃ ca yad uktaṃ nāradīyapurāṇe,

	darśaṃ ca pūrṇamāsaṃ ca pituḥ sāṃvatsaraṃ dinam |

	pūrvaviddham akurvāṇo narakaṃ pratipadyate ||

iti, tad api sāvitrīvrataviṣayam ity anusaṃdheyam | upavāse tu parānvitaiva grāhyā | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	ekādaśy aṣṭamī ṣaṣṭhī paurṇamāsī caturdaśī |

	amāvāsyā tṛtīyā ca tā upoṣyāḥ parānvitāḥ || iti |

vṛddhavasiṣṭho 'pi |

	dvitīyā pañcamī vedhāt daśamī ca trayodaśī |

	caturdaśī copavāse hanyuḥ pūrvottare tithī ||

	upavāse saptamī tu vedhā dhanty uttaraṃ dinam || iti |

dvitīyādyās tithayo vedhāt upavāse svapūrvottare tithī hanyuḥ, saptamī tu svottarām evety arthaḥ | anena pratipat tṛtīyā ca dvitīyāviddhe na grāhye ity uktaṃ bhavati | evaṃ pañcamyādiṣv api draṣṭavyam | evaṃ ca yan nigamavākye caturthyā uttaraviddhatvam uktam, tad upavāsavyatiriktaviṣayam ity avagantavyam, asmin vākye pūrvaviddhāyā upādeyatvasmaraṇāt | yad api brahmakaivarte,

	pratipatsaṃmukhā kāryā dvitīyā dvijasattama |

iti pratipadviddhāyā upādeyatvam uktam, tad apy upvāsavyatiriktaviṣayam | upavāse parividdhāyā evopādeyatvasmaraṇāt | tathā ca śrīviṣṇupurāṇe |

	ekādaśy aṣṭamī ṣaṣṭhī dvitīyā ca caturdaśī |

	amāvāsyā tṛtīyā ca upoṣyāḥ syuḥ parānvitāḥ || iti |

atra caturdaśyāṃ paraviddhatvaṃ śuklapakṣābhiprāyam | ata eva nigamaḥ |

	ekādaśy aṣṭamī ṣaṣṭhī śuklapakṣe caturdaśī |

	puṇyāḥ pareṇa saṃyuktāḥ parāḥ pūrveṇa saṃyutāḥ || iti |

parā anantarā ity arthaḥ,

	nāgaviddhā tu yā ṣaṣṭhī rudraviddho divākaraḥ |

	kāmaviddho bhaved viṣṇur na grāhyās teṣu vāsarāḥ ||

	navamy ekādaśī caiva diśā viddhā yadā bhavet |

	tadā varjyā viśeṣeṇa gaṅgāmbhaḥ śvadṛtau yathā ||

iti purāṇasmaraṇāt | nāgaḥ pañcamī rudro 'ṣṭamī divākaraḥ saptamī kāmas trayodaśī | viṣṇuḥ dvādaśī | dik dasamī | evam aṣṭamy api draṣṭavyā | ata eva smṛtyantaram |

	kṛṣṇapakṣe 'ṣṭamī caiva kṛṣṇapakṣe caturdaśī |

	pūrvaviddhā tu kartavyā parividdhā na kasyacit ||

	śuklapakṣe 'ṣṭamī caiva śuklapakṣe caturdaśī |

	pūrvaviddhā na kartavyā kartavyā parasaṃyutā ||

	upavāsādikāryeṣu hy eṣa dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ || iti |

trayodaśyāḥ paraviddhatvaṃ kṛṣṇapakṣābhiprāyam | ata eva nigamaḥ |

	ṣaṣṭy aṣṭamī tathā darśaḥ kṛṣṇapakṣe trayodaśī |

	etāḥ parayutāḥ pūjyāḥ parāḥ pūrvayutās tathā ||

parā anantarā ity arthaḥ | evaṃ ca yad uktaṃ mārkaṇdeyena,

	śuklapakṣe tithir grāhyā yasyām abhyudito raviḥ |

	kṛṣṇapakṣe tithir grāhyā yasyām astamito raviḥ ||

iti, tat śuklakṛṣṇapakṣavyavasthayā vyavasthitacaturdaśyādiviṣayam ity avagantavyam | yad api devalenoktam,

	yāṃ tithiṃ samanuprāpya udayaṃ yāti bhāskaraḥ |

	sā tithiḥ sakalā jñeyā snānadānajapādiṣu ||

iti, tad yāsāṃ tithīnām uttaraviddhānām upādeyatvam uktaṃ tadviṣayam | yad api tenaivoktam,

	yāṃ tithiṃ samanuprāpya astaṃ yāti divākaraḥ |

	sā tithiḥ sakalā jñeyā dānādhyayanakarmasu ||

iti, tad api yās tithayaḥ pūrvaviddhāḥ satyo grāhyāḥ tadviṣayam | sakalā saṃpūrṇety arthaḥ | etac ca udayavyāpinyās tither alpatvena tithyantarānuṣṭhāne 'pi tasyām eva tithāv anuṣṭhitaṃ bhavatīti vaktum | anenaivābhiprāyeṇa bhaviṣyatpurāṇe 'pi |

	vratopavāsaniyame ghaṭikaikā yadā bhavet |

	sā tithiḥ sakalā jñeyā pitrarthe cāparāhṇikī || iti |

ato 'nyatra karmānuṣṭhāne tithivṛddhihrāsābhyām upayoga iti nirṇayaḥ | uktaṃ ca viṣṇudharmottare |

	sā tithis tad ahorātraṃ yasyām astamito raviḥ |

	tadā karmāṇi kurvīta hrāsavṛddhī na kāraṇam || iti |

yadā tu nottaredyuḥ udayavyāpinī kiṃ tu pūrvedyuḥ niṣiddhatithividdhaiva, tadā smṛtyantaroktam |

	ekādaśī tṛtīyā ca ṣaṣṭhī caiva trayodaśī |

	pūrvaviddhā tu kartavyā yadi n syāt pare 'hani || iti |

evaṃ ca yad uktam,

	vardhamānasya pakṣasya udayāt pūjyate tithiḥ |

	yadā pakṣaḥ kṣayaṃ yāti tadā syād āparāhṇikī ||

iti, tatra pakṣakṣaye prāyeṇa paredyur udayavyāpinyā asaṃbhavāt pūrvaviddhaiva parigrāhyeti pūrvavacanena samānārtham | atra viśeṣam āha ṛśyaśṛṅgaḥ |

	aviddhāni niṣiddhaiś ca na labhyante dināni tu |

	muhūrtaiḥ pañcabhir viddhā grāhyaivaikādaśī tithiḥ || iti |

niṣiddhair dinair aviddhāni dināni yadi na labhyante tadoktalakṣaṇāni grāhyāṇīty arthaḥ | yadā caivaṃvidhāpi tithiḥ na labhyate tadāpi tenaivoktam |

	aviddhānām alābhe tu payodadhighṛtena vā |

	sakṛd evālpam aśnīyād upavāsas tv asau bhavet || iti |

"sā tithiḥ sakalā jñeyā" ity asya kvacid apavādam āha nāradīyapurāṇe vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	pāraṇe maraṇe nṝṇāṃ tithis tātkālikī smṛtā |

	pitrye 'stamayavelāyāṃ spṛṣṭā pūrṇā nigadyate || iti |

pāraṇe maraṇe vā tātkāliky eva tithiḥ na punaḥ sā tithiḥ sakalā jñeyety etad bhavatīty arthaḥ | evaṃ manvādyādāv api draṣṭavyam | ata eva skandapurāṇam |

	manvādau ca yugādau ca grahaṇe candrasūryayoḥ |

	vyatīpāte ca vaidhṛtyāṃ tatkālavyāpinī tithiḥ |

	naktavrate ca saṃprāpte tatkālavyāpinī tithiḥ || iti |

tasya naktavratasya yaḥ kālaḥ pradoṣākhyaḥ tadvyāpinī tithiḥ grāhety arthaḥ | tathā ca vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	pradoṣavyāpinī grāhyā tithir nakavrate sadā |

	ekādaśīṃ vinā sarvāḥ śukle kṛṣṇe samāḥ smṛtāḥ || iti |

pradoṣaparimāṇaṃ tu skandapurāṇe uktam |

	udayāt prāktanī saṃdhyā ghaṭikātrayam ucyate |

	sāyaṃsaṃdhyā trighaṭikā astād upari bhāsvataḥ |

	trimuhūrtaṃ pradoṣaḥ syād ravāv astamite tataḥ || iti |

yad atra saṃdhyādvaye maunādi kāryam, tad etāvati kāle kāryam ity abhiprāyaḥ | yadā tu dinadvaye 'pi pradoṣavyāpinī tithir na bhavati, tadā tu skandapurāṇoktam |

	pradoṣavyāpinī na syād divā naktaṃ vidhīyate |

	ātmano dviguṇāṃ chāyām atikrāmati bhāskare ||

	tannaktaṃ naktam ity āhuḥ na naktaṃ niśi bhojanam |

	evaṃ jñātvā tato vidvān sāyāhne tu bhujikriyām ||

	kuryān naktavratī naktaphalaṃ prāpnoti niścitam || iti |

nakṣatropavāse tu viṣṇunoktam |

	upoṣitavyaṃ nakṣatraṃ yasminn astam iyād raviḥ |

	yatra vā yujyate rāma niśīthaḥ śaśinā saha || iti |

yatra vā niśītho 'rdharātraḥ śaśinā nakṣatrenāstamayād upary ārabdhena saṃyujyate tad vā nakṣatram upoṣitavyam ity arthaḥ | tathā ca sumantuḥ |

	yatrārdharātrād arvāk tu nakṣatraṃ prāpyate tithau |

	tan nakṣatravrataṃ kuryād atīte pāraṇaṃ bhavet || iti |

prāpyate prārabhyata ity arthaḥ | atīte tasmin nakṣatra iti śeṣaḥ | evaṃ tithiprayuktopavāse 'pi draṣṭavyam |

	tithinakṣatraniyame tithibhānte ca pāraṇam |

	ato 'nyathā pāraṇāt tu vratabhaṅgam avāpnuyāt ||

iti smaraṇāt | etan nakṣatraprayuktopavāsaviṣayam | nakṣatrayuktāyāṃ tithau śrīviṣṇupurāṇe uktam |

	yāḥ kāścit tithayaḥ proktāḥ puṇyā nakṣatrayogataḥ |

	tāsv eva tad vrataṃ kuryāc chravaṇadvādaśīṃ vinā || iti |

kathaṃ tarhi śravaṇadvādaśyām ity apekṣite matsyapurāṇam |

	dvādaśyāṃ śuklapakṣasya nakṣatraṃ śravaṇaṃ yadi |

	upoṣyaikādaśīṃ tatra dvādaśyāṃ pūjayed dharim || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ tithidvaidhanirṇayaḥ**

**atha tithiprasaṅgād ekādaśy api nirṇīyate**

tatrādau ekādaśīmahimā | tatra nāradīyapurāṇe vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	ekādaśīsamutthena vahninā pātakendhanam |

	bhasmatāṃ yāti rājendra api janmaśatodbhavam ||

	nedṛśaṃ pāvanaṃ kiṃcin narāṇāṃ bhūpa vidyate |

	yādṛśaṃ padmanābhasya dinaṃ pātakahānidam ||

	tāvat pāpāni dehe 'smin tiṣṭhanti manujādhipa |

	yāvan nopavasej jantuḥ padmanābhadinaṃ śubham ||

	aśvamedhasahasrāṇi vājapeyaśatāni ca |

	ekādaśyupavāsasya kalā nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm ||

	ekādaśendriyaiḥ pāpaṃ yat kṛtaṃ bhavati prabho |

	ekādaśyupavāsena tat sarvaṃ vikalaṃ nayet ||

	ekādaśīsamaṃ kiṃcit prāpatrāṇaṃ na vidyate |

	svargamokṣapradā hy eṣā rājyaputraprasādhinī ||

	sukalatrapradā hy eṣā śarīrārogyadāyinī |

	na gaṅgā na gayā bhūpa na kāśī na ca puṣkaram ||

	na cāpi kauravakṣetraṃ na revā na ca devikā |

	yamunā candrabhāgā ca tulyā na ca harer dināt ||

	anāyāsena rājendra prāpyate vaiṣṇavaṃ padam |

	cintāmaṇisamā hy eṣā atha vāpi nidheḥ samā ||

	sā kalpapādapaprakhyā devagor upamātha vā ||

nārado 'pi |

	ekām ekādaśīṃ vāpi samupoṣya janārdanam |

	kāmenāpi samabhyarcya saṃsārān muktim āpnuyāt ||

	prasaṅgād atha vā dambhāl lobhād vā tridaśādhipa |

	ekādaśyām anaśnan yaḥ sarvaduḥkhād vimucyate || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyām ekādaśīmahimā**

**athaikādaśīnirṇayaḥ**

tatra devalaḥ |

	na śaṅkhena pibet toyaṃ nāśnīyāt kūrmasūkarau |

	ekādaśyāṃ na bhuñjīta pakṣayor ubhayor api ||

kātyāyano 'pi |

	yāni kāni ca pāpāni brahmahatyāsamāni ca |

	annam āśritya tiṣṭhanti saṃprāpte harivāsare ||

	raṭantīha purāṇāni bhūyo bhūyo varānane |

	na bhoktavyaṃ na bhoktavyaṃ saṃprāpte harivāsare || iti |

na bhoktavyam upoṣitavyam ity arthaḥ | ata eva nāradaḥ |

	nityaṃ bhaktisamāyuktair narair viṣṇuparāyaṇaiḥ |

	pakṣe pakṣe tu kartavyam ekādaśyām upoṣaṇam || iti |

atropoṣaṇaṃ nityaṃ kartavyam ity anvayaḥ | anenaikādaśīvratasya nityatvam uktaṃ bhavati | ata evākaraṇe doṣaḥ purāṇe darśitaḥ |

	pratigrāsaṃ sa bhuṅkte 'nnaṃ kilbiṣaṃ śvānaviṭsamam |

	ekādaśyāṃ suraśreṣṭha yo bhuṅkte dvijajanmavān ||

	ekādaśyāṃ tu yo bhuṅkte śaktimān nirupadravaḥ |

	surāpānasamaṃ pāpaṃ bhavet tasya na saṃśayaḥ ||

	madyapānāt suraśreṣṭha pātaiva narakaṃ vrajet |

	ekādaśyannakāmas tu pitṛbhiḥ saha majjati || iti |

ataḥ pakṣadvaye 'py ekādaśyām upavased iti bhāvaḥ | etac ca pakṣadvayopavāsavidhānaṃ vanasthādiviṣayam (?) | ata eva gobhilaḥ |

	ekādaśyām na bhuñjīta pakṣayor ubhayor api |

	vanasthayatidharmo 'yaṃ śuklām eva sadā gṛhī || iti |

evaṃ brahmacāryāder api draṣṭavyam | ata eva smṛtyantaram |

	ekādaśyāṃ na bhuñjīta pakṣayor ubhayor api |

	brahmacārī ca nārī ca śuklām eva sadā gṛhī || iti |

gṛhī putravān iti śeṣaḥ, tasya kṛṣṇaikādaśyām upavāsaniṣedhasmaraṇāt |

	saṃkrāntyām upavāsaṃ tu kṛṣṇaikādaśivāsare |

	candrasūryagrahe caiva na kuryāt putravān gṛhī ||

	ekādaśyāṃ tu kṛṣṇāyāṃ saṃkrāntau ca raves tathā |

	pāraṇaṃ copavāsaṃ ca na kuryāt putravān gṛhī ||

smṛtyantare 'pi |

	ādityavāre saṃkrāntyām asitaikādaśīdine |

	vyatīpāte kṛte śrāddhe putrī nopavased gṛhī ||

putrāṇe 'pi |

	saṃkrāntyām upavāsena pāraṇena yudhiṣṭhita |

	ekādaśyāṃ ca kṛṣṇāyāṃ jyeṣṭhaḥ putro vinaśyati ||

na caivaṃ sati śuklaikādaśyāṃ saṃkrāntyādiyoge gṛhiṇaḥ putravato nopavāsa iti śaṅkanīyam | yata āha jaiiniḥ |

	āditye 'hani saṃkrāntau grahaṇe candrasūryayoḥ |

	pāraṇaṃ copavāsaṃ ca na kuryāt putravān gṛhī ||

	tannimittopavasasya niṣedho 'yam udāhṛtaḥ |

	nānuṣaṅgakṛto grāhyo yato nityam upoṣaṇam || iti |

tannimittasya ādityavārādinimittasya pratiṣedhaḥ, na punar ekādaśyām ādityavārādyanvayanibandhanopavāsaniṣedhaḥ, yata ekādaśyāṃ nityam upoṣaṇam ity arthaḥ | kecit: asyaikādaśīprakaraṇapāṭhāt tacchabdasya prakaraṇasaṃnihitaikādaśīparatvād anuṣaṅgakṛta ity asya kṛcchraprāptopavāsaparatvād gṛhiṇaḥ putravataḥ saṃkrāntyādiyuktāyām ekādaśyām upavāsaniṣedhaparam etad iti varṇayanti | tan mandam: vākyasaṃnidheḥ prakaraṇasaṃnidhitaḥ śīghrabhāvitvāt | anyathā ekādaśyāṃ rāhudarśanāsaṃbhavena tatra kathaṃ tacchabdopapattiḥ | atha rāhudarśanamātraparatvaṃ tarhi sakṛd uccharitasyārthadvayaparatvam iti vairūpyaṃ syāt, ataḥ pūrvoktaiva vyākhyā jyāyasī | ata eva nāradaḥ |

	bhānuvārasamopetā tathā saṃkrāntisaṃyutā |

	ekādaśī sadopoṣyā putrapautravardhinī ||

purāṇe 'pi |

	ekādaśyāṃ yadā vatsa ādityasya dinaṃ bhavet |

	tatropoṣyā prayatnena putrpautravivardhinī ||

anye: gṛhiṇaḥ putravataḥ śuklaikādaśyām upavāsaḥ kṛṣṇaikādaśyām niyamarahitam abhojanamātram iti vadanti, tat svabuddhimātraparikalpitam ity upekṣaṇīyam | yat tu nāradīyapurāṇe rukmāṅgadasya putrapautravato harivāsaramātropavāsaniṣedhāya brāhmaṇaṃ prati yamavacanam,

	manuṣyāḥ pitṛbhiḥ sārdhaṃ tathaiva ca pitāmahaiḥ |

	teṣām apīha pitaraḥ pitṝṇāṃ pitaras tathā ||

	atha mātāmahā yānti teṣāṃ ye janakās tathā |

	teṣām api janayitāro janitṝṇāṃ tu pūrvajāḥ ||

	prayānti vaiṣṇavaṃ lokam upoṣya harivāsaram |

	eṣa daṇḍaḥ paṭo hy eṣa tava padbhyāṃ niyojitaḥ ||

	lokapālatvam atulam ārjitaṃ yena bhūbhujā |

	tam ekaṃ vadatāṃ śreṣṭha saṃprāpte harivāsare ||

	yadi cālayase dhairyāt tato 'haṃ tava kiṃkaraḥ ||

iti, tatrāpi harivāsaragrahaṇaṃ rukmāṅgadasya vihitaikādaśīparam ity avagantavyam | ato gṛhiṇaḥ putravataḥ śuklaikādaśyām upavāsaḥ itareṣāṃ tu ubhayor iti siddham | evaṃ ca yad uktaṃ viṣṇudharmottare,

	brahmahā sa bhavet stenaḥ surāpo gurutalpagaḥ |

	vivecayati yo mohād ekādasyoḥ sitāsite || 

iti, yad api purāṇe, 

	mātṛhā pitṛhā caiva bhrātṛhā guruhā tathā |

	ekādaśyāṃ tu bhuñjānaḥ pakṣayor ubhayor api ||

iti, tat putravadgṛhivyatiriktaviṣayam ity anusaṃdheyam | evam uktarītyā vyavasthāsaṃbhave 'pi kecit "na kuryāt putravā gṛhī" ity evamādīnāṃ kāmyopavāsaviṣayatvaṃ parikalpya gṛhiṇaḥ putravato 'pi kṛṣṇaikādaśyām apy upavāsaṃ varṇayanti | yad atra yuktaṃ tad grāhyam | yat punar āpastambenoktam,

	āhitāgnir anaḍvāṃś ca brahmacārī ca te trayaḥ |

	aśnanta eva siddhyanti naiṣāṃ siddhir anaśnatām ||

iti, tat ekādaśīvyatirikaviṣayam | ata eva agnipurāṇam |

	gṛhastho brahmacārī ca āhitāgnis tathaiva ca |

	ekādaśyāṃ na bhuñjīta pakṣayor ubhayor api || iti |

yad api purāṇe,

	śrāddhe janmadine caiva saṃkrāntyāṃ rāhusūtake |

	upavāsaṃ na kurvīta yadīcchec chreya ātmanaḥ ||

iti śrāddhe upavāsaniṣedhaparaṃ ca vacanam, tad apy ekādaśīvyatiriktaviṣayam | ata eva smṛtyantaram |

	upavāso yadā nityaḥ śrāddhaṃ naimittikaṃ bhavet |

	upavāsaṃ tadā kuryād āghrāya pitṛsevitam || iti |

upavāsalakṣaṇaṃ vyāsenoktam |

	upāvṛttasya pāpebhyo yas tu vāso guṇaiḥ saha |

	upavāsaḥ sa vijñeyo sarvabhogavivarjitaḥ || iti |

pāpebhya upāvṛttasya guṇair ekabhakādiniyamaiḥ saha yo vāsaḥ tāmbūlādibhogarahita upavāsa ity arthaḥ | te ca guṇā nāradīyapurāṇe darśitāḥ |

	tasyaivaṃ krīḍamānasya mohinyā saha pārthiva |

	rukmāṅgadasya śrotrābhyāṃ paṭahadhvanirāgataḥ ||

	mattebhakumbhasaṃsthas tu dharmāṅgadamate sthitaḥ |

	prātar haridinaṃ lokās tiṣṭhadhvaṃ caikabhojanāḥ ||

	akṣāralavaṇāḥ sarve haviṣyānnaniṣeviṇaḥ |

	avanītalpaśayanāḥ priyāsaṅgavivarjitāḥ ||

	smaradhvaṃ devam īśānaṃ purāṇaṃ puruṣottamam |

	sakṛdbhojanayuktāś ca upavāse bhaviṣyatha ||

	aṣṭavarṣādhiko martyo hy aśītir na hi pūryate |

	yo bhuṅkte māmake rāṣṭre viṣṇor ahani pāpakṛt ||

	sa me vadhyaś ca daṇḍyaś ca nirvāsyo viṣayād bahiḥ || iti |

upavāse kṛte dvādaśyām ity arthaḥ | devalo 'pi |

	daśamyām ekabhuktas tu māṃsamaithunavarjitaḥ |

	ekādaśyām upavaset pakṣayor ubhayor api ||

	brahmacaryaṃ tathā śaucaṃ satyam āmiṣavarjanam |

	vrateṣv etāni catvāri variṣṭhānīti niścayaḥ ||

	strīṇāṃ tu prekṣaṇāt sparśāt tābhiḥ saṃkathanād api |

	niṣyandate brahmacaryaṃ na dāreṣv ṛtusaṃgamāt ||

	asakṛjjalapānāc ca akṛttāmbūlacarvaṇāt |

	upavāso viniśyeta divāsvāpāc ca maithunāt ||

vyāso 'pi |

	puṣpālaṃkāravastrāṇi gandhudhūpānulepanam |

	upavāse na duṣyeta dantadhāvanam añjanam || iti |

etat puṇyajanakopavāse strīviṣayam iti kaiścid uktam | dantadhāvanam atra parṇādinā, na kāṣṭhena,

	upavāse tathā śrāddhe na khāded dantadhāvanam |

	dantānāṃ kāṣṭhasaṃyogaḥ hanti sapta kulāny api ||

iti tenaivoktatvāt | viṣṇur api: "patitapāṣaṇḍasaṃbhāṣaṇānṛtasteyādikaṃ varjayet" iti | kūrmapurāṇe 'pi |

	kāṃsyaṃ māṃsaṃ masūraṃ ca caṇakaṃ kodramāṣakān |

	śākaṃ madhu parānnaṃ ca tyajed upavasan striyam || iti |

upavasan upavatsyann ity arthaḥ | ato daśamyām ete niyamāḥ | smṛtyantare 'pi |

	asatyabhāṣaṇaṃ dyūtaṃ divāsvāpaṃ ca maithunam |

	ekādaśyāṃ na kurvīta upavāsaparo naraḥ || iti |

brahmāṇḍapurāṇe 'pi |

	kāṃsyaṃ māṃsaṃ surāṃ kṣaudraṃ tailaṃ vitathabhāṣaṇam |

	vyavāyaṃ ca pravāsaṃ ca divāsvāpam athāñjanam ||

	tilapiṣṭaṃ masūraṃ ca dvādaśaitāni vaiṣṇavaḥ |

	dvādaśyāṃ varjayen nityaṃ sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ||

bṛhaspatir api |

	divānidrāṃ parānnaṃ ca punar bhojanamaithune |

	kṣaudraṃ kāṃsyāmiṣaṃ tailaṃ dvādaśyām aṣṭa varjayet ||

aṅgirā api |

	sāyam ādyantayor ahnoḥ sāyaṃ prātaś ca madhyame |

	upavāsaphalaprepsur jahyād bhaktacatuṣṭayam || iti |

na cātra phalaśravaṇāt kāmyopavāsaviṣayam iti śaṅkanīyam, nitye 'py upāttaduritakṣayādiphalasaṃbandhāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">kecit</span> tu: nitye phalābhāvād yāny ekabhaktānīti tāni,

	ya icched viṣṇusāyujyaṃ śriyaṃ santatim eva ca |

	ekādaśyāṃ na bhuñjīta pakṣayor ubhayor api ||

ityādivihitakāmyopavāsaviṣayāṇīti varṇayanti | yad atra yuktaṃ tad grāhyam | atropavāsagrahaṇavidhim āha devalaḥ |

	gṛhītvaudumbaraṃ pātraṃ vāripūrṇam udaṅmukhaḥ |

	upavāsaṃ tu gṛhṇīyāt yad vā saṃkalpayed budhaḥ || iti |

audumbaraṃ tāmramayaṃ pātraṃ jalapūrṇam udaṅmukhaḥ ādāya upavāsaṃ gṛhṇīyāt, yad vā saṃkalpayet saṃkalpamātraṃ kuryād ity arthaḥ | atra pātragrahaṇaṃ prathamasaṃkalpaviṣayaṃ kāmyopavāsaviṣayaṃ ceti <span style="text-decoration:underline;">kaiścid</span> uktam | saṃkalpamantro 'pi tenaiva darśitaḥ |

	ekādaśyāṃ nirāhāro bhūtvāham apare 'hani |

	bhokṣyāmi puṇḍarīkākṣa gatir mama bhavācyuta || iti |

viṣṇus tu mantrāntaram āha |

	ekādaśyāṃ nirāhāraḥ sthitvāham apare 'hani |

	bhokṣyāmi puṇḍarīkākṣa śaraṇaṃ me bhavācyuta || iti |

mantroccāraṇānantaraṃ kātyāyanaḥ |

	ity uccārya tato vidvān puṣpāñjalim athārpayet | iti |

evam upavāsasamarpaṇam api draṣṭavyam | tad āha nāradaḥ |

	mantram uccārya yatnena puṣpāñjalim athārpayet |

	ajñānatimirāndhasya vratenānena keśava ||

	prasīda sumukho nātha jñānadṛṣṭiprado bhava |

	evaṃ samarpayed vidvān pāraṇaṃ samanantaram || iti |

etac ca sūtakādāv api kāryam | tad uktaṃ viṣṇurahasye |

	paramāpadam āpanno harṣe vā samupasthite |

	sūtake mṛtake vāpi na tyājyaṃ dvādaśīvratam || iti |

atra varāhapurāṇokto viśeṣaḥ |

	sūtake tu naraḥ snātvā praṇamya manasā harim |

	ekādaśyāṃ na bhuñjīta vratam etan na lupyate ||

	dvādaśyāṃ tu tato bhuktvā sūtakānte janārdanam |

	pūjayitvā vidhānena pūjayec ca dvijottamān ||

	mṛtake 'pi na bhuñjīta ekādaśyāṃ sadā naraḥ |

	dvādaśyāṃ tu samaśnīyāt snātvā viṣṇuṃ praṇamya ca || iti |

upavāsāśaktau tu viṣṇurahasyoktam |

	asāmarthye śarīrasya vrate ca samupasthite |

	kāreyed dharmapatnīṃ tu putraṃ vā vinayānvitam ||

kātyāyano 'pi |

	pitur mātur bhrātur arthe ācāryārthe viśeṣataḥ |

	upavāsaṃ tu kurvāṇaḥ puṇyaṃ śataguṇaṃ labhet ||

	yam uddiśya kṛto vidvān so 'pi saṃpūrṇam āpnuyāt |

	nārī svapatim uddiśya ekādaśyām upoṣitā |

	puṇyaṃ śataguṇaṃ prāhuḥ munayaḥ pāradarśinaḥ ||

	upavāsaphalaṃ tasyāḥ patiḥ prāpnoty asaṃśayaḥ || iti |

atha vā smṛtyantaroktam |

	upavāse tv aśaktānām aśīter ūrdhvajīvinām |

	ekabhuktādikā kāryety āha bodhāyano muniḥ ||

anenaivābhiprāyeṇa mārkaṇḍeyo 'pi |

	ekabhuktena naktena tathaivayācitena ca |

	upavāsena dānena na nirdvādaśiko bhavet ||

nakte tu viśeṣam āha vyāsaḥ |

	haviṣyabhojanaṃ snānaṃ satyam āhāralāghavam |

	agnikāryam adhaḥśayyāṃ naktabhojī samācaret || iti |

evaṃ kurvataḥ phalam āha nāradīyapurāṇe vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	haridinam upavāsair yaḥ kṣapet prāpya jantuḥ 

		na viśati jaṭharaṃ viṇmūtrapūrṇaṃ jananyāḥ ||

	bahuvṛjinasametaḥ kāmarāgābhibhūto

		vrajati padam anantaṃ lokanāthasya viṣṇoḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyām ekādaśīnirṇayaḥ**

**athaikādaśīdvaidhanirṇayaḥ **

tatra skandapurāṇam |

	pratipatprabhṛtayaḥ sarvā udayādodayād raveḥ |

	saṃpūrṇā iti vikhyātā harivāsaravarjitāḥ || iti |

kīdṛśas tarhi saṃpūrṇo harivāsara ity apekṣite gāruḍapurāṇam |

	udayāt prāg yadā vipra muhūrtadvayasaṃyutā |

	saṃpūrṇaikādaśī nāma tatraivopavased gṛhī ||

	punaḥ prabhātasamaye ghaṭikaikā yadā bhavet |

	atropavāso vihitaś caturthāśramavāsinām ||

	vidhavāyāś ca tatraiva parato dvādaśī na cet || iti |

anena yatra trayodaśyāṃ dvādaśī nāsti kiṃ tv ekādaśy eva dinadvayayutā tatra yā saṃpūrṇaikādaśī tasyām upavāsaṃ gṛhī kuryād aparasyāṃ yatyādaya ity uktaṃ bhavati | uktaṃ ca smṛtyantare |

	saṃpūrṇaikādaśī yatra prabhāte punar eva sā |

	lupyate dvādaśī tasminn upavāsaḥ kathaṃ bhavet ||

	upoṣye dve tithī tatra viṣṇuprīṇanatatparaiḥ || iti |

tasmin trayodaśe 'hani yadā dvādaśī nāsti tadā pūrvoktādhikāribhedena dve tithī upoṣye na tv ekaivety arthaḥ | ata eva kūrmapurāṇe |

	saṃpūrṇaikādaśī yatra prabhāte punar eva sā |

	uttarāṃ tu yatiḥ kuryāt pūrvām upavased gṛhī || iti |

asminn eva viṣaye yadā trayodaśyām api dvādaśī tadā dvitīyaikādaśyām evopavāsaḥ | tathā ca bhṛguḥ |

	saṃpūrṇaikādaśī yatra prabhāte punar eva sā |

	tatropoṣyā dvitīyā tu parato dvādaśī yadi || iti |

asminn eva viṣaye yadā dvādaśyām ekādaśī nāsti tadā dvādaśyām evopavāsaḥ | tathā ca smṛtyantaram |

	ekādaśī bhavet pūrṇā parato dvādaśī yadi |

	ekādaśīṃ parityajya dvādaśīṃ samupoṣayet || iti |

evaṃ ca yatra daśamīśeṣasyodayāt prācīnamuhūrtadvayānanupraveśaḥ tatropavāsaḥ kārya ity uktaṃ bhaveti | anupraveśe tu gāruḍapurāṇoktam |

	udayāt prāk trighaṭikāvyāpiny ekādaśī yadā |

	saṃviddhaikādaśī nāma varjyā dharmārthakāṅkṣibhiḥ ||

	putrarājyasamṛddhyarthaṃ dvādaśyāṃ samupoṣayet |

	tatra kratuśataṃ puṇyaṃ trayodaśyāṃ tu pāraṇam ||

	ādityodayavelāyām āraddhā ṣaṣṭināḍikā |

	saṃkīrṇaikādaśī nāma jyājyā dharmaphalepsubhiḥ ||

	putrapautrapravṛddhyarthaṃ dvādaśyām upavāsayet |

	tatra kratuśataṃ puṇyaṃ trayodaśyāṃ tu pāraṇe || iti |

evaṃ ca yataikādaśī dvādaśyāṃ nāsti, dvādaśī na ca trayodaśyām, daśamīśeṣasyodayāt prācīnamuhūrtadvayānupraveśaḥ tatraikādaśīṃ parityajya dvādaśyām upoṣya trayodaśyāṃ pāraṇam ity uktaṃ bhavati | anenaivābhiprāyeṇa kaṇvo 'pi |

	aruṇodayavelāyāṃ daśamī yadi saṃgatā |

	tatropoṣyā dvādaśī syāt trayodaśyāṃ tu pāraṇam ||

	aruṇodayavelāyāṃ daśamī yadi saṃyutā |

	ravicakrārdhamātrāpi dvādaśīm upavāsayet ||

	tatra kratuśataṃ puṇyaṃ trayodaśyāṃ tu pāraṇam ||

	aruṇodayavelāyāṃ viddhā kācid upoṣitā |

	tasyāḥ putraśataṃ naṣṭaṃ tasmāt tāṃ parivarjayet ||

bhaviṣyatpurāṇe 'pi |

	aruṇodayavelāyāṃ daśamī yadi vidyate |

	pāpamūlaṃ sadā jñeyam ekādaśy upavāsinām ||

nārado 'pi |

	aruṇodayavelāyāṃ daśamī yadi dṛśyate |

	na tatraikādaśī kāryā dharmakāmārthanāśinī ||

gobiho 'pi |

	aruṇodayavelāyāṃ daśamī yadi saṃgatā |

	saṃyuktaikādaśīpuṇyaṃ mohinyai dattavān vibhuḥ ||

	udayād uparividdhā daśamy ekādaśī yadā |

	dānavebhyaḥ prīṇanārthaṃ dattavān pākaśāsanaḥ ||

	tasmāt sarvaprayatnena saṃkīrṇaikādaśīṃ tyajet |

	dvādaśyām upavāso 'tra trayodaśyāṃ tu pāraṇam ||

aruṇodayābhprāyeṇa nāradīyapurāṇe mohinīvākyam |

	agner vihārakāle tu vadhvā utthāpane tathā |

	gavāṃ dohanakāle 'pi pakṣisaṃnādane tathā ||

	nirgame sarvavedānāṃ mārjanīgrahaṇe tathā |

	dvārodghāṭanavelāyāṃ snānakāla upasthite ||

	vratināṃ dīkṣitānāṃ ca vāditraninade tathā |

	tathā prānto daśamyā yas tv ekādaśyā samanvitaḥ ||

	pradīyatāṃ nivāsārthaṃ kālo vibudhasattamāḥ |

	tan mohinyā vacaḥ śrutvā surāḥ sarve mahīyate ||

	saṃmantrya suciraṃ kālaṃ digambarapurogamāḥ |

	yamasya darśanārthāya vaikuṭhadhvaṃsanāya ca ||

	pāṣaṇḍināṃ vivṛddhyarthaṃ pāpasaṃjananāya ca |

	ūcus te mohinīṃ devāḥ lokasaṃmohanāya vai ||

	dattaṃ mohini te sthānaṃ pratyūṣasamaye hi tat |

	duṣṭaṃ haridinopetaṃ daśamyāḥ prāntam eva hi || iti |

aruṇodayaviddhāṃ parityajed iti bhāvaḥ | aruṇodayo 'pi purāṇe darśitaḥ |

	catasro ghaṭikāḥ prātar aruṇodaya ucyate |

	yatīnāṃ snānakālas tu gaṅgāmbusadṛśaḥ smṛtaḥ || iti |

yatayo 'tra niyatāḥ | teṣāṃ snānakāla iti | anena udayāt prācīnaṃ ghaṭikācatuṣṭayam aruṇodaya ity uktaṃ bhavati | aruṇodayābhiprāyeṇa nārado 'pi |

	daśamyānugatā yatra tithir ekādaśī bhavet |

	tatrāpatyavināśaś ca paretya narakaṃ vrajet |\

viṣṇurahasye 'pi |

	daśamīseṣasaṃyuktām upoṣyaikādaśīṃ kila |

	saṃvatsarakṛteneha naro dharmeṇa mucyate ||

	daśamīśeṣasaṃyuktā gāndhāryā samupoṣitā |

	tasyāḥ putraśataṃ naṣṭaṃ tasmāt tāṃ parivarjayet ||

brahmakaivarte |

	daśamīśeṣasaṃyuktāṃ yaḥ karoti vimūḍhadhīḥ |

	ekādaśīphalaṃ tasya na syād dvādaśavārṣikam || iti |

evaṃ ca yāni viddhopavāsaniṣedhaparāṇi tāni sarvāṇy aruṇodayavedhābhiprāyāṇīti mantavyam | ata eva bhaviṣyapurāṇam |

	aruṇodayaṃ yadā śuddhaṃ daśamīvedhavarjitam |

	sarvadoṣavinirmuktam upoṣyaṃ tad dinaṃ smṛtam || iti |

yadā tu śuddham aruṇodayaṃ vedharāhityena jānāti tadā sarvadoṣarahitaṃ tad dinam upoṣyam ity arthaḥ | evaṃ ca yat kaiścid uktam "yāni viddhopavāsaniṣedhaparāṇi tāny udayād ūrdhvaviṣayāṇi" iti, tad apāstam | tato yatra daśamīviddhaikādaśī dvādaśyāṃ nāsti tatra dvādaśyām upoṣya trayodaśyāṃ pāraṇaṃ kāryam iti siddham | yat tu hārītenoktam,

	trayodaśyāṃ yadā na syād dvādaśī ghaṭikādvayam |

	daśamy ekādaśī viddhā saivopoṣyā sadā tithiḥ ||

yad api ṛṣyaśṛṅgeṇa,

	pāraṇe na hi labhyeta dvādaśī kalayāpi cet |

	tadānīṃ daśamīviddhā upoṣyaikādaśī tithiḥ ||

iti, yad api viṣṇurahasye,

	daśamīśeṣasaṃyuktā upoṣyaikādaśī tathā |

	yadā na syāt trayodaśyāṃ muhūrtaṃ dvādaśī tithiḥ ||

iti, etat sarvam ekādaśīdinakṣayaviṣayam | ata eva nāradaḥ |

	daśamīśeṣasaṃyuktā nopoṣyaikādaśī tithiḥ |

	ekādaśyāṃ rātriśeṣe dvādaśī cen na dṛśyate || iti |

yadaikādaśīdivase kṣayo na bhavati tadā daśamīviddhā nopoṣyety arthaḥ | anenaikādaśīdinakṣaye daśamīviddhopoṣyety etad arthād uktaṃ bhavati | uktaṃ ca tenaiva |

	yadi daivāt tu saṃsiddhyed ekādaśyāṃ tithitrayam |

	tatra kratuśataṃ puṇyaṃ dvādaśyāṃ pāraṇaṃ bhavet ||

kūrmapurāṇe |

	dvispṛgekādaśī yatra tatra saṃnihito hariḥ |

	tām evopavaset kāmam akāmo viṣṇutatparaḥ ||

daśamīṃ dvādaśīṃ ca yā spṛśati sā dvispṛk | purāṇe 'pi |

	dinakṣayamṛte devi nopoṣyā daśamīyutā |

	saivopoṣyā sadā puṇyā parataś cet trayodaśī || iti |

yadaikādaśīdinakṣayaḥ trayodaśyāṃ ca na dvādaśī tadaiva daśamīviddhopoṣyā nānyathey arthaḥ | anena yasmin dinakṣaye trayodaśyām api dvādaśī tasmin naivopavased ity arthād uktaṃ bhavati | ata eva vyāsaḥ |

	ekādaśī yadā luptā parato dvādaśī bhavet |

	upoṣyā dvādaśī tatra yadīcchet paramāṃ gatim ||

luptā kṣayaṃ gatā | parataḥ trayodaśyām ity arthaḥ | yat tu gobhilenoktam,

	ekādaśyāṃ yadā brahman dinakṣayatithir bhavet |

	tadā hy ekādaśīṃ tyaktvā dvādaśyām upavāsayet ||

	tatra kratuśataṃ puṇyaṃ trayodaśyāṃ tu pāraṇam || 

iti, yad api pitāmahena,

	ekādaśyāṃ yadā vatsa dinakṣayatithir bhavet |

	atropoṣyā dvādaśī syāt trayodaśyāṃ tu pāraṇam ||

iti, tat putravadgṛhiviṣayam, tasyaiva dinakṣayopavāsaniṣedhāt | tathā ca matsyapurāṇam |

	dinakṣaye 'rkasaṃkrāntyāṃ grahaṇe candrasūryayoḥ |

	upavāsaṃ na kurvīta putrapautrasamanvitaḥ ||

vyāso 'pi |

	ekādaśīṣu naṣṭāsu ravisaṃkramaṇeṣu ca |

	pāraṇaṃ copavāsaṃ ca na kuryāt putravān gṛhī || iti |

pitāmaho 'pi |

	ekādaśīdinakṣaya upavāsaṃ karoti yaḥ |

	tasya putrā vinaśyanti maghāyāṃ piṇḍado yathā || iti |

evaṃ ca yāni viddhopavāsaniṣedhaparāṇi tāni sarvāṇy ekādaśīdinakṣayavyatiriktaviṣayāṇīti mantavyam | uktaṃ ca purāṇe |

	dinakṣayamṛte devi nopoṣyā daśamīyutā | iti |

anenaivābhiprāyeṇa kūrmapurāṇe 'pi |

	kalārdhenāpi viddhā syād daśamyaikādaśī yadā |

	tadā hy ekādaśīṃ tyaktvā dvādaśīṃ samupoṣayet ||

	dvādaśyām upavāso 'tra trayodaśyāṃ tu pāraṇam ||

vyāso 'pi |

	daśamīmiśritā pūrvā dvādaśī yadi lupyate |

	ekādaśyāṃ mahāprājña upavāsaḥ kathaṃ bhavet ||

	śuddhaiva dvādaśī rājann upoṣyā mokṣakāṅkṣibhiḥ |

	pāraṇaṃ tu trayodaśyāṃ pūjayitvā janārdanam ||

skandapurāṇe 'pi |

	śuddhaṃ haridinaṃ na syāt dvādaśīṃ grāhayet tataḥ |

	dvādaśyām upavāso 'tra trayodaśyāṃ tu pāraṇam ||

	evaṃ kurvan naro bhaktyā viṣṇusāyujyam āpnuyāt |

	anyathā kurute yas tu sa yāti narakaṃ dhruvam || iti |

evaṃ vedhasaṃdehe 'pi draṣṭavyam | ata eva kūrmapurāṇam |

	bahuvākyavirodhena saṃdeho jāyate yadā |

	dvādaśī tu tadā grāhyā trayodaśyāṃ tu pāraṇam || iti |

evaṃ ca yatra daśamīviddhaikādaśī dvādaśyāṃ nāsti dvādaśī ca trayodaśyām, tatra dvādaśyām upoṣya troyodaśyāṃ pāraṇaṃ kāryam ity uktaṃ bhavati | asminn eva viṣaye yadā dvādaśyām py ekādaśī tadā dvitīyaikādaśyām evopavāsaḥ | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	dvādaśyaikādaśī yatra saṃgatā tridaśādhipa |

	tām upoṣya tataḥ kuryāt trayodaśyāṃ tu pāraṇam || iti |

bodhāyano 'pi |

	kalāpy ekādaśī yatra parato dvādaśī na cet |

	tatra kratuśataṃ puṇyaṃ trayodaśyāṃ tu pāraṇam ||

purāṇe 'pi |

	dvādaśīmiśritā grāhyā sarvatraikādaśī tithiḥ |

	dvādaśī ca trayodaśyāṃ vidyate yadi vā na vā || iti |

asmin viṣaye yadā trayodaśyām api dvādaśī tadā dvitīyaikādaśyām evopavāsaḥ | tathā ca nāradīyapurāṇaṃ |

	dvādaśy ekādaśī yatra dvādaśī parato 'pi vā |

	dvādaśīpāraṇaṃ kuryāt kratukoṭiphalaṃ bhavet ||

purāṇe 'pi |

	ekādaśīkalāyuktā yena dvādaśy upoṣitā |

	kiṃ tasya bahubhir yajñair aśvamedhādibhir nṛpa ||

	ekādaśī dvādaśī ca tatra saṃnihito hariḥ |

	upoṣya rajanīm ekāṃ brahmahatyāṃ vyapohati || iti |

asminn eva viṣaye dvādaśyām ekādaśī nāsti tadā dvādaśyām evopavāsaḥ | tathā ca nāradīyapurāṇam |

	upoṣyā dvādaśī śūddhā dvādhyām eva pārayet |

	nirgatā cet trayodaśyāṃ kalā vā dvikalāpi vā || iti |

dvādaśīdinakṣaye kūrmapurāṇe |

	ekādaśī dvādaśī ca rātriśeṣe trayodaśī |

	tribhir miśrā tithiḥ karyā sarvapāpaharā smṛtā ||

	upavāsaḥ kṛtas tasyāṃ mahāpātakanāśanam |

	ekādaśī dvādaśī ca rātriśeṣe trayodaśī ||

	tatra kratuśataṃ puṇyaṃ trayodaśyāṃ tu pāraṇam ||

skandapurāṇe 'pi |

	dvādaśīsaṃgatā yatra bhavaty ekādaśī tithiḥ |

	dinakṣaye 'pi sā puṇyā nirasyā na kathaṃcana || iti |

yat tu vṛddhaśātātapenoktam,

	daśamyaikādaśī viddhā dvādaśī ca kṣayaṃ gatā |

	kṣīṇā sā dvadaśī jñeyā naktaṃ tatra vidhīyat ||

yad api viṣṇudharmottare,

	ekādaśī yadā viddhā dvādaśī ca kṣayaṃ gatā |

	kṣīṇā sā dvādaśī jñeyā naktaṃ tatra vidhīyate 

iti, tat putravadgṛhiviṣayam, tasyaiva dinakṣayopavāsaniṣedhāt | tathā ca matsyapurāṇam |

	ekādaśī dvādaśī ca viśeṣeṇa trayodaśī |

	upavāsaṃ na kurvīta putrapautrasamanvitaḥ ||

nanv anenopavāso niṣidhyate na naktavidhānam | maivam, niṣiddasyopavāsasya vāyupurāṇe naktavidhānāt |

	upavāsaniṣedhe tu bhakṣyaṃ kiṃcit prakalpayet |

	na duṣyaty upavāsena upavāsaphalaṃ labhet || iti |

bhakṣyaprakalpanam api tatraivānantaram uktam |

	naktaṃ haviṣyānnam anodanaṃ vā yavās tilāḥ kṣīram athāmbuvājyam |

	yat pañcagavyaṃ yadi vāpi vāyuḥ praśastam atrottaram uttaraṃ ca || iti |

evaṃ yad uktaṃ vyāsena,

	ekādaśī dvādaśī ca rātriśeṣe trayodaśī |

	dvādaśa dvādaśīr hanti trayodaśyāṃ tu pāraṇam ||
