iti, tat putravadgṛhiviṣayam ity anusaṃdheyam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca yāni trayodaśīpāraṇaparāṇi teṣv eva "tatra kratuśataṃ puṇyam" ityādiphalaśravaṇāt, tāni kāmyopavāsābhiprāyāṇi, viddhopavāsavidhiparāṇi tu nityopavāsaviṣayāṇīti vyavasthā kiṃ na syāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span>,

	yadi daivāt tu saṃsiddhyed ekādaśyāṃ tithitrayam |

	tatra kratuśataṃ puṇyaṃ dvādaśīpāreṇe kṛte ||

	dvādaśy ekādaśī yatra dvādaśī parato 'pi ca |

	dvādaśīpāraṇaṃ kuryāt kratukoṭiphalaṃ bhavet || 

iti dvādaśīpāraṇe 'pi phalaśravaṇāviśeṣāt | kiṃ ca,

	sarvatraikādaśī kāryā dvādaśīmiśritā naraiḥ |

	prātar bhavatu vā mā vā yato nityaṃ hi pāraṇam ||

	pāraṇaṃ tu trayodaśyāṃ niṣkāmānāṃ vimuktidam |

ityādiṣu trayodaśīpāraṇasyāpi nityatvaśravaṇāc ca | ato neyaṃ phalaśrutiḥ, api ty arthavāda it mantavyam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">kecit</span> tu,

	śuddhaiva dvādaśī rājann upoṣyā mokṣakāṅkṣibhiḥ |

	pāraṇaṃ tu trayodaśyāṃ pūjayitvā janārdanam ||

iti vacanād yatīnām eva mokakāṅkṣitvāt tadviṣayāṇy eva śuddhadvādaśyupavāsavidhiparāṇi | viddhopavāsavidhiparāṇi tu gṛhasthaviṣayāṇy eveti vyavasthāpayanti | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">tan mandaṃ</span>, svargādiphalasya bhaṅgitvena sarveṣām api mokṣakāṅkṣitvāviśeṣāt | kiṃ ca,

	upoṣyā sarvadā śuddhā dvādaśī tu dvijottamaiḥ |

	kṣatrair vaiśyaiś tathā śuddhaiḥ kim anyac chrtotum icchasi ||

iti śuddhadvādaśyupavāse yativyatiriktānām apy adhikāradarśanāt | tathā,

	ekādaśī diśā viddhā parato na nivartate |

	gṛhibhir yatibhiś caiva saivopoṣyā sadā tithiḥ ||

iti matsyapurāṇe yatīnām api viddhopavāsavidhānāc ca | yad <span style="text-decoration:underline;">anyair</span> uktam,

	saṃpūrṇaikādaśī yatra prabhāte punar eva sā |

	uttarāṃ tu yatiḥ kuryāt pūrvām upavased gṛhī ||

ity atra yatīnāṃ trayodaśyāṃ pāraṇadarśanāt tadviṣayāṇy eva trayodaśīpāraṇaparāṇi, viddhopavāsavidhiparāṇi tu gṛhasthaviṣyāṇy eveti, <span style="text-decoration:underline;">tad api</span> pūrvoktavacanadvayenaivāpāstam ity upekṣaṇīyam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">apare</span> tu viddhopavāsavidhiparāṇy aruṇōdayavedhaviṣayāṇi, dvādaśyupavāsavidhiparāṇi tūdayād ūrdhvaviṣayāṇīti manyante, <span style="text-decoration:underline;">tad api</span> trayodaśīpāraṇavidhiviruddham ity upekṣaṇīyam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca kathaṃ trayodaśyāṃ pāraṇaṃ, yāvatā kūrmapurāṇe,

	ekādaśyām upoṣyaiva dvādaśyāṃ pāraṇaṃ smṛtam |

	trayodaśyāṃ na tat kuryād dvādaśadvādaśīkṣayāt || 

iti trayodaśīpāraṇaniṣedhāt | śrīviṣṇurahaste 'pi |

	pāraṇaṃ tu na kartavyam upoṣyaikādaśīm iha |

	trayodaśyāṃ narair nityaṃ dharmavṛddhim abhīpsubhiḥ || iti |

smṛtyantare 'pi |

	daśamyanugatā hanti dvādaśadvādaśīphalam |

	dharmāpatyadhanāyūṃṣi trayodaśyāṃ tu pāraṇam || iti |

<span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span>: satyam evam, tathāpi yatra trayodaśyāṃ dvādaśīsaṃbhavaḥ tatra tām atikramya trayodaśyāṃ pāraṇaṃ na kāryam ity evaṃparam, na punaḥ śuddhatrayodaśyām | ata eva kūrmapurāṇam |

	yadā bhavati cālpā tu dvādaśī pāraṇe dine |

	uṣaḥkāle dvayaṃ kuryāt prātarmādhāhnikaṃ tathā ||

nāradīyapurāṇe 'pi |

	alpāyām atha viprendra dvādaśyām aruṇodaye |

	snānārcanakriyāḥ kuryād dānahomādisaṃyutāḥ ||

	trayodaśyāṃ tu śuddhāyāṃ pāraṇam pṛthivīphalam |

	śatayajñādhikaṃ vāpi naraḥ prāpnoty asaṃśayaḥ ||

	etasmāt kāraṇād viprāḥ pratyūṣe snānam ācaret |

	pitṛtarpaṇasaṃyuktam alpāṃ dṛṣṭvaiva dvādaśīm ||

	mahāhānikarī hy eṣā dvādaśī laṅghitā nṛṇām |

	karoti dharmaharaṇam asnāteva sarasvatī  ||

na ca,

	yāṃ tithiṃ samanuprāpya udayaṃ yāti bhāskaraḥ |

	sā tithiḥ sakalā jñeyā snānadānajapādiṣu ||

iti devalavacanād dvādaśyatikrame 'pi na doṣa iti śaṅkanīyam | yata āha nāradīyapurāṇe vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	pāraṇe maraṇe nṝṇāṃ tithis tātkālikī smṛtā | iti |

yasmin kāle pāraṇaṃ maraṇaṃ vā tatra tātkāliky eva tithiḥ na punaḥ sā tithiḥ sakalā jñeyety etad bhavatīty arthaḥ | yatra punas trayodaśyāṃ kalāmātraiva dvādaśī tatra purāṇoktam |

	trayodaśyāṃ yadā rājan dvādaśyās tu kalā bhavet |

	sā tithiḥ sakalā ceti vasiṣṭhaḥ prāha dharmavit || iti |

evaṃ ca yāni trayodaśīpāraṇaniṣedhaparāṇi tāni trayodaśyāṃ dvādaśīsaṃbhavaviṣayāṇīti siddham | yāni punaḥ,

	kalā kāṣṭhā muhūrtaṃ vā yadi ced apare 'hanit |

	dvādaśa dvādaśīr hanti trayodaśyāṃ tu pāraṇam ||

iti, trayodaśyāṃ dvādaśīsaṃbhavam anūdya pāraṇaniṣedhaparāṇi, tāni,

	viddhāpy ekādaśī grāhyā parato dvādaśī na cet |

	dvādaśa dvādaśīr hanti tradaśyāṃ tu pāraṇam ||

ityādibhiḥ samānārthānīty anavadyam | evaṃ ca yat kaiścid uktaṃ trayodaśyāṃ dvādaśīsaṃbhave 'pi trayodaśīpāraṇaṃ na doṣāyeti, tad apāstam ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyām ekādaśīdvaidhanirṇayaḥ **

**aparāhṇanirṇayaḥ**

evaṃ prasaktan anuprasaktaṃ ca parisamāpyādhunā prakṛtā aprāhṇanirṇayaḥ kriyate | tatra śātātapaḥ |

	darśaśrāddhaṃ tu yat proktaṃ pārvaṇaṃ tat prakīrtitam |

	aparāhṇe pitṝṇāṃ ca tatra dānaṃ praśasyate ||

aparāhṇo 'pi pañcadhāvibhaktasyādhnaś caturtho bhāga ity āha vyāsaḥ |

	muhūrtatritayaṃ prātaḥ tāvān eva ca saṅgavaḥ |

	madhyāhnas trimuhūrtaḥ syād aparāhṇo 'pi tādṛśaḥ ||

	sāyāhnas trimuhūrtas tu sarvakarmabahiṣkṛtaḥ || iti |

vājasaneyaśrutir api: "ādityo vai sarvā ṛtavaḥ sa yadaivodety atha vasanto yadā saṅgavo 'tha grīṣmo yadā madhyandino 'tha śarad yadāparāhṇas tadā varṣā yadāstam ety atha hemantaḥ" iti | śrutyantare tu tredhā vibhaktasyāhnas tṛtīyabhāge 'parāhṇaśabdaḥ prayuktaḥ: "pūrvāhṇo vai devānāṃ madhyaṃdinaṃ manuṣyāṇām aprāhṇaḥ pitṝṇām" iti | manus tu dvedhā vibhaktasyāhno dvitīyabhāge 'parāhṇaśabdam āha |

	yathā caivāparaḥ pakṣaḥ pūrvapakṣād viśiṣyate |

	tathā śrāddhasya pūrvāhṇād aparāhṇo viśiṣyate ||

skandapurāṇe 'pi |

	āvartanāt tu pūrvāhṇo hy aparāhṇas tataḥ paraḥ | iti |

āvartanāvadhiḥ pūrvāhṇaḥ ity arthaḥ | evam anekadhāparāhṇaśabdaprayoge 'pi manūkta evāparāhṇaśabdārthaḥ svīkriyate |

	śuklapakṣasya pūrvāhṇe śrāddhaṃ kuryād dvijottamaḥ |

	kṛṣṇapakṣāparāhṇe tu rauhiṇaṃ tu na laṅghayet ||

iti mārkaṇḍeyena dvedhā vibhaktasyāhno dvitīyabhāge śrāddhāvadhānāt, tathā "rauhiṇaṃ tu na laṅghayet" iti caturthabhāgād arvāg eva samāptividhānāc ca | rauhiṇo navamo muhūrtaḥ | kiṃ ca,

	bhūtaviddhā tv amāvāsyā pratipanmiśritāpi vā |

	pitrye karmaṇi vidvadbhiḥ grāhyā kutapakālikī ||

iti hārītaḥ śrāddhāṅgatvena kutapakālaṃ vidhatte, tad api na syāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> nānena kutapakālasya śrāddhāṅgatvam avagamyate | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span>, kutapakālikīgrahaṇavidheḥ dṛṣṭārthatvāyāṅgatvasyaivocitatvāt | uktaṃ ca purāṇe |

	kuṃ yatra gopatir gobhiḥ kārtsnyena tapati kṣaṇe |

	sa kālaḥ kutapo nāma śrāddhaṃ tatra pardīyate || iti |

kuḥ pṛthvī | gopatiḥ sūryaḥ | atra yat <span style="text-decoration:underline;">kaiścid</span> uktam "ekoddiṣṭaṃ tu madhyāhne" iti vacanāt kutapakālavidhānam ekoddiṣṭaviṣayam eveti, tad anena darśaśrādde 'pi kutapakālavidhānenāpāstam | na caivaṃ sati kutapāparāhṇavidhyor vikalpaḥ syād iti śaṅkanīyam, kutapottarārdhasyāparāhṇantarbhāvaḥ | kutapo hi nāma pañcadaśamuhūtātmakasyāhno 'ṣṭamo muhūrtaḥ | tathā ca matsyapurāṇam |

	ahno muhūtā vikhyātā daśa pañca ca sarvadā |

	tatrāṣṭamo muhūrto yaḥ sa kālaḥ kutapaḥ smṛtaḥ || iti |

vāyupurāṇe 'pi |

	muhūrtā saptamād ūrdhvaṃ muhūrān navamādayaḥ |

	sa kālaḥ kutapo nāma pitṝṇāṃ dattam akṣayam || iti |

evaṃ ca yad aparāhṇe vihitaṃ tad aparāhṇāntargatakutape kāryaṃ vidhīyata ity avirodhaḥ | etad api prārambhābhiprāyam | tad āha matsyaḥ |

	madhyāhne sarvā yasmān mandībhavati bhāskaraḥ |

	tasmād anantaphaladaḥ tatrārambho viśiṣyate ||

gautamo 'pi |

	prārabhya kutape śrāddhaṃ kuryād ārauhiṇaṃ budhaḥ |

	vidhijño vidhim āsthāya rauhiṇaṃ tu na laṅghayet || iti |

etac ca kutapādiśrāddhavidhānam anagnikaviṣayam, sāgneḥ kṛtapiṇḍapitṛyajñasyaiva manunā śrāddhavidhānāt,

	pitṛyajñaṃ tu nirvartya vipraś candrakṣaye 'gnimān |

	piṇḍānvāhāryakaṃ śrāddhaṃ kuryān mānānumāsikam ||

iti piṇḍapitṛyajñasyāpy aparāhṇakālatvena śrāddhasya kutapāditvāsaṃbhavād iti bhāvaḥ | na ca,

	pitṛyajñaṃ tu nirvartya tarpaṇākhyaṃ tu yo 'gnimān |

	piṇḍānvāhāryakaṃ śrāddhaṃ kuryād indukṣaye sadā ||

iti matsyapurāṇavacanāt pitṛyajñaśabdaḥ tarpaṇākhyapitṛyajñapara iti sāgner api kutapādy eva śrāddham iti śaṅkanīyam,

	pakṣāntaṃ karma nirvartya vaiśvadevaṃ ca sāgnikaḥ |

	piṇḍayajñaṃ tataḥ kuryāt tato 'nvāhāryakaṃ budhaḥ ||

iti laugākṣinā sāgneḥ piṇḍapitṛyajñānantaram eva śrāddhavidhānāt | atas tarpaṇaśabdo 'pi kathaṃcit piṇḍapitṛyajñapara ity avagantavyam | evaṃ ca yatra śrāddhadine candradarśanena piṇḍapitṛyajñaprāptiḥ tatrāgnimān kṛtvaiva piṇḍapitṛyajñaṃ śrāddhaṃ kuryāt | anyathā tu sāgner api kutapādy eva śrāddham ity anusaṃdheyam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> kutapādirauhināntatvāc chrāddhakālasya tasya ca karmadvayāparyāptatvāt katham agnimac chrāddasyāpi piṇḍapitṛyajñānantaryam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span>, matsyapurāṇe rauhinād upary api kālavidhānāt,

	ūrdhvaṃ muhūrtaṃ kutapād yan muhūrtacatuṣṭayam |

	muhūrtapañcakaṃ hy etat svadhābhavam iṣyate ||

iti kutapādimuhūrtapañcakaṃ śrāddhasyāṅgam ity arthaḥ | yat tu yamenoktam,

	caturthe prahare prāpte yaḥ śrāddhaṃ kurute naraḥ |

	āsuraṃ tad bhavec chrāddhaṃ dātā ca narakaṃ vrajet ||

iti, tat caturthaprahare prāpte sati yo 'ntime muhūrtatraye śrāddhaṃ karoti tasya doṣa ity evaṃparam, na punaḥ praharaniṣedhaparaṃ pūrvoktamatsyapurāṇavacanavirodhāt | uktaṃ ca tatraiva |

	sāyāhnas triuhūrthaḥ syāc chrāddhaṃ tatra na kārayet |

	rākṣasī nāma sā velā garhitā sarvakarmasu || iti |

yad api kātyāyanoktam,

	piṇḍānvāhāryakaṃ śrāddhaṃ kṣīṇe rājani śasyate |

	vāsarasya tṛtīye 'ṃśe nāstisaṃdhyāsamīpataḥ || 

iti, tad api kūrmapurāṇavacanavirodhāt "vāsarasya tṛtīye 'ṃśe nātisaṃdhyāsamīpataḥ" iti dināntime muhūrtatraye na kāryam ity evaṃparam, na punar viśeṣeṇa tṛtīyāṃśae vidhiparam iti | yad api vyāghrapādavacanam,

	vidhijñaḥ śraddhayopetaḥ samyakpātraniyojakaḥ |

	rātrer anyatra kurvāṇaḥ śreyaḥ prāpnoty asaṃśayam ||

iti, tad apy uktayuktyaiva nāharmātravidhiparam iti sarvam anavadyam | rātriniṣedhasya kvacid apavādam āha viṣṇuḥ |

	saṃdhyārātryor na kartavyaṃ śrāddhaṃ khalu vicakṣaṇaiḥ |

	tayor api ca kartavyaṃ yadi syād rāhudarśanam || iti |

atra śātātapaḥ |

	kālātītaṃ tu yat kuryāc chrāddhaṃ homaṃ japaṃ tathā |

	vyarthībhavati tat sarvam amṛte tu viṣaṃ yathā ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyām aparāhṇanirṇayaḥ**

**athānyāny api śrāddhakālaviṣyāṇi kānicid vacanāni likhyante**

tatra viṣṇudharmottare mārkaṇḍeyaḥ |

	uttarād ayanād rājan śreṣṭhaṃ syād dakṣiṇāyanam |

	yāmyāyanāc caturmāsaṃ tatra supte tu keśave ||

	proṣṭhapadyaparaḥ pakṣaḥ tatrāpi ca viśeṣataḥ |

	pañcamyūrdhvaṃ tu tatrāpi daśamyūrdhvaṃ tato 'pi ca ||

	maghāyuktāpi tatrāpi śastā rājan trayodaśī || iti |

śrāddhakāleṣūdagayanā dakṣiṇāyanaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ yāmyāyanād dakṣiṇāyanād ity arthaḥ | tatra dakṣiṇāyane keśave supte sati māsacatuṣṭayaṃ śreṣṭham, yāmyāyane 'py āṣāḍhīṃ paurṇamāsīm ārabhya māsacatuṣṭayaṃ śreṣṭham iti yāvat | tatrāpi proṣṭhapadamāsasyāparapakṣo viśeṣataḥ śreṣṭhaḥ | tatrāpi pañcamyā ūrdhvaṃ darśāntāni dināni śreṣṭhāni | tatrāpi daśamyā ūrdhvaṃ pañcadināni śreṣṭhāni | teṣv api makhānakṣatrayuktā trayodaśī atipraśastety arthaḥ | ādityapurāṇe 'pi |

	āṣāḍhīm avadhiṃ kṛtvā yaḥ syāt pakṣas tu pañcamaḥ |

	śrāddhaṃ tatra tu kurvīta kanyāṃ gacchatu vā na vā ||

pañcame pakṣe sūryaḥ kanyārāśiṃ gacchatu vā na vety arthaḥ | atra na veti pakṣaḥ kanyāgatatvābhāve 'pi tatra śrāddhaṃ kurvīteti vidhātuṃ noktam, kiṃ tu pañcamaḥ pakṣaḥ kanyāgatasūryarahito 'pi śreṣṭhaḥ kiṃ punas tatsahita iti darśayitum iti mantavyam | ata eva śāṭyāyaniḥ |

	nabhasyasyāpare pakṣe tithiṣoḍaśakas tu yaḥ |

	kanyāgatānvitaś cet syāt sa kālaḥ śrāddhakarmaṇi || iti |

tithiṣoḍaśaka iti kadācit pakṣavṛddheḥ ṣoḍaśadinātmako 'pi nabhasyasyāparaḥ pakṣaḥ śrāddhakarmaṇi kālo na tu tatra pañcadaśadinātmaka eveti darśayitum uktam | yad vā amāvāsyāyā anantarabhūtā yā pratipattithiḥ tasyā api saṃgrahaṇārthaṃ tithiṣoḍaśaka ity uktam, pratipado 'pi kṣīṇacandratvenāparapakṣatulyatvāt | na caivaṃ vācyam, nabhasyasyāpare pakṣe kanyāgate sūrye sati taddināt prabhṛti tithiṣoḍaśakaṃ śrāddhakālaḥ syād ity anena pratipādyata iti | yata āha vṛddhamanuḥ |

	madhye vā yadi vāpy ante yatra kanyā ravir vrajet |

	sa pakṣaḥ sakalaḥ pūjyaḥ śrāddhaṃ tatra vidhīyate || iti |

yatra yasmin pañcame pakṣe yatra kutracit kanyāgate savitari sati sakalaḥ sa pakṣaḥ śrāddhe praśastatarakālaḥ | tena tatra pratidinam ekasmin vā dine śaktyanusāreṇa śrāddhaṃ kartavyam ity avagantavyam | tathā ca ādityapurāṇam |

	pakṣāntare 'pi kanyāsthe ravau śrāddhaṃ praśasyate |

	kanyāgate pañcame tu viśeṣeṇaiva kārayet ||

pakṣāntare 'pi pañcamapakṣāt pakṣāntare 'pīty arthaḥ | pañcamapakṣasya praśastataratvam "viśeṣeṇaiva kārayet" ity anenoktam | anenaivābhiprāyeṇa jātūkarṇyaḥ |

	ākāṅkṣanti sma pitaraḥ pañcamaṃ pakṣaṃ āśritāḥ |

	tasmāt tatraiva dātavyaṃ dattam anyatra niṣphalam ||

praśastakāle dattam atyantādhikaphalasādhakam ity arthaḥ | kiṃ punaḥ praśastatarakāle dattasya phalam ity apekṣite kārṣājiniḥ |

	putrān āyus tathārogyam aiśvayram atulaṃ tathā |

	prāpnoti pañcame datvā śrāddhaṃ kāmāṃś ca puṣkalān ||

purāṇe 'pi |

	kanyāgate savitari yāny ahāni tu ṣoḍaśa |

	kratubhis tāni tulyāni pitṝṇāṃ dattam akṣayam || iti |

tad etac chāṭyāyanivacanena samānārthatayā vyākhyeyam | praśastatarakālātikrame doṣo 'pi kārṣṇājininā darśitaḥ |

	pretās taṃ caiva hiṃsanti pañcamaṃ yo vyatikramet |

	tasmān nātikramed vidvān pañcame paitṛkaṃ vidhim ||

yadā tu pañcame pakṣe kathaṃcid etac chrāddhaṃ na kṛtaṃ tadā tv āha sumantuḥ |

	kanyārāśau mahārāja yāvat tiṣṭhed vibhāvasuḥ |

	tasmāt kālād bhaved deyaṃ vṛścike yāvad āgataḥ ||

	yeyaṃ dīpānvitā rājan khyātā pañcadaśī bhuvi |

	tasyāṃ dadyān na ced dattaṃ pitṝṇāṃ vai mahālaye || iti |

mahālaye mahālayākhye pañcame pakṣe pitṝṇāṃ pitṛbhyo na dattaṃ cet tadā kanyārāśau yāvad vibhāvastus (?) tiṣṭhet tāvad anyasmin pakṣe 'pi dadyāt | tasmāt kālāt kanyāgatasūryānvitakālāt paścāt tulārāśigatasūryānvite 'pi śrāddhaṃ deyaṃ bhavet | tatrāpi kāle yadi kathaṃcin na dattaṃ tadā dīpāvalyākhyāyāṃ pañcadaśyāṃ dadyād ity arthaḥ | purāṇe 'pi |

	kanyāgate savitari pitaro yānti vai sutān |

	śūnyā pretapurī sarvā yāvad vṛścikadarśanam ||

	tato vṛścikasaṃprāptau nirāśāḥ pitaro gatāḥ |

	punas tv abhavanaṃyānti śāpaṃ datvā sudāruṇam ||

	sūrye kanyāgate kuryāc chrāddhaṃ yo na gṛhāśramī |

	dhanaṃ putrāḥ kutas tasya pitṛniḥśvāsapīḍanāt ||

ādityapurāṇe 'pi |

	prāvṛṣy ṛtau yamaḥ pretān pitṝṃś cātha yamālayāt |

	visarjayitvā mānuṣye kṛtvā śūnyaṃ svakaṃ puram ||

	kṣudhārtāḥ kīrtayantaś ca duṣkṛtaṃ ca svayaṃkṛtam |

	kāṅkṣantaḥ putrapautrebhyaḥ pāyasaṃ madhusaṃyutam ||

	tasmāt tāṃs tatra vidhinā tarpayet pāyasena tu |

	madhvājatilamiśreṇa tathā śītena cambhasā ||

	grāsamātraṃ paragṛhād annaṃ yaḥ prāpnuyān naraḥ |

	bhikṣāmātreṇa yaḥ prāṇān saṃdhārayati vā svayam ||

	yo vā saṃvardhayed dehaṃ pratyahṃ svātmavikrayāt |

	śrāddhaṃ tenāpi kartavyaṃ tais tair dravyaiḥ susaṃcitaiḥ || iti |

yamālayāt pretān pitṝṃś ca visarjayitvā svakaṃ puraṃ śūnyaṃ kṛtvā manuṣyaloke prāvṛṣi bhādrapadamāsakṛṣṇapakṣaprabhṛti yāvad vṛścikadarśanaṃ vāsayati tāvad ity adhyāhṛtena saṃbandhaḥ | kṣudhārtāḥ pretāḥ pitaras tiṣṭhantīty adhyāhṛtena saṃbandhaḥ | vidhinā tarpayet putra iti śeṣaḥ | caturviṃśatimate 'pi |

	ācāryaguruśiṣyebhyaḥ sakhijñātibhya eva ca |

	tatpatnībhyaś ca sarvābhyas tathaiva ca jalāñjalīn ||

	piṇḍadānaṃ ca tebhyas tu dadyād bhādrapade naraḥ |

	tīrtheṣu caiva sarveṣu māghamāse tathaiva ca ||

	ekasmin brāhmaṇe sarvān ācāryādīn prapūjayet |

	daś dvādaśa piṇḍāṃś ca dadyād akaraṇaṃ na tu ||

	niyāmako vidhir nūnaṃ pakṣe vai pañcame smṛtaḥ |

	tasmin dattaṃ havir nūnaṃ pitṝṇām akṣayaṃ bhavet || iti |

ekasmin brāhmana ity asamarthaviṣayam | samarthas tu svasāmarthyānusāreṇa pratyekam ekaikasmin brāhmaṇe ācāryādīn sarvān ekasmin dine prapūjayet | ekaikam ācaryādikam ekaikasmin vā dine prapūjayet | tatra tadā prathamaḥ svīkriyate tadā ekapākena samānatantram āśritya prapūjayet | tathā ca bhṛguṇā,

	ekakāle gatāsūnāṃ bahūnām atha vā dvayoḥ |

	tantreṇa śrapaṇaṃ kṛtvā kuryāc chrāddhaṃ pṛthak pṛtha ||

	pūrvakasya mṛtasyādau dvitīyasya tataḥ punaḥ |

	tṛtīyasya tataḥ kuryāt ................ ||

ity uktvoktam "saṃnipāteṣv ayaṃ kramaḥ" iti | saṃnipāteṣu samasamaye nānāśrāddheṣu kartavyatayāpatiteṣu ayaṃ kramaḥ tantreṇa śrapaṇaṃ kṛtvā jyeṣṭhānukrameṇa śrāddhānuṣṭhāne kramo 'nusaṃdheya ity arthaḥ | atra yad uktaṃ smṛtyarthasāre,

	ekaḥ pāko vaiśvadevaṃ tantraṃ piṇḍaṃ barhiś caikam |

iti, tatra "vaiśvadevaṃ tantram" iti cintyam, "ācāryaguruśiṣyasakhijñātyādīnām ekoddiṣṭavidhānenaiva śrāddhaṃ kāryam" iti smṛtivacanair uktatvāt, tatra vaiśvadevāsaṃbhavāt "navamiśrapurāṇānīti trividhāny ekoddiṣṭāni" ity uktatvena sarvaikoddiṣṭeṣu daivaṃ nāstīti smṛtyarthasāra evoktatvāc ca | smṛtivacanāni tv adūre darśayiṣyāmaḥ | yamo 'py asmarthaṃ praty āha |

	haṃse varṣāsu kanyāsthe śākenāpi gṛhe vasan |

	pañcamyor antare dadyād ubhayor api pakṣayoḥ ||

varṣāsu prāvṛṣi haṃse sūrye kanyārāśisthe pañcamapakṣasya pañcamīprabhṛtyanantarapakṣasya pañcamīparyantaseṣv anyatame divase yathāsaṃbhavaṃ gṛhī pitṛbhyo dadyād ity arthaḥ | pañcamyor antare caturdaśīvvyatirkta iti śeṣaḥ | tad āha marīciḥ |

	viṣaśastraśvāpadāhitiryagbrāhmaṇaghātinām |

	caturdaśyāṃ kriyā kāryā anyeṣāṃ tu vigarhitā ||

viṣādibrāhmaṇāntaiḥ kṛtaḥ ghātaḥ eṣāṃ te piṣaśastraśvāpadāhitiryagbrāhmaṇaghātinaḥ | kriyā śrāddhakriyā ekoddiṣṭavidhāneneti śeṣaḥ | tathā ca sumantuḥ (?) |

	samatvam āgatasyāpi pituḥ śastrahatasya tu |

	ekoddiṣṭaṃ sutaiḥ kāryaṃ caturdaśyāṃ mahālaye ||

samatvam ekatvam āgatasyāpi kṛtasapiṇḍīkaraṇasyāpīty arthaḥ | śastrahatasya pituḥ mahālaye caturdaśyām ekoddiṣṭaśrāddhe kṛte 'pi dināntare pārvaṇaśrāddhaṃ kāryam, ekoddiṣṭaśrāddhena pitāmahāditṛptyasiddheḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanv</span> evaṃ mṛtāhe 'py ekoddiṣṭaśrāddhe kṛte pārvaṇaśrāddham api pitāmahāditṛptisiddhyarthaṃ kartavyaṃ syāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span>, pitṛmṛtāhe pitāmahādes tarpaṇīyatvāsmaraṇena tattṛptyarthaṃ śrāddhasyānanuṣṭheyatvāt | mahālayaprakaraṇe,

	kāṅkṣanti putrapautrebhyaḥ pāyasaṃ madhusaṃyutam |

	tasmāt tāṃs tatra vidhinā tarpeyet pāyasena tu ||

	madhvājyatilamiśreṇa ............. ||

iti pitāmahāder api tarpaṇīyatvasmaraṇāt tattṛptaye dināntare pārvaṇaśrāddhaṃ kāryam eva | yasya tu pitāmaho 'pi śastrādinā hataḥ tasya mahālaye pitāmahaśrāddham api caturdaśyām ekoddiṣṭarūpaṃ karyam | tathā ca smṛtyantaram "ekasmin dvayor vaikoddiṣṭavidhiḥ" iti | ekasmin pitari śastrādinā hate dvayor vā pitṛpitāmahayoḥ caturdaśyām ekoddiṣṭavidhinā pratyekaṃ śrāddhaṃ kāryam ity arthaḥ | dvayor ekoddiṣṭavidhānena pratyekaṃ śrāddhe kṛte prapitāmatṛptisiddhyarthaṃ dināntare pāraṇaśrāddhaṃ kāryam, "ekasmin dvayor vā" ity abhidhānāt | triṣu pitṛpitāmahaprapitāmaheṣu śastrādinihateṣu naikoddiṣavidhir iti gamyate | teṣu triṣu śastrādihateṣu caturdaśyāṃ pārvaṇavidhir eva | yuktaṃ caitat, sapiṇḍīkṛtānāṃ śastrādihatānāṃ trayāṇām api caturdaśīrūpavihitakālasaṃbhave 'pi vihitakālasaṃbhavanibandhanaikoddiṣṭavidher anavatārāt | anenaivābhiprāyeṇ aparārkeṇāpy uktam: "tatra caikasya śastrahatatve ekoddiṣṭavidhānaṃ na tu trayāṇāṃ tathātve tatra tu pārvaṇam eva" iti | trayāṇāṃ tathātve śastrahatatve naikoddiṣṭavidhānam, kiṃ tu pārvaṇam eveti tasyārthaḥ | devasvāminā tu "triṣv api śastrahateṣu pṛthag ekoddiṣṭatrayam eva kāryam, āhatya vacanābhāvān na pārvaṇam" ity uktam | yad atra yuktaṃ tad grāhyam | yat punaḥ śākaṭāyanenoktam,

	jalāgnibhyāṃ vipannānāṃ saṃnyāse vā gṛhe pathi |

	śrāddhaṃ kurvīta teṣāṃ vai varjayitvā caturdaśīm ||

iti, tat prāyaścittārthaṃ vihitajalāgnyādikṛtamaraṇayuktaviṣayam | ye hi pāpamṛtyavaḥ teṣām eva jalāgnyādivipannānāṃ caturdaśī grāhyā,

	vṛkṣārohaṇalohādyair vidyujjvālāviṣādibhiḥ |

	nakhidaṃṣṭrivipannānāṃ teṣāṃ śastā caturdaśī ||

iti pracetaso vacanena vidyujjvālādisamabhivyāhāreṇa pāpamṛtyūnāṃ (?) caturdaśī śastety avagamāt | eteṣām api mṛtāhādau yac chrāddhaṃ tat pārvaṇavidhānenaiva kāryam,

	caturdaśyāṃ tu yac chrāddhaṃ sapiṇḍīkaraṇāt param |

	ekoddiṣṭavidhānena tat kāryaṃ śastraghātinaḥ ||

iti gārgyasmaraṇāt | śastraghātine yadāparapakṣikaśrāddhaṃ caturdaśyāṃ kriyate, tatraivaikoddiṣṭavidhānena nānyadety arthaḥ | na ca śastrādihatānāṃ kathaṃcic caturdaśyatikrame vihitakālātikrame śrāddasyākaraṇam eveti vācyam, praśastatarakālālābhe 'pi mahālayaśrāddhasyānuṣṭhānam āvaśyakam iti prāgdarśitatvāt | tataś ca śastrahastānām api praśastatarapañcamapakṣacaturdaśyatikrame pārvaṇavidhānenaiva dināntare 'pi kāryam,

	saṃkrāntāv uparāge ca varṣotasavamahālaye |

	nirvaped atra piṇḍāṃs trīn .............. ||

iti prajāpatismaraṇāt | saṃkrāntyādāv api aputrasyaikoddiṣṭam eva | yathāha gargaḥ |

	aputrā ye mṛtāḥ kecit striyo vā puruṣās tathā |

	teṣām api ca deyaṃ syād ekoddiṣṭaṃ na pārvaṇam || iti |

striyo bhaginyādayaḥ | puruṣāḥ bhrātrādayaḥ | tathā ca sumantuḥ |

	sapiṇḍīkaraṇād ūrdhvaṃ yatra yatra pradīyate |

	bhrātre bhaginyai putrāya svāmine mātulāya ca ||

	mitrāya gurave śrāddham ekoddiṣṭaṃ na pārvaṇam || iti |

yatra yatra saṃkrāntyuparāgavarṣotsavamahālayagayādau bhrātrādibhyaḥ pradīyate tadaikoddiṣṭavidhānena kartavyam ity arthaḥ | kātyāyano 'pi |

	saṃbandhivāndhavādīnām ekoddiṣṭaṃ tu sarvadā || iti |

yat tu jātūkarṇyena sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ prakṛtyoktam,

	ata ūrdhvaṃ na kartavyam ekoddiṣṭaṃ kadācana |

	sapiṇḍīkaraṇāntaṃ ca tat proktam iti mudgalaḥ ||

	pretatvaṃ caiva nistīrṇaḥ prāptaḥ pitṛgaṇaṃ tu saḥ |

	cyavate pitṛlokāt tu pṛthakpiṇḍena yogitaḥ ||

	sapiṇḍīkaraṇād ūrdhvaṃ pṛthaktvaṃ nopapadyate |

	pṛthaktve tu kṛte paścāt punaḥ kāryā sapiṇḍatā || 

iti, yac ca kārṣṇājininā,

	ata ūrdhvaṃ na kartavyam ekoddiṣṭaṃ kadācana |

	sapiṇḍīkaraṇāntaṃ ca pretasyaitad amaṅgalam ||

yac ca yamena,

	yaḥ sapiṇḍīkṛtaṃ pretaṃ pṛthakpiṇḍena yojayet |

	vidhighnas tena bhavati pitṛhā copajāyate ||

	ekam uddiśya yad dānaṃ pretakarma tad ucyate |

	pitṛbhyo dīyate śrāddham āhus tatra dvijottamāḥ || 

iti, yac ca purāṇe,

	pradānaṃ yatra yatraiṣāṃ sapiṇḍīkaraṇāt param |

	tatra pārvaṇavac chrāddham ekoddiṣṭaṃ tyajed budhaḥ ||

iti, tad etat sarvaṃ prātipadyenaikoddiṣṭavidhyabhāve draṣṭavyam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span>,

	madhāyuktā tu tatrāpi śastā rājan rayodaśī |

iti pūrvoktamārkaṇḍeyavacanena maghānakṣatrayuktatrayodaśyāṃ yat prāśastyam uktaṃ tad ayuktam iva pratibhāti,

	kṛṣṇapakṣe trayodaśyāṃ yac chrāddhaṃ kurute naraḥ |

	pañcatvaṃ tasya jānīyāj jyeṣṭhaputrasya niścitam ||

	madhāsu kurvataḥ śrāddhaṃ jyeṣṭhaputro vinaśyati |

ityādivacanaiḥ kṛṣṇapakṣatrayodaśyāṃ maghānakṣatre ca śrāddhānuṣṭhāne doṣasmaraṇāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span>, kiṃ tu prāguktaprāśastyaṃ mātāmahavargasahitapitṛvargaśrāddhaviṣayam, "kṛṣṇapakṣatrayodaśyām" ityādidoṣābhidhāyakavacanaṃ tu kevalapitṛvargaśrāddhaviṣayam iti viṣayabhedān madhānakṣatrayuktatrayodaśyāḥ prāśastyaṃ yuktam eva | ata eva smṛtyantaram |

	icchet trayodaśīśrāddhaṃ putravān yaḥ sutāyuṣoḥ |

	ekasyaiva tu no dadyāt pārvaṇaṃ tu samācaret || iti |

yaḥ putravān sutāyuṣor abhivṛddhim icchet sa ekasya vargasya trayodaśīśrāddhaṃ no dadyāt | vargadvayasya pārvaṇaṃ samācared ity arthaḥ | ayam evārthaḥ kārṣṇājininā spaṣṭīkṛtaḥ |

	śrāddhaṃ naivaikavargasya trayodaśyām upakramet |

	na tṛptās tatra ye yasya prajā hiṃsanti tasya te || iti |

tena vargadvayasya śrāddhaṃ kāryam ity abhiprāyaḥ | tasya phalam āha śaṅkhaḥ |

	proṣṭhapadyām atītāyāṃ maghāyuktāṃ trayodaśīm |	

	prāpya śrāddhaṃ tu kartavyaṃ madhunā pāyasena ca ||

	prajām iṣṭāṃ yaśaḥ svargam ārogyaṃ ca dhanaṃ tathā |

	nṝṇāṃ śrāddhe sadā prītāḥ prayacchanti pitāmahāḥ ||

mārkaṇdeyapurāṇe 'pi |

	prajām iṣṭāṃ (?) paśūn medhyāṃt svātantryaṃ buddhim uttamām |

	dīrgham āyus tathaiśvaryaṃ kurvāṇas tu trayodaśīm || iti |

maghātrayodaśīśrāddhaṃ kurvāṇaḥ prajādikaṃ prāpnotīty arthaḥ | mahābhāratam api |

	jñānināṃ tu bhavec chreṣṭhaḥ kurvan śrāddhaṃ trayodaśīm |

	nāvaśyaṃ tu yuvāno 'sya pramīyante narā gṛhe ||

atra maghātrayodaśīśrāddhakartuḥ gṛhe yuvāno narā avaśyaṃ niścitaṃ na pramīyanta ity arthaḥ | asmin śrāddhe piṇḍapradānaṃ putravadbhiḥ putrarahitaiś ca na kāryam, maghātrayodaśyāḥ yugāditvāt | tathā ca pulastyaḥ |

	ayanadvitaye śrāddhaṃ viṣuvaddvitaye yathā |

	yugādiṣu ca sarveṣu piṇḍanirvāpaṇād ṛte ||

kartavyam iti śeṣaḥ | putravadgṛhiṇā tu piṇḍanirvāpaṇaṃ sutarāṃ na kartavyaṃ maghānakṣatrānvitatvāt,

	saṃkrāntyām upavāsena pāraṇena ca bhārata |

	maghāyāṃ piṇḍadānena jyeṣṭhaputro vinaśyate ||

iti purāṇe doṣaśravanāt | tasamāt piṇḍamātravarjaṃ vargadvayasya śrāddhaṃ maghātrayodaśyāṃ putravadgṛhiṇā putrarahitena vā kartavyam | na ca vācyam,

	śrāddaṃ naivaikavargasya trayodaśyām upakramet |

	na tṛptās tatra ye yasya prajā hiṃsanti tasya te ||

iti vacanāt, mātāmahavargasya pṛthaguddeśena śrāddhavan mātṛvargasyāpi maghātrayodaśyāṃ pṛthaguddeśena śrāddham āvaśyakam iti, pṛthaguddeśābhāve 'pi mātṛvargasya tṛptisaṃbhavāt | tathā ca smṛtiḥ |

	na mātṛṣu pṛthak śrāddhaṃ munibhir yatra kīrtitam |

	pituḥ piṇḍodake sādhvī bhuṅkte yānapacāriṇī || iti |

bṛhaspatir api |

	svena bhartrā samaṃ śrāddhaṃ mātā bhuṅkte sadaivatam |

	pitāmahī sadā svena svenaiva prapitāmahī || iti |

sadaivataṃ śrāddhaṃ pārvaṇaśrāddham ity arthaḥ | etat patyā saha strīṇāṃ sapiṇḍīkaraṇaviṣayam | śvaśureṇa saha sapiṇḍīkaraṇaviṣaye tu tena saha pārvaṇaśrāddhaṃ bhuṅkte | tathā ca śātātapaḥ |

	ekamūrtitvam āyāti sapiṇḍīkaraṇe kṛte |

	patnī patipitṝṇāṃ tu tasmād aṃśeṣu bhāginī || iti |

patyuḥ pitrā saha sapiṇḍīkaraṇe patyuḥ pitraṃśabhāginīti vivekaḥ | smṛtyantare 'pi |

	sapiṇḍīkaraṇād ūrdhvaṃ yat pitṛbhyaḥ pradīyate |

	sarvatrāṃśaharā mātā iti dharmeṣu niścayaḥ ||

sarvatreti vacanān mahālayākhye bhādrapadāparapakṣe gayākhye ca deśaviśeṣe kriyamāṇe pārvaṇe 'tyantaprītijanake 'pi mātur aṃśahāritvam astīti mahālayagayādāv api putreṇa mātuḥ pṛthaguddeśena śrāddhaṃ na kāryam iti gamyate | ata eva caturviṃśatimate,

	ṣayāhaṃ varjayitvaikaṃ strīṇāṃ nāsti pṛthakkriyā |

ity uktam | yat punas tatraivoktam,

	kecid icchanti nārīṇāṃ pṛthakchrāddhaṃ maharṣayaḥ |

iti, tat yatra nārīṇāṃ pitāmahyādibhiḥ saha sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ kṛtaṃ tadviṣayam, tatra pitṛpiṇḍeṣv aṃśabhāgitvābhāvāt | evaṃ ca sāṃvatsarikaśrāddhād anyatra pārvaṇaśrāddhe 'pi pitrādyuddeśena kriyamāṇe patyādibhiḥ saha sapiṇḍīkṛtānāṃ pṛthaguddeśena śrāddhaṃ na kartavyam | pitāmahyādibhiḥ sārdhaṃ sapiṇḍīkṛtānāṃ pṛthaguddeśena śrāddhaṃ kartavyam iti sthitam | kathaṃ tarhi vṛddhiśrāddhe 'nvaṣṭakye ca patyādibhiḥ saha sapiṇḍīkṛtānām api mātrādīnāṃ pṛthakchrāddhānuṣṭhānam, aṃśahāriṇīnāṃ pṛthakchrāddhābhāvāt | ucyate,

	anvaṣṭakāsu vṛddhau ca pratisaṃvatsare tathā |

	atra mātuḥ pṛthakśrāddham anyatra patinā saha ||

iti smṛtyantaravacanabalāt,

	anvaṣṭake tathā mātṛśrāddhe caiv mṛte 'hani |

	ekoddiṣṭaṃ tathā muktvā triṣu nānyat pṛthag bhavet ||

iti śaṅkhavacanabalāc ca anvaṣṭakādau pṛthag anuṣṭhānam | mātṛśrāddhaṃ nāndīśrāddham | evaṃ ca yatra śrāddhaṃ strīṇāṃ patyādibhāgahāritvaṃ na saṃbhavati, saṃbhavaty api vacanāt pṛthakchrāddhavidhānaṃ tadviṣayam,

	kecid icchanti nārīṇāṃ pṛthakchrāddhaṃ maharṣayaḥ |

iti caturviṃśativacanam iti mantavyam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">apare</span> tv evaṃ manyante:

	ekamṛtitvam āyāti sapiṇḍīkaraṇe kṛte |

	patnī patipitṝṇāṃ tu tasmād aṃśeṣu bhāginī ||

iti vacanena sapiṇḍīkaraṇānantarakālaṃ patyādidevatye śrāddhe mātṝṇāṃ sahabhāvena devatātvaṃ bhavatīty etanmātraṃ vidhīyate | na tu yena saha sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ kṛtaṃ taddevatye śrāddhe sahabhāvena daivatātvam iti, asmin vacane tathāvidhaviśeṣānavagamāt | ataś ca pitāmahyādibhiḥ saha sapiṇḍīkṛtāyā api mātur na pṛthakchrāddham | etac ca mātur apṛthakchrāddham anityam,

	kecid icchanti nārīṇāṃ pṛthakchrāddhaṃ maharṣayaḥ |

iti caturviṃśatimate pṛthakchrāddhapakṣasyāpy abhidhānāt | evaṃ cānvaṣṭakāditraye mātṝṇāṃ śrāddhaṃ pṛthag eva, gayāmahālayādideśakālavaiśiṣṭyāt tṛptyādhikyāpādakaśrāddhe tu pṛthak saha vā svabhartṛbhir iti vikalpo na sarvatrāmāvāsyādiṣv apīti | yad atra yuktaṃ tad grāhyam |

	kanyāgate savitari mahālayākhye pañcamāparapakṣe śrāddhaṃ kartavyam ity uktam | yadā tu kanyāgatatvābhāvaḥ tadā śrāddhaṃ na kāryam | yad āha jyotiḥparāśaraḥ |

	arke nabhasyakanyāsthe śrāddhapakṣaḥ prakīrtitaḥ |

	sinīvālīm atikramya yadā kanyāṃ vrajed raviḥ ||

	tadā kālasya vṛddhatvād atītaiva pitṛkriyā ||

kālasya vṛddhatvāt vṛddhiyuktatvāt atītaiva pañcamapakṣam atikrāntaiva  pitṛkriyā, tatra mahālayaśrāddhaniṣedhāt | tathā ca bhṛguḥ |

	ekarāśisthite sūrye yadā darśadvayaṃ bhavet |

	havyakavyakriyāhantā tadā jñeyo 'dhimāsakaḥ ||

	vṛddhiśrāddhaṃ tadā somam agnyādheyaṃ mahālayam |

	rājābhiṣekaṃ kāmyaṃ ca na kuryād bhānulaṅghitaḥ || iti |

mahālayaṃ mahālayaśrāddham | jyotiḥpitāmaho 'pi |

	ṣaṣṭyā tu divasair māsaḥ kathito vādarāyaṇaiḥ |

	pūrvārdhaṃ tu parityajya kartavyā uttare kriyā ||

ṣaṣṭidinātmakamāsasya pūrvārdhaṃ parityajya uttarārdhe śrāddhakriyā yathākālam anuṣṭheyety arthaḥ | jyotiḥparāśaro 'pi |

	yātudhānapriyo māsaḥ kanyārke jāyate yadā |

	pitryaṃ daivaṃ tathā karma uttare māsi yujyate ||

yadā kanyāgate 'rke yātudhānapriyo māso jāyate asaṃkrāntiko bhādrapado māso jāyate ity arthaḥ | "naiṛtayātudhānānām asaṃkrāntiko 'dhimāsaḥ" iti brahmasiddhānte | naiṛtadigvartirākṣasasaṃbandhitayā asaṃkrāntikamāsasyābhidhānād evaṃ vyākhyātam | uttare māsi yujyate ity asyāyam arthaḥ |

	ṣaṣṭyā tu divasair māsaḥ kathito bādarāyaṇaiḥ |

iti matānusāreṇa bhādrapadamāsasya dvaiguṇye sati triṃśaddinasya pakṣasyānīyatvād uttaro māsa uttaraṃ triṃśaddinaṃ ṣaṣṭidinātmakabhādrapadamāsasyāparapakṣo bhavati | kanyāsaṃkrāntiyuktaś ceti mahālaye kartavyaṃ pitryādikarma tatraiva yujyata iti, tatrāpi śuklapakṣāt kṛṣṇapakṣaḥ praśastatara iti śāstrāntarato 'vagantavyam | yat tu tenaivoktam,

	māsaḥ kanyāgate bhānau asaṃkrānto yadā bhavet |

	pitryaṃ deyaṃ tathā karma tulāsthe kartur akṣayam ||

iti, tat pūrvoktakāle kathaṃcic chrāddhasyākaraṇe draṣṭavyam, pūrvoktakālāpekṣayā jaghanyakālatvāt |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ śrāddhakālaviṣayāṇi**

**athānyāny apy adhimāsaviṣayāṇi kānicid vacanāni likhyante**

tatra paiṭhīnasiḥ |

	śrautasmārtāḥ kriyāḥ sarvā dvādaśe māsi kīrtitāḥ |

	trayodaśe tu sarvās tā niṣphalā iti saṃjñitāḥ ||

	tasmāt trayodaśe māsi kuryāt tā na kathaṃcana || iti |

tāḥ śrautasmārtakriyā ity arthaḥ | trayodaśe māsi adhimāsīty arthaḥ | ata eva gabhastiḥ |

	na kuryād adhike māsi tasmin karma kadācana |

iti adhikamāsasya kālamalatvena karmānarhatvād ity abhiprāyaḥ | tathā ca gṛhyapariśiṣṭe |

	malaṃ vadanti kālasya māsaṃ kālavido 'dhikam | iti |

adhikaṃ māsaṃ kālasya malaṃ vadantīty anvayaḥ | evaṃvidho māsaḥ kadā bhavatīty apekṣite brahmasiddhānta uktam |

	caitrād arvāṅ nādhimāsaḥ paratas tv adhiko bhavet | iti |

caitrād arvāk kanyāsaṃkrāntim ārabhyety arthaḥ | ata eva jyotiḥsiddhānta uktam |

	ghaṭakanyāgate sūrye vṛścike vātha dhanvani |

	makare vātha kumbhe vā nādhimāso vidhīyate ||

kanyātulāvṛścikadhanurmakarakumbhagate sūrye adhimāso na saṃpadyate, kiṃ tv avaśiṣṭarāśigate sūrye kadācit kālavṛddhau saṃpadyata iti śeṣaḥ | tathā ca vāsiṣṭhasiddhānta uktam |

	dvātriṃśadbhir gatair māsair dinaiḥ ṣoḍaśabhis tathā |

	ghaṭikānāṃ catuṣkeṇa pataty adhikamāsakaḥ ||

atītādhikamāsād ārabhya dvātriṃśanmāsād upari ṣoḍaśadineṣu ghaṭikācatuṣṭayādhikeṣu gateṣv adhimāso bhavatīty arthaḥ | yat tu kāṭhakagṛhye 'bhihitam,

	yasmin māse na saṃkrāntiḥ saṃkrāntidvayam eva vā |

	malamāsaḥ sa vijñeyo māse triṃśattame bhavet ||

iti, tat triṃśanmāsād arvāṅ na saṃbhavatīty evaṃparam | yat tu brahmasiddhānte 'bhihitam,

	māsadvaye 'bdamadhye tu saṃkrāntir na yadā bhavet |

	prākṛtas tatra pūrvaḥ syād adhimāsas tathottaraḥ ||

iti, atra triṃśanmāsād ūrdhvaṃ yaḥ saṃkrāntirahito māsaḥ so 'dhimāsaḥ | tato 'rvāg yo 'saṃkrānto māsaḥ sa prākṛtaḥ nādhimāsa ity etāvanmātraṃ vivakṣitaṃ na punaḥ paurvāparyam iti mantavyam | yadā tv ekasmin saṃvatsare asaṃkrāntamāsadvayaṃ saṃkrāntidvayayuto māsaḥ tatrāpi triṃśanmāsād ūrdhvaṃ yo 'saṃkrānto māsaḥ so 'dhimāsaḥ | śeṣau tu saṃsarpāṃhaspatisaṃjñakāv iti boddhavyam | tathā ca bāhaspatye jyotirgranthe 'bhihitam |

	yasmin māse na saṃkrāntiḥ saṃkrāntidvayam eva vā |

	saṃsarpṃhaspatī māsāv adhimāsaś ca ninditāḥ || iti |

yasmin māse caitrād arvāṅ na saṃkrāntiḥ saṃkrāntidvayam eva vā bhavati tau saṃsarpāṃhaspatisaṃjñakau māsau, caitrāt parato yo 'saṃkrānto māsaḥ so 'dhmāsasaṃjñakaḥ | ete ca trayo māsā ninditā ity arthaḥ | eteṣv adhimāso 'tininditaḥ, kālamalarūpatvāt tasya | tathā taraivoktam: "adhimāso 'tiduṣṭatvāt" iti, ata evāsya malimlucasaṃjñā laghuhārītena darśitā |

	indrāgnī yatra hūyete māsādiḥ saṃprakīrtitaḥ |

	agnīṣomau smṛtau madhye samāptau pitṛsomapau ||

	tam atikramya cānyasmin māse gacchet kadācana |

	ādyo malimluco jñeyo dvitīyaḥ prākṛtaḥ smṛtaḥ || iti |

"indrāgnī yatra hūyete" ity anena vacobhaṅgyā kṛṣṇapratipan nirdiṣṭā | "agnīṣomau smṛtau madhye" ity anena śuklapratipan nirdiṣṭā | "samāptau pitṛsomapau" ity anenāmāvāsyā | etena cāndro māsa upalakṣitaḥ | pūrvādhimāsād ārabhya triṃśanmāsāt parato yo bhavati tam atikramyānyasmin māse yadā sūryo rāśyantaraṃ gacchati tadā pūrvo saṅkrānto māso malimluco jñeyaḥ | uttaraḥ sasaṅkrāntimasaḥ prākṛto jñeya ity arthaḥ | parāśaro 'pi |

	raviṇā laṅghito māsaś cāndraś cādyo malimlucaḥ |

	tatra yad vihitaṃ karma uttare masi kārayet ||

smṛtyantare 'pi |

	evaṃ ṣaṣṭidino māsaḥ tadardhaṃ tu malimlucaḥ |

	tyaktvā tad uttare kuryāt pitṛdaivādikāḥ kriyāḥ ||

malimlucam apy ardhaṃ kāsāṃcit pitṛdevakriyāṇām anuṣṭhāne ca tyājyam ity āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	nityanaimittake kuryāt prayataḥ sa malimluce | iti |

yasya nityasyākaraṇe kālātyayanimittaṃ prāyaścittam āmnāyate, tad yathā: "agnaye pathikṛte puroṣāśam aṣṭākapālaṃ nirvaped yo darśapūrṇamāsayājī sann amāvāsyāṃ vā paurṇamāsīṃ vātipādayet" iti | tathābhūtasya nityasya grahaṇam, na tu nityamātrasya | tena darśapūrṇamāsāgnihotrapañcamahāyajñāder anuṣṭhānaṃ malimluce kartavyam, svakālātikrame prāyaścittāmnānāt | evaṃ ca nityāpi somayāgakriyā malimluce māsi ca kāryā, malimlucamāsātikrame 'pi vasantādikālasya somayāgāṅgabhūtasyānatikrāntatvenātra prāyaścittaprāpter asambhavāt | evaṃ yasya naimittikasya gṛhadāheṣṭyāder nimittānantarakāle kartavyasya māsāntare vihitakālālābhaḥ tathābhūtāvaśyakakriyāviṣaya eva malimluce māsi kuryād iti vidhānam | jāteṣṭyāder naimittikasyāpi śiśusaṃrakṣaṇārthaṃ nimittānantarakālam apahāya kālāntare kartavyasya yathā daśarātrādisūtakakālamadhye 'nuṣṭhānam anyāyyam, tathā malimlucakālamadhye 'pīti tasya na malimluce 'nuṣṭhānam | evaṃ ca nityatvaṃ naimittikatvaṃ cāvivakṣitam | yasyātikrame prāyaścittaprāptiḥ yasya ca māsāntare vihitakālālābhenāvaśyakaṃ malimluce 'nuṣṭhānaṃ tat sarvaṃ malimluce kuryād iti bārhaspatyavacanatātparyārthaḥ pratyetavyaḥ | tathā ca smṛtyantare |

	ananyagati yan nityaṃ kuryān naimittikaṃ tathā | iti |

gṛhyapariśiṣṭe 'pi |

	malaṃ vadanti kālasya māsaṃ kālavido 'dhikam |

	nehetātra tv aśeṣejyām anyatrāvaśyakād vidheḥ || iti |

anenāvaśyako vidhir adhikamāse 'nuṣṭheya ity arthād uktaṃ bhavati | uktaṃ ca sākṣād api tatraiva,

	avaṣaṭkārahomāś ca parva cāgrayaṇaṃ tathā |

	malamāse tu kartavyam .................. || iti |

avaṣaṭkāramomāḥ agnihotraupāsanavaisvadevādayaḥ | parva darśapūrṇamāsau, pārvaṇaḥ sthālīpākaś ca | āgrayaṇam āgrayaṇeṣṭiḥ | yady apy āgrayaṇam "varṣāsu śyāmākair yajeta" iti māsadvayātmakavarṣākhyartau vihitaṃ tat amalimlucamāse 'pi tatkālasaṃbhavād ananyagatikaṃ na bhavati | tathāpi durbhikṣe navaśyāmākavyatiriktadhānyāsaṃbhave jīvanārthaṃ navaśyāmākānnbhojanam akṛtāgrayaṇenākartavyam ity āgrayaṇānuṣṭhānaṃ jīvanārtham āvaśyakam iti yuktam uktam āgrayaṇaṃ tatheti | yadā tu durbhikṣābhāvād anāvaśyakaṃ tadādhimāse navaśyāmākāgrayaṇaṃ na kartavyam | anenaivābhiprāyeṇa paiṭhīnasinā,

	saṃkrāntirahite māsi kuryād āgyaṇaṃ na vā |

iti vikalpa uktaḥ | anyāny api kānicin malimluce kāryāṇīty uktāni yamena |

	garbhe vārdhuṣike bhṛtye śrāddhakarmaṇi māsike |

	sapiṇḍīkaraṇe nitye nādhimāsaṃ vivarjayet ||

	tīrthasnānaṃ japo homo yavavrīhitilādibhiḥ |

	jātakarmāntyakarmāṇi navaśrāddhaṃ tathaiva ca ||

	makhātrayodaśīśrāddhaṃ śrāddhāny api ca ṣoḍaśa |

	candrasūryagrahe snānaṃ śrāddhaṃ dānaṃ japādikam ||

	kāryāṇi malamāse 'pi nityaṃ naimittikaṃ tathā | iti |

garbhe garbhanimittake garbhamātraprayuktyā vihite puṃsavanasīmantādika iti yāvat | vārdhuṣike,

	aśītibhāgo vṛddhiḥ syāt māsi māsi sabandhake |

ityādivacanoktavṛddhigrahaṇe | bhṛtye saṃvatsarādiparyantakālakṛte bhṛtye | māsike śrāddhakarmaṇi, amāvāsyāśrāddhakarmaṇīty arthaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">anye</span> <span style="text-decoration:underline;">tu</span> manyanta: amāvāsyāśrāddhaṃ trayodaśe 'pi māsi ṛśyaśṛṅgavacanena niṣiddham, tena māsikaśabdo nāmāvāsyāśrāddham āha, kiṃ tu prathamasaṃvatsaravihitamāsikaśrāddham āheti | ṛśyaśṛṅgavacanaṃ caivaṃ paṭhanti |

	saṃvatsarātireko vai māso yaḥ syāt trayodaśaḥ |

	tasmāt trayodaśe śrāddhaṃ na kuryād indusaṃkṣaye || iti |

apare tu:

	tasmāt trayodaśaṃ śrāddhaṃ na kuryān nopatiṣṭhate |

iti paṭhanti | ayam eva pāṭho yuktaḥ | indusaṃkṣaya iti pāṭhe piṇḍapitṛyajñavat tadanantaram avaśyānuṣṭheyasyāmāvāsyāśrāddhasya pratiṣedhānarhasya pratiṣedhaprasaṅgāt,

	jātakarmaṇi yac chrāddhaṃ darśaśrāddhaṃ tathaiva ca |

	pratisaṃvatsaraṃ yac ca pūrvamāse prakīrtitam ||

iti vacanavirodhaprasaṅgāc ca | tasmāt "śrāddhakarmaṇi māsike" ity anena amāvāsyāśrāddham uktam iti vyākhyānam eva yuktam | ṛśyaśṛṅgavacanārtha upariṣṭād bhaviṣyati | nitye nityadāne | homo 'traupāsanahomaḥ, "yavavrīhitilādibhiḥ" iti tatra hotavyadravyānuvādāt | atyantakarmāṇi dahanodakapiṇḍadānāsthisaṃcayanādīni | śeṣaṃ vyaktam | jātakarmagrahaṇaṃ jātaśrāddhāder upalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva smṛtyantaram |

	śrāddhajātakanāmāni ye ca saṃskārasavratāḥ |

	malimluce 'pi kartavyā iṣṭīḥ kāmyāś ca varjayet |

saṃskārāḥ annaprāśananiṣkramaṇādayaḥ | savratā janārdanaśayanād ārabhya yāvad utthānaṃ dhāraṇapāraṇādikaṃ kariṣyāmīty evaṃ saṃkalpasahitāḥ | kāmyā iti grahaṇaṃ kāmyapaśubandhādikarmopalakṣaṇārtham, sarveṣām api kāmyānām anāvaśyakatvena varjanīyatvāt | ata eva hārītaḥ |

	adhimāse na kartavyaṃ śrāddham abhyudayaṃ tathā |

	tathaiva kāmyaṃ yat karma ................ || iti |

yat kāmyaṃ karma iṣṭyādikaṃ tat sarvam adhimāse na kartavyam ity arthaḥ | ābhyudayikaṃ śrāddhaṃ cūḍākaraṇāt prāktanasaṃskāreṣu vihitābhyudayikaśrāddhavyatiriktaṃ draṣṭavyam, jātakarmādau viśeṣeṇābhyudayikaśrāddhavidhānasya pūrvam eva pradarśitatvāt | anyāny api ca varjyāny āha vṛddhamanuḥ |

	agnyādheyaṃ pratiṣṭhāṃ ca yajñadānavratāni ca |

	vedavratavṛṣotsargacūḍākaraṇamekhalāḥ ||

	māṅgalyam abhiṣekaṃ ca malamāse vivarjayet |

	bāle vā yadi vā vṛddhe śukre cāstam upāgate ||

	malamāsa ivaitāni varjayed devadarśanam || iti |

"agnyādheyaṃ pratiṣṭhāṃ ca yajñadānavratāni ca" ity atra anāvasyakatve satīty viśeṣo draṣṭavyaḥ | tena malamāse 'pi prāyaścittabhūtam agnyādheyam agnyanugatyanantaraṃ kartavyaṃ na pratiṣidhyate | evaṃ pratimādināśe punaḥpratiṣṭhā na pratiṣidhyate | evaṃ prāyaścittabhūtasaṃsargeṣṭyādiyajño na pratiṣidhyate | yad yat prāyaścitte deyam iti prāyaścittadānaṃ ca "brāhmaṇaṃ tu vasatyai nāparundhyāt" ityādivrataṃ ca | vṛṣotsargasya caikādaśādikasya pratiṣedhaḥ, ṣoḍaśaśrāddhādivat tasyāpi pretopakārakatvāt | śukrāstamayādāv apy anāvaśyakatve saty eva agnyādheyādi pratiṣidhyate | malamāsa ity evābhidhānāt | "varjayed devadarśanam" iti pratiṣedhaḥ prathamadarśanaviṣaya evety āhuḥ | hārīto 'pi |

	........................... vatsarāt prathamād ṛte |

	sapiṇḍīkaraṇād ūrdhvaṃ yat kiṃcic chrāddakaṃ bhavet ||

	iṣṭaṃ vāpy atha vā pūrtaṃ tan na kuryān malimluce || iti |

sapiṇḍīkaraṇād ūrdhvaṃ yat prathamasaṃvatsare pratimāsaṃ punaḥ kriyamāṇaṃ traipuruṣikaṃ māsikaṃ śrāddhaṃ tan malimluce 'pi māse kāryam iti vaktum "vatsarāt prathamād ṛte"ity uktam | asminn eva viṣaye vasiṣṭho 'pi: "saṃvatasramadhye 'dhimāso bhavet māsikārthaṃ dinam ekaṃ vṛddhiṃ nayet" iti | smṛtyantare 'pi |

	saṃvatsare vivṛddhe 'pi pratimāsaṃ ca māsikam || iti |

sapiṇḍīkaraṇāt prāk kriyamāṇamāsikaviṣaye tu gabhastinoktam |

	ekoddiṣṭaṃ tu yac chrāddhaṃ tan naimittikam ucyate |

	tat kāryaṃ pūrvamāse ca kālādhikye 'pi dharmataḥ || iti |

caśabdād uttaramāse 'pi kāryam iti gamyate | tad etat sapiṇḍīkaraṇāt prāktanamāsikaviṣayam, ekoddiṣṭarūpamāsikaviṣyatvāt | yat tu ṛśyaśṛṅgenoktam,

	saṃvatsarātireko yo māsaś caiva trayodaśaḥ |

	asurāṇāṃ tu māso 'sau tasmād devavigarhitaḥ ||

	tasmāt trayodaśaṃ śrāddhaṃ na kuryān nopatiṣṭhate ||

iti, tat sapiṇḍīkaraṇāt prāktanamāsikeṣu sapiṇḍīkaraṇāt prāk kathaṃcid akṛteṣu vacanabalāt sapiṇḍīkaraṇād ūrdhvam anuṣṭhātavyeṣv ekoddiṣṭeṣu pratimāsaṃ kriyamāṇeṣu trayodaśe māsi prāptamāsikaśrāddhaviṣayam | vigarhite māsi pratiprasavam antareṇa kriyamāṇaṃ yato nopatiṣṭhate atas trayodaśaṃ śrāddhaṃ na kuryād ity arthaḥ | asya vacanasyoktā viṣayavyavasthā devasvāminā darśitā: "yasya tāratamyāc chīghrataram upasthite piṇḍapitṛyajñādau deśakālānurodhato dravyabrāhmaṇābhāvāt ṣoḍaśaśrāddhāny akṛtvā saṃvatsarād arvāk sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ kṛtam, tasya kṛte 'pi sapiṇḍīkaraṇe,

	māsikaṃ codakumbhaṃ ca deyaṃ tasyāpi vatsaram |

iti vākyāt yadā trayodaśaṃ śrāddhaṃ prāptamāsikākhyāṃ pretaśrāddhaṃ tad anena ṛśyaśṛṅgavākyena niṣidhyate" iti granthena | evaṃ ca trayodaśamāsaśālini saṃvatsare pramītasya māsikāni śrāddhāni trayodaśa bhavanti | yadā tu dravyabrāhmaṇādyalābhena sapiṇḍīkaraṇād ūrdhvam eva māsikaśrāddhāni kriyante tadā tāni dvādaśa bhavantīti mantavyam | evaṃ ca yat <span style="text-decoration:underline;">kaiścid</span> uktam: saṃvatsaravimokāntam ānumāsikāni kurvan malamāse naiva kuryād uttare kuryād eva | saṃvatsarānte sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ saṃvatsaravimokaṃ ca yathākālaṃ māsikāni kurvann api malamāse naiva kuryād uttare kuryād eveti, <span style="text-decoration:underline;">tat</span> "māsikārthaṃ dinam ekaṃ vṛddhiṃ nayet,"

	saṃvatsare vivṛddhe 'pi pratimāsaṃ ca māsikam |

	pūrvamāse ca kartavyaṃ kālādhikye 'pi dharmataḥ ||

iti vacanadvayādarśananibandhanam ity upakṣaṇīyam | māsikaśrāddhābhiprāyeṇa vṛddhavasiṣṭhenāpy uktam |

	śrāddhīyāhani saṃprāpte adhimāso bhaved yadi |

	śrāddhadvayaṃ prakuravīta evaṃ kurvan na muhyati || iti |

śrāddhadvayaṃ prakurvīta adhimāse taduttaramāse ca māsikaśrāddhaṃ prakurvītety arthaḥ | yat tu jyotiḥparāśarenoktam,

	upākarma tathotsargaḥ prasavāhotsavāṣṭakāḥ |

	māsavṛddhau parāḥ kāryāḥ varjayitvā tu paitṛkam ||

iti, parāḥ kāryāḥ uttare māsi kāryā ity arthaḥ | tatra prasavāhotsavaśabdena jāteṣṭir eva gṛhyate | na punar ābhyudayikaṃ śrāddhaṃ jātakarma ca, tayor api grahaṇe,

	śrāddhajātakanāmāni ye ca saṃskārasavratāḥ |

	malimluce 'pi kartavyā iṣṭīḥ kāmyāś ca varjayet ||

iti smṛtivrodhāpatteḥ | paitṛkaśabdena sāṃvatsarikarūpaṃ gṛhyate na tu sāmānyam,

	pratisaṃvatsaraśrāddhe nādhimāsaṃ vivarjayet |

	malamāse 'pi kartavyaṃ śrāddhaṃ yat prativatsaram ||

	pratisaṃvatsaraṃ yac ca pūrvamāse prakīrtitam ||

ityādivacaneṣu tasyaiva spaṣṭam abhidhānāt | sarvāṇy etāni vacanāni malamāsamṛtasya punar malamāsaprāptau draṣṭavyāni,

	māsapakṣatithispṛṣṭe yo yasmin mriyate 'hani |

	pratyabdaṃ tu tathābhūtaṃ kṣayāhaṃ tasya taṃ vidhuḥ ||

iti smaraṇāt | evaṃ ca malamāsamṛtasya malamāsasaṃbhave sati malamāsagatakṣayāha evābdikaśrāddhaṃ kartavyam | na tu śuddhamāsagatakṣayāhe, atathābhūtatvāt | malamāsāsaṃbhave tu guṇalopanyāyāt malamāsāspṛṣṭe 'pi kṣayāhe mṛtāhaśrāddhaṃ kartavyam evety avagantavyam | yat tu satyavratenoktam,

	varṣe varṣe tu yac chrāddhaṃ mātāpitror mṛte 'hani |

	malamāse na kartavyaṃ vyāghrasya vacanaṃ yathā ||

iti, tat adhikamāsād anyatra mṛtasya mṛtāhaśrāddhaviṣayam | śuddhe māsi mṛtasya śuddhamāsaspṛṣṭa eva mṛtāhaḥ tathābhūto na tu malamāsaspṛṣṭaḥ, malamāsagatakṣayāhasyāvihitakālatvāt | ata eva paiṭhīnasiḥ |

	malamāse mṛtānāṃ tu śrāddhaṃ yat prativatsaram |

	malamāse tu kartavyaṃ nānyeṣāṃ tu kathaṃcana || iti |

anyeṣāṃ malamāsād anyatra mṛtānām ity arthaḥ | malamāse 'pi kartavyaṃ tatraiva vihitakālasadbhāvad ity abhiprāyaḥ | bhṛgur api |

	malamāsamṛtānāṃ tu śrāddhaṃ yat prativatsaram |

	malamāse 'pi tat kāryaṃ nānyeṣāṃ tu kathaṃcana ||

yat tu vṛddhavasiṣṭhenoktam,

	śrāddhiyāhani saṃprāpte adhimāso bhaved yati |

	śrāddhadvayaṃ prakurvīta evaṃ kurvan na muhyati || 

iti, na tat sāṃvatsarikaśrāddhaviṣayam, sāṃvatsarikaśrāddhe uttare māsi malamāsaspṛṣṭakṣayāhāsaṃbhavāt | tena māsikaśrāddhaviṣayam etad vacanam | evaṃ ca māsikaśrāddhaṃ malamāse uttaramāse ca kāryam | sāṃvatsarikaṃ tv anyataramāse, tatra malamāsamṛtānām ādyamāse tadanyamāsamṛtānām uttare  māsīty anusaṃdheyam | "nānyeṣāṃ tu kathaṃcana" iti yo 'yaṃ pratiṣedhaḥ sa tu prathamābdikavyatiriktaviṣayaḥ, prathamābdikasya malamāse vacanabalena kartavyatvāt | tathā ca hārītaḥ |

	asaṃkrānte tu kartavyam ābdikaṃ prathamaṃ dvijaiḥ || iti |

smṛtyantare 'pi |

	ābdikaṃ prathamaṃ yat syāt tat kurvīta malimluce || iti,

	trayodaśe ca saṃprāpte kurvīta punar ābdikam ||

punarābdikaṃ prathamābdikaṃ trayodaśe uttare māsi saṃprāpte kurvītety arthaḥ | laghuhārīto 'pi |

	pratyabdaṃ dvādaśe māsi kāryā piṇḍakriyā dvijaiḥ |

	kvacit trayodaśe 'pi syād ādyaṃ muktvā tu vatsaram ||

piṇḍakriyā mṛtāhaśrāddhakriyā dvādaśe māsi paripūrṇe sati trayodaśe māsīti yāvat | kvacid adhimāsayuktasaṃvatsare trayodaśe māsi paripūrṇe sati caturdaśe māsa iti yāvat | ādyam ābdikaṃ tv adhimāsavaty api saṃvatsare dvādaśe māsi paripūrṇe sati kāryam, trayodaśe māsi kāryam ity arthaḥ | yat tu śātātapenoktam,

	ekasaṃjñau yadā māsau syāyāṃ saṃvatsare kvacit |

	tatrādye pitṛkāryāṇi devakāryāṇi cottare ||

iti, yac ca paiṭhīnasinā,

	dvau māsāv ekanāmānau syātāṃ saṃvatsare yadi |

	pūrve tu pitṛkāryāṇi devakāryāṇi cāpare ||

iti, tat yeṣāṃ pitṛkāryāṇāṃ malimluce vidhiḥ, yeṣāṃ ca devakāryāṇām uttare māsi vidhiḥ, tathāvidhapitṛdevakāryaparam ity avagantavyam | yady apy asaṃkrāntiḥ saṃkrāntidvayayuto vā saṃsarpasaṃjño 'ṃhaspatisaṃjñaś (?) ca māsaḥ kadācic caitrād arvāg bhavati, tathāpi tatra na pūrvoktavidhiniṣedhavacanāni vidhāyakāni niṣedhakāni vā, teṣāṃ vacanānām adhimāsaviṣayatvāt | na ca saṃsarpāṃhaspatisaṃjñakāvadhimāsau,

	caitrād arvāṅ nādhimāsaḥ paratas tv adhiko bhavet |

	dṛṣṭā hi sarvaśāstreṣu tasmin mūrtis trayodaśī ||

iti vacanena caitrāt parata evādhimāsasmaraṇāt | tasmin caitrād uttaratraiva trayodaśī mūrtir adhimāsamūrtiḥ sarvagaṇitaśāstreṣu yato dṛṣṭvety arthaḥ | evaṃ ca saṃsarpāṃhaspatisaṃjñakau na karmānarhakalau kiṃ tu praśastāv eveti mantavyam ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyām adhimāsaviṣayāṇi**

**athānyāny api mṛtāhaviṣayāṇi kānicid vacanāni likhyante**

tatra gargaḥ |

	vivāhādau smṛtaḥ sauro yajñādau sāvanaḥ smṛtaḥ |

	ābdike pitṛkārye 'pi cāndramāsaḥ praśasyate ||

yajñādau māsasaṃvatsarasādhyayajñavrataprāyaścittakriyādiṣv ity arthaḥ | tatra māsasādhyayajñāḥ "darśapūrṇamasābhyāṃ yajeta, māsaṃ vaiśvadevena" ity evamādivākyaiḥ vihitāḥ | māsasādhyavratāni māsopavāsādīni | māsasādhyaprāyaścittakiryās tu,

	goṣṭhe vasan brahmacārī masam ekaṃ payovrataḥ |

	gāyatrījapanirato mucyate sa pratigrahāt ||

ityādivākyavihitāḥ | saṃvatsarasādhyā yajñāḥ gavāmayanādyāḥ satrayāgāḥ | saṃvatsarasādhyavratāni tu "nāśnīyāt" ityādiśrutivihitāni | saṃvatsarasādhyāḥ prāyaścittakriyāḥ dvādaśavārṣikādyā draṣṭavyāḥ | ābdike sāṃvatsarikaśrāddhe | pitṛkārye ṣāṇmāsikaśrāddhādau | apiśabdān māsasaṃvatsarasādhye yajñavyatirikte sarvasmin devakārye cāndro māsaḥ praśasyata ity uktam | uktaṃ ca pitāmahena |

	daive karmaṇi pitrye ca māsaś cāndramasaḥ smṛtaḥ | iti |

kaḥ punar bhedaś cāndrasāvanasaurāṇām ity apekṣite brahmasiddhānta uktam |

	darśād darśaś cāndras triṃśad divasas tu sāvano māsaḥ |

	ravisaṃkrāntikacihnaḥ sauro māso nigadyate tajjñaiḥ ||

asyārthaḥ smṛtyantare spaṣṭīkṛtaḥ |

	cāndraḥ śuklādidarśāntaḥ sāvanas triṃśatā dinaiḥ |

	ekarāśau ravir yāvat kālaṃ māsaḥ sa bhāskaraḥ ||

śuklapratipadādidarśāntaś cāndro māsa ity etad dakṣiṇāpathe draṣṭavyam | uttarāpathe tu kṛṣṇapratipadādipaurṇamāsyantaḥ cāndro māsa iti veditavyaḥ, tatra paurṇamāsyante cāndramāsavyavahārāt | ata eva dvividhacāndramāsasaṃgrahārtham,

	yasmin māse dine yasmin vipattir upajāyate |

	parvānataḥ sa tu vijñeyo maso naimittikaṃ prati ||

iti gārgyeṇa parvānta iti sāmānyenoktam | naimittikaṃ pratisāṃvatsarikaśrāddhaṃ pratīty arthaḥ | dine tu viśeṣaḥ smṛtyantare darśitaḥ |

	māsapakṣatithispṛṣṭe yo yasmin mriyate 'hani |

	pratyabdaṃ tu tathābhūtaṃ kṣayāhaṃ tasya taṃ viduḥ || iti |

tithiśabdena cāndra evāhorātra ucyate | na tu sauraḥ sāvano vāhorātraḥ, "tadādyās tithayo dvayoḥ" ity amarasiṃhena cāndrāhorātreṣv eva tithiśabdānuśāsanāt | tadādyāḥ pratipadādyāḥ tithiśabdābhidheyā ity arthaḥ | kaḥ punaḥ sāvanasauracāndrāhorātrāṇāṃ bheda ity apekṣite brahmasiddhānte uktam |

	sāvanaṃ syād ahorātram udayād odayād raveḥ |

	sauras triṃśas tu rāśyaṃśaḥ tithiḥ saṃyogam aindavam ||

meṣādirāśeḥ triṃśam aṃśaṃ yāvatā kālena ravir bhuṅkte tāvān kālaḥ sauraḥ ahorātraḥ | pratipadāditithiparimitaḥ kālaś cāndraḥ ahorātra ity arthaḥ | sa ca sāvanāhorātravat sūryodayād ārabhya punaḥ śūryodayaparyanto yadā bhavati tadā saṃpūrṇa iti nigadyate,

	pratipatprabhṛtayaḥ sarvā udayād odayād raveḥ |

	saṃpūrṇā iti vikhyātāḥ .................. ||

iti smaraṇāt | yadā tv evaṃbhūto na bhavati tadā khaṇḍatithir iti vyatirekād gamyate | pratyabdaṃ maraṇamāsapakṣatithispṛṣṭakālābhāve 'pi tatsadṛśakāla evābdikaśrāddhakāla iti vaktum,

	pratyabdaṃ tu tathābhūtaṃ kṣayāhaṃ tasya taṃ viduḥ |

ity uktam | tathābhūtaṃ maraṇamāsapakṣatithispṛṣṭakālasadṛśam ity arthaḥ | yadā punar dinadvayaṃ tathābhūtaṃ pūrvadine tu karmakāle tithiyogaḥ, uttaradine tu karmakāle tithiyogābhāvaḥ tadā pūrvam ahaḥ srāddhakāla ity āha sumantuḥ |

	dvyahavyāpinī vet syān mṛtāhasya tu yā tithiḥ |

	pūrvasyāṃ nirvapet piṇḍam ity āṅgirasabhāṣitam ||

pūrvasyāṃ pūrvadinavyāpinyām ity arthaḥ | anena pūrvadine caturthapraharottarārdhavyatiriktāparāhṇe tithiyuktasamaya eva sāṃvatsarikaśrāddhaṃ kāryam ity uktaṃ bhavati | yadā tu pūrvadine caturthapraharottarārdhavyatirikte 'parāhṇe caramamuhūrte tithiyogaḥ tadā uttaradine kutapād ārabhya muhūrtapañcake mṛtatithiyukte 'pi pūrvadine tithiyogasamaye śrāddham upakramya rātreḥ prāg eva samāpanīyam, svakālopakrānte karmaṇi kālāntare 'py avilambena tatsamāpanasya vidhinākṣiptatvāt | evaṃ ca ya vyāghrapādavacanaṃ,

	vidhijñaḥ śraddhayopetaḥ samyak pātraniyojakaḥ |

	rātrer anyatra kurvāṇaḥ śreyaḥ prāpnoty anuttamam ||

iti, tat svakālopakrāntasrāddhaviṣayam ity avagantavyam | tad etat sarvam abhisaṃdhāya aparārkeṇāpy uktam: "sāṃvatsarikādiśrāddhaṃ tithiyukte 'parāhṇakāle yatr kutracit kāryam | sā cet sāyāhnamātravyāpinī syāt tadā sāyāhna eva vyāghrapādavacanabalena śrāddhaṃ kāryam | na punar udayavyāpinyām aparāhṇaparyantāyām" iti | yadā tu pūrvadine karmakālāsaṃsparśiny apy astagāminī tithiḥ uttaradine karmakālasaṃsparśiny anastagāminī tadāpi pūrvam evāhaḥ śrāddhakālaḥ "śrāddhādāv astagāminī" iti smaraṇāt | astagāminī tithiḥ sāṃvatsarikaśrāddhādau grāhyety arthaḥ | na ca pūrvavad atrāpi tithiyuktasamaye śrāddham upakramya rātreḥ prāksamāpanaṃ yuktam, caturthapraharottarārdhasya śrāddhakālatvābhāvāt | tathā coktaṃ matsyapurāṇe |

	ūrdhvaṃ muhūrtāt kutapād yan muhūrtacatuṣṭayam |

	muhūrtapañcakaṃ hy etat svadhābhavanam iṣyate || iti |

kātyāyanenāpy uktam |

	vāsarasya tṛtīye 'ṃśe nātisaṃdhyāsamīpataḥ | iti |

na cātra caturthapraharottarārdhavyatiriktāparāhṇakāle tithiyogāsaṃbhavena tithiyuktāparāhṇakālābhāvād ananuṣṭhānam eva śrāddhasyeti vācyam | yad āha nāradīyapurāṇe vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	pāraṇe maraṇe nṝṇāṃ tithis tātkālikī smṛtā |

	pitrye 'stamayavelāyāṃ spṛṣṭā pūrṇā nigadyate || iti |

astamayavelāyāṃ spṛṣṭā mṛtatithis tattithau kartavye pitrye ābdikādiśrādddhe pūrṇā nigadyata ity arthaḥ | astamayavelāyāṃ spṛṣṭety anenāstamayasamaye kalāmatrasadbhāve 'pi. mṛtatitheḥ pūrṇatvam uktam iti mantavyam | yat tu smṛtyantaram,

	dinānte pañcanāḍyas tu puṇyāḥ proktā manīṣibhiḥ |

	udaye ca tathā pitrye daive caiva ca karmaṇi ||

iti, pitrye karmaṇi kālatvena coditatithisaṃbandhinyo dinānte vartamānāḥ pañca nāḍyaḥ puṇyāḥ tataḥ prāktananāḍīnāṃ tithiyogajanyapuṇyāpādikāḥ na tu tato nyūnāḥ | daive karmaṇi kālatvena coditatithisaṃbandhinya udaye sati vartamānāḥ pañca nāḍyaḥ puṇyāḥ tata uparitananāḍīnāmapi tithiyogajanyapuṇyāpādikāḥ na tato nyūnā iti tasyārthaḥ | tad etat,

	pratiapddhanalābhāya dvitīyā dvipadapradā |

ityādinā,

	śrāddhaṃ kurvann amāvāsyāṃ yatnena puruṣaḥ śuciḥ |

	sarvān kāmān avāpnoti ................ ||

ityantena kāmyaśrāddhakālatayā vihitakṛṣṇapakṣapratipadāditithidvaidhaviṣayam, na tu śrāddhāntarakālatayā vihitatithidvaidhaviṣayam,

	pitryaṃ śrāddhaṃ kṛṣṇapakṣe dine 'stamayayogini |

iti prastutya tatraiva viśeṣaparatvābhidhānād asya vacanasya | tena pūrvoktavasiṣṭhavacanena saha na kaścid virodhaḥ | bhaviṣyatpurāṇe 'pi,

	vratopavāsaniyame ghaṭikaikā yadā bhavet |

	sā tithiḥ sakalā jñeyā pitrye caivāparāhṇikī || iti |

saṃdhyāsamīpasthāparāhṇake ghaṭikaikā yadā bhavet sā tithiḥ pitryarthe sakalā jñeyety arthaḥ | evaṃ caivaṃvidhaviṣaye,

	prārabhya kutape śrāddhaṃ kuryād ārauhiṇaṃ budhaḥ |

iti vacanārtha eva kāryaḥ, tadatikrame kāraṇābhāvāt | ekoddiṣṭarūpamṛtāhaśrāddhe tu navamuhūrthād uparitanamuhūrte mṛtadināsaṃbhave 'pi madhyāhnavyāpitvāt "sā tithiḥ sakalā jñeyā" iti nyāyena na kutape prārabhya śrāddhaṃ rauhiṇe samāpanīyam, "ekoddiṣṭaṃ tu madhyāne" iti smaraṇāt | yadā tu pūrvadine astamayāt pūrvakṣaṇe tithiyogaḥ uttaradine tv astamayād upari trimuhūrtayuktā tadā uttaram āha śrāddhakālaṃ sumantuḥ |

	udite daivataṃ bhānau pitryaṃ cāstamite ravau |

	dvimuhūtrā trirahno yā sā tithir havyakavyayoḥ ||

asyārthaḥ: udite bhānau saty ahaḥsaṃbandhinī daivakarmāṅgabhūtā tithir yā dvimuhūrtā bhavati sā saṃpūrṇatithivat kṛtsnasyāhno havyadānakālatām āpādayati | tena tasminn ahanit daivataṃ karma kuryāt | pitṛkarmāṅgabhūtā tithir astamite ravau sati yā trimuhūrtam anuvartate sā kavyadānakālatāṃ svasaṃbaddhasyāhna āpādayati | tena tatsaṃbaddhe 'hni paitṛkaṃ pitṛsaṃbandhi sāṃvatsarikādi śrāddhaṃ kuryād iti | tenottaradine 'stamayād upari trimuhūrtānuvṛttyabhāve astagāminī pūrvatithir eva grāhyety uktaṃ bhavati | evaṃ ca yad uktaṃ nāradīyapurāṇe,

	darśaṃ ca pūrṇamāsaṃ ca pituḥ sāṃvatsaraṃ dinam |

	pūrvaviddham akurvāṇo narakaṃ pratipadyate ||

iti, tat uttaradine astamayād upari muhūrtatrayānuvṛttyabhāve draṣṭavyam | yadā tu pūrvedyur astagāminī tithir na bhavati uttaredyur apy astamite ravau trimuhūrtavyāpinī na bhavati kiṃ tv astagāminī bhavati tadāpi saiva grāhyā "śrāddhādāv astagāminī" iti smaraṇāt | yadā tu dinadvaye 'py astagāminī tithir na bhavati tata uttaredyur evāstagāmitvarūpaguṇābhāve 'pi guṇalopanyāyena sāṃvatsarikaśrāddhaṃ kartavyam, tithiyuktāparāhnakālasaṃbhavāt | akaraṇe vihitātikrameṇa pratyavāyāpatteś ca ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ mṛtāhaviṣayāṇi**

**atha māsapakṣatithispṛṣṭamṛtāhāparijñānaviṣayāṇi**

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	na jñāyate mṛtāhaś cet pramīte proṣite sati |

	māsaś cet prativijñātaḥ taddarśaḥ syān mṛte 'hani ||

	yadā māso na vijñāto vijñātaṃ dinam eva tu |

	tadā mārgaśire māsi māghe vā taddinaṃ bhavet ||

	dinamāsau na vijñātau maraṇasya yadā punaḥ |

	prasthānadinamāsau tu grāhyau pūrvoktayā diśā || iti |

dinaśabdena mṛtatithir evādhigantavyā | proṣite pitrādāv apragalbhasvajanasamīpe pramīte sati kālaviśeṣajñānādyabhāvena mṛtāho yadi na vijñāyeta māsamātram eva tu jñātaṃ tadā mṛtāhe yat kāryaṃ tat sarvaṃ mṛtamāsasyāmāvāsyāyāṃ kartavyam iti prathamaślokasyārthaḥ | "taddarśas syān mṛte 'hani" ity atra darśagrahaṇaṃ tanmāsasaṃbandhinyā ekādaśyā api pradarśanārtham | ata eva marīciḥ |

	śrāddhavighne samutpanne avijñāte mṛte 'hani |

	ekādaśyāṃ tu kartavyaṃ kṛṣṇapakṣe viśeṣataḥ ||

"pūrvoktayā diśā" ity asyāyam arthaḥ | yadi prasthānamāsamātraṃ jñātaṃ tadā tanmāsasyāmāvāsyāyāṃ sāṃvatsarikaśrāddhaṃ kāryam | yadi prasthānatithipakṣāv eva jñātau tadā mārgaśīrṣe māghe vā māsi jñātapakṣatithispṛṣṭadine kāryam | yadā tu prasthānadinamāsādy api na jñātaṃ tadā maraṇavārtāśravaṇamāsapakṣatithispṛṣṭadine kāryam | "aparijñāte amāvāsyāyāṃ śravaṇadine vā" iti precetasoktatvāt | yadā tu maraṇavārtāśravaṇasyāpy abhāvaḥ tadā tv āha jātūkarṇyaḥ |

	pitari proṣite yasya na vārtā naiva cāgatiḥ |

	ūrdhvaṃ pañcadaśād varṣāt kṛtvā tat pratirūpakam ||

	kuryāt tasya ca saṃskāraṃ yathoktavidhinā tataḥ |

	tadādīny eva sarvāṇi śeṣakāryāṇi saṃcaret || iti |

sarvāṇīti vacanān mṛtāhakāryam api dahanamāsapakṣatithispṛṣṭadine kartavyam iti gamyate ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ māsapakṣatithispṛṣṭamṛtāhāparijñānaviṣayāṇi**

**atha kāmyaśrāddhakālāḥ**

tatra viṣṇuḥ |

	saṃkrāntiviṣuve caiva viśeṣeṇāyanadvayam |

	vyatīpāto 'tha janmarkṣaṃ candrasūryagrahas tathā ||

	ity etān śrāddhakālāṃs tu kāmyān āha prajāpatiḥ |

	śrāddham eteṣu yad dattaṃ tad ānantyāya kalpate || iti |

"śrāddhakālān kāmyān āha" ity anena saṃkrāntyādikālalakṣaṇo guṇaḥ kāmyaphalasādhako na punaḥ śrāddhalakṣaṇaṃ karmeti darśayati | śrāddhalakṣaṇakarmaṇas tu kāmyaphalaṃ "pitṝn śrāddhena tarpayet" iti śāstreṇa darśitam | yathā jāteṣṭiḥ pitrā kriyamāṇā putrasya pūtatvādikaṃ phalaṃ niṣpādayatīti "pūta eva tejasvy annāda indriyāvī paśumān bhavati" iti śāstrapramāṇyād āśritam, tathā putrādināpi kriyamāṇaṃ śrāddhaṃ tatpitrādīnāṃ tṛptirūpaṃ phalaṃ sādhayatīti "pitṝṃc chrāddhena tarpayet" iti śāstraprāmāṇyād āśrayaṇīyam | saṃkrāntyādikālalakṣaṇaguṇasādhyaṃ phalam atra śrāddhasādhyapitṛtṛptyāśritātiśayādhikyarūpam iti rātrisatranyāyenāvagantavyam,

	śrāddham eteṣu yad dattaṃ tad ānantyāya kalpate |

iti vākyaśeṣe śrāddhasādhyapitṛtṛpter ānantyaśravaṇāt | ānantyaśabdena vastuna ānantyāsaṃbhavāt tṛptyāśritātiśayādhikyam ucyate | evaṃ caitad uktaṃ bhavati: saṃkrāntyādau pitṛtṛptyatiśayakāle putrādinā śrāddhaṃ kāryam iti | saṃkrāntiśabdo gobalīvardanyāyenātra viṣuvadvayāyanadvayavyatiriktasūryasaṃkrāntiṣu vartate | kāḥ punar viṣuvādayaḥ saṃkrāntaya ity apekṣite jyotirvasiṣṭhaḥ |

	mṛgakarkaṭasaṃkrāntī dve tūdagdakṣiṇāyane |

	viṣuve ca tulāmeṣe tayor madhye tataḥ parāḥ ||

sūryasaṃkrāntaya iti śeṣaḥ | tayor ayanadvayaviṣuvadvayayor madhya ity arthaḥ | tatra dakṣiṇāyanatadūrdhvaviṣuvayor madhye dve sūryasaṃkrāntī viṣuvatadūrdhvottarāyaṇayor madhye dve, uttarāyaṇaviṣuvayor madhye dve, viṣuvatadūrdhvadakṣiṇāyanayor (?) dve, ity evam aṣṭau sūryasaṃkrāntayo veditavyāḥ | tāsu viṣuvāyanebhyaḥ uparibhāvās tu saṃkrāntyantareṇāvyavahitāḥ saṃkrāntayo viṣṇupadasaṃjñikāḥ jñeyāḥ, tābhya uparibhavās tu ṣaḍaśītimukhasaṃjñikā jñeyāḥ | tathā ca sa eva |

	vṛṣavṛścikakumbheṣu siṃhe caiva yadā raviḥ |

	etad viṣṇupadaṃ nāma viṣuvād adhikaṃ phalam ||

	kanyāyāṃ mithune mīne dhanuṣy api raver gatiḥ |

	ṣaḍaśītimukhāḥ proktā ṣaḍaśītiguṇāḥ phalaiḥ || iti |

prathamaśokasyaivaṃ yojanā: vṛṣavṛścikamumbhasiṃheṣu yadā raviḥ saṃkramati tadā tatsaṃkramaṇacatuṣṭayaṃ viṣṇupadasaṃjñakam iti | evaṃ nirūpitaviṣuvāyanaviṣṇupadaṣaḍaśītimukhanāmakāḥ kālāḥ yady api nimeṣād api svalpatarāḥ, tathāpi tatsaṃbaddhapūrvāparakālānugṛhītāḥ santo dīrghakālasādhyakarmānuṣṭhānāya vidhīyanta iti nāyogyatvaparāhatā iti mantavyam | tathā coktaṃ tenaiva |

	saṃkrāntisamayaḥ sūkṣmaḥ durjñeyaḥ piśitekṣaṇaiḥ |

	tadyogāc cāpy adhaś cordhvaṃ triṃśan nāḍyaḥ pavitritāḥ || iti |

evaṃ ca "saṃkrāntau śrāddhaṃ kuryāt" ityādivakyeṣu saṃkrāntiśabdābhidheyasūkṣmakālayogāt pavitritakāle śrāddhādikaṃ kartavyam ity arthād avagamyate | yat tu jyotirbṛhaspatinoktam |

	bhaviṣyaty ayane puṇyāḥ triṃśad eva tu dakṣiṇe |

	atīta uttare nāḍya iti prāhur manīṣiṇaḥ || iti |

tasyāyam arthaḥ: triṃśad eva tu nāḍikāḥ puṇyādhikyāpādikāḥ pavitratarā iti yāvat | evaṃ ca,

	tadyogāc cāpy adhaś cordhvaṃ triṃśan nāḍyaḥ pavitritāḥ |

ity anena saha na kaścid virodhaḥ | "atīta uttare nāḍyaḥ" ity atrānuṣaṅganyāyena triṃśad iti yady api saṃbandhaḥ pratibhāti, tathāpi vacanāntarāvirodhāya viṃśatir ity adhyāhṛtya tena saṃbandhaḥ kāryaḥ | anyathā,

	triṃśatkarkaṭake nāḍyo makare viṃśatiḥ smṛtāḥ |

	vartamāne tulāmeṣe nāḍyas tūbhayato daśa ||

iti vasiṣṭhavacanavirodhāt | karkaṭake anāgate triṃśat makare atīte viṃśatir nāḍyaḥ pavitratamā ity arthaḥ,

	atītānāgate puṇye dve tūdagdakṣiṇāyane |

iti tenaivābhidhānāt | "ubhayato daśa" ity atrāpi pavitratamā iti śeṣo draṣṭavyaḥ | yad apy anantaraṃ tenaivoktam,

	uparāge ca tatkālam atīte cottarāyaṇe |

iti, tatra caśabdād anāgate 'py uttarāyaṇe viṃśatir nāḍyaḥ puṇyā iti sūcayituṃ punar atīte cottarāyaṇe ity uktam, na punar uttarāyaṇe atīta eva viṃśatir nāḍyaḥ puṇyā ti vaktum iti na pūrvoktena virodhaḥ (?) | evaṃ ca dakṣiṇāyane saṃkrāntisamaye 'nāgate triṃśan nāḍyaḥ puṇyādhikyāpādikāḥ, uttarāyaṇe saṃkrāntisamaye triṃśaṇ nāḍyaḥ puṇyādhikyāpādikāḥ, uttarāyaṇe saṃkrāntisamaye ubhayato viṃśatir nāḍyaś ca puṇyādhkyāpādikāḥ, viṣuvadvaye tu saṃkrāntisamaye ubhayato daśa nāḍyaḥ puṇyādhikyāpādikā ity anusaṃdheyam | yat tu smṛtyarthasāre 'bhihitam: "uttarāyaṇe paścāc catvāriṃśad ghaṭikāḥ puṇyāḥ pūrvaṃ ca catvāriṃśad ghaṭikāḥ puṇyā āhuḥ" iti, tasya mūlaṃ cintyam, prasiddhasmṛtisamudāye tasya mūlabhūtavacanādarśanāt | yat tu marīcinoktam,

	nāḍyaḥ ṣoḍaśa pūrveṇa saṃkrānter apareṇa ca |

	rāhor darśanamātreṇa puṇyakālaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ||

iti, tatra saṃkrānter iti yady api saṃkrāntisāmānyasyāvadhitvaṃ pratibhāti, tathāpi viṣuvadvayāyanadvayavyatiriktaviṣayam iti sāmānyaviśeṣanyāyenāvagantavyam | ata eva vasiṣṭhenokam |

	puṇyākhyā viṣṇupadyāṃ ca prāk paścād api ṣoḍaśa |

iti | caśabdāt,

	ṣaḍaśītimukhāyāṃ ca prāk paścād api ṣoḍaśa |

iti gamyate | puṇyākhyāḥ puṇyatarākhyā ity arthaḥ | yat tu gargeṇoktam,

	bhaviṣyaty ayane viṣṇau vartamāne tathā viṣau |

	ṣaḍaśītimukhe caiva atīte cottarāyaṇe ||

iti, viṣau vartamāne madhye ity arthaḥ | tat phalabhūyastvābhiprāyeṇa na tu niyamārtham iti na pūrvoktavirodhaḥ | ataḥ smṛtyantaram |

	madhye viṣuvati dānaṃ viṣṇupade dakṣiṇāyane cādau |

	ṣaḍaśītimukhe 'tīte udagayane cāpi bhūri phalam ||

evaṃ puṇyatvena puṇyatamatvena coktanāḍīṣv api saṃkrāntitadabhidheyasūkṣmasamayasaṃnidhitāratamyānusāreṇa prathamadvitīyatṛtīyādināḍīnāṃ phalātiśayahetutve tāratamyam avaseyam | ata eva vasiṣṭhena,

	yāyāt saṃnihitā nāḍyaḥ tās tāḥ puṇyatamāḥ smṛtaḥ |

ity uktam | yat punas tenaivoktam,

	ahni saṃkramaṇe puṇyam ahaḥ kṛtsnaṃ prakīrtitam |

iti, tad atyantaviprakṛṣṭanāḍīnāṃ puṇyatvaṃ nāstīti vyatirekamātraparam iti mantavyam | 

	tadyogāc cāpy adhaś cordhvaṃ triṃśan nāḍyaḥ pavitritāḥ |

ity asya kvacid viṣaye 'pavādam āha sa eva |

	rātrau saṃkramaṇe puṇyaṃ dinārdhaṃ snānadānayoḥ | iti |

vyavahitam api dinārdham eva puṇyaṃ na tu saṃnihitā rātrigatā nāḍyaḥ puṇyā ity arthaḥ | etac cāyanavyatiriktaviṣayam | yad āha sa eva,

	ardharātrād adhas tasmin madhyāhnasyopari kriyā |

	ūrdhvaṃ saṃkramaṇe cordhvam udayāt praharadvayam ||

	pūrṇe ced ardharātre tu yadā saṃkramaṇaṃ raveḥ |

	prāhur dinadvayaṃ puṇyaṃ muktvā makarakarkaṭau ||

iti, etat tu viṣṇupadaṣaḍaśītimukhavyatiriktaviṣuvamātraviṣayam,

	viṣṇupadyāṃ dhanur mīnanṛyukkanyāsu vai sadā |

	pūrvottaragate rātrau bhānoḥ saṃkramaṇaṃ bhavet ||

	pūrvāhṇe pañca nāḍyaś ca puṇyāḥ proktā manīṣibhiḥ |

	aparāhṇe tu pañcaiva śraute smārte ca karmaṇi ||

iti viṣṇupadaṣaḍaśītimukheṣu tenaivānyathābhidhānāt | nṛyuk mithunarāśiḥ | pūrvottaragate pūrvottarabhāgasthe kāle | ardharātre saṃkramaṇe dinadvaye pañca puṇyā ity ūhyam, pratyāsattiviseṣābhāvalakṣaṇanyāyasāmyāt | ayanadvaye tu divā rātrau vā na saṃnihitanāḍīnāṃ sati saṃbhave parityāgaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span>,

	rātrau snānaṃ na kurvīta dānaṃ caiva viśeṣataḥ |

ityādivacanena rātrau snānadānādiniṣedhād rātrāv ayane 'pi saṃnihitānāṃ nāḍīnāṃ parityāgaḥ kāryaḥ, vaktavyo vā viśeṣaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span>, 

	rāhudarśanasaṃkrāntivivāhātyayavṛddhiṣu |

	snānadānādikaṃ kuryān niśi kāmyavrateṣu ca ||

itivacanena saṃkrāntyādāv api pratiprasavas tāvad asti | na cāyaṃ pratiprasavaḥ saṃkrāntiṣu yujyate, ayanadvayavyatiriktasaṃkrāntau rātrau gatāyāṃ dina eva saṃkrāntikṛtyābhidhāyakavacanavirodhāpatteḥ | tenāyanadvayaviṣaya evāyaṃ pratiprasava iti kalpanīyam | tasmād ayanadvaye rātrāv api na saṃnihitanāḍīnāṃ parityāgaḥ ||

	prakrtam ucyate | saṃkrāntyādayaḥ kāmyāḥ śrāddhakālāḥ sati saṃbhave kutapādiśrāddhakālena saha samuccīyante, sati saṃbhave sarveṣāṃ śrāddhāṅgānām upasaṃhārasyāvaśyakatvāt | asaṃbhave tu candrasūryagrahaṇavad asamuccaye 'pi na phalasiddhivirodhaḥ, asaṃbhavādinā aṅgānanuṣṭhānasya vidhyanumatatvāt | vyatīpātayogas tu kutapādikālayogī grāhyaḥ, saṃbhavāt | janmanakṣatraṃ kutapādikālayogi sati saṃbhave grāhyam | nakṣatraṃ tu śrāddhārthe yadā dinadvayavyāpi śuklapakṣa audayikam "yat pūrvāhṇavyāpi tad grāhyam" iti devasvāminoktatvāt | candrasūryagrahe tu grahaṇakāla eva śrāddhaṃ kartavyam,

	tridaśāḥ sparśasamaye tṛpyanti pitaras tathā |

	manuṣyā madhyakāle tu mokṣakāle tu rākṣasāḥ ||

devakārye pitṛkārye ca grahaṇakālavidhānāt | mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe 'pi kāmyaśrāddhakālā darśitāḥ |

	kṛttikāsu pitṝn arcan svargam āpnoti mānavaḥ |

	apatyakāmo rohiṇyāṃ saumye caujavitāṃ labhet ||

	ārdrāyāṃ śauryam āpnoti kṣetrādi tu punarvasau |

	puṣṭiṃ puṣye pitṝn arcan āśloṣāsu varān sutān ||

	madhāsu svajanaśraiṣṭhyaṃ saubhāgyaṃ phalgunīṣu ca |

	pradānaśīlo bhavati sāpatyaś cottarāsu ca ||

	prāpnoti śreṣṭhatāṃ satsu haste śrāddhaprdo naraḥ |

	rūpavanti ca citrāsu tathāpatyāny avāpnuyāt ||

	vāṇijyalābhadā svātī viśākhā putrakāmadā |

	kurvatāṃ cānurādhāś ca dadyuś cakrapravartanam ||

	jyeṣṭhā svargādhipatyaṃ ca mūle cārogyam uttamam |

	āṣāḍāsu (?) śriyaḥ prāptim uttarāsu viśokatām ||

	śravaṇe ca śubhān lokān dhaniṣṭhāsu dhanaṃ mahat |

	vedavit syād abhijiti bhiṣaksiddhiṃ tu vāruṇe ||

	ajavikaṃ proṣṭhapade vindate gās taduttare |

	revatīṣu tathā kupyam aśvanīṣu turaṅgamān ||

	śrāddhaṃ kurvan tathāpnoti bharaṇīṣv āyur uttamam |

	tasmāt kāmyāni kurvīta ṛkṣeṣv eteṣu tattvavit || iti |

saumyaṃ somadevatākaṃ mṛgaśīrṣam iti yāvat | ojaḥ ātmaśaktyatiśayaḥ | śauryaṃ nirbhayatvena vartanam | kṣetrādi ca kṣetraphalaṃ cety arthaḥ | puṣṭiḥ śrīrapuṣṭiḥ | varān sutān guṇopetān sutān | saubhagyaṃ janapriyatām | sāpatyaś ca apatyavān bhavatīty arthaḥ | satsu satpuruṣeṣu | rūpavanti surūpāṇi | cakrapravartanaṃ pratihatirāhityena ājñāyāḥ pravartanam | abhijit abhijitsaṃjñakaṃ nakṣatram | tat tu vede nirūpitam: "abhijin nāma nakṣatram upariṣṭād āṣāḍhānām adhastāc chroṇāyai" iti | bhiṣaksiddhiḥ auṣadhaphalāvāptiḥ | vāruṇaṃ śatabhiṣaṅnakṣatram | kupyaṃ trapusīsādidravyam | ṛkṣeṣv eteṣu pūrvokteṣu nakṣatreṣu | tattvavit samyakchrāddhavidhānavit | viṣṇudharmottare 'pi |

	arogyam atha saubhāgyaṃ samare vijayaṃ tathā |

	sarvakāmāṃs tathā vidyāṃ dhanaṃ jīvitam eva ca ||

	ādityādidineṣv evaṃ śrāddhaṃ kurvan sadā naraḥ |

	krameṇaitān samāpnoti nātra kāryā vicāraṇā || iti |

etān ārogyādīn ādityādidinakrameṇa (?) tat tad dinaśrāddhaṃ kurvan naraḥ prāpnotīty arthaḥ | etad uktaṃ bhavati: ādityavāre śrāddham ārogyakāmaḥ kuryāt, somavāre saubhāgyakāmaḥ, bhaumavāre saṃgrāmavijayakāmaḥ, budhavāre sarvakāmaḥ, bṛhaspativāre vidyākāmaḥ, śukravāre dhanakāmaḥ, śanivāre jīvitakāma iti | yājñavalkyenāpi kāmyaśrāddhakālā darśitāḥ |

	kanyāṃ kanyāvedinaś ca paśūṃś caiva sutān api |

	dyūtaṃ kṛṣiṃ ca vāṇijyaṃ dviśaphaikaśaphāṃs tathā ||

	brahmavarcasvinaḥ putrān svarṇaraupye sakupyake |

	jñātiśraiṣṭhyaṃ sarvakāmān āpnoti śrāddhadaḥ sadā ||

	pratipatprabhṛtiṣv ekāṃ varjayitvā caturdaśīm || iti |

kanyā rūpalakṣaṇaśīlavatī, prāyeṇa tādṛśyā evātikāmyatvāt | kanyāvedino jāmātaraḥ śrutavanto rogarahitāḥ | paśūn śīlalakṣaṇapaṃpannān, evaṃbhūtānām eva kāmyatvāt | kāmyaṃ tu kṛṣṇapakṣe pratipadi śrāddhaṃ kanyākāmaḥ kuryāt, dvitīyāyāṃ varakāmaḥ, tṛtīyāyāṃ paśukāmaḥ, caturthyāṃ putrakāmaḥ, pañcamyāṃ tu vijayakāmaḥ, ṣaṣṭhyāṃ kṛṣiphalakāmaḥ, saptamyāṃ vāṇijyalābhakāmaḥ, aṣṭamyāṃ dviśaphagavādipaśukāmaḥ, navamyām ekaśaphāśvādipaśukāmaḥ, daśamyāṃ vṛttādhyayanabahulaputrakāmaḥ, ekādaśyāṃ svarṇarūpyakāmaḥ, dvādaśyāṃ trapusīsādidravyakāmaḥ, trayodaśyāṃ jñātiśraiṣṭhyakāmaḥ, amāvāsyāyāṃ yogasiddhyadhikaraṇoktanyāyānusāreṇa krameṇa sarvakāma iti | atra,

	kṛṣṇapakṣe 'parāhṇe tu rauhiṇaṃ tu na laṅghayet |\

iti smṛtyantarokto viśeṣo draṣṭavyaḥ | rauhiṇaḥ ahno navamo muhūrtaḥ | evaṃ ca kutapādighaṭikātrayasaṃyuktāyāṃ pratipadāditithau kāmyaśrāddhaṃ kāryam, na tu kutapādyasaṃyuktāyām iti mantavyam | pratipadāditithidvaidhe tu pūrvasyām uttarasyāṃ vā kutapādighaṭikātrayayuktāyāṃ eva śrāddhaṃ kāryam | tathā coktaṃ devasvāminā: "yasmin kāle yad vihitaṃ tat karma upakramopasaṃhārayuktaṃ tasmin kāle tasyāṃ tithau yasmin ahani saṃbhāvayituṃ śakyate tad uttaraṃ pūrvaṃ vā grāhyam" iti | ubhayadine 'pi yadi saṃbhavayituṃ śakyate tadā tu svataḥ pūrvadinaṃ grāhyam, kathaṃcit tatrānuṣṭhānābhāve uttaradinaṃ grāhyam | upakramopasaṃhārayor ubhayor ubhayatrāsaṃbhavaviṣaye tu yad devasvāminoktam: "yasmin samāptiḥ tasyāṃ tithau tasmin kāle saṃbhavati tasminn ahany upakramya samāpanīyam" iti | samāptiḥ upasaṃhāraḥ | tasminn ahany asvakāle 'py upakramya svakāle samāpanīyam ity arthaḥ | tad etad ayuktam, kālasyāpy adhikāriviseṣaṇatvena svakāle 'nāgate karmaṇy adhikārābhāvād asvakāle karmopakramasyānyāyyatvāt | tasmād asmin viṣaye svakāle upakramyāsvakāle samāpanīyam | svakālopakrānte karmaṇi kālāntare 'pi samāpanasya vidhinākṣiptatvāt | yadā tu svakāle 'py upakramo na saṃbhavati tadā smṛtyantroktaṃ draṣṭavyam |	pitryaṃ śrāddhaṃ kṛṣṇapakṣe dine 'stamayayogini |

	śukle tūdayasaṃyukte dānaṃ yajñādikaṃ tathā || iti |

kṛṇapakṣe "pratipaddhanalābhāya" ityādinā yad vihitaṃ śrāddhaṃ tad astamayayogipratipadāditithyanvite dine kartavyam | śuklapakṣe tithiviśeṣollekhena vihitaṃ dānaṃ devakāryādikam udayayogitithiviseṣānvitadine kartavyam ity arthaḥ | astamayayogitve udayayogitve ca viśeṣas tatraiva |

	dinānte pañca nāḍyas tu puṇyāḥ proktā manīṣibhiḥ |

	udaye ca tathā pitrye daive caiva ca kamaṇi || iti |

pitrye karmaṇi dinānte pañca nāḍyaḥ puṇyāḥ proktāḥ, daive karmaṇy udaye pañca nāḍyaḥ puṇyāḥ proktā ity anvayaḥ | khaṇḍatithis tu kāmyakarmaṇi prathamopakrame parityajyā, saṃpūrṇatithāv evopakramasaṃbhavāt | upakrāntasya kāmyakarmaṇaḥ śrāddhādeḥ kāmyasiddhiparyantam ekasaṃvatsaraparyantaṃ vā svakāle punaḥ punar anuṣṭhāne kartavye khaṇḍatithāv apy uktadine 'vaśyaṃ karmānuṣṭhānaṃ kartavyam | tathā ca devasvāminā nakṣatraśrāddham udāhṛtyoktam: "nakṣatreṣu kāmyaśrāddheṣu tatkāmapradanakṣatraprāptau yāvat tatkāmaprāpte tasmin ṛkṣe śrāddhaṃ kuryād abdam ekaṃ yāvat" iti | atra hārītaḥ |

	kāmyaśrāddhāni kāmyārthī samyag yatnena sādhayet |

	śarīrārambhahetutvāt mumukṣus tāni nācaret ||

	kāmaprāptāni vihitaśrāddhāny uktāni yāni tu |

	tāni vidhyantaroktatvāt svargamokṣārtham ācaret ||

	yathā kathaṃcin nityāni kuryād indukṣayādiṣu |

	pātradravyādisaṃpatsu satsu kāmyaphalaṃ labhet ||

vidhyantaroktatvād iti, "dvividha eva saṃskāro bhavati brāhmo daivaś ca | garbhādhānādiḥ smārto brāhmaḥ, pākayajñahaviryajñasaumyāś ceti daivaḥ | brāhmasaṃskārasaṃskrta ṛṣīṇāṃ samatāṃ samānalokatāṃ sāyujyaṃ gacchati | daivenottareṇa saṃskṛtaḥ devānāṃ samānalokatāṃ sāyujyaṃ gacchati" ity evamādirūpeṇa vidhyantareṇa, 

	śrāddhakṛt satyavādī ca gṛhastho 'pi vimucyate |

ity evamādirūpeṇa vidhyantareṇa coktatvād iti ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ kāmyaśrāddhakālāḥ **

**atha gauṇaśrāddhakālāḥ**

tatra ṛśyaśṛṅgaḥ |

	daive pitṝṇāṃ śrāddhe tu āśaucaṃ jāyate yadi |

	āśaucādau vyatikrānte tebhyaḥ śrāddhaṃ pradīyate ||

mukhyakāle pākopakramāt prāk yadā śrāddhādhikāriṇa āśaucaṃ jāyate tadā mukhyakāle pratyāsanne āśaucena dūṣite āśaucāpagamānantarakāla eva paitṛkaṃ karma kāryam ity arthaḥ | yatu tu smṛtyantaram,

	tad ahaś cet praduṣyeta kenacit sūtakādinā |

	sūtakānantaraṃ kuryāt punas tad ahar eva vā ||

iti, tat śrāddhāhe sūtakena praduṣṭe sūtakānantaraṃ kuryād iti pakṣas tāvat ṛśyaśṛṅgavacanāviruddha eva | "punas tad ahar eva vā" iti pakṣas tv ādiśabdoktanimittāntareṇa vihitamukhyakālābhāvaviṣaya iti pūrvavacanāvirodhāya kalpanīyam | etac ca pakṣāntaraṃ kṣayāhe pratimāsaṃ kriyamāṇaśrāddhaviṣayam | tatra māsaspṛṣṭakālābhāve 'pi pakṣatithimātrapṛṣṭasyāpi grāhyatvāt | ata eva smṛtyantaram |

	ekoddiṣṭe tu saṃprāpte yadi vighnaḥ prajāyate |

	anyasmin tattithau tasmin śrāddhaṃ kuryāt prayatnataḥ ||

anyasmin anantare māsi | tattithau mṛtatithau | yasmin śukle kṛṣṇe vā mṛtaḥ tasmin pakṣe śrāddhaṃ vighnavaśād atikrāntaṃ kuryād ity arthaḥ | yadi vighna ity atrāpi ṛśyaśṛṅgavacanāvirodhāyāśaucavyatiriktanimitteneti śeṣo draṣṭavyaḥ | āśaucanimittena tu vighnite māsikaviṣaye 'pi sūtakānantaram eva śrāddhānuṣṭhānaṃ ṛśyaśṛṅgoktan anusaṃdheyam | ata eva devasvāmināpy uktam: "etad ṛśyaśṛṅgavacanaṃ sūtakāśaucaviṣayam | nimittāntaratas tadahar vighāte,

	ekoddiṣṭe tu saṃprāpte yadi vighnaḥ prajāyate |

ityādismṛtyantaravacanam" iti | yat punaḥ smṛtyantaram,

	śrāddhavighne samutpanne antarā mṛtasūtake |

	amāvāsyāṃ prakurvīta śuddhāv eke manīṣiṇaḥ ||

iti antarā mṛtasūtake śrāddaprayogamadhye pākopakramāt pūrvaṃ sūtake mṛtake vā jāte amāvāsyāyāṃ śuddhau śudhyantaram | etat sāṃvatsarikaśrāddaviṣayam | amāvāsyāgrahaṇaṃ kṛṣṇaikādaśyāś copalakṣaṇārtham | amāvāsyāgrahaṇaṃ kṛṣṇaikādaśyāś copalakṣaṇārtham | at eva marīciḥ |

	śrāddhavighne samutpanne avijñāte mṛte 'hani |

	ekādaśyāṃ tu kartavyaṃ kṛṣṇapakṣe viśeṣataḥ || iti |

kṛṣṇapakṣe yā ekādaśī tasyāṃ viśeṣataḥ kartavyam ity anvayaḥ | pitṛkārye svataḥ kṛṣṇapakṣasyaiva grāhyatvāt kṛṣṇaikādaśīto 'py (?) amāvāsyāyāḥ pitṛkārye śraiṣṭhyaṃ daṇḍāpūpikānyāyasiddham iti boddhavyam | yat tu ṣaṭtriṃśatmatam,

	māsike 'bde tu saṃprāpte tv antarā mṛtasūtake |

	vadanti śuddhau tat kāryaṃ darśe vāpi vicakṣaṇāḥ ||

iti, tad etat "tāny eva tu punaḥ kuryāt" iti vihitānumāsikaśrāddhaviṣayam | ekoddiṣṭamāsike pūrvam evānukalpakālasyoktatvāt | tatra śuddhyanantarakālo mukhyakālatvāc śreṣṭhaḥ | darśakālas tato jaghanyaḥ, mukhyakālapratyāsattyabhāvād iti mantavyam | tathā ca ṛśyaśṛṅgaḥ |

	śucibhūtena dātavyaṃ yā tithiḥ pratipadyate |

	sā tithis tasya kartavyā na tv anyā vai kadācana || iti |

ayam arthaḥ: śucibhūtena tāvad dātavyam | tena mukhyakāle śuddhyasaṃbhave śuddyanantaraṃ vā tithiḥ pratipadyate labhyate sā tithis tasya kartavyā karmopakramāt prāk sādhyatayā kathaṃcid anuṣṭheyā na tv anyā, mukhyā tithir āśaucadūṣitā kadācana nānuṣṭheyeti | āśaucadūṣitā mukhyā tithir nānuṣṭheyety āha sa eva |

	tithicchedo na kartavyo vināśaucaṃ yadṛcchayā |

	piṇḍaṃ śrāddhaṃ ca dātavyaṃ vicchittiṃ naiva kārayet ||

yadṛcchayā svecchayā | śrāddhaṃ brāhmaṇatarpaṇam | caśabdenāgnaukaraṇam api kartavyam iti samuccinoti | śrāddhaśabdenātra brāhmaṇatarpaṇamātram upacārād ucyate, na mukhārthatayā, agnaukaraṇabrāhmaṇatarpaṇapiṇḍadānātmakakarmatrayasamudāyasyaiva mukhyārthatvāt | tathā ca devasvāminā śrāddhaśabdārthaṃ evam eva samyaṅ nirūpitaḥ |

	piṇḍābhāve 'pi nityādau śrāddhaśabdaprayogataḥ |

	śrāddhaśabdo na piṇḍeṣu nāpi ca dvijabhojane ||

	atithyādau bhujāsatyāṃ śrāddhaśabdāprayogataḥ |

	pitṝn uddiśya vittādityāgamātraṃ na caiva hi ||

	tarpaṇāder api prāptes tyāgas tatrāpi dṛśyate |

	vidvanmatāny upādāya mama tv etad dhṛdi sthitam ||

	homaś ca piṇḍadānaṃ ca tathā brāhmaṇatarpaṇam |

	śrāddhaśabdābhidheyaṃ syād ekasminn aupacārikaḥ || iti |

"vicchittiṃ naiva kārayet" iti ṛśyaśṛṅgavacanasyāyam arthaḥ: kṛtsnasya śrāddhaśabdārthasya kartum aśakyatve 'pi tadekadeśamātraṃ vā yathāsāmarthyaṃ kuryāt | sarvathā karmavicchittiṃ naiva kuryād iti | ata eva nigamaḥ: "āhitāgneḥ pitrarcanaṃ piṇḍair eva brāhmaṇān api vā bhojayet" iti | atra yathāsāmarthyaṃ vyavasthā | tataś ca dvitīyapakṣāsāmarthye prathamoktaḥ pakṣaḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ gauṇaśrāddhakālāḥ**

**atha śrāddhadeśāḥ**

tatra viṣṇudharmottare |

	dakṣiṇāpravaṇe deśe tīrthādau vā gṛhe 'pi vā |

	bhūsaṃskārādisaṃyukte śrāddhaṃ kuryāt prayatnataḥ ||

tīrthaṃ ṛṣisevitaṃ jalam, tatsamīpe | ādiśabdena ṛṣisevitāśramādi gṛhyate | bhūsaṃskārādisaṃyukte, bhūsaṃskāro gomayādilepanādiḥ | ādiśabdena keśādyaśucidravyāpasāraṇaṃ gṛhyate | tathā caoktaṃ tatraiva |

	gomayenopalipteṣu vivikteṣu gṛheṣu ca |

	kuryāc chrāddham athaiteṣu nityam eva yathāvidhi || iti |

eteṣu pūrvokteṣu gṛheṣu gṛhādiṣu gomayenopalipteṣu keśādidravyaviyukteṣu śrāddhaṃ nityaṃ kuryād ity arthaḥ | manur api |

	śuciṃ deśaṃ viviktaṃ tu gomayenopalepayet |

	dakṣiṇāpravaṇaṃ caiva prayatnenopapādayet || iti |

ayam arthaḥ: svataḥśuciṃ tīrthādipradeśaṃ gṛhapradeśaṃ vā parakṛtāśuciparihārārthaṃ viviktaṃ keśādyasaṃyuktaṃ kṛtvā bhūsaṃskārātiśayārthaṃ gomayenopalepayet | svato dakṣiṇāpravaṇatvābhāve 'pi pitṛyajanatvasiddhaye dakṣiṇāpravaṇatvaṃ coddhananādinā (?) prayatnenopapādayet kuryād iti | atra yamaḥ |

	parakīyapradeśeṣu pitṝṇāṃ nirvapet tu yaḥ |

	tadbhūmisvāmipitṛbhiḥ śrāddhakarma vihanyate ||

tena tatra śrāddhaṃ na kuryād ity abhiprāyaḥ | parakīyapradeśāḥ paraparigṛhītagṛhagoṣṭhādipradeśāḥ, na punas tīrthādipradeśāḥ | tathā ca purāṇam |

	aṭavīparvatāḥ puṇyā nadītīrāṇi yāni ca |

	sarvāṇy asvāmikāny āhuḥ na hi teṣu parigrahaḥ ||

	vanāni girayo nadyaḥ tīrthāny āyatanāni ca |

	devakātāś ca gartāś ca na svāmī teṣu vidyate || iti |

devakhātāś ca gartāś ca devakhātagartāś cety arthaḥ | kṛtrimagartasyāsvāmikatvaniyamāsaṃbhavāt | yasmād eteṣu paraparigrahābhāvaḥ, tasmād eteṣu svagṛheṣv iva śrāddhaṃ deyam ity uktam | viṣṇudharmottare |

	tasmāc chrāddhāni deyāni puṇyeṣv āyataneṣu ca |

	nadītīreṣu tīrtheṣu svabhūmau ca prayatnataḥ || iti |

svabhūmyām api kṛttrimapradeśād anyatra deyāni, tatra pratiṣedhāt | tathā ca śaṅkhaḥ |

	gogajāśvādipṛṣṭeṣu kṛtrimāyāṃ tathā bhuvi |

	na kuryāc chrāddham eteṣu pārakyāśucibhūmiṣu ||

kṛttrimāyāṃ bhuvi vedikāyām ity arthaḥ | anena akṛttrimāyām eva bhuvi pitṛtṛptir bhavatīty arthād uktam | uktaṃ ca sākṣād devalena |

	sthalīṣu giripṛṣṭeṣu tīrtheṣv āyataneṣu ca |

	goṣṭheṣu ca vivikteṣu tuṣyanti pitaras tathā ||

sthalīṣu akṛttrimonnatadeśeṣv ity arthaḥ | "jānapadakuṇḍagolasthala" ityādinā pāṇinīyasūtreṇa (Pāṇ 6.2.129) sthalaśabdād akṛttrimārthe ṅīppratyayavidhānāt | śaṅkho 'pi kṛttrimasthale niṣedham āha: "neṣṭakacite pitṝṃs tarpayet" iti | yamas tu varjyapradeśam āha |

	rūkṣaṃ krimihataṃ klinnaṃ saṃkīrṇāniṣṭagandhikam |

	deśaṃ tv aniṣṭaśabdaṃ ca varjayec chrāddhakarmaṇi ||

rūkṣam asnigdham | klinnaṃ sakardamam | saṃkīrṇaṃ padārthāntarair ākīrṇam | aniṣṭagandhikaṃ pūtigandhikam | aniṣṭaśabdam aśrāvyaśabdam | madālasāvākyam api |

	varjyā jantumatī rūkṣā kṣitiḥ pluṣṭā tathāgninā |

	aniṣṭaduṣṭaśabdogrā durgandhā śrāddhakarmaṇi ||

agninā pluṣṭā dagdhā | ugrā vyāghrādisaṃnikṛṣṭā ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ śrāddhadeśāḥ**

**atha kāmyaśrāddhadeśāḥ**

tatra vyāsaḥ |

	puṣkare tv akṣayaṃ śrāddhaṃ japahomatapāṃsi ca |

	mahodadhau prayāge ca kāśyāṃ ca kurujāṅgale || iti |

puṣkare puṣkarākhyatīrthe | kāśī vārāṇasī | kurujāṅgalaśabdau janapadaviśeṣavacanau | śaṅkho 'pi |

	vārāṇasyāṃ kurukṣetre bhṛgutuṅge himālaye |

	narmadābāhudātīre sarvam ānantyam aśnute ||

	gaṅgādvāre prayāge vā naimiśe puṣkare tathā |

	saṃnihatyāṃ gayāyāṃ ca dattam akṣayyatāṃ vrajet ||

naimiśe sarasvatītiravartini naimiśāraṇye | saṃnihatiḥ kurukṣetravartī tīrthaviśeṣaḥ | gayā prasiddhā | gayākṣetrasya tu pramāṇaṃ purāṇe darśitam |

	mahānadī devanadyoḥ sarvatīrthādyanantaram |

	udakkanakanandāyā gayāmadhyaṃ prakīrtitam ||

	pañcakrośaṃ gayākṣetraṃ krośamātraṃ gayāśiraḥ ||

pañcakrośapramāṇake gayākṣetre sārabhūtaṃ krośamātraṃ gayāśira iti prasiddham ity arthaḥ | tac ca tatraiva nirūpitam |

	mahānadyāḥ paścimena yāvad gṛdhreśvaro giriḥ |

	uttare brahmayupasya yāvad dakṣiṇamānasam ||

	etad gayāśiro nāma triṣu lokeṣu viśrutam || iti |

gayāśritovad anyāny api gayāyāṃ viśrutāni mahānadyādīni śrāddhasthalāni tatraiva darśitāni |

	mahānadī brahmasado 'kṣayo vaṭaḥ prabhāsam udyantam atho gayāśiraḥ |

	sarasvatī dhenukadharmapṛṣṭham ete kurukṣetrasamā gayāyām || iti |

udyantākyaḥ parvataviśeṣaḥ | sarasvatī prācī sarasvatīti viśrutā | vyāso 'pi |

	brahmāraṇyaṃ dharmapṛṣṭhaṃ dhenukāraṇyam eva ca |

	triṣv eteṣu pitṝn arcan vaṃśān sapta samuddharet ||

brahmakaivarte 'pi |

	gayāyāṃ muṇḍapṛṣṭhaṃ tu aravindaṃ ca parvatam |

	tṛtīyaṃ krauñcapādaṃ tu dṛṣṭvā pāpaiḥ pramucyate ||

gayāyās tacchiraso muṇḍapṛṣṭhasya ca māhātmyaṃ tatraiva darśitam |

	svargapātālamartyeṣu nāsti tīrthaṃ gayāsamam |

	pitaro yānti devatvaṃ prāptapiṇḍā gayāśire ||

	gayāśīrṣe yadā piṇḍaṃ nāmnā yeṣāṃ prakurvate |

	narakasthā divaṃ yānti svargasthā mokṣagāminaḥ ||

	muṇḍapṛṣṭhe padaṃ nyastaṃ mahādevena dhīmatā |

	bahūny abdasahasrāṇi tapas taptvā sudāruṇam ||

	alpenāpy atra kālena naro dharmaparāyaṇaḥ |

	pāpaṃ vimocayaty āśu jīrṇāṃ tvacam ivoragaḥ || iti |

akṣayavaṭasya māhātmyaṃ tatraiva darśitam |

	tatrākṣayavaṭo nāma triṣu lokeṣu viśrutaḥ |

	pitṝṇāṃ tatra vai dattam akṣayaṃ bhavati prabho ||

	vaṭavṛkṣaṃ samāsādya śākenāpy udakena vā |

	ekasmin bhojine vipre koṭir bhavati bhojitā ||

dhenukāraṇyamāhātmyaṃ purāṇāntare darśitam |

	tato gaccheta rājendra dhenukāṃ likaviśrutām |

	tatra cihnaṃ pradṛśyeta adyāpi hi na saṃśayaḥ ||

	kapilāyāḥ savatsāyā dṛśyante kurusattama |

	vicarantyāḥ padāni syuḥ dṛśyante pañca kḷptavat ||

	padāni tāni saṃspṛśya kapilāyā narādhipa |

	teṣu dṛṣṭeṣu yat puṃsaḥ pāpaṃ tat sampraṇasyati ||

gṛdhreśvaramāhātmyaṃ tatraiva darśitam |

	tato gṛdhranagaṃ gacchet sthānaṃ devasya dhīmataḥ |

	snātvā tu bhasmanā tatra adhigacchen maheśvaram ||
