	brāhmaṇena bhavec cīrṇaṃ vrataṃ dvādaśavārṣikam |

	itareṣāṃ tu varṇānāṃ sarvapāpakṣayo bhavet || iti |

gṛdhreśvaragirimāhātmyaṃ tatraiva darśitam |

	tato gacchet samaṃ tv annaparvataṃ girivāritam |

	sāvitryās tasya dṛśyante padāni bharatarṣabha ||

	tatra saṃdhyām upāsīta brāhmaṇaḥ saṃśitavrataḥ |

	tenopāsitā bhavati saṃdhyā dvādaśavārṣikī ||

	dharmapṛṣṭhasya māhātmyaṃ tac ca tatraiva darśitam |

	tato gaccheta rājendra dharmapṛṣṭhaṃ samāhitaḥ ||

	yatra dharmo mahārāja nityam āste yudhāṃvara |

	tatrādhigamya rājendra hayamedhaphalaṃ bhavet ||

tīrthāntarāṇāṃ ca gayāyāṃ prasiddhānāṃ māhātmyaṃ darśitam |

	tato viśālām āsādya nadīṃ trailokyaviśrutām |

	agniṣṭomam avāpnoti svargalokaṃ ca gacchati ||

	atha māheśvaraṃ dhāma samāsādya naraḥ śuciḥ |

	hayamedham avāpnoti kulaṃ caiva samuddharet ||

	divaukasāṃ puṣkariṇīṃ samāsādya naraḥ śuciḥ |

	na durgatim avāpnoti viṣṇulokaṃ ca gacchati ||

	tatra koṭis tu tīrthānāṃ viśrutā bharatarṣabha |

	kūrmarūpeṇa rājan dānavena durātmanā ||

	hriyamāṇoddhṛtā rājan viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā |

	tatrābhiṣekaṃ kurvīta tīrthakoṭyā yudhāṃvara ||

	pauṇḍarīkam avāpnoti viṣṇulokaṃ ca gacchati |

	gopracārasamīpasthā āmrā brahmaprakalpitāḥ ||

	taiḥ saktaiḥ puruṣasyeha pitaro mokṣam āpnuyuḥ |

	eko muniḥ kumbhakarāgrahastaḥ āmreṣu nityaṃ salilaṃ dadāti |

	āmrāś ca siktāḥ pitaraś ca tṛptāḥ ekā kriyā dvyarthakarī babhūva ||

	yā sā vaitaraṇī nāma triṣu lokeṣu visrutā |

	sāvatīrṇā gayāśīrṣe pitṝṇāṃ tāraṇāya vai ||

	tatra snātvā mahārāja godānaṃ yaḥ prayacchati |

	ekaviṃśatiṃ vaṃśyāṃs tān tārayen nātra saṃśayaḥ ||

	tatra dhenupradānena pitaro mokṣam āpnuyuḥ || iti |

pauṇḍarīkaṃ pauṇḍarīkākhyayajñaphalam | brahmakaivarte 'pi |

	brahmahā ca kṛtaghnaś ca goghātī pañcapātakī |

	sarve niṣkṛtim āyānti gayāyāṃ piṇḍapātanāt ||

	brahmaghnaś ca surāpaś ca bālavṛddhagurudruhaḥ |

	nāśam āyāti vai pāpaṃ gayāyām anuyāti yaḥ ||

	ātmajatvam avāptas tu gayākūle yathā tathā |

	yan nāmnā pātayet piṇḍaṃ taṃ nayed brahma śāśvatam || 

iti |

	makare vartamāne tu grahaṇe candrasūryayoḥ |

	durlabhaṃ triṣu lokeṣu gayāyāṃ piṇḍapātanam ||

brahmaṇā saha śāśvataṃ brahmaprāptyāpādakaṃ brahmalokaṃ nayed ity arthaḥ | vyāso 'pi |

	gayāṃ gatvā tu yaḥ kaścit pitṝn saṃtarpayen naraḥ |

	daśa pūrvāparān vaṃśyān ātmānaṃ ca punāti saḥ ||

purāṇāntare |

	snānaṃ dehaparityāgo gaṅgāyāṃ tu viśiṣyate |

	śrāddhaṃ piṇḍapradānaṃ ca gayāyāṃ tu viśiṣyate ||

	brahmajñānaṃ gayāśrāddhaṃ gogṛhe maraṇaṃ tathā |

	vāsaḥ puṃsāṃ kurukṣetre muktir uktā caturvidhā ||

	gayāśīrṣe vasen nityaṃ snānaṃ phalgau samācaret |

	gayāśīrṣe sadā piṇṣam etat svarge 'pi durlabham ||

	phalgutīrthe naraḥ snātvā devaṃ dṛṣṭvā gadādharam |

	gayāśiraḥ parikramya mucyate brahmahatyayā ||

	gayāyāṃ pitṛrūpeṇa svayam eva janārdanaḥ |

	taṃ dṛṣṭvā puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ svayam eva janārdanaḥ ||

	taṃ dṛṣṭvā puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ mucyate ca ṛṇatrayāt |

	yenākrāntaṃ sakṛd api dharmapṛṣṭhaṃ gayāśiraḥ ||

	naśyati brahmahatyādi pātakaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ |

	trir dadat pṛthivīṃ kṛtsnāṃ na mucyet paitṛkād ṛṇāt ||

	yāvac chrāddhaṃ na vai putraḥ kuryād gatvā gayāśiraḥ |

	gayāyāṃ dharmapṛṣṭhe ca sadasi brahmaṇas tathā ||

	gayāśīrṣe pade caiva pitṝṇāṃ dattam akṣayam |

	śamīpatrapramāṇena piṇḍaṃ dadyād gayāśire ||

	narakasthā divaṃ yānti svargasthā mokṣam āpnuyuḥ || iti |

śamīpatragrahaṇaṃ svavittānusāreṇa piṇḍadānam āvaśyakam iti jñāpanārtham, ata evoktaṃ tatraiva |

	vittaśāṭhyaṃ na kurvīta gayāṃ prāpya sadā naraḥ |

	vittaśāṭhyaṃ ca kurvāṇo na tīrthaphalabhāg bhavet ||

ato vittānusāreṇa śarīrabalānusāreṇa ca gayāśrāddhaṃ kāryam | etad api tatraivoktam |

	ato nirvartayc chrāddhaṃ yathāśakti yathābalam |

	kāmān sa labhate divyān svargadvāraṃ tu tat smṛtam || iti |

tena sati saṃbhave savarṇādibhyo 'pi kṛpayā piṇḍadānādikaṃ deyaṃ etad api tatraivoktam |

	savarṇā jñātayo ye ca bāndhavāḥ suhṛdaś ca ye |

	tebhyo bhūya gayābhūmau piṇḍā deyā vidhānataḥ ||

	dauhitrebhyaś ca putrebhyaḥ kaniṣṭhebhyo 'pi sarvaśaḥ |

	ye mṛtāś cānyajanmānaḥ piṇḍāṃs tebhyo vinirvapet ||

	te 'pi yānti divaṃ sarve piṇḍe datta iti śrutiḥ ||

savarṇādīnāṃ gotrādīnm ajñāne tu teṣāṃ piṇḍadānamantro 'pi tatraiva darśitaḥ |

	pitṛvaṃśasamutpannā mātṛvaṃśyās tathaiva ca |

	guruśvaśurabandhūnāṃ ye cānye mānavā dvijāḥ ||

	ye me kule luptapiṇḍāḥ putradāravivarjitāḥ |

	virūpā āmagarbhāś ca jñātājñātās tathaiva ca ||

	kiryālopagatā ye ca ye cānye garbhasaṃsthitāḥ |

	tebhyo datto mayā daṇḍo ky akṣayyam upatiṣṭhatām ||

āmagarbhā apakvagarbhā apūrṇagarbhā iti yāvat | savarṇādibhyaḥ piṇḍadānavad ātmārtham api tilarahitaṃ piṇḍaṃ janārdanadevasaṃnidhau nikṣepadravyasthāpanavan nirvapet | etad api tatraivoktam |

	ātmanas tu mahābuddhe gayāyāṃ tu tilair vinā |

	piṇḍanirvapaṇaṃ kāryaṃ mṛtānāṃ tu tilaiḥ saha || iti |

gayāyāṃ yatra yatra śrāddhādikaṃ kriyate tatra tatratyā eva viprāḥ jātimātropajīvino 'pi brāhmaṇārthe parigrāhyāḥ | tathā ca purāṇāntaram |

	yadi putro gayāṃ gacchet kadācit kālaparyayāt |

	tān eva bhojayed viprān brāhmaṇā ye prakalpitāḥ ||

	eṣāṃ brahmamayaṃ sthānaṃ somapānaṃ tathaiva ca |

	brahmakāritasaṃsthānā viprā brahmasamāḥ smṛtāḥ ||

	amānuṣā gayāviprā brāhmaṇā ye prakalpitāḥ |

	teṣu tuṣṭeṣu saṃtuṣṭāḥ pitṛbhiḥ saha devatāḥ ||

	pitṛrūpān gayāviprān pūjayitvā samāhitaḥ |

	sarvapāpaviśuddhātmā svargaloke mahīyate ||

	teṣāṃ ca hastadattaṃ vai gayāyāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ |

	tad akṣayyaṃ bhavet tasya pitṝṇāṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ ||

	na vicāryaṃ kulaṃ śīlaṃ vidyā ca tapa eva ca |

	pūjitais tais tu saṃtuṣṭāḥ devāḥ sapitṛguhyakāḥ || iti |

"yadi putro gayāṃ gacchet" ity atra putragrahaṇaṃ pautrādīnāṃ pitrādigataśreyaḥkāmānāṃ sarveṣāṃ gayāgantṝṇām upalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva brahmakaivarte,

	udyatas tu gayāṃ gantuṃ śrāddhaṃ kṛtvā vidhānataḥ |

	vidhāya karmaśeṣaṃ ca grāmaṃ kṛtvā pradakṣiṇam ||

	tato grāmāntaraṃ gacchec chrāddhaśeṣānnabhuṅ naraḥ |

	tataḥ pratidinaṃ gacchet pratigrahavivarjitaḥ ||

iti sāmānyenaivoktam | ata eva mahābhārate vyāsenāpi sāmānyenaivoktam |

	gṛhe śrāddhaṃ prakurvīta samyak saṃkalpya buddhimān |

	pitṛtīrthaṃ samuddiśya saṃkalpya pitṛsaṃnidhau ||

	pratigrahaṃ parānnaṃ ca kaliṃ caiva dvijottamaḥ || iti |

pitṛsaṃnidhau pitrarthaṃ nimantritabrāhmaṇasaṃnidhau pitṛtīrthaṃ samuddiśya gayāyātrārthaṃ śrāddhaṃ kariṣye iti samyag bhaktipūrvakaṃ saṃkalpya svagṛhe yātrārthaṃ śrāddhaṃ kuryād ity arthaḥ | kaliḥ kalahaḥ | varjyāntaram api tenaivoktam |

	keśaśmaśrunakhādīnāṃ vapanaṃ na ca śasyate |

	ato na kāryaṃ vapanaṃ gayāśrāddhārthinā sadā || iti |

evaṃ gayāyātrāṃ kurvataḥ phalam api tatraivoktam |

	ye bhārate 'smin pitṛkarmatatparāḥ saṃdhārya keśān atibhaktinamrāḥ |

	ṛṇakṣayārthaṃ pitṛtīrtham āgatāḥ teṣām ṛṇaṃ saṃkṣayam eṣyati dhruvam || iti |

bhārate bhāratavarṣe ṛṇakṣayārthaṃ devarṣipitṛṛṇakṣayārthaṃ pitṛtīrthaṃ gayā ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ kāmyaśraddhadeśāḥ**

**śrāddhe bhojanīyabrāhmaṇanirūpaṇam**

tatra manuḥ |

	tatra ye bhojanīyāḥ syur ye ca varjyā dvijottamāḥ |

	yāvantaś caiva yaiś cānnais tān pravakṣyāmy aśeṣataḥ ||

tatra śrāddhakarmaṇīty arthaḥ | dvijottamāḥ dvijeṣu traivarṇikeṣūttamāḥ brāhmaṇā iti yāvat | bhojanīyān abhojanīyāṃś ca brāhmaṇān vettuṃ guṇadoṣādiparīkṣaṇaṃ kāryam ity āha sa eva |

	dūrād eva parīkṣeta brāhmaṇaṃ vedapāragam | iti |

bhojanīyabrāhmaṇasya prapitāmahād ārabhya bhojanīyaparyantaṃ parīkṣā dūrāt parīkṣā | vedapāragagrahaṇam upādeyaguṇānām upalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva chāgaleyaḥ |

	uktalakṣaṇasaṃyuktaiḥ vidyāśīlaguṇānvitaiḥ |

	puruṣatrayavikhyātaiḥ sarvaṃ srāddhaṃ. prakalpayet ||

uktalakṣaṇair vipraiḥ sarvaṃ pārvaṇābhyudayikādiśrāddhaṃ prakalpayen nirvartayed ity arthaḥ | purāṇe 'pi |

	jātakarmādibhir yas tu saṃskāraiḥ saṃskṛtaḥ śuciḥ |

	vedādhyayanasaṃpannaḥ ṣaṭsu karmasv avasthitaḥ ||

	śaucārāre sthitaḥ samyak vighasāśī gurupriyaḥ |

	nityaṃ vratī satyaparaḥ sa vai brāhmaṇa ucyate ||

	tapaḥ śrutaṃ ca yoniś cāpy etad brāhmaṇyakāraṇam |

	satyaṃ dānaṃ tapo droham ānṛśaṃsyaṃ kṣamā ghṛṇā ||

	tapaś ca dṛśyate yatra sa brāhmaṇa iti smṛtaḥ || iti |

ṣaṭsu yajanayājanādhyayanādhyāpanadānapratigrahātmakeṣu | vighaso yajñaśeṣaḥ, atithiprabhṛtibhiḥ bhuktaśeṣaś ca | atithiprabhṛtibhiḥ bhuktaśeṣaś ca | yonir anvayaśuddhiḥ | ānṛśaṃsyam akrūratā | hārīto 'pi: "kulīnāḥ śrutaśīlavanto vṛttasthāḥ satyavādino 'vyaṅgāḥ pāṅkteyāḥ" iti | svayam eva kulādīn vivṛṇoti: sthitiḥ avicchinnavedaveditā ayonisaṃkaritvam ārṣeyatvaṃ ceti kulaguṇāḥ | vedā aṅgāni dharmo 'dhyātmaṃ vijñānaṃ smṛtiś ceti ṣaḍvidhaṃ śrutam | brahmaṇyatā vedapitṛbhaktatā samatā saumyatā aparopatāpitā anasūyatā anuddhatatā apāruṣyaṃ mitratā priyavāditvaṃ kṛtajñatā śaraṇyatā praśāntiś ceti trayodaśavidhaṃ śīlam | kṣamā dayā damo dānam ahiṃsā gurupūjanaṃ śaucaṃ japo homaḥ tapaḥ svādhyāyaḥ satyavacanaṃ santoṣo dṛḍḥavratatvam upavratatvam iti ṣoḍasaguṇaṃ vṛttam iti | sthitiḥ saṃtatirūpena ca kālasthitiḥ | avicchinnavedadevitety atra vediśabdena havirāsādanārthadeśaviśeṣavācinā haviḥsādhyo yāga upalakṣyate | etad uktaṃ bhavati: pūrvapuruṣeṣv api vedādhyayanayāgānuṣṭhānayoḥ sattā kulaguṇā iti | ārṣeyatvaṃ svīyapravarāgataṛṣijātatvam | dharmo dharmaśāstram | vijñānaṃ vaiśeṣikādiśāstrajñānam | smṛtiḥ vedādīnām avismaraṇam | upavratatvaṃ daśamyādāv ekabhaktaniṣṭhatvam | viṣṇur api |

########## p. 156 MISSING

	pūrvam eva parīkṣeta brāhmaṇān vedapāragān |

	sarīraprabhavair doṣair viśuddhāṃś caritavratān ||

pūrvam eva nimantraṇāt prāg evety arthaḥ | caritavratān snātakān | tathā ca sa eva |

	gṛhastho brahmacārī ca yajurvedavid eva ca |

	vedavidyāvratasnātaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ paṅktipāvanaḥ ||

caśabdād yatir apy uktaḥ | uktaṃ ca sākṣād vasiṣṭhena: "yatīn gṛhasthān sadhūn vā" iti | bhojayed iti śeṣaḥ | brahmāṇḍapurāṇe 'pi |

	śikhibhyo dhāturaktebhyaḥ tridaṇḍibhyaś dāpayet | iti |

śikhino brahmacāriṇaḥ | dhāturaktā dhāturaktavastradhāriṇaḥ vānaprasthaḥ | atra paraḥ paraḥ śreṣṭhaḥ | ata eva nāradaḥ |

	yo vai yatīn anādṛtya bhojayed itarān dvijān |

	vijānan vasato grāme kavyaṃ tad yāti rākṣasān ||

grāme svagrāme vasato yatīn jānann api tān anādṛtyetarān dvijān vānaprasthādīn yo bhojayet, tat tadīyaṃ kavyaṃ pitrarthaṃ saṃkalpitam annādikaṃ rākṣasān eva gacchatīty arthaḥ | tena sati saṃbhave yatīn bhojayet | teṣām abhāve vānaprasthān, teṣām abhāve brahmacāriṇaḥ, teṣām abhave gṛhasthān iti mantavyam | ata eva brahmāṇḍapurāṇe |

	alābhe dhyānibhikṣūṇāṃ bhojayed brahmacāriṇam |

	tadalābhe hy udāsīnaṃ gṛhastham api bhojayet ||

dhyānam asyāstīti dhyānī vānaprasthaḥ | bhikṣur yatiḥ | udāsīno dātur asaṃbandhī | tathā ca āpastambaḥ: "brāhmaṇān bhojayed brahmavidaḥ yonigotramantrāntevāsyasaṃbandhān" iti | yonisaṃbandhā mātulādayaḥ, gotrasaṃbandhāḥ sapiṇḍādayaḥ, mantrasaṃbandhā vedādhyāpakādayaḥ, antevāsisaṃbandhāḥ śiṣyaśāstropādhyāyādayaḥ | evaṃvidhasaṃbandhavyatiriktān brāhmaṇān gṛhasthān bhojayet | brahmajñān brāhmaṇān | yatnena bhojayed ity arthaḥ | tathā ca pitṛgāthā (?) |

	api syāt sa kule jantuḥ bhojayed yas tu yoginam |

	vipraṃ śrāddhe prayatnena tena tṛpyāmahe vayam ||

prayatnena bhojayed ity anena atyantaśraiṣṭhyaṃ yogina uktam | uktaṃ ca suspaṣṭaṃ purāṇe |

	gṛhasthānāṃ sahasreṇa vānaprasthaśatena ca |

	brahmacārisahasreṇa yo yogī sa viśiṣyate ||

padmapurāṇe 'pi |

	sāṅgān yaś caturo vedān adhīte saṃskṛto 'rthavit |

	janmavākkarmasaṃśuddhaḥ sa śrāddhe prathamo mataḥ ||

	tādṛśād ayutāc chreyān naro yogaṃ samāśritaḥ |

vṛddhaśātātapo 'pi |

	yoginaṃ bhojayen nityaṃ dṛṣṭatattvaṃ manīṣiṇam |

	teṣāṃ tu dattam akṣayyaṃ bhavatīti na saṃśayaḥ ||

ye samyagvarnāśramācārāḥ tebhyas tatpūrvārdhenoktaṃ paramaṃ pātram ity arthaḥ | etad yogināṃ praśaṃsāmatram, śātātapena "dṛṣṭatattvaṃ manīṣiṇam" iti viśeṣitatvāt,

	ye tu vṛtte sthitā nityaṃ jñānino dhyāninas tathā |

iti brahmāṇḍapurāṇe vṛttasthānām eva jñānināṃ dhyānināṃ ca bhojanīyatvābhidhānāc ca | ātmādisvarūpaparicchittiḥ jñānam | dhyānaṃ tu vijānīyapratyayatiraskāreṇātmādeḥ svarūpasākṣātkaraṇam | evaṃ ca yad uktaṃ vṛddhaśātātapena,

	jñānī yasya gṛhe 'śnāti udakaṃ vā pibed yadi |

	kṛtaṃ teneha yat kṛtyaṃ tāritaṃ ca kulatrayam ||

	yoginaṃ samatikramya gṛhasthaṃ yadi bhojayet |

	na tatphalam avāpnoti svargastham api pātayet ||

	yoginaṃ tu vyatikramya pūjayanti parasparam |

	bhoktāras tv atha dātāro narake syuḥ sabāndhavāḥ ||

ity etat sarvaṃ vṛttasthadṛṣṭatattvayogiviṣayam iti mantavyam | tatra manuḥ |

	eṣām anyatamo yasya bhuñjīta śrāddham arcitaḥ |

	pitṝṇāṃ tasya tṛptiḥ syāc chāśvatī sāptapauruṣī ||

	eṣa vai prathamaḥ kalpaḥ pradāne havyakavyayoḥ |

	anukalpas tvayaṃ jñeyaḥ sadā sadbhir anuṣṭhitaḥ ||

	mātāmahaṃ mātulaṃ ca svasrīyaṃ śvaśuraṃ gurum |

	dauhitraṃ viṭpatiṃ bandhum ṛtvigyājyau ca bhojayet || iti |

eṣāṃ pūrvoktānāṃ vedapāragādīnām eṣa bhinno vipravargaḥ prathamaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ | anukalpaḥ prathamakalpād adhamakalpaḥ, "mukhyaḥ syāt prathamaḥ kalpo 'nukalpas tu tato 'dhamaḥ" ity amarasiṃhābhidhānāt | ayam "mātāmahaṃ mātulaṃ ca" ityādinā vakṣyamāṇaḥ adhamaḥ kalpaḥ sadā sadbhir anuṣṭhita ity arthaḥ | gurur atra vidyāguruḥ, na tu pitā, "viṭpatiḥ jāmātā atithir vā, atithir ity anye vadanti" iti devasvāminābhidhānāt | prathamakalpalābhe 'nukalpānuṣṭhāne tu doṣam āha sa eva |

	prabhuḥ prathamakalpasya yo 'nukalpena vartate |

	na sāṃparāyikaṃ tasya durmater vidyate phalam ||

prabhuḥ saṃpādane samarthaḥ | sāṃparāya uttarakālaḥ | "yuddhāyatyoḥ sāṃparāyaḥ" ity amarasiṃhābhidhānāt | evaṃ cāyam arthaḥ: sāṃparāye bhaviṣyatkāle svargādikaṃ phalaṃ na vidyate na siddhyati | viṣṇupurāṇe 'py anukalpa uktaḥ |

	pitṛvyagurudauhitrān ṛtviksvasrīyamātulān |

	pūjayed dhavyakavyena vṛddhān anatibāndhavān ||

svasrīyo bhāgineyaḥ | atra pitṛvyam ṛtvijaṃ ca havyena pūjayet | gurudauhitrādītarān (?) kavyeneti saṃbandhaḥ kāryaḥ | "ṣaḍbhyas tu puruṣebhyo 'rvāg aśrāddheyās tu gotriṇaḥ" iti ṣaḍbhyo 'rvācīnasya pitṛvyādeḥ kavyena pūjanasya atriṇā niṣedhāt, tathā,

	pitā pitāmaho bhrātā putro vātha sapiṇḍakaḥ |

	na parasparam arghyāḥ syur na śrāddhe ṛtvijas tathā ||

	ṛtvikputrādayo hy ete sakulyā brāhmaṇā dvijāḥ |

	vaiśvadeve niyoktavyāḥ yady ete guṇavattarāḥ ||

iti havyena pūjanīyatvasya tenaiva vidhānāc ca | yady āmantrayītety anuvṛttau kātyāyanenoktam: "abhāve śiṣyān svācāryān" iti | atrāpi vaiśvadevārtham iti śeṣo draṣṭavyaḥ | "guṇavadalābhe sodaryo 'pi bhojayitavyaḥ" ity abhidhāyānantaram "etenāntevāsino vyākhyātāḥ" ity āpastambenābhidhānāt | sodaryo 'pi vaiśvadevasthāne bhojayitavyo na punaḥ pitrādibrāhmaṇasthāna iti hi prākpratipaditam | tena antevāsinām apit tatsthān eva niṣedhaḥ | yatu tu paṅktipāvanān uktvā bodhāyanenoktam "tadabhāve rahasyaṃ ṛco yajūṃṣi sāmāni śrāddhmahimānaḥ tasmād evaṃvidaṃ sapiṇḍam apy āśayet" iti, tad apy ātreyavacanānurodhāya ṣaḍbhyaḥ puruṣebhyo 'rvācīnasapiṇḍaviṣayaṃ na bhavati, kiṃ tu samānodakaviṣayam, sapiṇḍaśabdasya samānodake 'py upacāreṇa prayogasaṃbhavāt | atriṇā tu spaṣṭam uktam |

	ṣaḍbhyas tu parato bhojyāḥ śrāddhe syuḥ gotrajā api | iti |

atha vā sapiṇḍaśabdo mukhyo 'stu, kiṃ tu śreṣṭhasya samānodakasyāpy abhāve tribhyaḥ sapiṇḍapuruṣebhyaḥ paro yaḥ sapiṇḍaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ tam āśayed ity artho 'vagantavyaḥ | tathā ca sapiṇḍa ity anuvṛttau gautamaḥ: "bhojayed ūrdhvaṃ tribhyo guṇavantam" iti | manus tv anukalpāntaram āha |

	kāmaṃ śrāddhe 'rcayen mitraṃ nābhirūpam api tv arim |

	dviṣatā hi havir bhuktaṃ bhavati pretya niṣphalam || iti |

abhirūpam api vidvāṃsam apīty arthaḥ | kāmam ity abhidhānāt, anukalpo 'yam iti gamyate | ayaṃ tv anukalpaḥ pūrvoktānām anukalpānām abhāve draṣṭavyaḥ,

	na śrāddhe bhojayen mitraṃ dhanaiḥ kāryo 'sya saṃgrahaḥ |

	nāriṃ na mitraṃ yaṃ vindyāt taṃ śrāddhe bhojayed dvijam ||

	yasya mitrapradhānāni śrāddhāni ca havīṃṣi ca |

	tasya pretya phalaṃ nāsti śrāddheṣu ca haviḥṣu ca ||

iti nindārthavādena svenaiva niṣiddhasya mitrasya "kāmaṃ śrāddhe 'rcayen mitram" iti punar anuśayābhyupagamenānukalpād apy adhamatvāvagamāt | vasiṣṭho 'pi saguṇānām anukalpānām abhāve nirguṇānām anukalpatayā svīkāram āha |

	ānṛśaṃsyaṃ paro dharmo yācate yat pradīyate | 

	ayācataḥ sīdamānān sarvopāyair nimantrayet ||

ānṛśaṃsyaṃ paraḥ utkṛṣṭo dharmaḥ | tena saguṇānām anukalpānām abhāve nirguṇāyāpi yācate yat pradīyate tad apy anukalpo bhavati | ayācataḥ sīdamānān ayācanaśīlata eva kāraṇāt sīdato nirguṇān api saguṇānām anukalpānām alābhe sarvopāyair yādṛśais te nimantraṇam abhyupagacchanti tādṛśair upāyair nimantrayed ity arthaḥ | sarvopāyair nimantrayed ity ādareṇa nimantraṇaṃ vadan ayācanena sīdatām alābhe yācate pradānam iti darśayati | evaṃvidhavipreṣu sadācāravaikalyadarśane 'pi nindā na karyety aha sa eva |

	yuge yuge tu ye dharmāḥ teṣu dharmeṣu ye dvijāḥ |

	teṣāṃ nindā na kartavyā yugarūpā hi te dvijāḥ ||

yuge yuge tu ye dharmāḥ yugānurūpāḥ rāgadveṣāditāratamyanibandhanā ye 'py asatyabhāṣaṇādayo duḥsvabhāvās teṣu dharmeṣu ye dvijāḥ teṣāṃ nindā na kartavyā | yugānurūpavipreṣv api yathāsaṃbhavaṃ śreṣṭhā eva grāhyāḥ | ata eva bhaviṣyapurāṇe apraśastaviprāṇāṃ dānādāv aparigrāhyatvam uktam |

	vaiśvadevena ye hīnā ātithyena ca varjitāḥ |

	sarve te vṛṣalā jñeyā prāptavedā api dvijāḥ ||

	na yasya vedo na japo na vidyā ca viśāṃpate |

	sa śūdra iva mantavya ity āha bhagavān vibhuḥ ||

	avratānām amantrāṇām adayānāṃ (?) ca bhārata |

	pratigraho na dātavyo na śilā tātayec chilām ||

	brāhmaṇātikramo nāsti mūrkhe vedavivarjite |

	jvalantam agnim utsṛjya na hi bhasmani hūyate ||

vaiśvadevagrahaṇaṃ pañcamahāyajānām upalakṣaṇārtham | śilā śilāntaram | vedavivarjite bhojanādyapradāne 'pi nāsti brāhmaṇātikrama ity arthaḥ | etad atyantāsaṃbandhibrāhmaṇaviṣayam | kathaṃcit saṃbandhibrāhmaṇaviṣaye 'pi tatraivoktam |

	gāyatrīmātrasāro 'pi brāhmaṇaḥ pūjyatāṃ gataḥ |

	guhāsaṃno viśeṣeṇa na bhavet patitaḥ sa cet ||

gṛhāsaṃnaḥ prātiveśyādiḥ | viśeṣeṇeti vadan kathaṃcit saṃabandhy api nātikramaṇīya iti darśayati | śreṣṭhasaṃnikṛṣṭātikrame tu ṣaṭtriṃsanmate doṣa uktaḥ |

	saṃnikṛṣṭam adhīyānaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ yo vyatikramet |

	bhojane caiva dāne ca hanyāt tripuruṣaṃ kulam ||

vastu saṃnikṛṣṭo 'nadhīyānaḥ tasyātikrame 'pi na doṣaḥ | tathā ca tatraivoktam |

	yasya tv ekagṛhe mūrkho dūrasthaś ca guṇānvitaḥ |

	guṇānvitāya dātavyaṃ nasti mūrkhe vyatikramaḥ ||

vyatikramo vyatikramadoṣo nastīty arthaḥ | mūrkhagrahaṇaṃ nirguṇasyāpy upalakṣaṇārtham,

	vyatikrāntur na doṣo 'sti nirguṇaṃ prati karhicit |

iti bhaviṣyapurāṇe 'bhidhānāt | yat punaḥ purāṇāntare 'bhihitam,

	yas tv āsannam atikramya brāhmaṇaṃ patitād ṛte |

	dūrasthaṃ bhojayen mūḍho guṇāḍhyaṃ narakaṃ vrajet ||

	tasmāt saṃpūjayed enaṃ guṇaṃ tasya na cintayet |

	kevalaṃ cintayej jātiṃ na guṇānvitatān sadā ||

	saṃnikṛṣṭaṃ dvijaṃ yas tu yuktajātiṃ priyaṃvadam |

	mūrkhaṃ vā patitaṃ vāpi vṛttahīnam athāpi vā ||

	nātikramen naro vidvān dāridryābhihataṃ tathā ||

iti, tat anukalpatayoktaśarīrasaḥ saṃnikṛṣṭadauhitrajāmātrādiviṣayam | pūrvoktaṃ tu deśataḥ saṃnikṛṣṭaprātiveśyādiviṣayam iti na virodhaḥ | ata eva sarīrataḥ saṃnikṛṣṭam ekam udāhṛtyoktaṃ manunā |

	vratastham api dauhitraṃ śrāddhae patnena bhojayet | iti |

vratasthaṃ vratamātrastham adhyayanarahitam iti yāvat | dvividhasaṃnikṛṣṭaviṣaye 'pi guṇādibhiḥ śreṣṭhe 'tikrānte sati bhavaty eva doṣaḥ | tad apy uktaṃ purāṇe |

	sapta pūrvān sapta parān puruṣān ātmanā saha |

	atikramya dvijavaraṃ narake patayet khaga ||

	tasmān nātikramet prājñaḥ brāhmaṇān prātiveśikān |

	saṃbandhinas tathā sarvān dauhitraṃ viṭpatiṃ tathā ||

	bhāgineyaṃ viśeṣeṇa tathā bandhūn khagādhipa |

	nātikramen naras tv etān amurkhān api gopate ||

	atikramya mahāraudraṃ rauravaṃ narakaṃ vrajet || iti |

amūrkhān apīty apiśabdaḥ padapūraṇārthaḥ |

	ajñātakulanāmānaṃ tatkālaṃ samupasthitam |

	bubhukṣum āgataṃ śrāddhaṃ yācamānam akiṃcanam ||

	brāhmaṇaṃ prāhur atithim ................... |||

ityuktātithilakṣaṇalakṣito 'pi vipro nātikramaṇīyaḥ,

	atithir yasya nāśnāti tacchrāddhaṃ na praśasyate |

iti śātātapasmaraṇāt | atitheir apy āsannasyeva guṇavidyāparīkṣaṇaṃ na kartavyam | tathā purāṇam |

	avijñātaṃ dvijaṃ śrāddhe na parīkṣet sadā budhaḥ |

	siddhā hi viprarūpeṇa carantīha mahītale ||

avijñātam avijñātakulanāmādikam atithim iti yāvat | siddhāḥ viditātmatattvāḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ śrāddhabhojanīyabrāhmaṇanirūpaṇam**

**atha bhojanīyatayoktaśrotriyādibrāhmaṇeṣu **

**ye doṣasadbhāvād varjyās te nirūpyante**

atra manuḥ |

	ye stenāḥ patitāḥ klībā ye ca nāstikavṛttayaḥ|

	tān havyakavyayor viprān anarhān manur abravīt ||

	jaṭilaṃ cānadhīyānaṃ durvālaṃ kitavaṃ tathā |

	yājayanti ca ye pūgān tāṃś ca śrāddhe na bhojayet ||

	cikitsakān devalakān māṃsavikrayiṇas tathā |

	vipaṇena ca jīvanto varjyāḥ syur havyakavyayoḥ ||

	preṣyo grāmasya rājñaś ca kunakhī śyāvadantakaḥ |

	pratiroddhā guroś caiva tyakāgnir vārdhuṣis tathā ||

	yakṣmī ca paśupālaś ca parivettā nirākṛtiḥ |

	brahmadviṭ parivittiś ca gaṇābhyantara eva ca ||

	kuśīlavo 'vakīrṇī ca vṛṣalīpatir eva ca |

	paunarbavaś ca kāṇaś ca yasya copapatir gṛhe ||

	bhṛtakādhyapako yaś ca bhṛtakādhyāpitaś ca yaḥ |

	śūdraśiṣyo guruś caiva vāgduṣṭaḥ kuṇḍagolakau ||

	akāraṇaparityaktā mātāpitror guros tathā |

	brāhmair yaunaiś ca saṃbandhaiḥ saṃyogaṃ patitair gataḥ ||

	agāradāhī garadaḥ kuṇḍāśī somavikrayī |

	samudrayāyī bandī ca tailikaḥ kūṭakārakaḥ ||

	pitrā vivadamānaś ca kekaro madyapas tathā |

	pāparogy abhiśastaś ca dāmbhiko rasavikrayī ||

	dhauḥśarāṇāṃ kartā ca yaś cāgredidhiṣūpatiḥ |

	mitradhruk dyūtavṛttiś ca putrācāryas tathaiva ca ||

	bhrāmarī gaṇḍamālī ca śvitry atho piśunas tathā |

	unmatto 'ndhaś ca varjyāḥ syur vedanindaka eva ca ||

	hastigo'śvoṣṭradamako nakṣatrair yaś ca jīvati |

	pakṣiṇāṃ poṣako yaś ca yuddhācāryas tathaiva ca ||

	srotasāṃ bhedako yaś ca teṣāṃ cāvaraṇe rataḥ |

	gṛhasaṃveśako dūto vṛkṣāropaka eva ca ||

	śvakrīḍī śyenajīvī ca kanyādūṣaka eva ca |

	hiṃsro vṛṣalaputraś ca gaṇānāṃ caiva yājakaḥ ||

	ācārahīnaḥ klībaś ca nityaṃ yācanakas tathā |

	kṛṣijīvī ślīpadī ca sadbhir nindita eva ca ||

	aurabhrako māhiṣakaḥ parapūrvāpatis tathā |

	pretaniryātakaś caiva varjanīyāḥ prayatnataḥ ||

	etān vigarhitācārān apāṅkteyān narādhamān |

	dvijātipravaro vidvān ubhayatra vivarjayet || iti |

atra yad yad vyākhyāgamyaṃ tat tad vyākhyāyate | stenā brāhmaṇasuvarṇavyatiriktadravyāpahartāraḥ, brāhmaṇasvarṇahartṝṇāṃ patitapadenaiva varjyatvasyābhidhānāt | svakarmatyāgino vā stenā,

	ye vyapetāḥ svakarmabhyaḥ stenās te parikīrtitāḥ |

iti yamasmaraṇāt | patitā mahāpātakinaḥ | klībās tu ṣaḍvidhāḥ devalena darśitāḥ |

	ṣaṇḍako vātajaś caiva ṣaṇḍaḥ klībo napuṃsakaḥ |

	kīlakaś ceti ṣoḍhāyaṃ klībabhedo vibhāṣitaḥ ||

ṣaṇḍakādīnāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ svayam eva darśayati |

	teṣāṃ strītulyavākceṣṭaḥ strīdharmā ṣaṇḍako bhavet |

	pumān bhūtvā svaliṅgāni paścāc chindyāt tathaiva ca ||

	vātajo nāma ṣaṇḍaḥ syāt strīṣaṇḍo vāpi nāmataḥ |

	asalliṅgo 'tha ṣaṇḍaḥ syāt ṣaṇḍas tu mlānamehanaḥ ||

	amedhyāśī pumān klībo naṣṭaretā napuṃsakaḥ |

	na kīlaka iti jñeyo yaḥ klaibyād ātmanaḥ striyam ||

	anyena saha saṃyojya paścāt tām eva sevate || iti |

nāsti lokāntarphaladaṃ karma nasti devatetyādimatimanto nastikāḥ | tebhyo vṛttir jīvanaṃ yeṣāṃ śrotriyādīnāṃ te nāstikavṛttayaḥ | jaṭilo brahmacārī anadhīyāno vedādhyayanarahitaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanv</span> anadhīyānajaṭilasya aśrotriyatvena prāptyabhāvād ayuktaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> |

	vratastham api dauhitraṃ śraddhe yatnena bhojayet |

ity anenānukalpatayā bhojanīyabrāhmaneṣu dauhitraḥ brahmacārī vratamātrasthaḥ anadhīyāno 'pi bhojanīyatayoktaḥ | tatra dauhitragrahaṇam atantram iti bhrāntyā kathaṃcit prāpto 'tra niṣidhyata iti nātīv vyarthaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">kecit</span>: anadhīyānagṛhasthasyāśrotriyasyāpi prāptyartham ity āhuḥ | tad <span style="text-decoration:underline;">ayuktam</span>,

	vedavidyāvratasnātān śrotriyān gṛhamedhinaḥ |

	bhojayed dhavyakavyena viparītāṃs tu varjayet ||

iti viśeṣeṇa varjyatayoktasya gṛhasthasy prāptyasaṃbhavāt | durvālaḥ khaly āṭakaḥ, kapilakeśo vā atyantakopano vā | tad etat sarvaṃ saṃgrahakāreṇoktam |

	niścitādhyayanenaiva guṇena svīkṛto 'khilaḥ |

	mūrkho yo brahmacārī tu jaṭilas taṃ na bhojayet ||

	dauhitrādivad atrāpi bhrāntyā prāpto niṣidhyate |

	īdṛśasya gṛhasthasya prāptyartham apare viduḥ ||

	tan na yuktam avidvāṃś ca gṛhasthaś ca nirudhyate |

	kalvāṭakaś ca durvālaḥ kapilaś caṇḍa eva vā || iti |

pūgayājakāḥ bahūnāṃ pratyekaṃ yājakāḥ | śrāddhagrahaṇam atra daive 'bhyanujñānārtham | daivasyāp pradarśanārthatve tu vyartham eva syāt | pūrvāparaparyālocanayaiva daive pitrye ca pratiṣedhāvagateḥ | ata eva saṃgrahakāraḥ |

	durvālādīn śrāddha eva sūtreṇāha ca gautamaḥ | iti |

manvādīnāṃ matatveneti śeṣaḥ | tathā ca brāhmaṇaparīkṣādhikāre gautamaḥ: "haviḥṣu caivaṃ durvālādīn śrāddhe evaike" (GDh 15.30) | haviḥṣu daive 'pi ca evaṃ pitryavat parīkṣya durvālādīn vivarjayet | eke tu manvādayaḥ durvālādīn na pitrye bhojayet na punar daive 'pīti manyanta iti | cikitsakā vṛttyarthaṃ dharmārthaṃ ca | taittirīyakaśrutau "tasmād brāhmaṇena bheṣajaṃ na kāryam apūto hy eṣo 'medhyo yo bhiṣak" ity aviśeṣeṇa bhiṣajo nindādarśanāt | devalakasya svarūaṃ devalena darśitam |

	devārcanaparo vipro vittārthī vatsaratrayam |

	sa vai devalako nāma havyakavyeṣu garhitaḥ ||

	devakośopajīvī tu nāmnā devalako bhavet |

	apāṅkteyaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ sarvakaramasu sarvadā || iti |

vipaṇo vāṇijyam, tenānādady api jīvanto brāhmaṇāḥ vipaṇajīvinaḥ | vipaṇajīvitaiva pratiṣiddhasya māṃsavikrayiṇaḥ punaḥ pratiṣedho 'tyantavarjyatvakhyāpanārthaḥ | tena adhyayanādivikrayiṇāṃ śrotriyādīnām anukalpatayopādeyatvam avagamyate | atha vā āpady api māṃsavikrayiṇo varjyāḥ | preṣyaḥ paricārikaḥ | kunakhī svabhāvād eva mṛtanakhaḥ | śyāvadantaḥ svabhāvāt kṛṣṇadantaḥ | anayoḥ purākṛtakarmaśeṣasaṃbandhād eva pratiṣedhaḥ | guroḥ pratiroddhā spardhī | tyakāgniḥ śāstroktatyāgakāraṇam antareṇa tyaktaśrautasmārtāgniḥ | vārdhuṣikaḥ svalpavṛddhyā dhanam ādāya adhikavṛddhyā puruṣāntare dhanaprayoktā, svalpamūlyena paṇyaṃ krītvā tadvikrayeṇa bahumūlyasādhako vā | tathā ca smṛtiḥ |

	samārghaṃ dhanam utddhṛtya mahārghaṃ ya prayacchati |

	sa vai vārdhuṣiko nāma brahmavādiṣi garhitaḥ ||

	samārghaṃ paṇyam ādāya mahārghaṃ yaḥ prayacchati |

	sa vai vārdhuṣiko nāma brahmavadiṣu garhitaḥ ||

yakṣmī kṣayarogī | paśupālaḥ anāpadi pāśupālyavṛttyupajīvī brāhmaṇaḥ | parivettṛparivittyoḥ svarūpaṃ manunā svenaiva pradarśitam |

	dārāgnihotrasaṃbandhaṃ kurute yo 'graje sthite |

	parivettā sa vijñeyaḥ parivittis tu pūrvajaḥ ||

agnihotraśabdenāgnihotrādyuttarakratuprayojyam ādhānam uktam | uktaṃ ca sākṣād gargeṇa |

	sodarye tiṣṭhati jyeṣṭhe na kuryād dārasaṃgraham |

	āvasathyaṃ tathādhānaṃ patitas tu tathā bhavet ||

āvasathyam āvasathyādhānam, dāyavibhāgakāle kriyamāṇam aupāsanādhānam iti yāvat, vivāhakāle kriyamāṇaupāsanāgneś ca "na kuryād dārasaṃgraham" ity anenaivārthān nirastatvāt | ataḥ,

	aupāsanaṃ samādadhyāt svakāle parivedayan |

iti brahmagarbhavacane 'pi svakālaśabdena dāyavibhāgakāla uktaḥ, na tu vivāhakālo 'pīty avagantavyam | ādhānaṃ gārhapatyādyādhānam | patito bhavet, upapātakī bhaved ity arthaḥ | upapātakiparigaṇanavacane parivettṛparivittyoḥ kīrtitatvāt | sodaryagrahaṇād asodarye tiṣṭhati jyeṣṭhe kaniṣṭhasya dārasaṃgrahādau kṛte 'pi na pātityadoṣa iti gamyate | śātātapena tu asodaryaviṣaye doṣābhāvaḥ sākṣād uktaḥ |

	pituḥ putrāś ca sāpatnāḥ paranārīsutās tathā |

	dārāgnihotrasaṃyoge na doṣaḥ parivedane || iti |

sāpatnāḥ asodarabhrātaraḥ | paranārīsutāḥ svapitrā parakṣetre utpāditāḥ dvyāmuṣyāyaṇabhūtāḥ | pitṛvyaputrādiṣu jyeṣṭheṣu dārāgnihotrasaṃyogarahiteṣu tiṣṭhatsv api kaniṣṭhena dārāgnihotrasaṃyoge kṛte parivedanadoṣo nāstīty arthaḥ | paranārīputragrahaṇaṃ dattaputrāder api pradarśanārtham | ata eva yamaḥ |

	pitṛvyaputrān sāpatnān paraputrāṃs tathaiva ca |

	dārāgnihotradharmeṣu nādharmaḥ parivindataḥ ||

paraputrāḥ dānakrayādinā svapituḥ putratvam āpannāḥ bhrātaraḥ | sodarye jyeṣṭhe dārāgnihotrasaṃyogarahite tiṣṭhati parivedane kvacid doṣo nāstīty āha śātātapaḥ |

	klībe deśāntarasthe ca patite bhukṣuke 'pi vā |

	yogaśāstrābhiyukte ca na doṣaḥ parivedane ||

bhikṣukaḥ parivrājakaḥ | yogaśāstrābhiyukto viraktaḥ | kātyāyano 'pi |

	deśāntarasthaklībaikavṛṣaṇāṃś ca sahodarān |

	veśyātisaktapatitaśūdratulyātirogiṇaḥ ||

	jaḍamūkāndhabadhirakubjavāmanakhoḍakān |

	ativṛddhān abhāryāṃś ca kṛṣisaktān nṛpasya ca ||

	dhanavṛddhiprasaktāṃś ca kāmatokāriṇas tathā |

	kuhakonmattacorāṃś ca parivindan na duṣyati ||

khoḍakaḥ bhagnacaraṇadvayaḥ | abhāryāḥ naiṣṭhikabrahmacāriṇaḥ | kāmatokāriṇaḥ svecchayaiva vivāhanivṛttikāriṇaḥ | atra ye vivāhe 'nadhikāriṇaḥ klībādayaḥ teṣāṃ kālapratīkṣaṇābhāvenāpi nāsti parivedanadoṣaḥ | ye tu vivāhādhikāriṇo deśāntarasthaviraktaveśyātisakta-śūdratulyātivṛddhakṛṣisaktarājadhanavṛddhiprasaktakāmatokārikuhakacorāḥ, teṣāṃ kālapratīkṣaṇena parvedane tu na doṣaḥ | tatra deśāntarasthe aṣṭavarṣādikālaḥ pratīkṣaṇīya ity āha vasiṣṭhaḥ: "aṣṭau daśa dvādaśa varṣāṇi jyeṣṭhabhrātaram aniviṣṭam apratīkṣamāṇaḥ prāyaścittī bhavati" iti | deśāntaragatasya vivāhadāv adhikārasaṃbhavād ity abhiprāyaḥ | aniviṣṭam akṛtavivāham ity arthaḥ | atra dvādaśavarṣapratīkṣaṇaṃ dharmārthaṃ vārthārthaṃ vā deśāntaragate jyeṣṭhe draṣṭavyam | tathā ca smṛtiḥ |

	dvādaśaiva tu varṣāṇi jyāyān dharmārthayor gataḥ |

	nyāyyaḥ pratīkṣituṃ bhrātā śrūyamāṇaḥ punaḥ punaḥ ||

bhrātā sahodaraḥ | dharmārthayor iti vidyāyā api pradarśanārtham | ata eva gautamena: "naṣṭe bhartati" iti prakramya, "dvādaśa varṣāṇi brāhmaṇasya vidyāsaṃbandhena" iti bhāryāyāḥ bhartṛpratīkṣaṇakālam uktvā uktam: "bhrātari caivaṃ jyāyasi yavīyān kanyāgnyādheyeṣu" iti | naṣṭe bhartari kutra gata ity ajñāte bhartari atyantadūradeśāntaragata iti yāvat | dvādaśavarṣāṇi brāhmaṇasya vidyāsaṃbandhena brāhmaṇasya bhartuḥ vidyāgrahaṇārthaṃ deśāntaragamane sati bhāryayā dvādaśavarṣāṇi pratīkṣaṇīyānīty arthaḥ | bhrātarīti | jyeṣṭhe bhrātari akṛtavivāhe akṛtāgnyādheye vā vidhyāgrahaṇārthaṃ deśāntaragate kaniṣṭho bhrātā kanyāparigrahe agnyādhāne caiva dvādaśavarṣāṇi pratīkṣya tad upari pravartetety arthaḥ | kāryāntarārthaṃ deśāntaragataviṣaye tu aṣṭau daś ceti pakṣadvayam | atredaṃ vivakṣitam: deśāntaragatasyābhilaṣitakāryaṃ nirvartya pratyāgamanayogyakāle 'py anāgatasya iha loke sthitisaṃdehena vivāhasaṃbhāvanānivṛttau na parivedanaṃ doṣāvaham iti | evam eva viraktaveśyātisaktādiṣv api tattatsvabhāvasya dvādaśavarṣādicirakālānuvṛttyā vivāhasaṃbhāvanānivṛttau parivedanaṃ na doṣāvaham ity abhiprāyo veditavyaḥ | anenaivābhiprāyeṇa sumantunāpy uktam |

	vyasanāsaktacitto vā nāstiko vā tathāgrajaḥ |

	kanīyān dharmakāmas tu ādhānam atha kārayet ||

ādhānagrahaṇaṃ vivāhasyāpy upalakṣaṇārtham | klībādayas tu bhrātaraḥ kiṃcit kālam api na pratīkṣaṇīyāḥ, teṣāṃ vivāhādau svata evāyogyatvenānadhikārāt | tathā ca smṛtiḥ |

	unmattaḥ kilbiṣī kuṣṭhī patitaḥ klība eva ca |

	rājayakṣmyāmayāvī ca na nyāyyaḥ syāt pratīkṣitum ||

	khañjavāmanakubjeṣu gadgadeṣu jaḍeṣu ca |

	jātyandhe badhire mūke na doṣaḥ parivedane || iti |

evam ādhānādhikāriṇi jyeṣṭhe sthite 'pi tadanumatyā parivedane tu na doṣaḥ | tathā ca vṛddhavariṣṭhaḥ |

	agrajaś ca yadānagnir ādadhyād anujaḥ katham |

	agrajānumataḥ kuryād agnihotraṃ yathāvidhi ||

ādhānādhikāry apy agrajo yadā ādhānādividhim atikramyānāhitāgnir yāvajjīvam āsta iti kaniṣṭhasya niścayaḥ tadā tad anumatiṃ labdhvādhānaṃ kuryād ity arthaḥ | ayam evārthaḥ sumantunāpy uktaḥ |

	jyeṣṭhabhrātā yadā tiṣṭhed ādhānaṃ naiva kārayet |

	anujñāto hi kurvīta śaṅkhasya vacanaṃ yathā ||

jyeṣṭhabhrātṛgrahaṇaṃ pitur api pradarśanārtham | tathā ca sa eva |

	pitur yasya tu nādhānaṃ kathaṃ putras tu kārayet |

	agnihotrādhikāro 'sti śaṅkhasya vacanaṃ yathā ||

pitṛgrahaṇaṃ pitāmahasyāpi pradarśanārtham | ata eva uśanā |

	pitā pitāmaho yasya agrajo vātha kasyacit |

	tapo 'gnihotramantreṣu na doṣaḥ parivedane ||

pūrvokta eva viṣaye satyām anujñāyām etad api vacanaṃ draṣṭavyam | mantraśabdo vedopalakṣaṇārthaḥ | tathā ca śātātapaḥ |

	nāgnayaḥ parivindanti na vedā na tapāṃsi ca |

	na ca śrāddhaṃ kaniṣṭhasya yā ca kanyā virūpikā ||

yathā vedāṃs tapāṃsi śrāddhaṃ ca adhikṛtya jyeṣṭhe adhyayanatapaḥśrāddharāhityena sthite 'pi tadanujñām antareṇāpi kaniṣṭhenānuṣthitāni parivedanahetavo na bhavanti, tathāgnayo 'pi jyeṣṭhāder abhyanujñayā kaniṣṭhenāhitā ity arthaḥ | "yā ca kanyā virūpikā" ity asyāyam arthaḥ: vivāhādhikāriṇyāṃ jyeṣṭhāyāṃ kanyāyāṃ virūpāyām anūḍhāyāṃ sthitāyāṃ tadanujñāṃ vināpi kaniṣṭhāyā vivāhādikālātikramabhītyā kṛto vivāho na doṣāyeti | evaṃ caivaṃvidhaviṣayavyatiriktaviṣaye kanyāsv api parivedane varaparivedanoktaṃ sarvam anusaṃdheyam | anujasya tu jyeṣṭhabhrātranujñayāpi vivāhadoṣo 'stīty āha hārītaḥ |

	sodarāṇāṃ tu sarveṣāṃ parivettā kathaṃ bhavet |

	dārais tu parividyante nāgnihotreṇa nejyayā ||

vivāhādāv adhikāribhūtajyeṣṭhenānujñātasodaraviṣayam etat "dārais tu parividyante" iti | vṛddhayājñavalkyas tu jyeṣṭho 'pi kadācid ādhānena parivettā bhavatīty āha |

	āvasathyam anādṛtya tretāyāṃ yaḥ pravartate |

	so 'nāhitāgnir bhavati parivettā tathocyate || iti |

ayam arthaḥ: yathā dāyavibhāgakāle aupāsanādhānaṃ yasya svagṛhyoktam, asau tad akṛtvā brahmaudanapākaṃ nirmanthyāginā kṛtvā gārhapatyādyādhānaṃ yadi kurute so 'nāhitāgnir bhavati | prathamādhāne nirmanthyāgninā brahmaudanapākasyāśāstrārthatayā gārhapatyādiśabdavācyālaukikasaṃskārasyānutpatteḥ | tathā ca prathamam ādheyam aupāsanāgnim anādhāya gārhapatyādyādhānakaraṇāt parivettety api gīyata ity alaṃ parivettṛparivittiśabdārthakathanaprapañcena |

	nirākṛtiśabdārthas tu devalena darśitaḥ |

	adhītya vismṛte vede bhaved vipro nirākṛtiḥ || iti |

kātyāyanas tv anyathā nirākṛtiśabdārtham āha |

	yas tv ādhāyāgnim ālasyād devādīn iha neṣṭavān |

	nirākartāmarādīnāṃ sa vijñeyo nirākṛtiḥ || iti |

brahmadviṭ brāhmaṇānāṃ dveṣṭā | parivittiśabdas tu parivettṛśabdavyākhyānāvasare vyākhyātaḥ | gaṇaḥ madyapāyī brāhmaṇādiḥ, tanmadhyago gaṇābhyantaraḥ | kuśīlavo gāyakanartakādiḥ | avakīrṇinam āha devalaḥ |

	gūḍhaliṅgy avakīrṇī syāt yaś ca bhagnavratas tathā | iti |

gūḍhaliṅgī daṇḍamekhalādibrahmacāriliṅgatyāgī | bhagnavrataḥ stryupagamanena skhalitabrahmacaryaḥ,

	vratī yaḥ striyam abhyeti so 'vakīrṇī nirucyate |

iti yamasmaraṇāt | vṛṣalīpatir api devalena darśitaḥ |

	vandhyā tu vṛṣalī jñeyā vṛṣalī ca mṛtaprajā |

	aparā vṛṣalī jñeyā kumārī yā rajasvalā ||

	yas tv enām udvahet kanyām brāhmaṇo jñānadurbalaḥ |

	aśrāddheyam apāṅkteyaṃ taṃ vidyād vṛṣalīpatim ||

kanyāvasthāyāṃ yā rajasvalā jātā tāṃ ya udvahet tam aśrāddheyam apāṅkteyaṃ vṛṣalīpatiṃ vidyād ity anvayaḥ | evaṃ ca tṛtīyavṛṣalīpatir evātra manunokta iti mantavyam | punarbhūḥ dvirūḍhā tasyāḥ yo dvitīyavivāhe sati patiḥ tena tasyām utpāditaḥ putraḥ paunarbhavaḥ | kāṇa ekacakṣuḥ | "yasya copapatir gṛhe" ity etad devalo na spaṣṭīkṛtam |

	paradārābhigo mohāt puruṣo jāra ucyate |

	sa evopapatir jñeyo yaḥ sadā saṃvased gṛhe ||

vetanena bhṛta upādhyāyo bhṛtakaḥ | svārthe kapratyayaḥ | bhṛtakaś cāsāv adhyāpakaś ceti bhṛtakādhyāpakaḥ | bhṛtakenādhyāpakenādhyāpitaḥ śiṣyo bhṛtakādhyāpitaḥ | etāv upapātakinau,

	bhṛtakādhyāpako yaś ca bhṛtakādhyāpitaś ca yaḥ |

	tāv ubhau patitau viprau svādhyāyakrayavikrayāt ||

iti devalasmaraṇāt | patitau upapātakināv ity arthaḥ, upapātakamadhye etayor api gaṇanāt | śūdrasya śiṣyaḥ śūdraśiṣyaḥ | guruḥ śūdraseti śeṣaḥ, tasya buddhisthatvāt | vāgduṣṭaḥ kātyāyanena darśitaḥ |

	huṃkāraṃ hasanaṃ caiva loke yac ca vigarhitam |

	anukuryād anubrūyād vāgduṣṭaṃ taṃ naraṃ viduḥ ||

kuṇḍagolakau svenaiva manunā darśitau |

	paradāreṣu jāyete dvau sutau kuṇḍagolakau |

	jīve bhartari kuṇḍaḥ syān mṛte bhartari golakaḥ ||

samabrāhmaṇabhūtābhyāṃ jāyāpatibhyām utpāditaḥ suto brāhmaṇo bhavati, na punar brāhmaṇabhūtajāreṇa brāhmaṇajātīyajāriṇyāṃ samutpāditaḥ,

	sarvavarṇeṣu tulyāsu patnīṣv akṣatayoniṣu |

	ānulomyena saṃbhūtāḥ jātyā jñeyās tathaiva te ||

iti jātinirṇaye manunaivādhidhānāt | tena kuṇḍalogakayor abrāhmaṇayoḥ śrāddhe abhojanīyatvena kathaṃcid api prāptir nāstīti "vāgduṣṭaḥ kuṇḍagolakau" ity atra kuṇḍagolakayor upādānaṃ vyarthaṃ syāt | atrottaram uktaṃ saṃgrahakāreṇa |

	niyogotpāditau śrāddhe niṣiddhau kuṇḍagolakau |

	abrāhmaṇyāt kutaḥ prāptiḥ śūdravaj jārajātayoḥ || iti |

yady api jātajātayoḥ kuṇḍagolakayoḥ brāhmaṇatvābhāvena śūdravad eva śrāddhaprāptyabhāvāt niṣedho na saṃbhavati | tathāpi niyogotpāditayoḥ kuṇḍagolakayoḥ paradārotpannayor api śāstrīyamārgānusāreṇotpāditatvāt brāhmaṇyam astīti tāv eva kuṇḍagolakau manunā śrāddhe niṣiddhāv ity arthaḥ | tad etad ayuktam, niyogotpāditayor ajārajātatvenākuṇḍagolakatvāt, ajāratvaṃ ca niyuktasyājāratvāt | tathā ca devalaḥ |

	paradārābhigo mohāt puruṣo jāra ucyate | iti |

mohād iti padaṃ niyogāt paradārābhigaḥ puruṣo na jāra ity āha | ajārajātau na kuṇḍagolakau | tathā ca sa eva |

	amṛte jārajaḥ kuṇḍo mṛte bhartari golakaḥ | iti |

jāraja iti vadan niyukto na kuṇḍo na golakaś cety āha | bṛhaspatinā tv aniyuktajāv eva kuṇḍagolakāv iti spaṣṭam uktam |

	pāradāryam adharmyaṃ tu tajjātau kuṇḍagolakau |

	aśrāddheyāv abhojyānnau kṣetrajādyās tathā sutāḥ || iti |

yad adharmyaṃ pāradāryaṃ tajjātāv eva kuṇḍagolakau, na punaḥ pāradāryamātrajāv ity arthaḥ | ataś ca niyoge sati pāradāryasyādharmyatvābhāvāt tadutpannau na kuṇḍagolakau | kuṃ tu kṣetrajāv eva | atas tayoḥ pṛthak pratiṣedhārtham "kṣetrajādyās tathā sutāḥ" ity uktam | tasmāt,

	niyogotpāditau śrāddhe niṣiddhau kuṇḍagolakau |

iti saṃgrakāroktam ayuktam eva | ato 'nyathā samādhir abhidhīyate: "vāgduṣṭaḥ kuṇḍagolakau" ity atra kuṇḍagolakaśabdau gauṇyā vṛttyā niyogotpāditakṣetrajaputrayor vartete | tatra jīvati bhartari paradāreṣu jātatvasāmyāt kuṇḍaśabdo vartate | mṛte bhartari jāte kṣetraje mṛte bhartari paradāreṣu jātatvasāmyāt golakaśabdaḥ | evamuktakuṇḍagolakayor brāhmaṇatvena śrāddhe prāptisambhavāt pratiṣedho 'rthavān | evaṃ tarhi pūrvokte "pāradāryam adharmyaṃ tu" ityādibārhaspatyavacane "kṣetrajādyās tathā sutāḥ" ity anenaiva kṣetrajaputrapratiṣedhasya siddhatvāt "kuṇḍagolakāv aśrāddheyau" ity etan mukhyakuṇḍagolakapratiṣedhārtham ity avaśyaṃ vaktavyam | tac cāyuktam, mukhyakuṇḍagolakayor abhrāhmaṇatvena śūdravad aprāpteḥ pratiṣedhānarthakyāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> — kuṇḍagolakayor jātyantaratvena vyavahārābhāvāt brāhmaṇyāṃ brāhmaṇotpāditatvamātreṇa brāhmaṇo 'yam iti śrāddhādau svīkāro bhavati | tena mandānugrahārthaṃ paramārthato 'prāptayor api tayoḥ pratiṣedho bṛhaspatinā kṛta ity alaṃ kuṇḍagolakapratiṣedhaprayojanasamarthanaprapañcena ||

	akāraṇaparityaktety asyāyam arthaḥ | "tyajet pitaraṃ rājaghātakam" ityādiśāstroktatyāgakāraṇe 'vidyamāne 'pi mātāpitaror guror vā parityakteti | gurur atrācāryo na pitā, tasya svaśabdenaivopāttatvāt | tyāgo "jīvator vākyakaraṇam" ityādiśāstroktaśuśrūṣādyakaraṇam |

	brāhmair yaunaiś ca saṃbandhaiḥ saṃyogaṃ patitair gataḥ |

iti pratiṣedho vyarthaḥ, "ye stenapatitāḥ klībāḥ" ity atra patitagrahaṇena pañcavidhapatitapratiṣedhasya prāg eva kṛtatvāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span>, brāhmair yaunaiś ca saṃbandhaiḥ saṃyogam upapātakibhir yo gatas tasyāgatyā kadācid bhojanīyatvāṅgīkārārtho 'yaṃ punaḥ pratiṣedha iti na vyarthaḥ | saṃgrahakāras tu pañcavidhapatitavyatiriktapatitapratiṣedhakatayā ślokārtham uktvā, vaiyarthyaṃ parihṛtavān |

	brāhmair yaunaiś ca saṃbandhaiḥ saṃbaddhā brahmahādibhiḥ |

	sadyo ye patitās tair saṃyogaṃ patitair gataḥ ||

	patitaḥ sa niṣiddhatvāt tṛtīyo 'tra niṣidhyate || iti |

brahmahādisaṃbandhāt sadyo ye patitāḥ taiḥ patitair yaḥ saṃyogaṃ gataḥ so 'tra tṛtīyaḥ pratiṣidhyate | "tatsaṃyogī ca pañcamaḥ" ity uktasya patitasya prāg eva niṣiddhatvāt ity arthaḥ | agāradāhī tu dvidhā devalena darśitaḥ |

	agāradāhī sa jñeyaḥ pretadagdhā dhanena yaḥ |

	sa cāpy agāradāhī syād dveṣād yo veśmadāhakaḥ || iti |

kuṇḍāśī kuṇḍagolakayor annabhoktā | tathā ca kuṇḍagolakāv abhidhāya manunaivābhihitam |

	yas tayor annam aśnāti sa kuṇḍāśy ucyate dvijaḥ | iti |

somavikrayī somalatāyā vikretā | samudrayāyī vahitram āruhyeti śeṣaḥ | bandī nṛpādistutipāṭhakaḥ | tailakaḥ tailavṛttyupajīvī | kūṭakārakaḥ kūṭasya aparamārthasyālekhyādeḥ kārakaḥ | pitrā vivadamānaḥ smṛtyācāravyapetamārgeṇa pitrā saha vipratipadyamānaḥ | kekaro 'rdhadṛṣṭiḥ | madyapaḥ surāvyatiriktamadyapaḥ | surāpasya patitapadena prāg eva pratiṣedhāt | pāparogī "unmādas tvagdoṣo rājayakṣmā śvāso madhumedho bhagaṃdaro mahodaram aśmarīty aṣṭau pāparogāḥ" iti devaloktapāparogeṣv anyatamarogavān | abhiśastaḥ doṣakāritayā kenacit sabhāyām āveditaḥ | dāmbhikaḥ darmācaraṇe śāṭhyavān | rasavikrayī kṣārādirasavikrayī | dhanuḥśarāṇāṃ kartā dhanuṣaḥ śarāṇāṃ ca kartā | agredidhiṣūpatiḥ agredidhiṣvāḥ patiḥ | kā punaḥ agredidhiṣūr ity apekṣite devalaḥ |

	jyeṣṭhāyāṃ yady anūḍhāyāṃ kanyāyām uhyate 'nujā |

	sā cāgredidhiṣūr jñeyā pūrvā tu didhiṣūr matā || iti |

mitradhruk mitradrohī | dyūtavṛttiḥ dyūtajīvanaḥ | putrācāryo nāma grāmagatagṛhasthakumārāṇām akṣaraśikṣakaḥ | tathā ca saṃgrahakāraḥ |

	putrācāryaḥ sa vijñeyo grāme yo 'kṣarapāṭhakaḥ | iti |

atha vā putra evācāryo yasya sa putrācāryaḥ | tathā ca sa eva |

	putrād avāptavidyo vā putrācāryo nigadyate | iti |

bhrāmarī bhramaravad vṛttyartham evārthārjakaḥ | tathā ca sa eva |

	yaḥ poṣayati vṛttyarthaṃ vibhavān bhrāmarī tu saḥ | iti |

gaṇḍamālī gaṇḍamālākhyarogavān | śvitrī kuṣṭhavyādhinā śvetatvak | piśunaḥ svabhāvato vṛttyarthaṃ vā paradoṣasūcakaḥ | unmattādayaḥ prasiddhāḥ |pakṣiṇāṃ poṣakaḥ baddhānāṃ krīḍārthaṃ poṣayitā |yuddhācāryo dhanurvedopādhyāyaḥ | srotasāṃ bhedakaḥ pravāhasya digantare netā, teṣāṃ cāvaraṇe āvaraṇe  rataḥ āvaraṇe gatipratibandhārthaṃ mṛdādinā mārganirodhane rataḥ | gṛhasaṃveśakaḥ vardhakivṛttyā vartamānaḥ | dūtaḥ sandeśaharaḥ | vṛkṣāropakaḥ mūlyaṃ gṛhītveti śeṣaḥ | "pañcāmravāpī narakaṃ na yāti" ityādiśāstreṇa dharmārthaṃ vṛkṣāropaṇavidhānāt | "śvakrīḍī" ityādayo nigadavyākhyātāḥ | vṛṣalas tu svenaiva manunā nirūpitaḥ |

	vṛṣo hi bhagavān dharmaḥ tasya yaḥ kurute 'tyayam |

	vṛṣalaṃ taṃ vidur devās tasmād dharmaṃ na lopayet || iti |

alaṃ nivāraṇam | evaṃ ca vyavahāradraṣṭṛṣu yo dharmavādhanaṃ (?) kurute sa vṛṣalaḥ | tatputro vṛṣalaputraḥ | sa ca brāhmaṇa eveti nāyam aprāptapratiṣedha iti mantavyam | gaṇānāṃ yājakaḥ anekayajamānakāhīnadvādaśāhādiyajñayājakaḥ | tathā ca smṛtiḥ: "tasmād dvādaśāhena na yājyaṃ pāpmano vyāvṛttyai" iti | evaṃ ca "yājayanti ca ye pūgān" ity anena sahāsyāpaunarukthyaṃ siddham | ācārahīno durācāraḥ | klībo 'nutsāhī samartho 'pi svāśramadharmānuṣṭhānarahita ity arthaḥ | evaṃ ca "ye stenapatitaklībāḥ" ity anena apaunaruktyaṃ sphuṭam | nityaṃ yācanakaḥ saty api vibhave yācakaḥ | ślīpadī ślīpadākhyarogavān, ucchūnapada iti yāvat | urabhrāḥ avayaḥ tā eva jīvikārthaṃ pālyāḥ yasyāsāv aurabhrakaḥ | evaṃ sāhiṣakaḥ | atha vā vyabhicāriṇīsuto sāhiṣakaḥ | yad āha devalaḥ |

	mahiṣīty ucyate bhāryā yā caiva vyabhicāriṇī |

	tasyāṃ yo jāyate garbhaḥ sa vai māhiṣakaḥ smṛtaḥ || iti |

tasyāṃ yaḥ svabhartur jāyate putraḥ sa sāhiṣakaḥ smṛta ity arthaḥ | pūrvam anyasmai dattā parapūrvā tasyāḥ patiḥ parapūrvāpatiḥ | pretaniryātako mūlyena pretanirhārakaḥ | dharmārthaṃ tu praśasta eva | kasmād vacanād etad avagatam ity apekṣite saṃgrahakāraḥ |

	etān vigarhitācārān ity asmād avagamyate |

	dharmārthaṃ pretaniryāṇam adṛṣṭaṃ vṛkṣaropaṇam || iti |

etān stenapatitaklībādipretaniryātakaparyantān ubhayatra daive pitrye vety arthaḥ | brahmapurāṇe 'pi varjyā brāhmaṇā uktāḥ |

	bhoktuṃ śrāddheṣu nārhanti daivopahatacetasaḥ |

	ṣaṇḍo mūkaś ca kunakhī khalvāṭo dantarogavān ||

	śyāvadantaḥ pūtināsaḥ chinnāṅgaś cādhikāṅguliḥ |

	galarogī ca gaḍumān sphuṭitāṅgaś ca sajvaraḥ ||

	khañjatūparamandāś ca tathānye dīrgharogiṇaḥ || iti |

gaḍumān vātavaśād urasi pṛṣṭhe ca unnatāsthisaṃsthānānvitaḥ | khañjaḥ bhagnacaraṇaḥ | tūparo yauvanakāle śmaśruvihīnaḥ | mandaḥ alasaḥ | yamo 'pi |

	na kharair upayātasya na raktolbaṇavāsasaḥ |

	dvyaṅgulātītakarṇasya bhuñjate pitaro haviḥ ||

karṇavedhasthāne tālapatrādipraveśenābhivardhanaṃ dvyaṅgulādhikaṃ niṣiddham | tena dvyaṅgulātītakarṇo 'py anarhaḥ | śaṅkho 'pi |

	anadhyāyeṣv adhīyānāḥ śaucācāravivarjitāḥ |

	śūdrānnaparipuṣṭāṅgāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ paṅktidūṣakāḥ ||

śātātapo 'pi |

	agniṣṭomādibhir yajñair ye yajanty alpadakṣiṇaiḥ |

	teṣām annaṃ na bhoktavyam apāṅkteyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ||

	pracaranti ca ye mūḍhās taṃ kratuṃ hīnadakṣiṇam |

	te mṛtā narakaṃ yānti pūyaśoṇitakardamam ||

alpadakṣiṇaiḥ "saptaikaviṃśatiṣaṣṭtiśatadvādaśasahasram" ityādi sūtroktagosaṅkhyāvikalpeṣu vittaśāṭhyena svīkṛtālpasaṅkhyākadakṣiṇair ity arthaḥ | āpastambo 'pi |

	nīlīkarṣaṇakārī tu nīlavastropadhārakaḥ |

	kiṃcit tasya na dātavyaṃ caṇḍālasadṛśo hi saḥ ||

nīlīsaṃsargajadoṣavān varjya ity arthaḥ | marīcir api varjyam āha: "vaidhavyo vidhavāpatiḥ" iti | śrāddhānarha iti śeṣaḥ | vaidhavyaḥ vaidhaveyaḥ | punaḥ pariṇītavidhavāputra iti yāvat | vidhavāpatiḥ vidhavāyāḥ punaḥpariṇītāyāḥ patiḥ | devalo 'pi |

	cāturāśramyabāhyebhyo dattaṃ bhavati niṣphalam | iti |

purāṇe 'pi |

	catvāras tv āśramāḥ pūjyā daive śrāddhe ca sarvadā |

	cāturāśramyabāhyebhyaḥ śrāddhaṃ naiva pradāpayet ||

	anāśramī tapas tepe yas tu taṃ na nimantrayet |

	pravṛttā vā nivṛttā vānāśramāḥ paṅktidūṣakāḥ ||

manus tu paṅktidūṣakān āha |

	vikṣyāndho navateḥ kāṇaḥ ṣaṣṭeḥ śvitrī śatasya ca |

	pāparogī sahasrasya dātur nāśayate phalam ||

	yāvataḥ saṃspṛśed aṅge brāhmaṇān śūdrayājakaḥ |

	tāvatāṃ na bhaved dātuḥ phalaṃ dānasya paurthikam ||

andhasya darśanābhāvena paṅktigatatvamātreṇa navatināśakatvam, na tu vīkṣaṇena | saṃspṛśed ity anenaikapaṅktigatatvaṃ lakṣyate | mukhyārthasvīkāre sparśanābhāve paṅktidūṣakatābhāvaḥ syāt | sa cāyuktaḥ | śūdrayājakaḥ sthapatīṣṭyām ṛtvik, svavṛttyarthaṃ pratārya śūdrārthaṃ pākayajñādikartā vā | yadi punar ajñānād agatyā vā paṅktidūṣakaparigrahaḥ kriyate tadā tv āha manuḥ |

	apāṅkteyahatā paṅktiḥ pāvyate yair dvijātibhiḥ |

	tān nibodhata kārtsnyena dvijāgryān paṅktipāvanān ||

	agryā vedeṣu sarveṣu sarvapravacaneṣu ca |

	śrotriyānvayajāś caiva vijñeyā paṅktipāvanāḥ ||

	triṇāciketaḥ pañcāgnis trisuparṇaḥ ṣaḍaṅgavit |

	brahmadeyānusaṃtānaś chandogī jyeṣṭhasāmagaḥ ||

	vedārthavit pravaktā ca brahmacārī sahasradaḥ |

	śatāyur caiva vijñeyā brāhmaṇāḥ paṅktipāvanāḥ ||

brahmadeyānusaṃtāno brāhmavivāhoḍhāyāḥ putraḥ | paṅktipāvanāḥ paṅktyupaviṣṭakāṇādinibandhanadoṣāpanodakāḥ | tena vaiśvadevārtham aparīkṣya svīkṛtā vāpatsv agatyā svīkṛtāḥ kāṇādayaḥ sarvavedāgryādibhiḥ paṅktivāvanair miśritā yathā bhavanti tathā niyoktavyā ity abhiprāyaḥ | ata eva sumantuḥ |

	kāṇāḥ kubjāś ca khañjāś cāpy acarmāṇaḥ kacair vinā |

	sarve śrāddhe niyoktavyā miśritā vedapāragaiḥ ||

acarmāṇaḥ śipiviṣṭāḥ | kacair vinā khalvāṭa ity arthaḥ | saṃgrahakāras tu miśraṇe niṣedham āha |

	kāṇādīn bhojayed daive śrāddhe dāne tu varjayet | iti |

śrāddhe dāne śrāddhadāna ity arthaḥ | paiṭhīnasir api paṅktipāvanān āha: "athātaḥ paṅktipāvanā bhavanti triṇāciketaḥ trimadhuḥ trisuparṇaḥ cīrṇavrataś chandogo jyeṣṭhasāmago brahmadeyānusaṃtānaḥ sahasrado rudrādhyāyī cuturvedaḥ ṣaḍaṅgavid atharvaśiro 'dhyāyī pañcāgnir vedajāpī ceti paṅktipāvanāḥ | teṣām ekaikaḥ punāti niyuktaḥ paṅktimūrdhani sahasrair apy upasevitām" iti ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ varjanīyabrāhmaṇanirūpaṇam**

**atha śrāddhadināt prācīnadinakṛtyam**

tatra varāhapurāṇam |

	vastraśaucādi kartavyaṃ śvaḥ kartāsmīti jānatā |

	sthānopalepanaṃ bhūmiṃ kṛtvā viprān nimantrayet ||

	dantakāṣṭhāni visṛjet brahmacārī śucir bhavet ||

śrāddhabhūmiṃ parigṛhya parigṛhītasthānopalepanaṃ kṛtvā vastraśuddhyādikam ahni kartavyam | rātrau tu viprān nimantrayet | devapitṛkāryasaṃpattyartham apratyākhyeyena niyogenopakalpayed ity arthaḥ | apratyākhyeyo niyogo nimantraṇam iti gīyate | madālasāvākyam api |

	nimantrayīta pūrvedyuḥ pūrvoktān dvijasattamān |

	daive niyoge pitrye ca tāṃs tathaivopakalpayet ||

tathaiva daive niyoge yūyam, pitrye niyoge yūyam iti viśeṣanirdhāraṇayaivety arthaḥ | devalo 'pi |

	śvaḥ kartāsmīti niścitya dātā viprān nimantrayet |

	nirāmiṣaṃ sakṛd bhuktvā bhukte sarvajane gṛhe ||

svagṛhe yaj janajātam asti tasmin sarvasmin bhuktavati sati paścān nimantrayed ity arthaḥ | yamo 'pi |

	jātikriyāvabodhādyair yuktān dāntān alolupān |

	prārthayīta pradoṣānte bhuktān aśayitān dvijān ||

avabodho vedārthāder avagatiḥ | aśayitān akṛtaśayanakriyān | prārthanā ca kathaṃ kartavyety apekṣite pracetāḥ |

	kṛtāpasavyaḥ pūrvedyuḥ pitṝn pūrvaṃ nimantrayet |

	bhavadbhiḥ pitṛkāryaṃ naḥ saṃpādyaṃ ca prasīdata ||

	savyena vaiśvadevārthaṃ praṇipatya nimantrayet ||

kṛtāpasavyaḥ prācīnāvītī bhūtvā naḥ asmakaṃ śvaḥ pitṛkāryaṃ bhaviṣyati tad bhavadbhiḥ āhavanīyakāryakaratvenānugṛhya saṃpādyam, tataś cāhavanīyarthaṃ prasīdatety evaṃ nimantrayed ity arthaḥ | savyena svyāṃsasthayajñopavītenānvitaḥ | praṇipatya nimantraṇaṃ śūdrakartṛkaśrāddhaviṣayam, (?)

	dakṣiṇaṃ caraṇaṃ vipraḥ savyaṃ vai kṣatriyas tathā |

	pāvāv ādāya vaiśyo dvau śūdraḥ praṇatipūrvakam ||

	nimantrayīta pūrvedyuḥ .................. ||

iti purāṇasmaraṇāt | dakṣiṇacaraṇagrahaṇe tu pradeśaviśeṣo mātsye darśitaḥ |

	dakṣiṇaṃ jānum ālabhya tvaṃ mayā tu nimantritaḥ | iti |

brūyād iti śeṣaḥ | "pitṝn pūrvaṃ nimantrayet" iti niyamārtham | 

	daive niyoge pitrye ca tāṃs tathaivopakalpayet |

iti daivapūrvakanimantraṇasyāpi madālasāvākyena smṛtatvāt,

	upavītī tato bhūtvā devatārthaṃ dvijottamān |

	apasavyena pitrye tu svayaṃ śiṣyo 'tha vā sutaḥ ||

iti bṛhaspatismaraṇāc ca | nimantraṇaṃ prāk kartavyam | tad āha paiṭhīnasiḥ: "śvaḥ śrāddhaṃ kariṣyāmīti saṃkalpya brāhmaṇān sapta pañca vā śrotriyān nimantrayet" iti | sapta pañca veti paitṛkavaiśvadevabrāhmaṇānāṃ militānāṃ saṅkhyā, asyaiva vākyasyāntyabhāge "prāṅmukhān vaiśvadevān upaveśayet pitṝn dakṣiṇapūrveṇa" ity abhidhānāt | atra paitṛke vaiśvadeve ca kathaṃ brāhmaṇasaṃkhyayā vibhāga ity apekṣite aṅgirāḥ |

	ayujo bhojayec chrāddhe na samā daivike samāḥ |

"na saṃaḥ" samasaṃkhyākāḥ pitrarthe na grahyā ity arthaḥ | ata eva manuḥ: "dvau daive pitṛkṛtye trīn" iti | etat pañcasaṃkhyāpakṣe draṣṭavyam | saptasaṃkhyāpakṣe tu catvāro daive trayaḥ pitrye iti vibhāga ūhyaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> dvau daive pañca pitrya iti vibhāgaḥ kasmān na bhavati | tathā hi "daive yugmān yathāśakti pitrya ekaikasya" iti kātyāyanena pitrye ekaikasya yathāśakty ayugmān iti vadatā pitṛpitāmahaprapitāmahānāṃ pratyekam ayugmabrāhmaṇakalpanaṃ na punaḥ samudāyasyeti darśitam | tataś ca pañcānām "samaṃ syād aśrutatvāt" iti nyāyena pratyekam ayugmasaṃkhyayā samavibhāga ūhanīyaḥ | na yatheṣṭam | na ca pitrādiṣu triṣu pañcānāṃ samatayā vibhāgaḥ saṃbhavati, saṃbhavati tu trayāṇām | tasmāc catvāro daive, pitrye tu traya ity eva vibhāgaḥ kāryaḥ | pitrarthabrāhmaṇeṣv evādhikasaṃkhyām apy āha śaunakaḥ: "ekaikam ekaikasya dvau dvau trīṃs trīn vā" iti | dvau dvau iti vṛddhiśrāddhābhiprāyam | pārvaṇaśrāddhe tu "ayujo bhojayec chrāddhe na samān" iti samasaṃkhyāniṣedhāt | ekaikam ekaikasyeti pakṣe pitṛkṛtye trayo nimantraṇīyāḥ | trīṃs trīn ekaikasyeti pakṣābhiprāyeṇa gautamenāpy uktam: "navāvarān bhojayet" iti | yat tu manunoktam,

	pūrvedyur vā paredyur vā śrāddhakarmaṇy upasthite |

	nimantrayīta tryavarān samyag viprān yathoditān ||

iti, atra pratyekam iti śeṣo draṣṭavyaḥ | tataś ca gautamavacanasamānārthatvān na tenasya virodhaḥ | pratyekam ity adhyāhāraparihārāya pitṛkṛtye tryavarān iti vyākhyāne tu "dvau daive pitṛkṛtye trīn" iti svoktena paunaruktyaṃ prasajyeteti tathā vyākhyānam ayuktam | tryavarān ity abhidhānāt pratyekaṃ pañcasaṃkhyā madhyamaḥ pakṣaḥ, pratyekaṃ saptasaṃkhyā tūttamaḥ pakṣa iti mantavyam | ata eva gautamaḥ: "ayujo vā yathotsāham" iti | pitrādiṣu pratyekaṃ pañcasaṃkhyā saptasaṃkhyā vā yathotsāhaṃ yathāvibhavam ayujo viprān bhojayed ity arthaḥ | evaṃ ca susamṛddhatamasya satkriyādisamarthasya saptabhiḥ saptabhir vipraiḥ pitṛkṛtyaṃ kāryam, susamṛddhatarasya pañcabhiḥ pañcabhir vipraiḥ, susamṛddhasya tibhis tribhiḥ, samṛddhasya tribhir eveti boddhavyam | yat punar manunoktam,

	dvau daive pitṛkṛtye trīn ekaikam ubhayatra vā |

	bhojayet susamṛddho 'pi na prasajyeta vistare ||

	satkriyāṃ deśakalau ca śaucaṃ brāhmaṇasaṃpadam |

	pañcaitān vistaro hanti tasmān neheta vistaram ||

yac ca bṛhaspatinā,

	ekaikam atha vā dvai trīn daive pitrye ca bhojayet |

	satkriyākālapātrādi na saṃpadyeta vistare ||

iti, yad api purāne,

	deśakālabalālābhād ekaikam ubhayatra vā |

	śeṣān vittānusāreṇa bhojayed anyaveśmani ||

	yasmāt brāhmaṇabāhulyāt doṣo bahutaro bhavet |

	śrāddhanāśo maunanāśaḥ śrāddhatantrasya vismṛtiḥ ||

	ucchiṣṭocchiṣṭasaṃsparśo nindā cāpy annabhoktṛṣu |

	vitaṇḍayā parīvādo jalpās te 'pi pṛthagvidhāḥ ||

iti, śeṣān āmantritān atithiprabhṛtīn, tad etat susamṛddhasyāpi yasya brāhmanabāhulye satkriyādisaṃpādanāsāmarthyaṃ tad viṣayam | yasya tu saṃpādanasāmarthyam asti tadviṣayaṃ śaunakādivacanam iti sarvam anavadyam | na cātrānāḍhyatayā vyavasthā saṃbhavati, 

	dvau daive pitṛkṛtye trīn ekaikam ubhayatra vā |

	bhojayet susamṛddho 'pi

iti manunā āḍhyaviṣaye 'py alpasaṃkhyābhidhānāt | yat tu śaṅkhenoktam,

	bhojayed atha vāpy ekaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ paṅktipāvanam |

iti, tad etad anekabrāhmaṇāsyalābhaviṣayam | evaṃ nirūpitasaṃkhyānvitān viprān svagṛha eva sthitān upagamya nivedayet | tathā coktam atriṇā |

	prathame 'hni nivāsasthān śrotriyādīn nimantrayet |

	kathayet tu tadaivaiṣāṃ niyogaṃ pitṛdaivikam ||

	sarvāyāsavinirmuktaiḥ kamakrodhavivarjitaiḥ |

	bhavitavyaṃ bhavadbhir naḥ śvo bhūte śrāddhakarmaṇi || iti |

prathame 'hni pūrvedyur ity arthaḥ | nivāsasthān svakīyanivāsasthitān | mātsye 'pi |

	etān nimantryaniyamān śrāvayet paitṛkān budhaḥ |

	akrodhanaiḥ śaucaparaiḥ satataṃ brahmacāribhiḥ ||

	bhavitavyaṃ bhavadbhiś ca mayāpi śrāddhakāriṇā ||

akrodhanair ityādivacanaṃ paṭhan paitṛkān pitṛkarmāṅgabhūtān nimantritaviprān śrāvayed ity arthaḥ | akrodhādiniyamaḥ śrāddhakartur yathā mamāvaśyakas tathā bhavatām apīti vaktuṃ mayāpi śrāddhakāriṇety aṃśasyāpi pāṭhaḥ | nimantritaviprāṇāṃ kartavyam āha atriḥ |

	te taṃ tathey avighnena gateyaṃ rajanī yadi |

	yathāśrutaṃ pratīkṣetan śrāddhakālam atandritaḥ ||

nimantritā viprās taṃ nimantraṇakartāraṃ "tathāstu yady avighneneyaṃ rajanī gatā" ity uktvā dharmaśāstrādau yathā niyamajātaṃ śrutaṃ tathaiva tan niyamajātaṃ pratīkṣeran pratipālayeyuḥ | śrāddhakālaṃ śvo 'py annapariṇāmaparyantam ity arthaḥ | tathā ca pracetāḥ |

	syād annaparimānāt tu brahmacaryaṃ dvayos tataḥ | iti |

brahmacaryagrahaṇaṃ dvayor nimantritakayor vihitaniyamopalakṣaṇārtham | nirāhāraniyamas tu nimantraṇaprabhṛti śrāddhakarmaparisamāptiparyantam evety āha āpastambaḥ: "ārabdhe cābhojanam ā samāpanāt" iti | yat tu vṛddhamanunoktam,

	nimantrya viprān tad aho varjayen maithunaṃ kṣuram |

	pramattatāṃ (?) ca svādhyāyaṃ krodhāśaucaṃ tathānṛtam ||

iti, tat sadyaḥkālaśrāddhaviṣayam,

	nimantrayīta pūrvedyuḥ tad ahar vā dvijottamān |

iti purāṇe sadyaḥkālapakṣasyāpy uktatvāt | ayaṃ ca sadyaḥkālapakṣaḥ pūrvedyuḥ kathaṃcin nimantraṇāsaṃbhave bhavati,

	asaṃbhave paredyur vā brāhmaṇāṃs tān nimantrayet |

iti devalasmaraṇāt,

	tasmāt tu prathamaṃ kāryaṃ prājñenopanimantraṇam |

	aprāptau taddine vāpi varjyā yoṣitprasaṅginaḥ ||

iti madālasāvākye 'py uktatvāc ca | upanimantraṇaṃ sati saṃbhave pūrvedyuḥ kāryam | tatra kathaṃcid upanimantraṇāprāptau śrāddhadine vā karyam ity arthaḥ | yadā tu taddine nimantraṇaṃ kriyate tadā taddina eva nimantritatvanibandhantvān niyamānuṣṭhānaṃ syāt | nimantraṇaṃ kadācid anyenāpi kārayed ity āha yamaḥ |

	nimantrayīta savyena devatārthaṃ dvijottamān |

	apasavyena pitrye tu svayaṃ śiṣyo 'tha vā sutaḥ || iti |

precatā api |

	savarṇaṃ preṣayed āptaṃ dvijānām upamantraṇe | iti |

eteṣu pakṣeṣu pūrvanyāyaḥ śreyān, sarvābhāve tv asavarṇam api śūdravyatiriktaṃ preṣayet,

	abhojyaṃ brāhmaṇasyānnaṃ vṛṣalena nimantritam |

iti yamena sūdranimantritasyaiva niṣedhasmaraṇāt | viśeṣapratiṣedhasya sāmānyābhyanujñānārthatā prasiddhaiva | evaṃ ca bhojyānnena svayaṃ kṛtaṃ śiṣyakṛtaṃ śūdravyatiriktāsavarṇakṛtaṃ ca nimantraṇam anindyam, tac ca bhoktuṃ samarthānāṃ brāhmaṇānām apratyākhyeyam,

	kāmaṃ pratiśravas teṣām anindyāmantraṇe kṛte |

iti devalasmaraṇāt | anindyāmantraṇe kṛte teṣāṃ nimantritānāṃ kāmam astv iti pratiśravaḥ prativacanaṃ kartavyam ity arthaḥ | kātyāyanenāpy uktam: "anindyenāmantrite nāpakramet śaktena na pratyākhyānaṃ kartavyam" iti | anenārthān nindyāmantraṇe bhoktum asāmarthye ca pratyākhyānaṃ kartavyam eveti gamyate | aṅgīkṛtanimantranasyāṅgīkārāt paścād api bhoktum asāmarthye saty atikramo yukta ity arthāj jñāpayitum āha sa eva: "vidhivat ketanaṃ parigṛhya śaktaḥ saṇ napakramet" iti | ketanaṃ parigṛhya āmantraṇam akgīkṛtyety arthaḥ | yat tu yamenoktam,

	brāhmaṇaṃ tu mukhaṃ kṛtvā devatāḥ pitṛbhiḥ saha |

	tad annaṃ samupāśnanti tasmāt tan na vyatikramet ||

iti, tad anindyāmantritaśaktaviṣayam iti pūrvoktena na virodhaḥ | yas tu nimantritaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ tyajati taṃ praty āha nārāyaṇaḥ |

	ketanaṃ kārayitvā tu nivarayati durmatiḥ |

	brahmahatyām avāpnoti śūdrayonau ca jāyate ||

	etasminn enasi prāpte brāhmaṇo niyataḥ śuciḥ |

	yaticāndrāyaṇaṃ kṛtvā tasmāt pāpāt pramucyate ||

enaḥ pāpam | yaticāndrāyaṇaṃ nāma cāndrāyaṇaviśeṣaḥ | tad etad sṅgīkṛtaketanasya bhojanasamarthasya nivāraṇe sati draṣṭavyam | yas tu nimantraṇam aṅgīkṛtya bhojane samartho 'pi bhojayitāraṃ tyajati taṃ praty āha manuḥ |

	ketitas tu yathānyāyaṃ havyakavye dvijottamaḥ |

	kathaṃcid apy atikrāman pāpaḥ sūkaratāṃ vrajet ||

kathṃcid mṛṣṭānnabahudakṣinālobhādinā, na punaḥ bhojanāsāmarthyenety arthaḥ | tad etad āḍhyavipraviṣayam,

	vidyamānadhano yas tu bhojyānnena nimantritaḥ |

	kathaṃcid apy atikrāman pāpaḥ sūkaratāṃ vrajet ||

iti smṛtyantare vidyamānadhanasya doṣasmaraṇāt | evaṃ ca yad ucyate yamena,

	āmantritas tu yaḥ śrāddhe kurvītānyasya tu kṣaṇam |

	saṃvatsarakṛtaṃ puṇyaṃ tasya naśyati durmateḥ ||

iti, yad api matsyena,

	nimantritās tu guṇinā nirdhanenāpi saddvijāḥ |

	nānyamṛṣṭānnalobhena tam atikramya yānti hi ||

	nimantritās tu yenādau tasmād gṛhṇanti nānyataḥ ||

iti, tato 'nyair api prathamanimantrayitāram anatikramya tata eva grahītavyam ity abhiprāyaḥ, tad etat sarvam āḍhyaviṣayam iti mantavyam | yas tu tasmād gṛhṇan anyasmād api grahītum icchati taṃ pratiṣeddhum āha kātyāyanaḥ: "āmantrito 'nyad annaṃ na pratigṛhṇīyāt" iti | āmantritaḥ pūrvam anyena nimantritas tadīyād annād anyad annaṃ paścān nimantrakasyānnaṃ taṇḍulādirūpakam api na pratigṛhṇīyad ity arthaḥ | yaḥ punaḥ pratigṛhṇāti tasya doṣam āha devalaḥ |

	pūrvaṃ nimantrito 'nyena kuryād anyapratigraham |

	bhuktāhāro 'tha vā bhuṅkte sukṛtaṃ tasya naśyati ||

yas tv āmantrita āhūto 'py anāgamanena kutapādiśrāddhakalātipattiṃ karoti, tasya doṣa ādipurāṇe darśitaḥ |

	āmantritaś ciraṃ naiva kuryād vipraḥ kadācana |

	devatānāṃ pitṝṇāṃ ca datur annasya caiva hi ||

	cirakālī bhaved drohī pacyate narakāgninā || iti |

yas tu nimantrito vā śrāddhakartā vā brahmacaryaṃ na karoti, tasya doṣam āha manuḥ |

	ṛtukāle niyukto vā naiva gacchet striyaṃ kvacit |

	tato gacchann avapnoti hy aniṣṭaṃ phalam eva tu ||

ṛtukāla iti vadan svabhāryāgamane 'pi doṣa ity āha | niyukta iti vadan rāgataḥ pravṛttibhāve 'pi doṣa ity āha | gautamas tu śrāddhakartur vṛṣalīgamane doṣādhikyam āha: "sadyaḥ śrāddhī śūdrātalpagas tatpurīṣe māsaṃ nayate pitṝn" iti | śrāddhaṃ kariṣyamāṇaṃ krtaṃ ca vidyate yaseti śrāddhī dātā | sadyaḥ tatkṣaṇam ārabhya māsaṃ nayatīty arthaḥ | manus tv āmantritasya śūdrātalpagamane doṣam āha |

	āmantritas tu yaḥ śrāddhe vṛṣalyā saha modate |

	dāturyad duṣkṛtaṃ kiṃcit tat sarvam atipadyate ||

yamas tv atra doṣāntaram āha |

	āmantritas tu yaḥ srāddhe vṛṣalyā saha modate |

	bhramanti pitaras tasya tan māsaṃ śuklabojanāḥ ||

niyamāntarāṇām atikrame 'pi sa eva doṣam āha |

	āmantritas tu yaḥ srāddhe adhvānaṃ pratipadyate |

	bhavanti pitaras tasya tanmāsaṃ pāṃsubhojanāḥ ||

	āmantritas tu yaḥ śrāddhe kalahaṃ kurute naraḥ |

	bhavanti pitaras tasya tanmāsaṃ tv aśrubhojanāḥ ||

	āmantritas tu yaḥ śrāddhe bhāram udvahate dvijaḥ |

	bhavanti pitaras tasya tanmāsaṃ svedabhojanāḥ ||

	āmantritas tu yaḥ śrāddhe hiṃśāṃ vā kurute dvijaḥ |

	tanmāsaṃ pitaras tasya bhaveyū raktabhojanāḥ ||

	āmantritas tu yaḥ śrāddhe āyāsaṃ kurute dvijaḥ |

	bhavanti pitaras tasya tanmāsaṃ pittabhojanāḥ || iti |

uśanā api |

	āmantritas tu yaḥ śraddhe dyūtaṃ saṃsevate dvijaḥ |

	bhavanti pitaras tasya tanmasaṃ malabhojanāḥ || iti |

evam uktadoṣaparihārāya brahmacaryādiniyameṣv avahitās tiṣṭheyur ity āha yamaḥ |

	āmantritās tu ye viprāḥ śraddhakāla upasthite |

	vaseyur niyatāhārā brahmacaryaparāyaṇāḥ ||

	ahiṃsā satyam akrodho 'dūrād āgamanakriyā |

	abhārodvahanaṃ kṣāntiḥ śrāddhasyaupaśamo vidhiḥ || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ śrāddhadināt prāgdinakṛtyam**

**atha śrāddhadinapūrvāhaṇkṛtyam**

tatra pracetāḥ |

	śrāddhabhuk prātar utthāya prakuryād dantadhāvanam |

	śrāddhakartā na kurvīta dantānāṃ dhāvanaṃ budhaḥ ||

kiṃ tarhi śrāddhakartā kuryād ity apekṣite devalaḥ |

	tathaiva yantrito dātā prātaḥ snātvā sahāmbaraḥ |

	ārabheta navaiḥ pātrair annārambhaṃ ca bāndhavaiḥ ||

tathaiva śrāddhakartuḥ uktaniyamānatikrameṇaiva yantrito niyataḥ annārambhaṃ śrāddhārthānnapākārambham ārabheta kuryād ity arthaḥ | navaiḥ pātraiḥ anupahataiḥ pākopayogibhir bhāṇḍaiḥ bāndhavaiḥ pākopayogibhir bhāṇḍaiḥ bāndhavaiḥ pākopayogibhir upetaḥ dātā śrāddhādikārī | pāke śrāddhādhikāriṇā yat prathamaṃ kartavyaṃ tad āha uśanāḥ: "gomayodakair bhūmibhājanabhāṇḍaśaucaṃ kuryāt" iti | gomayānulepanena mahānasabhūmiśuddhiṃ kuryāt | udakair abhyukṣaṇāharaṇaprakaraṇoktaprakāreṇāhūtaiḥ bhājanānāṃ gaudhūmapiṣṭādiprakṣepaṇārthānāṃ śuddhiṃ kuryād ity arthaḥ | mahānasabhūmisaṃskārānantaram āha devalaḥ |

	tilān avakiret tatra sarvato bandhayed ajam |

	asuropahataṃ sarvaṃ tilaiḥ śuddhyaty ajena ca ||

pākasthānabhājanabhāṇḍaśuddhyanantaraṃ pākādinānnādikaṃ niṣpādayet | tathā ca sa eva |

	tato 'nnaṃ bahusaṃskāraiḥ naikavyañjanabhakṣyavat |

	coṣyapeyasamṛddhaṃ ca yathāśakty upakalpayet ||

bahusaṃskāro rājabhojyānne yo yaḥ saṃskāraḥ tena tenānvitam | naikavyañjanabhakṣyavat anekavyañjanabhakṣyopetam | vyajyate 'nenānnasya rasa iti vyañjanam atra sūpaśārādikam | yasya rasāṃśa eva sevyo na dravyāṃśaḥ ikṣukhaṇḍādi tac coṣyam | pānārthaṃ cāpakvaphalarasādau guḍādipiṣṭaṃ saṃsṛjya yat kriyate tat peyam | coṣyapeyayor anekavidhayor aniṣiddhayoḥ saṃbhavāc coṣyapeyasamṛddham ity uktam | caśabdāl lehyasamṛddhaṃ cety avagantavyam | annādikaṃ vihitavrīhyādiprakṛti | kāni dravyāṇi vihitānīty apekṣite pracetāḥ |

	kṛṣṇam āpās tilāś caiva śreṣṭhāḥ syur yavaśālayaḥ |

	mahāyavā vrīhiyavās tathaiva ca madhūlikāḥ ||

	kṛṣṇāḥ śvetāś ca grāhyāḥ syuḥ śrāddhakarmaṇi ||

yavāḥ sphītaśūkāḥ | śālayaḥ kalamāḥ | rājaśālimahāśālisugandhikādayo jalajāḥ | mahāyavā vrīhiyavāś ca yavaviśeṣāḥ | madhūlikākhyaṃ dhānyāntaram | kṛṣṇāḥ sthalajāḥ kṛṣṇavarṇā vrīhayaḥ | śvetāḥ sthalajā mahāvrīhayaḥ | lohāḥ jalajā raktaśālayaḥ, sthalajāḥ ṣāṣṭikāś ca | atrir api |

	agodhūmaṃ ca yac chrāddhaṃ kṛtam apy akṛtaṃ bhavet |

	vinā māṃsena yac chrāddhaṃ kṛtam apy akṛtaṃ bhavet ||

	kravyādāḥ pitaro yasmād abhāve pāyasādinaḥ || iti |

anena godhūmaprakṛtidravyam apūpādi bhakṣyaṃ māṃsamayaṃ ca bhakṣyam avaśyam upakalpanīyam iti vacobhaṅgyā darśitam | tatra māṃsabhakṣyopakalpanaprakāram āha kātyāyanaḥ: "chāgosrameṣān ālabhya śeṣān krītvā labdhvā vā svayaṃmṛtānāṃ vāhṛtya pacet" iti | usrā gauḥ | ālabhya saṃjñapanaṃ kṛtvety arthaḥ | etac ca kaliyugavyatiriktadvāparādiyugaviṣayam | tathā ca kaliyugadharmaprakaraṇe,

	varātithipitṛbhyaś ca paśūpakaraṇakriyā |

ityādivacane śrāddhādyarthaṃ gavādipaśvālambhananiṣedho 'smābhiḥ pradarśitaḥ | kaliguye krayādināpy āsādya gomāṃsaṃ na pacet, lokavidviṣṭatvāt | anyāny api krītvā yathā kathaṃcil labdhvā vā upakalpyāni vāyupurāṇe darśitāni |

	bilvāmalakamṛdvīkāḥ panasāmrātadāḍimam |

	cavyapāleyakākṣoṭakharjūrāṇāṃ phalāni ca ||

	kaśeruḥ kovidāraś ca tālakandas tathā viśam |

	kāleyaṃ kālaśākaṃ ca suniṣaṇṇaṃ suvarcalā ||

	karduraḥ koṅkaṇī drākṣā likucaṃ mocam eva ca |

	karkandhūḥ grāvakaṃ cāru tindukaṃ madhusāhvayam ||

	vaikaṅkataṃ nālikeraṃ śṛṅgāṭakavarūṣakam |

	pippalaṃ maricaṃ caiva paṭolaṃ bṛhatīphalam ||

	sugandhi matsyamāṃsaṃ ca prakalpyāḥ sarva eva ca |

	evamādīni cānyāni svādūni madhurāṇi ca |

	nāgaraṃ cātra vai deyaṃ dīrghamūlakam eva ca || iti |

mṛdvīkā drākṣā, "mṛdvīkā gostanī drākṣā" ity amarasiṃhenābhidhānāt | āmrātakaṃ cūtavṛkṣasadṛśapītanavṛkṣaḥ, "dvau pītanakapītanau | āmrātakaḥ" iti tenaivābhidhānāt | akṣoṭaḥ girisaṃbandhas taruḥ | kaśeruḥ jalakandaviśeṣaḥ bhadramustākhyaḥ | kāleyaṃ dāruharidrā | suniṣpaṇṇaṃ vitunnakākhyaṃ patraśākam "vitunnaṃ suniṣaṇṇakam" iti śākaprakaraṇe amarasiṃhenābhidhānāt | karduraḥ śrīparṇikākhyo vṛkṣaviśeṣaḥ, "śrīparṇikā kumudikā kumbhīkaiṭaryakaṭphalau" iti tenaivābhidhānāt | koṅkaṇī koṅkaṇadeśaprabhavā drākṣā | likucaṃ jambīraphalatulyakharvaphalavān gulmaviśeṣaḥ | mocaṃ kadalīphalam | karkandhūḥ badarī | tindukaḥ sitasārakākhyavṛkṣaḥ | "tindukaḥ sphūrjakaḥ kālaskandhaś ca sitasārakaḥ" ity amaraḥ | śṛṅgāṭakaṃ jalajatrikāṇḍakam | bṛhatī kaṇṭakādikā | "nidigdhakā spṛśī vyāghrī bṛhatī kaṇṭakārikā" ity amaraḥ | tasyāḥ phalaṃ bṛhatīphalam | śeṣāṇi bilvāmalakapanasadāḍimacavyakharjūratālakandaviśavaikaṅkatanālikerapippalimaricapaṭolāni prasiddhāni | itarāṇy aprasiddhāni | evamādīni evaṃprakārāṇi | nāgaraṃ śuṇṭhī | dīrghamūlā tuṇḍikerī tasyāḥ phalaṃ dīrghamūlakam | etac cāmrātakādikaṃ vihitasaṃskāradravyair eva saṃskāryam | tāni ca ādityapurāṇe darśitāni |

	madhūkaṃ rāmaṭhaṃ caiva karpūraṃ maricaṃ guḍam |

	śrāddhakarmaṇi śastāni saindhavaṃ mānasaṃ tathā ||

brahmāṇḍapurāṇe 'pi |

	saindhavaṃ lavaṇaṃ caiva tathā mānasasaṃbhavam |

	pavitre parame hy ete pratyakṣam api nityaśaḥ ||

evaṃ mṛṣṭānnopakalpanaṃ na śrāddhamātraviṣayam ity āha devalaḥ |

	iṣṭāpūrtamṛtāheṣu darśaśrāddhāṣṭakāsu ca |

	pātrebhyas teṣu kāleṣu deyaṃ naiva kubhojanam ||

caśabdān mahālayādiviśiṣṭakāleṣv api kubhojanaṃ na deyam iti samuccinoti | evaṃ ca nityaśrāddhādau daridrakartṛke kubhojanādyanujñā gamyate | atra yamaḥ |

	bhakṣyaṃ bhojyaṃ tathā peyaṃ yat kiṃcit pacyate gṛhe |

	na bhoktavyaṃ pitṝṇāṃ tad anivedya kathaṃcana ||

pitṝṇām anivedya tasmād annād vaiśvadevādikam api na kāryam | tathā ca paiṭhīnasiḥ |

	pitṛpākaṃ samuddhṛtya vaiśvadevaṃ karoti yaḥ |

	āsuraṃ tad bhavec chrāddhaṃ pitṝṇāṃ nopatiṣṭhati || iti |

yamas tu pakvānnopahatiparihārāya pākasthānādito bahiṣkāryān āha

	madyapaḥ svairiṇī yā ca parapūrvāpatis tathā |

	naiva śrādde 'bhivīkṣetann āvāpāt prabhṛti kvacit ||

āvāpaḥ pākaṃ kartuṃ taṇḍulādīnāṃ piṭharādau prakṣepaḥ, tatprabhṛti bhojananiṣpattiparyantaṃ kvacit pākasthāne bhojanasthāne 'nyatra vā sthitān bhojyapadārthān bhuñjānāṃś ca viprān śrāddhakarmāṇi yathā madyapādayo nābhivīkṣeran tathā te dūrata evāpākaraṇīyā ity arthaḥ | madyapādigrahaṇam apraśastaprāṇitām upalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva manuḥ |

	caṇḍālaś ca varāhaś ca kukkuṭaś ca tathaiva ca |

	rajasvalā ca khañjaś ca nekṣerann aśnato dvijān ||

	home pradāne bhojye ca yad ebhir abhivīkṣitam |

	daive karmaṇi pitrye vā tad gacchati yathātatham || iti |

home agnaukaraṇadeśe | pradāne annatyāgadeśe | bhojye bhojyopakalpanadeśe mahānasādau | caśabdād anyasminn api sthāne yad annādikaṃ caṇḍālādibhir abhivīkṣitaṃ tad yathātathaṃ gacchati asamyag bhavatīty arthaḥ | tasmāc chrāddhadeśād atidūrato 'panetavyā ity abhiprāyaḥ | varāho viḍvarāhaḥ, tasyaivāpraśastatvāt | ata eva uśanasā viśeṣitaḥ: "viḍvarāhakamārjārakukkuṭanakulaśūdrarajasvalāśūdrībhartāraś ca dūrato 'panetavyāḥ" iti | śrāddhakāla iti śeṣaḥ | tathā ca yamaḥ |

	kukkuṭo viḍvarāhaś ca kākaś śvātha biḍālakaḥ |

	vṛṣalīpatiś ca vṛṣalaḥ ṣaṇḍau nārī rajasvalā ||

	ete tu śrāddhakāle vai varjanīyāḥ prayatnataḥ ||

śrāddhakāle pākopakramaprabhṛtīty (?) arthaḥ | tathā ca vyāsaḥ |

	kāṣāyavāsāḥ kuṣṭhī vā patito bhrūṇahāpi vā |

	saṃkīrṇayoniviprasya saṃbandhī patitasya yaḥ ||

	varjanīyā budhair ete nivāpe samupasthite ||

nivāpaḥ pitṛbhyo dānam, "pitṛdānaṃ nivāpaḥ syāt" ity amarasiṃhenābhidhānāt | samupasthitaśabdāt pākopakramaprabhṛti varjanīyāḥ na tu pitṛbhyo dānasamaya eveti gamyate | yamo 'pi puruṣeṣv apaneyān āha |

	khañjaḥ kāṇaḥ kuṇiḥ śvitrī dātuḥ preṣyakaro bhavet |

	nyūnāṅgo vātiriktāṅgas tam apy apanayet tataḥ ||

khañjaḥ pādavikalaḥ | kāṇa ekākṣaḥ | kuṇiḥ ekakaraḥ | svitrī kuṣṭhī | devalo 'pi |

	bībhatsam aśuciṃ nagnaṃ mattaṃ dhūrtaṃ rajasvalām |

	nīlakāṣāyavasanaṃ chinnakarṇaṃ ca varjayet ||

bībhatso jugupsitaḥ | brahmāṇḍapurāṇe 'pi |

	nagnādayo na paśyeyuḥ śrāddham etat kadācana |

	gacchanty etais tu dṛṣṭena pitaro 'dhaḥ pitāmahāḥ ||

śrāddhaṃ śrāddhārtham annādikam | nagno vedaparityāgī | ādiśabdena tatprakāravaidikakarmānuṣṭhānaparityāgino gṛhyante | tathā ca atraivokam |

	sarveṣām eva bhūtānāṃ trayī saṃvaraṇaṃ yataḥ |

	ye vai tyajanti tāṃ mohāt te vai nagnādayaḥ smṛtāḥ ||

trayī vedaḥ, tāṃ te tyajanti te nagnāḥ smṛtāḥ | ye tu tad arthānuṣṭhānatyāginaḥ te nagnādayaḥ smṛtā ity arthaḥ | vāyupurāṇe 'pi |

	vṛthājaṭī vṛthāmuṇḍī vṛthānagnaś ca yo naraḥ |

	mahāpātakino ye ca te vai nagnādayo narāḥ ||

vṛthā vaidikavidhim antareṇety arthaḥ | yadi tu nagnādayaḥ śrāddhārtham annādikaṃ paśyeyus tadā kiṃ kāryam ity apakṣite tatraivoktam |

	annaṃ paśeyur ete tu yadi vā havyakavyayoḥ |

	utsraṣṭavyaṃ pradānārthaṃ saṃskāras tv āpadi smṛtaḥ ||

nagnādibhiḥ dṛṣṭam annam utsraṣṭavyam | āpadi tu tasyaiva nagnādidarśanajanitadoṣāpākaraṇārthaṃ smṛtaḥ saṃskāraḥ | kaḥ punaḥ saṃskāra ity apekṣite brahmapurāṇam |

	haviṣāṃ saṃskṛtānāṃ tu pūrvam evāpavarjanam |

	mṛtsaṃpṛktābhir adbhiś ca prokṣaṇaṃ tu vidhīyate ||

	siddhārthakaiḥ kṛṣṇatilaiḥ kāryaṃ cāpy avakīraṇam |

	gurusūryāgnibastānāṃ darśanaṃ tu prayatnataḥ ||

asyārthaḥ: haviṣāṃ havyakavyānāṃ nagnādidarśane saty apavarjanam eva pūrvaṃ parityāga eva mukhyaḥ kalpaḥ | āpadi tu doṣāpagamahetubhūtasaṃskārasiddhaye praśastamṛttikāsaṃspṛṣṭābhir adbhiḥ prokṣaṇam, tathā gaurasarṣapaiḥ kṛṣṇatilaiś ca avakīraṇaṃ dṛṣṭahavyakavyayor upari kṣepaṇaṃ kāryam | tathā gurusūryāgnicchāgānāṃ darśanaṃ yathānnasya siddhyati tathā prayatnato vyavadhāyakapariśrayaṇāpanodanadvārā kāryam iti | atha vā jamadagninoktām annaśuddhiṃ kuryāt |

	śuddhavatyo 'tha kūśmāṇḍyaḥ pāvamānyas taratsamāḥ |

	pūtena vāriṇā darbhair annadoṣān apānudet ||

śuddhavatyādimantrair abhimantritam udakaṃ darbhair ādāya madyapasvairiṇyādyabhivīkṣaṇaprabhavānnadoṣāpanodārtham avokṣaṇaṃ kuryād ity arthaḥ | "etonvindraṃ stavāma" ityādyā ṛcaḥ śuddhavatyaḥ | "yad devā devahelanam" ityādyāḥ kūśmāṇḍyaḥ | "pavamānaḥ suvarjanaḥ" ityādyāḥ pāvamānyaḥ | "taratsamandī dhāvati" ityādyāḥ taratsamāḥ | yadi tu madyapādidarśanaprabhavam annadoṣaṃ tadapanodakena saṃskāreṇa pūrvoktena vakṣyamāṇena vā mṛdbhasmodakahiraṇyasparśanena vāpanudet tadā srāddhe tad annaṃ bhojyam ity āha sumantuḥ: "caṇḍālādyavekṣitam annam abhojyam anyatra mṛdbhasmahiraṇyodakasparśanāt" iti | mṛdbhasmahiraṇyodakasparśanarūpasaṃskāranirdeśaḥ pūrvoktadviprakārasaṃskārayor api pradarśanārthaḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ śrāddhadinapūrvāhṇakṛtyam**

**atha śrāddhakarmaṇi varjyadravyāṇi**

tatra madālasāvākyam |

	yac cotkocādinā prāptaṃ patitād yad upārjitam |

	anyāyakanyāśulkotthaṃ dravyaṃ cātra vigarhitam ||

	pitrartham eva me yacchety uktvā yac cāpy upārjitam |

	tad varjanīyaṃ vidvadbhiḥ tat tad vai śrāddhakarmaṇi ||

utkocādinā spṛhāhetunā steyādinā | anyāyakanyāśulkaṃ gomithunād adhikakanyāśulkam, tena prāptam anyāyakanyāśulkottham | atra śrāddhakarmaṇi vigarhitaṃ varjyam ity arthaḥ | vyāso 'pi varjyam āha |

	vedavikrayajaṃ neṣṭaṃ striyā yac cārjitaṃ dhanam |

	na deyaṃ pitṛdevebhyo yac ca klībād upārjitam ||

dhānyādiṣv api varjyān āha sa eva |

	aśrāddheyāni dhānyāni kodravāḥ pulkās tathā |

	hiṅgudravyeṣu śākeṣu kālānalaśubhās tathā ||

kodravāḥ koradūṣakāḥ "koradūṣas tu kodravaḥ" ity amarasiṃhenābhidhānāt | pulakā pulākā kodravāpekṣayā svalpadhānyāni "syāt pulākas tucchadhānye" iti tenaivābhidhānāt | evaṃ ca pulakās tatheti vyāsavacane pulakaśabdamadhyākṣare dīrghābhāva (?) ārṣatvān na doṣa iti mantavyam | dravyeṣu śākādisaṃskārārthadravyeṣu hiṅgvākhyaṃ dravyam aśrāddheyam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> hiṅgupratiṣedho na yuktaḥ,

	madhūkaṃ rāmaṭhaṃ caiva karpūraṃ maricaṃ guḍam |

	śrāddhakarmaṇi śastāni saindhavaṃ mānasaṃ tathā ||

ity ādityapurāṇe tasya grāhyatvena smaraṇāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span>, vidhipratiṣedhayoḥ dvayor api darśanād dhiṅguviṣaye vikalpo draṣṭavyaḥ | evam anyatrāpi yatra yatra vidhipratiṣedhāv ekasyaiva dṛśyete tatra vikalpo veditavyaḥ | śākeṣu śākānāṃ madhye kālānalaśubhākhyāḥ śākaviśeṣā aśrāddheyāḥ | tatra kālākhyaḥ śākaviśeṣaḥ kuṭherakākṛtir iti devasvāminā nirūpitaḥ | kuṭherako 'rjakasadṛśaḥ parṇāsaḥ, "atha parṇāse kaṭhiñjarakuṭherakau | site 'rjakotra" ity amarasiṃhenābhidhānāt | evaṃ ca kṛṣṇārjakaḥ kālaśabdenokta iti mantavyam | analaḥ citrakaḥ, "citrako vahnisaṃjñakaḥ" ity amaraḥ | yal loke śubhaṃ śākam iti vyapadiśyate tad evātra śubhaśabdenoktam iti devasvāminābhihitam | bharadvājo 'pi: "mudgāḍhakīmāṣavarjaṃ dvidalāni dadyāt" iti | yāni pāṣāṇayantrabhramaṇena dvidhā prāyaśo bhidyante tāni dhānyāni dvidalāni | āḍhakī śimbīdhānyaviśeṣaḥ tuvarīnāmnā prasiddhaḥ | mudgamāṣāv api śimbīdhānyaviśeṣau mudgamāṣanāmnaiva prasiddhau | māṣaśabdena rājamāṣo gṛhyate, na punaḥ kṛṣṇamāṣaḥ,

	varjyā markaṭakāḥ śrāddhe rājamāṣās tathaiv ca |

iti smṛtyantare viśeṣitatvāt | markaṭakāḥ tṛṇadhānyaviśeṣāḥ | tathā ca tṛṇadhānyaprakaraṇe vaijayantyām uktam: "atha vanyo markaṭakaḥ samau" iti | rājamāṣāḥ prāyeṇa prādeśamātraśimbīyuktāḥ, śuṣkadaśāyā (?) pāṭalavarṇā alasāndranāmnā prasiddhāḥ | ata eva vaijayantyām "alasāndro rājamāṣaḥ" ity uktam | mudgaśabdān nātra kṛṣṇetaramudgo gṛhyate | na punaḥ kṛṣṇamugo 'pi,

	kṛṣṇadhānyāni sarvāṇi varjayec chrāddhakarmaṇi |

	na varjayet tilāṃś caiva mudgān māṣāṃs tathaiva ca ||

iti smṛtyantare kṛṣṇānāṃ tilamudgamāṣāṇāṃ pratiprasavadarsanāt | kṛṣṇadhānyeṣu kulutthādayo 'pi varjyāḥ,

	kodravā rājamāṣāś ca kulutthā varakās tathā |

	niṣpāvāś ca viseṣeṇa pañcaitāṃs tu vivarjayet ||

	yāvanālān api tathā varjayanti vipaścitaḥ ||

iti caturviṃśatimate 'bhidhānāt | kulutthā mudgavat sūpayūṣādyanekopakārakatayā prasiddhāḥ | kṛṣṇā akṛṣṇāś ceti dvividhā api varjyāḥ, kṛṣṇamudgādivat pratiprasavābhāvāt | varakā vanamudgāḥ,

	vanamudge tu varakanigūḍhakulīmakāḥ |

iti vaijayantyām uktatvāt | niṣpāvā api kulutthavat sūpādyanekopakārakatayā śvetaśimbīdhānyatayā ca prasiddhāḥ | ata eva vaijayantyām "niṣpāvaḥ śvetaśimbikā" ity uktam | ayaṃ niṣpāvapratiṣedhaḥ kṛṣṇaniṣpāvaviṣayaḥ,

	kṛṣṇadhānyāni sarvāṇi varjayec chrāddhakarmaṇi |

iti smaraṇāt | evaṃ ca yad uktaṃ mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe,

	yavavrīhī sagodhūmau tilamudgāḥ sasarṣapāḥ |

	priyaṅgavaḥ kovidārā niṣpāvāś cātra śobhanāḥ ||

iti, tat kṛṣṇetaraviṣayam iti mantavyam | yāvanālā vindhyadakṣiṇato māhārāṣṭrādideśe johalāpaparyayaprasiddhāḥ | ata eva vaijayantyām "yāvanālās tu johalāḥ" ity uktam | marīcināpy uktāni varjyāni |

	kulutthāś caṇakāḥ śrāddhe na deyāś caiva kodravāḥ |

	kaṭukāni ca sarvāṇi virasāni tathaiva ca ||

caṇakāḥ aśvānām atyantapriyāḥ pratyantadeśavyatiriktadeśeṣu sarvatra prasiddhāḥ | viṣṇupurāṇe 'pi |

	śrāddhe na deyāḥ pālaṅkyāḥ tathā niṣpāvakodravāḥ |

	masūrakṣāravārtākakulutthāḥ śaṇaśigravaḥ  ||

pālaṅkyā mukundākhyaṃ gandhadravyam, "pālaṅkyā mukundaḥ kundakundarū" ity amarasiṃhena gandhadravyanām anuśāsanaprakaraṇe 'bhidhānāt | masūro 'pi pratyantadeśavyatiriktadeśeṣv atiprasiddho dvidalaviśeṣo maṅgalyakāparaparyāyaḥ | tathā amarasiṃhaḥ: "maṅgalyako masūraḥ" iti | kṣāro yavakṣārādiḥ | vārtākaṃ kṣudravārtākasaṃjñakabṛhatīphalaṃ kaṇṭakārikākhyabṛhatīphalāt kiṃcit sthūlam | śaṇaśabdo dhānyaviśeṣavacanaḥ, "śaṇaḥ saptadalāni dhānyāni" iti dhānyaprabhedeṣv abidhānāt, asya ca svayaṃjātasya sarvadā pratiṣiddhatvāt | atra prāptyasaṃbhave 'pi kṛṣyādijātasya prāptisaṃbhavāt pratiṣedho nānarthakaḥ | śigruḥ dvividhaḥ śvetapuṣpo raktapuṣpaś ca | tatra raktapuṣpasya sarvaniṣiddhatvena prāptyabhāve 'pi śvetapuṣpasya patraśākatvena prāptir astīti pratiṣedho 'rthavān | viṣṇur api varjyān āha: "bhūtṛṇaśigrusarṣapasurasārjakakūṣmāṇḍālābukīvārtāka-pālaṅkyātaṇḍulīyakakusumbamahiṣīkṣirāṇi varjayet" iti | bhūtṛṇaḥ: "chatrāticchatrapālaghnau mālātṛṇakabhūstṛṇau" ity amaraḥ | visargābhāvaḥ chāndasaḥ | yasya nāle granthishāneṣu parimaṇḍalā avaṣṭambhakā bhavanti sa bhūtṛṇākhyaḥ śākaviśeṣaḥ | sarṣapo 'tra rājasarṣapo vivakṣitaḥ, na tu sarṣapamātram "kusumbhaṃ rājasarṣapam" iti smṛtyantare veśeṣapratiṣedhāt, viśeṣapratiṣedhaś ca śeṣābhyanujñānārthaḥ, tataś ca tadavirodhāya tatraiva sāmānyaśabdaḥ paryavasyati | rājasarṣapasurasānirguṇḍīlehyeṣv āmrarasapraveśanāt prāptau pratiṣidhyate | arjakaḥ śvetārjakaḥ | kūśmāṇḍālābukīśabdau prasiddhau | vārtākapālaṅkyāśabdau prāg eva vyākhyātau | taṇḍulīyakaḥ prasiddhaḥ | ata eva amarasiṃhena "taṇḍulīyolpamāriṣaḥ" iti taṇḍulīyakam uddiśyālpamāriṣo 'nuśiṣṭaḥ | kusumbaśabdenātra kaṇṭakīkusumbhasya grahaṇam, akaṇṭakīkusumbhasya sadāpratiṣiddhatvāt | dvividhasyāpi kusumbhasya navapatrāṇi śākatvenopayujyante | tena śākatvena prāptisaṃbhavāt pratiṣedho 'rthavān | matsyo 'pi |

	kusumbhaṃ bījapūraṃ ca kapitthaṃ madhukātasī |

	etāny api na deyāni pitṛbhya prītim icchatā ||

kapitthasya phalatvena prāptisaṃbhavāt pratiṣedhaḥ | madhukaṃ yaṣṭimadhukam asya gandhadravyatayā prāptisaṃbhavāt pratiṣedhaḥ | atasīśākatvena prasiddhaiva | sumantur api: "bījapūramāṣāṃś ca śrāddhe na dadyāt" iti | bījapūrako mātuliṅgakaḥ, "phalapūro bījapuro rucako mātuliṅgakaḥ" ity amaraḥ | māṣāḥ kṛṣṇamāṣavyatiriktāḥ | mārkaṇḍeyo 'pi |

	varjyāś cābhiṣavā nityaṃ śatapuṣpā gavedhukā |

	jambīrajaṃ phalaṃ varjyaṃ kovidāras tu nityaśaḥ |

abhiṣavāḥ klinnāḥ śuktā iti yāvat | śatapuṣpā śākaprakaraṇe amarasiṃhenābhihitā | gavedhukā śāṅkhāratṛṇadhānyasaṃpādikā oṣadhiḥ, tasyā adanīyatvāyogāt tad dhānyaṃ pratiṣidhyate | jambīraphalam ārdrakādiśākasaṃskārakatayā bhakṣyatayā ca pratiṣidhyate | kovidāro yugapatrakavṛkṣaviśeṣaḥ | tasya puṣpaṃ phalaṃ vā kovidāram, tatkomalāvasthaṃ śākatvena prāptaṃ pratiṣidhyate | śāṭyānayo 'pi |

	māriṣaṃ nālikā caiva raktā yā ca kalambakā |

	āsurānnam idaṃ sarvaṃ pitṝṇāṃ nopatiṣṭhate || iti |

māriṣo jīvaśākam "māriṣo jīvaśākaḥ syāt" iti vaijayantyāṃ tac ca kuṇḍalīyakasadṛśaṃ tato 'pi sthūlataram | ata eva vaijayantyām "māriṣo jīvaśākaḥ syāt" ity uktvoktam " atrālpe kuṇḍalīyakaḥ" iti | nālikā dīrghanālā śirasi svalpaphalānvitā | tasyāḥ phalasya nālabhāgasya ca śākatvena prāpte pratiṣedhaḥ | kalambakā jalasaṃbhavā veṇupatrākṛtiḥ pallavānvitā | dvividhā śvetā rakātā ca śākatvena prāptā rakete viśeṣaṇopādānān na śvetāyāḥ pratiṣedhaḥ | smṛtir api |

	gāndhārikāpaṭolāni śrāddhakarmaṇi varjayet | iti |

"gāndhārikā taṇḍulīyakaḥ" iti devasvāminā vyākhyātam | paṭolāni | na tu latā | latāyāḥ pulliṅgatvasyaiva sādhutvāt, ata eva amarasiṃhena latāparyāyeṣu "paṭolaḥ tiktakaḥ paṭuḥ" iti pulliṅgatayā darśitaḥ | hārīto 'pi: "pālaṅkyāpotikānālikākusumbhasurasāniṣpāvacaṇakādi śrāddhe na dadyāt" iti | potikā sutāhvayā, vaijayantyām "potikā tu sutāhvayā" ity abhidhānāt | yasyāḥ patraśākasevā nidrātiśayakāriṇī sā potikā jñeyā | śeṣāṇi prāg vyākhyātāni | śaṅkho 'pi |

	kṛṣṇajājī bidaś caiva śitapākī tathaiva ca |

	varjayel lavaṇaṃ sarvaṃ tathā jambūphalāni ca ||

	avakṣutād abhihataṃ tathā śrāddheṣu varjayet ||

kṛṣṇajājī kṛṣṇajīrakam | bidaḥ bidākhyaṃ lavaṇam | śitapākī tu kīdṛśīti cintyam | lavaṇaṃ kṛtalavaṇam "kṛtaṃ ca lavaṇaṃ sarvaṃ vaṃśāgraṃ ca vivarjayet" iti tenaivābhidhānāt | uśanāpi |

	nālikāśaṇachatrākakusumbhālābuviḍvarān |

	kumbhīkañcukavṛntākakovidārāṃś ca varjayet ||

	varjayed gṛñjanaṃ śrāddhe kāñjikaṃ piṇḍamūlakam |

	karañjaṃ ye 'pi cānye vai rasagandhotkaṭās tathā || iti |

chatrākaṃ śilīndhram "chatrāke tu ślīndhaḥ syāt" iti vaijayantyām | alābūphalasya patrāder api śākatvena prāptatvāt pratiṣedhaḥ | kumbhī śrīparṇikā, kharvakārṣmaryaphalam, "śrīparṇikā kumudikākumbhī kaiṭaryakaṭphalau" ity amarasiṃhenābhidhānāt | vṛntākaṃ bṛhatīsadṛśasthūlodbhidaḥ phalaṃ vṛntabhāgena saha phalaśākatvena prasiddham | kāñjikamāranālakaṃ dhānyāmlam iti yāvat | piṇḍamūlakaṃ cintyam | karañjaṃ ciribilvaphalam "ciribilvo naktamālaḥ karajiś carakañjake" ity amaraḥ | gṛñjanaṃ palāṇḍuviśeṣaḥ | etac ca laśunādīnāṃ daśavidhapalāṇḍuviśeṣāṇām api pradarśanārtham, te ca viśeṣāḥ,

	laśunaṃ dīrghapatraś ca picchagandho mahauṣadham |

	pharaṇḍaś ca palāṇḍuś ca latārkaś ca parārikā ||

	gṛñjanaṃ yavaneṣṭaṃ ca palāṇḍor daśa jātayaḥ |

iti vadan daśavidhāvāntarajātiṣv api palāṇḍuśabdaḥ sāmānyena vartata iti darśayati | ata eva amarasiṃhena "palāṇḍus tu sukandakaḥ" iti sāmānyanāmatayoktam | avāntarajātiveśeṣe 'pi palāṇḍuśabdo vartate "pharaṇḍaś ca palāṇḍuś ca" iti viśeṣyātraiva prayuktatvāt | purāṇe 'pi daśavidhānāṃ pradarśanārthaṃ kecana viśeṣā niṣiddhāḥ |

	laśunaṃ gṛñjanaṃ caiva palāṇḍuḥ piṇḍamūlakam |

	kalambī yāti cānyāni hīnāni rasagandhataḥ ||

	pippalaṃ maricaṃ caiva paṭolaṃ bṛhatīphalam |

	vāṃśaṃ karīraṃ surasasarjakaṃ bhūstṛṇāni ca ||

	avedoktāś ca niryāsā lavaṇāny auparāṇi ca |

	śrāddhakarmaṇi varjyāni yāś ca nāryo rajasvalā || iti |
