haridraktakandaviśeṣo gṛñjanaḥ, "haridrakte tu gṛñjanaḥ" iti vaijayantyām uktatvāt | śvetakandaviśeṣaḥ palāṇḍuḥ, "palāṇḍau tu śvetakando mukundakaḥ" iti tatraivoktatvāt | laśunākhyasya viśeṣasya bhedakadharmo vaidyakādau draṣṭavyaḥ | vāṃśaṃ karīraṃ vaṃāṅkuraḥ | "vaṃśāṅkure karīro 'strī" ity amaraḥ | sarjakaḥ pītasālakaḥ | "atho pītasālake | sarjakāsanabandhūkapuṣpapriyakajīvakāḥ" ity amaraḥ | avedoktaniryāsāḥ vede grāhyatvenoktaniryāsavyatiriktaniryāsāḥ lohitaniryāsāḥ vraścanaprabhavāś ceti yāvat | "atho khalu ya eva lohito yo vāvraścanān niryeṣati tasya nāśyaṃ kāmam anyasya" iti śrutiḥ | lavaṇāny auṣarāṇi ūṣaraprabhavāṇi kṛtalavaṇānīti yāvat | yāś ca nāryo rajasvalāḥ | trirātrād ūrdhvam apy anivṛttarajaskāḥ | tāś ca varjyā ity arthaḥ | kṣīraviśeṣā api varjyāḥ purāṇe darśitāḥ |

	āvikaṃ mārgam auṣṭraṃ ca sarvam aikaśaphaṃ ca yat |

	māhiṣaṃ cāmaraṃ caiva payo varjyāni jānatā ||

āvikam avīnāṃ payaḥ | mārgaṃ mṛgīṇāṃ payaḥ | auṣṭram uṣṭrīṇāṃ payaḥ | ekaśaphā baḍavādayaḥ tāsāṃ payaḥ aikaśapham | cāmaraṃ camarīpayaḥ | bharadvājo 'pi |

	naktoddhṛtaṃ tu yat toyaṃ palvalāmbu tathaiva ca |

	svalpāmbu kūśmāṇḍaphalaṃ vajrakandaṃ ca pippalī ||

	taṇḍulīyakaśākaṃ ca māhiṣaṃ ca payo dadhi |

	śimbikāni karīrāṇi kovidāraṃ gavedhukā ||

	kulutthaśaṇajambīrakarambhāni tathaiva ca |

	nīrasāny api sarvāṇi bhakṣyabhojyāni kānicit ||

	etāni naiva deyāni sarvasmin śrāddhakarmaṇi ||

vajrakandaṃ kīdṛśam it cintyam | śimbikāni śimbīdhānyāni caṇakādīni | karambhaḥ dadhimiśrāḥ saktavaḥ | "karambho dadhisaktavaḥ" ity amaraḥ | māhiṣaṃ tu ghṛtaṃ deyam, payo dadhīti viśeṣitatvāt | sarvasmin śrāddhakarmaṇīti vacanāt yady api kūśmāṇḍaphalādīni nityaśrāddhe 'pi na deyānīti pratibhāti, tathāpi pratidinaṃ śrāddhiyānnasaṃpādanasyātiduṣkaratvān nityaśrāddhetarasarvaśrāddhakarmaṇīti vyākhyeyam | ata eva rāmāyaṇe 'bhihitam |

	iṅgudair badarair bilvaiḥ rāmas tarpayate pitṝn |

	yad annaṃ puruṣo bhuṅkte tadannās tasya devatāḥ || iti |

caturviṃśatimate 'pi |

	yāvanālān api tathā varjayanti vipaścitaḥ |

	tailam apy āpadi prājñāḥ saṃprayacchanti yājñikāḥ ||

	kandamūlaphalālābhe evam āhur manīṣiṇaḥ ||

tailam ity atrāpi varjayantīti saṃbadhyate | yāvanālatailādiniṣiddham api aniṣiddhakandamūlaphalālābhe yājñikāḥ prayacchantīty evaṃ manīṣiṇa āhur ity arthaḥ | kandamūlaphalalābhe tu yāvanālādikaṃ na deyam iti vyatirekād gamyate | mṛṣṭānnalābhe tu sutarāṃ na deyam iti daṇḍāpūpanayād (?) gamyate | smṛtyantare tu varjyam uktam |

	atiśuktogralavaṇaṃ virasaṃ bhāvadūṣitam |

	rājasaṃ tāmasaṃ caiva havyakavyeṣu varjayet ||

atiśuktam atyarthaṃ svābhāvikarasatyāgena kālavaśāt kutsitarasāntarāpannam | ugralavaṇaṃ lavaṇādhikyenāsahyam | purāṇe 'pi |

	āsanārūḍham annādyaṃ pādopahatam eva ca |

	amedhyā āgataiḥ spṛṣṭaṃ śuktaṃ paryuṣitaṃ ca yat ||

	dviḥ svinnaṃ paridagdhaṃ ca tathaivāgrāvalehitam |

	śarkarākīṭapāṣāṇaiḥ keśair yac cāpy upadrutam ||

	piṇyākaṃ mathitaṃ caiva tathātilavaṇaṃ ca yat |

	siddhāḥ kṛtāś ca ye bhakṣyāḥ pratyakṣalavaṇīkṛtāḥ ||

	vāgbhāvaduṣṭāś ca tathā duṣṭaiś copahatās tathā |

	vāsasā cāvadhūtāni varjyāni śrāddhakarmaṇi || iti |

yad annam avaśrayanāntayā pacikriyayā siddhaṃ sanmārdavārthaṃ punar udakaṃ ninīyāvaśrayaṇāntam eva punar auṣṇyanirvāhārtham agnāv adhiśriyate | "atyuṣṇaṃ sarvam annaṃ syāt" iti pacanād auṣṇyārthaṃ punar adhiśrayaṇābhyanujñānāt | yasya tu prathamapākena bhakṣaṇayogyataiva na bhavati tatra pūrvapākasyānivṛttatvāt punar udakaṃ ninīya pāke 'pi śrāddhe nityabhojanādau ca nāsti pratiṣedhaḥ | yatra bhakṣyaviśeṣasiddhyartham udakādinā pūrvaṃ paktvā tailādinā pākaḥ kriyate tatrāpi na dviḥ svinnatā, viśiṣṭabhakṣyasiddhiphalakapacikriyāyā udake taile ca kriyāyā ekatvāt | paridagdham atidagdham | agrāvalehitaṃ yad artham utpāditaṃ tannivṛtteḥ prāg anyena svāditam | śarkarāḥ sūkṣmapāṣāṇavatkaḍhinā mṛdviśeṣāḥ | kīṭo 'tra krimir amedhyasevī | pāṣāṇāḥ sūkṣmatarasarṣapādikalpāḥ | piṇyākas tailikayantre ghanībhūtatilacūrṇam, "tilakalke ca piṇyākaḥ" ity amarasiṃhenābhidhānāt | mathitaṃ jalamiśraṇena vinā viloḍitaṃ dadhi, "takraṃ hy udaśvinmathitaṃ pādāmbvardhāmby nirjalam" iti tenaivābhidhānāt | siddhā bhakṣyāḥ svata eva bhakṣyatayā siddhā āmalakādayaḥ | kṛtā bhakṣyā māṣapiṣṭādinā kṛtavaṭakādayaḥ | pratyakṣalavaṇīkṛtāḥ pratyakṣeṇa lavaṇena lavaṇīkṛtaḥ siddhabhakṣyāṇāṃ kṛtabhakṣyāṇāṃ ca pratyakṣalavaṇīkṛtā ity etad viśeṣaṇam | pratyakṣagrahaṇaṃ dadhyādinā vastvantareṇa pracchāditalavaṇena lavaṇīkṛtā grāhyā iti gamyate | yady api nityabhojane prayuṣitasya pratiṣiddhatvād atrāpi tadvarjanaṃ siddham, tathāpi tatrābhyanujñātasya yavagodhūmādipiṣṭavikārasyāpi paryuṣitasya śrāddhe varjanīyatvārthaṃ paryuṣitapratiṣedha iti mantavyam | atyarthapracuradravyeṣu kūśmāṇḍādiṣu doṣaśravaṇābhāve nivṛttir na bhavatīti doṣo 'pi smṛtyantare darśitaḥ |

	kūśmāṇḍaṃ māhiṣaṃ kṣīram āḍhakyo rājasarṣapāḥ |

	caṇakā rājamāṣāś ca ghnanti śrāddhaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ||

	piṇḍālūkaṃ ca tuṇḍīraṃ karamardāṃś ca nālikām |

	kūśmāṇḍaṃ bahubījāni śrāddhe dattvā vrajanty adhaḥ ||

piṇḍālūkatuṇḍīre kīdṛśe iti cintye | karamardaḥ kṛṣṇapākaphalaḥ | "kṛṣṇapākaphalāvignasuṣeṇāḥ karamardake" ity amaraḥ | bahubījāni mātuluṅgādīni | puruṣārthatayā pratiṣiddhasya sarvasya śrāddhapratiṣedhaḥ na siddha iti śrāddhe 'pi pratiṣedhārtham uktaṃ ṣaṭtriṃśanmate |

	kṣīrādi māhiṣaṃ varjyam abhakṣyaṃ yac ca kīrtitam |

ādigrahaṇān māhiṣaṃ dadhi gṛhyate, "māhiṣaṃ ca payo dadhi" iti bhadvājasmaraṇāt | māhiṣaṃ ca māṃsaṃ gṛhyate,

	māhiṣāṇi ca māṃsāni tathā śrāddhe vivarjayet |

iti viṣṇupurāṇe 'bhidhānāt | puruṣārthatayā pratiṣedhakaśāstreṣu yad abhakṣyaṃ prakīrtitaṃ tac ca sarvaṃ śrāddhe varjyaṃ śrāddhakarmaṇi na deyam ity arthaḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ śrāddhakarmaṇi varjyadravyāṇi**

**atha prasaṅgān nityabhojane varjyadravyaviṣayāṇi **

**kānicid vacanāni likhyante**

tatra devalaḥ |

	abhojyaṃ prāhur āhāraṃ śuktaṃ paryuṣitaṃ tathā |

	anyatra madhusaktubhyāṃ bhakṣebhyaḥ sarpiṣo guḍāt ||

atra śuktapadasyārtho bṛhaspatinā darśitaḥ |

	atyamlaṃ śuktam akhyātaṃ ninditaṃ brahmavādibhiḥ | iti |

asyāyam arthaḥ: yad odanasūpādikaṃ svato 'namlam īṣadamlaṃ vā hy astanam adyatanaṃ vā dīrghakālasthitibhyāṃ vā nijarasaṃ hitvātyartham amlībhavati tad eva loke śuktam ākhyātaṃ nisargato 'tyamlaṃ kāñjikādidravyam iti | paryuṣitam agnipakvaṃ sad rātryantaritaṃ sadā abhojyaṃ śrāddhabhojana iva nityabhojanādāv apy abhojyam ity arthaḥ | madhvādikaṃ paryuṣitam api bhojyam iti | bhakṣā apūpādayaḥ | madhuno 'pi surasatvāya guḍavad eva pākaḥ kriyate na bhojanadinād anyedyuḥ pakvaṃ madhu paryuṣitaṃ bhavati |

	nādyāc chāstraniṣiddhaṃ tu bhakṣyabhojyādikaṃ dvijaḥ | iti |

ayam arthaḥ: "nāpaṇīyam annam aśnīyān na dviḥpakvaṃ na paryuṣitam" iti | 

	ghṛtaṃ vā yadi vā tailaṃ vipro nādyān nakhacyutam |

	yamas tad aśuciṃ prāha tulyaṃ gomāṃsabhakṣaṇam ||

	hastadattāś ca ye snehā lavaṇaṃ vyañjanāni ca |

	dātāraṃ nopatiṣṭhanti bhoktā bhuñjati kilbiṣam ||

	ekena pāṇinā dattaṃ śūdradattaṃ na bhakṣayet |

	ghṛtaṃ tailaṃ ca lavaṇaṃ pānīyaṃ pāyasaṃ tathā ||

ityevamādiśāstraniṣiddham āpaṇīyam annādikaṃ dvijo nādyād iti | "nāpaṇīyam annam aśnīyāt" ity uktasya niṣiddhasya kvacid apavādam āha sa eva |

	apūpāḥ saktavo dhānās takraṃ dadhi ghṛtaṃ madhu |

	etat paṇeṣu bhoktavyaṃ bhāṇḍalepo na ced bhavet || iti |

dviḥpakvānnaniṣedhasyāpavādo 'pi: "yad yad dviḥpakvaṃ tat sarvaṃ nāśnīyāt" dviḥpakvaṃ nāma tad ucyate yat prathamapākata eva bhakṣaṇayogyatayā pakvaṃ sad api mārdavādiguṇāntaraṃ saṃpādayituṃ punaḥ pacyate | evaṃ ca yat tikte śākādau prathamapākamātreṇa bhakṣaṇayogyatā na bhavati kiṃ tu sahyatiktarasayukto bhavati tatra prathamapākasyāsamagratvāt punaḥ pāke kṛte 'pi na dviḥpakvatā bhavati | yatra bhakṣaviśeṣasiddhyartham udakādinā pūrvaṃ paktvā tailādināpi pākaḥ kriyate tatrāpi na dviḥpakvatā bhavati viśiṣṭabhakṣyasiddhiphalakapacikriyāyā udake taile ca kriyamāṇāyā ekatvād iti mantavyam | "na paryuṣitam aśnīyāt" ity asya apavādam āha yamaḥ |

	apūpāś ca karambhāś ca dhānā vaṭakasaktavaḥ |

	śākaṃ māṃsam apūpaṃ ca sūpaṃ kṛsaram eva ca ||

	yavāgūḥ pāyasaṃ caiva yac cānyat snehasaṃyutam |

	sarvaṃ paryuṣitaṃ bhojyaṃ śuktaṃ ca parivarjayet ||

apūpāḥ yavagodhūmapiṣṭavikārā maṇḍakādayaḥ | karambhāḥ dadhimiśritās saktavaḥ | dhānā bhṛṣṭayavataṇḍulāḥ | vaṭakāḥ māṣapiṣṭamayās tailapakvāḥ stokatayā kṛtāḥ prasiddhāḥ | śākaṃ māṃsaṃ cānyedyuḥ pakvam, na punar anyedur āhṛtaṃ tāvanmātreṇa paryuṣitatvāyogāt | evaṃ cānyedyuḥ pakvam odanaṃ tasminn eva dine saṃskāradravyāṇi prakṣipya śākaviśeṣatayā kalpitaṃ paryuṣitam api bhojyam evety avagantavyam | saktavo bhṛṣṭayavataṇḍulapiṣṭāni | punar apūpagrahaṇaṃ godhūmetaracaṇakādipiṣṭavikārasyāpūpaprāyasyāpi parigraṇārtham | sūpo mudgāḍhakyādikṛtaṃ vyañjanam | kṛsaraṃ bhṛṣṭatilacūrṇamiśram odanam | yavāgūḥ alpataṇḍulacūrṇamiśraṃ peyarūpam annam | pāyasaṃ payasā śṛtam annam | yac cāpūpādibhya uktebhyo 'nyad odanādikaṃ snehasaṃyuktaṃ dadhighṛtādinā snehadravyeṇābhighāritaṃ sat paryuṣitaṃ sarvaṃ bhojyaṃ yāvad aśuktaṃ vartate | yadā tu paryuṣitam apūpādikaṃ snehasaṃyuktam odanādikaṃ vā śuktaṃ jātaṃ tadā tad api varjayed ity arthaḥ | abhojyam ity anuvṛttau vasiṣṭho 'pi: "annaṃ paryuṣitaṃ kāmaṃ tu dadhnā ghṛtena yad abhighāritam upayuñjīta" iti | annaṃ paryuṣitam ity atrānuvṛttenābhojyam iti padena saṃbandhaḥ | dadhnā ghṛtena vābhighāritaṃ sat paryuṣitam annaṃ kāmam upayuñjīta aśnīyād ity arthaḥ | ata eva manuḥ |

	yat kiṃcit snehasaṃyuktaṃ bhakṣyabhojyam agarhitam |

	tat paryuṣitam apy ādyaṃ haviḥśeṣaṃ tu yad bhavet ||

upayojayed ity anuvṛttāv āpastambo 'pi: "udake 'vadhāya kṛtānnaṃ paryuṣitam" iti | yadā tu kṛtānnam udake 'vadhāya rātrau sthāpitaṃ tadā tad annaṃ paryuṣitam apy upayuñjītety arthaḥ | evaṃ kāñjikaṃ saṃpādayituṃ taṇḍulakṣālanodake nihitasyānnaniḥsravasya rātryantaritasya paryuṣitatve 'py abhojyatvaṃ nastīti tajjātasya kāñjikasyābhojyatvaṃ sutarāṃ nāstīti mantavyam | aśnīyad ity anuvṛttau śākkhalikhiāv api: "na paryuṣitam anyatra dadhiguḍagodhūmayavapiṣṭavikārebhyaḥ" iti | na paryuṣitam ity asya aśnīyād ity anuvṛttena padena saṃbandhaḥ | yady api dadhi guḍavan na pākasiddham iti na paryuṣitaṃ tena tasya paryudāso vyartha iti pratibhāti | tathāpi nānyeduḥ pākena siddhatvaṃ paryuṣitatve prayojakaṃ kiṃ tv adanīyatayā sādhyatvam iti dadhno 'py adanīyatayā sādhitasya paryuṣitatvam astīti tatparyudāso 'rthavān eva | yājñavalkyas tu "paryuṣitaṃ varjayet" iti svoktasya pratiprasavārtham āha |

	annaṃ paryuṣitaṃ bhojyaṃ snehāktaṃ cirasaṃsthitam |

	asnehā api godhūmayavagorasavikriyāḥ ||

cirasaṃsthitam iti padaṃ cirasaṃsthitā iti vipariṇāmena godhūmayavagorasavikriyā ity atrāpi saṃbandhanīyam | ata eva manuḥ |

	cirasthitam api tv ādyam asnehāktaṃ dvijātibhiḥ |

	yavagodhūmajaṃ sarvaṃ payasāṃ caiva vikriyāḥ || iti |

godhūmavikriyāḥ maṇḍakādayaḥ | yavavikriyāḥ saktvādayaḥ | gorasaḥ kṣīraṃ tadvikārāḥ kūrcikādyāḥ "kūrcikā kṣīravikṛtiḥ" ity amarasiṃhenoktatvāt | gorasavikṛtāv api "śuktaṃ cet parivarjayet" iti yamoktaṃ draṣṭavyam | bhojyatvenoktasya paryuṣitasya sarvasyāpi śrāddhe varjyatvaṃ pūrvasmin prakaraṇe 'bhihitam | tena bhojyatvāt śrāddhe 'py aniṣiddham iti bhramo na kāryaḥ | śaṅkhas tu śuktadravyeṣv api kiṃcid bhojyam ity āha |

	dadhi bhakṣyaṃ ca śukteṣu yac cānyad dadhi saṃbhavam |

	ṛbīṣapakvaṃ (?) bhakṣyaṃ syāt sarpir yuktam iti sthitiḥ ||

anagnikaḥ ūṣmā ṛbīṣam, tena pakvam ṛībīṣapakvam | dhānyarāśyādigatoṣmapakvam iti yāvat | tathā ca "nirbīṣapakvasyāśnīyāt" ity āpastambasūtraṃ vyācakṣāṇena dhūrtasvāminoktam: "anagnikaḥ ūṣmā ṛbīṣaṃ tatpakvasya pratiṣedhaḥ kriyate" it granthena | ṛbīṣapakvaṃ śuktam api sarpiṣā yuktaṃ bhakṣyaṃ syāt | na tadrahitam ity arthaḥ | dadhisaṃbhavaṃ takranavanītādi | bhakṣyaṃ bhakṣaṇārham ity arthaḥ | yamas tv āpadi śuktasya prakṣālanāt bhakṣaṇārhatā bhavatīty āha |

	śuktāni hi dvijo 'nnāni na bhuñjīta kadācana |

	prakṣālitāni nirdoṣāṇy āpaddharmo yadā bhavet ||

evaṃ paryuṣitasyāpadi pakṣālanād bhakṣaṇārhatā bhavati | ata eva tasya bhojane 'bhyanujñā tenaiva kṛtā |

	masūramāṣasaṃyuktaṃ tathā paryuṣitaṃ ca yat |

	tat tu prakṣālitaṃ kṛtvā bhuñjīta hy abhighāritam || iti |

bījabhūtadhānyādikaṃ bhojyam api bhāvibahuphalahetuvināśasyātyantānucitatvāt anāpadi paryuṣitavat nopabhuñjītety āha devalaḥ |

	na bījāny upayuñjīta rogāpattim ṛte budhaḥ |

	phalāny eṣām anantāni bījānāṃ hi vināśayet || iti |

eṣāṃ bījānām anantāni phalāni yasmād upayuñjāno vināśayet tasmād anāpadi bījāni nopayuñjītety arthaḥ | svato viśuddham apy āhāraṃ mṛtamakṣikādisaṃsargadūṣitaṃ varjayed ity āha sa eva |

	viśuddham api cāhāraṃ makṣikākrimijantubhiḥ |

	keśalomanakhair vāpi dūṣitaṃ parivarjayet ||

anāpadīti śeṣaḥ | ata eva sumantuḥ: "keśakṭṭakṣutavacobhihataṃ śvabhir āghrātaṃ prekṣitaṃ vādadhi paryuṣitaṃ punaḥ siddhaṃ caṇḍālāvekṣitam abhojyam anyatra hiraṇyodakaiḥ spṛṣṭāt" iti | kṣutavacaḥ kṣutavaśāj jāto dhvānaḥ tena abhihatam upahatam | śvabhir iti bahuvacanaṃ yeṣām avaghṛāṇaprekṣaṇe doṣāvahe tādṛśaprāṇināṃ smṛtyantroktagavādīnāṃ saṃgrahārtham | adadhi paryuṣitaṃ paryudastadadhyādivyatiriktaṃ paryuṣitam | punaḥsiddhaṃ dviḥpakvam | etad uktaṃ bhavati: viśuddhāhāraṃ makṣikādisaṃsargato duṣṭaṃ saṃtyajya aduṣṭāhāraṃ bhuñjīta asaṃbhave tu makṣikādim apāsyāhāraśuddhyartham udakena prokṣaṇaṃ hiraṇyasparśanaṃ vā kṛtvā bhuñjīteti | aduṣṭāhārāntarāsaṃbhave 'pi yad avaśyaṃ varjyaṃ tad āha devalaḥ |

	avalīḍhaṃ śvamārjāradhāṅkṣakukkuṭamarkaṭaiḥ |

	bhojane nopayuñjīta tad amedhyaṃ hi sarvataḥ ||

dhvāṅkṣaḥ kākaḥ | brahmapurāṇe 'pi |

	śūdrabhuktāvaśiṣṭaṃ tu nādyād bhāṇḍasthitaṃ kvacit | iti |

tena bhāṇḍād uddhṛtam anyasmin pātre nikṣipya deyam | śūdrocchiṣṭavallaśunādisaṃspṛṣṭam api nādyāt | tathā ca bhaviṣyatpurāṇe |

	surālaśuṇasaṃspṛṣṭaṃ pīyūṣādisamanvitam |

	saṃsargād ucyate tad dhi śūdrocchiṣavad ācaret || iti |

pīyūṣaṃ navaprasūtāyāḥ gavādeḥ kṣīram "pīyūṣo 'bhinavaṃ payaḥ" ity amareṇābhidhānāt | ādiśabdena chatrākādisaṃspṛṣṭaṃ gṛhyate | saṃsargaduṣṭavaj jātyā duṣṭam api śākādikaṃ nādyāt, "vṛntākanālikāpotakusumbhāśmantakāś ceti śākānām abhakṣyāḥ" iti paiṭhīnasismaraṇāt | vṛntākaṃ bṛhatīsadṛśasthūlodbhidaṃ phalaṃ vṛntabhāgena saha śākatvena prasiddham | nālikā dīrghanālā śirasi svalpaphalānvitā, tasyāḥ phalasya nālabhāgasya ca śākatvena prāpteḥ pratiṣedhaḥ |  potaṃ potikā, "potikā tu sutāhvayā" iti vaijayantyām abhidhānāt | yasyāḥ patraśākasevā nidrātiśayakāriṇī sā sutāhvayā jñeyā | asmākaṃ tv asya svarūpaṃ kīdṛśam iti cintyam | vṛntākaṃ śvetam evābhakṣyam,

	gaṇḍūlaṃ śvetavṛntākaṃ kūśmāṇḍaṃ ca vivarjayet |

iti devalena vṛntākaviśeṣasya pratiṣedhāt | viśeṣapratiṣedhaś ca śeṣābhyanujñānārtham iti nyāyena śvetetaravṛntākabhakṣaṇābhyanujñā gamyate | gaṇḍūlaṃ kaṇḍūlāphalam atyantakaṇḍūtijanakaṃ bahuromayuktaṃ varṣākālabhavam | ata eva amarasiṃhena "kaṇḍūlā pravṛṣāyaṇī" ity uktam | kūśmāṇḍaṃ kumbhavad vartulam adīrghālābusadṛśam | kusumbhaṃ kaṇṭakarahitam abhakṣyam, "akaṇṭakitvaviśiṣṭasya kusumbhasya smṛtyantare niṣedho vidyate" iti devasvāminoktatvāt | vṛntākanālikāpotakusumbhānāṃ ca bhakṣaṇe uśanasā doṣo darśitaḥ |

	kusumbhanālikāśākaṃ vṛntākaṃ potikaṃ tathā |

	bhakṣayan patitas tu syād api vedāntago dvijaḥ || iti |

bhaviṣyatpurāṇe jātiduṣṭānāṃ śākānām udāharaṇatayā kānicic chākāny uktāni |

	laśunaṃ gṛñjanaṃ caiva palāṇḍuṃ kavakāni ca |

	vārtākanālikālābu hy aveyāj jātidūṣitam ||

laśunādikaṃ dravyaṃ saṃsargeṇa vināpi laśunatvādijātyaiva dūṣitam aveyāj jānīyād ity arthaḥ | jātyā dūṣitam iti jñānasya phalam asaty api duṣṭasaṃsarge nivṛttiḥ | laśunākhyaviśeṣasya bhedako dharmo vaidyakādau draṣṭavyaḥ, laśunagṛñjanapalāṇḍukāḥ palāṇḍuviśeṣāḥ | tatra haridraktavarṇaviśeṣo gṛñjanaḥ | "haridrakto gṛñjanaḥ" iti vaijayantyām | śvetakandaviśeṣaḥ palāṇḍuḥ, "palāṇḍau tu śvetakando mukundakaḥ" iti tatraivoktatvāt | etac ca laśunāditrividhapalāṇḍuviśeṣābhidhānam |

	laśunaṃ dīrghapatraṃ ca picchagandho mahauṣadham |

	varaṇyaś ca palāṇḍuś ca latārkaś ca parārikā ||

	gṛñjanaṃ yavaneṣṭaś ca palāṇḍor daśa jātayaḥ ||

ityuktadaśavidhapalāṇḍūpalakṣaṇam | mahauṣadhavaraṇyādīnām api bhedo vaidyādau draṣṭavyaḥ | kavakaṃ chatrākam | vārtākaṃ kṣudravārtākasaṃjñakabṛhatīphalaṃ kaṇṭakārikākhyabṛhatīphalāt kiṃcit sthūlam | kavakabhakṣaṇe tu doṣā yamena darśitāḥ |

	bhūmijaṃ vṛkṣajaṃ vāpi chatrākaṃ bhakṣayanti ye |

	brahmaghnāṃs tān vijānīyād brahmavādiṣu garhitān || iti |

hārīto 'pi duṣṭadravyasaṃsargābhāve 'pi varjyān āha: "na vaṭaplakṣodumbaradadhitthanīpamātuluṅgāni vā bhakṣayet" iti | dadhitthaṃ kapitthaphalam | nīpaṃ kadambapatram | śeṣāṇi vyaktāni | manur api |

	lohitān vṛkṣaniryāsān vraścanaprabhavāṃs tathā |

	śeluṃ gavyaṃ ca pīyūṣaṃ prayatnena vivarjayet ||

lohitān vṛkṣaniryāsān lākṣādīn | vraścanaprabhavān niryāsān api śālmaliniryāsaprabhṛtīn | lohitagrahaṇāt niryāsatve 'pi pāṭalavarṇahiṃgvādeḥ śvetavarṇakarpūrādeś ca na niṣedhaḥ | śeluḥ śleṣmāntakākhyo vṛkṣaḥ | pīyūṣo 'bhinavaṃ payaḥ | gavyapīyūṣe tu viśeṣo brahmapurāṇe darśitaḥ |

	ghṛtāt phenaṃ ghṛtān maṇḍaṃ pīyūṣam atha vārdragoḥ |

	saguḍaṃ maricāktaṃ tu tathā paryuṣitaṃ dadhi ||

	dīrṇaṃ takram apeyaṃ ca naṣṭasvādukaphenavat ||

ayam arthaḥ: ghṛtād uddhṛtya tatphenamātraṃ tadagramātraṃ (?) ca na peyam | tathā ārdragoḥ pīyūṣaṃ yāvadārdratā sarajaskatā gāve (?) prasūtisamaye yonau pravṛttānuvartate tāvat kṣīram apeyam | tathā yad dadhi guḍamaricamiśraṃ yat paryuṣitaṃ tad apy apeyam | tathā yat takraṃ dīrṇaṃ darvīghaṭṭanaśūnyam agnitāpādinā svato vā sphuṭitaṃ bahudinasthityā saṃjātena phenena yuktam, atyarthaṃ śuktatayā naṣṭasvādukam apeyam iti | yājñavalkyo 'pi varjyakṣīram āha |

	saṃdhinyanirdaśāvatsagopayaḥ parivarjayet | iti |

tatra saṃdhinyāḥ goḥ payaḥ parivarjayed ity etat sphutam uktaṃ hārītena: "saṃdhinī vṛṣasyantī tasyāḥ payo na pibet tadṛtumad bhavati" iti | vṛṣasyantī kāmukī maithunecchāvatīti yāvat | tadīyaṃ payaḥ ṛtumad bhavati | ṛtumatyāḥ saṃbandhi bhavatīty arthaḥ | anena etad uktaṃ bhavati: yāvati kāle mauthunecchānuvṛttis tāvati kāle tasyāḥ payo na pibed iti | tena maithunecchānivṛttau tasyāḥ payo na niṣiddham iti mantavyam | "anirdaśāyāḥ payaḥ parivarjayet" ity asyāyam arthaḥ: prasavaprabhṛty anirgatadaśarātrāyāḥ payaḥ varjayed iti | etac ca rajonivṛttikālopalakṣaṇārtham | tena daśarātrād arvāg rajonivṛttau nāsti tatra pratiṣedhaḥ | daśarātrād upary api rajo'nuvṛttāv asti pratiṣedha iti boddhavyam | ata eva "navasūtāyāḥ payaḥ na pibet sarajastvāt" ity uktvā hārītenoktam: "saptarātrād ity eke daśrātrād ity apare māsenāpīyūṣaṃ bhavatīti dharmavidaḥ" iti | navasūtāyāḥ payaḥ saptarātrād upary api pīyūṣaṃ bhavatīty eke | daśarātrād upary api pīyūṣaṃ bhavatīty anye mantanta ity arthaḥ | eteṣu saptarātrādipakṣeṣu yathā rajonivṛtti vyavasthā draṣṭavyā | "avatsāyāḥ payaḥ parivarjayet" ity asyāyam arthaḥ: avatsā vatsaśūnyā mṛtavatseti yāvat | tasyāḥ payaḥ yāvad vatsaviyogaśokānuvṛttiḥ tāvat vivarjayed iti | ata eva "payo na pibet" ity anuvṛttau hārītenoktam: "hatavatsāyāḥ śokāviṣṭatvāt navasūtāyāḥ sarajastvāt" iti | na ca vācyaṃ śokāviṣṭatvād ity asya hetuvannigadarūpārthavādatvāc chokanivṛttāv api mṛtavatsāyāḥ payo na pibed iti | sarajastvād iti hetusamabhivyāhārāt | ato hetur evāyaṃ śokāviṣṭatvād iti, na hetuvannigadārthavādaḥ | na ca vācyaṃ sarajastvād ity api hetuvannigadārthavāda eva na tu hetur iti kathaṃ tatsāhacaryād asya hetutvaṃ niścīyata iti | hetuvivakṣayaiva sarajastvād ity asya prayuktatvāt | yadi hetuvivakṣayā sarajastvād iti na prayuktaṃ syāt tadā daśarātrāt prāg ūrdhvaṃ yadā rajonivṛttiḥ tadā navaprasūtāyāḥ payaḥ peyam ity ayam artho yaḥ pratipādayitum iṣṭaḥ so 'pratipādito (?) bhavet | tataś ca "saptarātrād ity eke daśarātrād ity apare māsenāpīyūṣaṃ bhavatīti dharmavidaḥ" ity anantaroktasya tadīyagranthasya anirvāhaḥ syāt | tasmād dhetutvenaiva sarajastvād ity asyānvayo nārthavādatvena | tatsamabhivyāhārāc chokāviṣṭatvād ity api hetutvenaivānvayo nārthavādatvenety alaṃ bahunātiprasaṅgena | dharmavidgrahaṇaṃ rajonivṛttisaṃdehasyāpy abhāvas tatreti jñāpanarthaṃ kṛtam | tena yadā saptarātrād api rajonivṛttiniścayaḥ tadā tatpayaḥpāne 'pi na dharmahāniḥ | gavyapīyūṣavad ajāmahiṣyor api pīyūṣam apeyam | tathā ca vasiṣṭhaḥ: "gomahiṣyajānām anirdaśam" iti | payo na peyam iti śeṣaḥ | gautamo 'pi varjyaṃ kṣīram āha: "saṃdhinīyamasūsyandinīnāṃ ca" iti | kṣīraṃ varjyam iti śeṣaḥ | syandinī svataḥ prasravatkṣīrastanī | yamasūḥ yamalaprasavinī | bodhāyano 'pi: "kṣīram apeyaṃ vivatsāyā anyavatsāyāś ca" iti | śaṅkho 'pi "sarvāsāṃ dvistanīnāṃ kṣīram abhojyatayā varjyam" iti | manur api |

	śraṇyānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ mṛgāṇāṃ mahiṣīṃ vinā | iti |

"mahiṣīṃ vinā" āraṇyamahiṣīvyatiriktānām ity arthaḥ | mṛgāṇām ity atra pūrvatra śrutena paya iti padena saṃbandhaḥ | varjyāvarjyatvam adhidhīyate | yady api mṛgāṇām iti pulliṅganirdeśāt puṃvyaktayaḥ pratīyante, tathāpi payaḥpadasaṃbandhāyogyatvaparihārāya puṃliṅgena vyaktimātrayeva vivakṣitam iti pratyetavyam | tataś cāyogyatvānavagateḥ payaḥpadena saṃbandho yujyata eva | gautamo 'pi: "nityam āvikam apeyam auṣṭtram aikaśaphaṃ ca" iti nityam abhinavadaśāyām cety arthaḥ | auṣṭram uṣṭryāḥ payaḥ | aikaśapham ekaśaphāyā vaḍavādeḥ payaḥ | evaṃ ca gomahiṣyajānām eva payaḥ peyaṃ nānyasyā ity anusaṃdheyam | ata eva śaṅkhaḥ |

	māhiṣaṃ gavyam ājaṃ bhojyaṃ kṣīreṣu nirdiśet |

āpastambas tu brāhmaṇavyatiriktasya kapilāpayo varjyam ity āha |

	kṣatriyaś caiva vṛttastho vaiśyaḥ śūdro 'atha vā punaḥ |

	yaḥ pibet kapilākṣīraṃ narakān ety apuṇyakṛt ||

tena brāhmaṇavyatiriktaḥ kapilāgokṣīraṃ prayatnena vivarjayed ity abhiprāyaḥ | brāhmaṇasyāpi hutaśeṣavyatiriktakapilākṣīrapāne doṣo bhaviṣyapurāṇe darśitaḥ |

	kāpilaṃ yaḥ pibec chūdro narakena vipacyate |

	hutaśeṣaṃ pibed vipro vipraḥ syād anyathā paśuḥ || iti |

hutaśeṣe pīte viprasya janmāntare 'pi vipratvaṃ bhavati | anyathā hutaśeṣavyatiriktakapilākṣīre pīte viprasya janmāntare paśutvaṃ bhavatīty arthaḥ | kṣīravarjanavidhānād eva tatspṛṣṭasyāpi varjanaṃ pīyūṣaspṛṣṭavarjanavad unneyam | kṣīravarjanavidhānād eva tavikārasyāpi kūrcāder varjyatvaṃ siddham, kūrcādivikāre kṣīrasya sadbhāvāt | ata eva kṣīre varjayitavye pāyasāder varjanaṃ kāryam iti mīmāṃsāyāṃ pratipāditam | ata eva niṣiddhakṣīravikārāṇāṃ bhakṣaṇe niṣiddhātikramasya kṛtatvāt prāyaścittam āha śaṅkhaḥ |

	kṣīrāṇi yāny abhakṣyāṇi tadvikārāśane budhaḥ |

	saptarātravrataṃ kuryāt prayatnena samāhitaḥ || iti |

bhakṣyavrīhyādivikārasyāpi devatābhyo nivedanārthaṃ vaidikamārgeṇa laukikamārgeṇa vopakalpitasya nivedanāt prāg aprāśyatvam uktaṃ yājñavalkyena |

	devatārthaṃ haviḥśigrulohitavraścanāṃs tathā | iti |

yathā saṃdhinyādipayaḥ parvarjayet tathā devārthaṃ devatābhyo nivedanārthaṃ laukikamārgeṇa parikalpitam annaṃ haviḥ vaidikamārgeṇa parikalpitaṃ puroḍāśādikaṃ śigrvādikaṃ ca parivarjayed ity arthaḥ | evaṃ ca saṃdhinyādipayovad yady api devatārthānnasya puroṣāśādihiviṣaś ca sadā parivarjanaṃ pratibhāti | tathāpi devatānivedanāt prāg eva pratiṣedho veditavyaḥ | ata eva pitrādidevatārtham udāhṛtyoktaṃ yamena |

	bhakṣyaṃ bhojyaṃ tathā peyaṃ yat kiṃcit pacyate gṛhe |

	na bhoktavyaṃ pitṝṇāṃ tad anivedya kathaṃcana || iti |

śigruḥ śobhāñjanaḥ | sa ca raktakusumaḥ parivarjanīyo na śvetakusumaḥ | smṛtyantare 'pi "raktaśigruṃ varjayet" iti "viśiṣṭasyaiva niṣedho vidyate" iti devasvāminābhidhānāt | śigrvādijātigarhitavad āśrayagarhitam api varjanīyam, tathā ca aṅgirāḥ |

	dvividhaṃ garhitaṃ proktaṃ nityam annaṃ manīṣibhiḥ |

	jātito garhitaṃ caiva tathaivāśrayagarhitam ||

	abhojyānāṃ vijānīyād annam āśrayagarhitam |

	laśunādikam annaṃ yat taj jñeyaṃ jātigarhitam || iti |

abhojyānām annaṃ yat tad āśrayagarhitaṃ vijānīyāt | yal laśunagṛñjanachatrākādikam annam adanīyaṃ duṣṭadravyasaṃsargeṇa vināpi laśunatvādijātitayaiva manvādibhir niṣiddhaṃ taj jātigarhitaṃ jñeyam ity arthaḥ | yājñavalkyas tu prātipadyenāśrayagarhitam āha |

	kadaryabaddhacorāṇāṃ klībaraṅgāvatāriṇām |

	vaiṇābhiśastavārdhuṣyagaṇikāgaṇadīkṣiṇām ||

	cikitsakāturakruddhapuṃścalīmattavidviṣām |

	krūrograpatitavrātyaḍāmbhikocchiṣṭabhojinām ||

	avīrastrīsvarṇakārastrījitagrāmayājinām |

	śastravikrayikarmāratantuvāyaśvavṛttinām ||

	celadhāvasurājīvasahopapativeśmanām |

	piśunānṛtinoś caiva tathā cākrikabandinām ||

	eṣām annaṃ na bhoktavyaṃ somavikrayiṇas tathā || iti |

yo lobhād vidyamānam api dhanaṃ na bhuṅkte na dadāti sa kadaryaḥ | tathā ca smṛtiḥ |

	ātmānaṃ dharmakṛtyaṃ ca putradārāṃś ca pīḍayet |

	lobhād yaḥ pitarau bhṛtyān sa kadarya iti smṛtaḥ ||

baddho nigalitaḥ, asiddho vā | coraklībau prasiddhau | raṅgāvatārī mallādiḥ | vaiṇo vīṇāvādī | abhiśastaḥ patanīyakarmakartvenābhiyuktaḥ | vārdhuṣyaṃ niṣiddhavṛddhyupajīvanaṃ tena tadvān lakṣyate | gaṇikā veśyā | gaṇaḥ saṅghaḥ | dīkṣī dīkṣaṇīyeṣṭyādijanitadīkṣākhyasaṃskāravān | dikṣākhyasaṃskāravt tvaṃ cāvabhṛtheṣṭeḥ prāg eva avabhṛtheṣṭyā tatsaṃskārāpagamāt evaṃ ca dīkṣaṇīyeṣṭyanuṣṭhānaprabhṛti avabhṛtheṣṭyanuṣṭhānaparyantaṃ dīkṣitasyābhojyānnatvam anayā smṛtyā pratipāditam iti yady api pratibhāti | tathāpi "saṃsthite 'gnīṣomīye yajamānasya gṛhe 'śitavyam" ityādiśrutyā saty api dīkṣākhyasaṃskāre agnīṣoīyapaśuyāgasamāpteḥ prāg eva abhojyānntavam anayā smṛtyāpy uktam iti mantavyam | cikitsako bhiṣak | āturaḥ pāparogagrastaḥ | pāparogāś ca devalena darśitāḥ |

	vātavyādhyaśmarīkuṣṭhamehodarabhagaṃdarāḥ |

	arśaḥ saṃgrahaṇīty aṣṭau pāparogāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ||

vātavyādhiḥ pakṣamārakādiḥ | aśmarī mūtrakṛcchram | meho madhumehādiḥ | udaraṃ jalodarādiḥ | itare prasiddhāḥ | kruddho dhṛtābhyantarakopaḥ | puṃścalī asatī | matto dhanādigarvitaḥ | paradhikkāraśīlaḥ | vidviṭ śatruḥ | krūro nirdayaḥ | ugraḥ paraduḥkhotpādanaparaḥ | patito mahāpātakī | vrātyaḥ patitasāvitrīkaḥ | ḍāmbhikaḥ khyātilābhādiprayojanānusaṃdhānenaiva dharmānuṣṭhātā | uccchiṣṭabhojī parabhuktojjhitānnabhojanaśīlaḥ | avīrastrī niṣpatisutā, "avīrā niṣpatisutā" ity amarasiṃhenābhidhānāt | svarṇakāraḥ kaṭakamakuṭādisvarṇavikārakārī | strījitaḥ sarvakāryeṣu strīvaśavartī | grāmayājī anekagrāmayājakaḥ śastravikrayī khaḍgādivikrayajīvī | śvavṛttiḥ śvavṛttavān sevaka iti yāvat | nṛśaṃso ghātukaḥ | rājā janapadapurapālakaḥ rajako vastrādirāgakartā | yaḥ prāṇivadhena (?) jīvati sa vadhajīvī | celadhāvaḥ vastraprakṣālakaḥ | surājīvaḥ surāvikrayī | sahopapativeśmā bhāryā jārasahitagṛhaḥ | eṣāṃ kadaryatvādidoṣaduṣṭānāṃ traivarṇikānām annaṃ somalatāvikrayādidoṣaduṣṭasya traivarṇikasyānnaṃ kadaryatvādidoṣaduṣṭasvāmisaṃbandhāt paramparayā duṣṭam annaṃ na bhoktavyam ity arthaḥ | yady api dīkṣitānnasyāśrayakṛtaduṣṭatvābhāvaḥ, tathāpi vacanabalād evābhojyatvam | anyad api traivarṇakānnaṃ svāśrayagarhitam abhojyaṃ vacobhaṅgyā paiṭhīnasir āha: "sāṃvatsarikaghaṇṭikagrāmakūṭānnaṃ viṣaṃ parivittiparivividānaviddhaprajananavṛṣalīpatididhiṣūpatipunarbhūputrāṇāṃ rudhiram" iti | sāṃvatsariko jyautiṣikaḥ | ghāṇṭiko nighaṇṭukāreṇa nirūpitaḥ: "rājñāṃ prabodhasamaye ghaṇṭāśilpas tu ghāṇṭikaḥ" iti | grāmakūṭo grāme 'nanyādhīnatakṣakaḥ "kūṭatakṣo 'nadhīnakaḥ" ity amaraḥ | viṣaṃ viṣavad abhakṣyam | yasmin akṛtadāre jyeṣṭhe kaniṣṭhena dāraparigrahaḥ kriyate sa jyeṭḥaḥ parivittiḥ | ya ādhānāni jyeṣṭhenākṛtāni karoty asau kaniṣṭhaḥ parivividānaḥ | viddhaprajanano viddhaśiśnaḥ | didhiṣūpatiḥ punarbhūpatiḥ | rudhiraṃ rudhiravad abhakṣyam | yamo 'pi |

	cakropajīvī gāndharvaḥ kitavas taskaras tathā |

	dhvajī dāropajīvī ca śūdrādhyāpakayājakau ||

	kulālaś citrakarmā ca vārdhuṣiś carmavikrayī || iti |

abhojyānna iti śeṣaḥ | cakropajīvī śākaṭikaḥ | dhvajī madyavikrayī | kulālaḥ kumbhāravṛttyupajīvī | śeṣāṇi prasiddhāni | smṛtyantare 'pi |

	tathā rājabhṛtasyānnaṃ corasyānnaṃ tathaiva ca |

	sūtake mṛtake cānnaṃ svargastham api pātayet ||

	avaliptasya mūrkhasya duṣṭavṛttasya durmateḥ |

	annam aśraddadhānasya yo bhuṅkte bhrūṇahā sa vai || iti |

rājabhṛtyādīnām annam atyantagarhitam, tena yatnād varjyam ity abhiprāyaḥ | avalipto garvitaḥ | sāṃvatsarikaghāṇṭikādīnām api traivarṇikāntargatānām annaṃ pratiṣidhyate | na tu śūdrādijātyantargatānām, teṣāṃ svarūpeṇa pratiṣedhāt | tathā ca smṛtyantare |

	brāhmaṇasya sadāśnīyāt kṣatriyas tu parvasu |

	prakṛteṣv atha vaiśyasya śūdrasya na kadācana ||

prakṛteṣu prastuteṣu vivāhādiṣu mahotsaveṣv ity arthaḥ | brāhmaṇasyetyādiṣu annam iti śeṣo draṣṭavyaḥ | evaṃ ca kṣatriyāṇām annaṃ parvasu bhoktavyam | kadaryādikṣatriyāṇām annaṃ parvasv api na bhoktavyam | vaiśyānām annaṃ vivāhādimahotsavād anyatra na bhoktavyam | kadaryādivaiśyānām annaṃ vivāhādyutsaveṣv api na bhoktavyam ity anusaṃdheyam | śūdrasya na kadācanety anenaiva śūdrāj jaghanyasya pratilomasyānnaṃ sutarāṃ nāśnīyād iti gamyate | yājñavalkyaḥ śūdreṣv api keṣāṃcid annaṃ bojyam ity āha |

	śūdreṣu dāsagopālakulamitrārdhasīriṇaḥ |

	bhojyānnā nāpitaś caiva yaś cātmānaṃ nivedayet \\

dāsaḥ krītakādiḥ | gopālo gavāṃ palayitā | kulamitraṃ pitṛpitāmahādikramāgataḥ sakhā | sīro lāṅgalam, tena kṛṣiphalaṃ lakṣyate, tataś ca kṛṣiphalam ardhasīrapadenoktam | nāpito vapanādikarmakartā śūdraḥ | ete dāsādayaḥ śūdreṣu śūdrāṇāṃ madhye bhojyānnāḥ | yaś ca śūdraḥ krītavadvijāyātmānaṃ (?) nivedayati tavaham iti samarpayati so 'pi bhojyānna ity arthaḥ | dāsādayaś cātra svakīyā eva vivakṣitāḥ | ata eva devalaḥ |

	svadāso nāpito gopaḥ kumbhakāraḥ kṛṣīvalaḥ |

	brāhmaṇair api bhojyānnāḥ pañcaite śūdrayonayaḥ ||

evaṃ ca yadīyā dāsādayas tasyaiva teṣām annaṃ bhojyaṃ nānyasyeti mantavyam | dāsādivyatiriktaśūdrannabhojane doṣam āha dakṣaḥ |

	śūdrānnarasapuṣṭāṅgas tv adhīyāno 'pi nityaśaḥ |

	juhvan vāpi japan vāpi gatim ūrdhvāṃ na vindati ||

vasiṣtho 'pi |

	śūdrānnenodarasthena yo 'pi gacchati maithunam |

	yasyānnaṃ tasya tat putraḥ annāc chuklaṃ pravartate ||

hārīto 'pi |

	śūdrānnena tu bhuktena jaṭharasthena yo mṛtaḥ |

	sa vesaratvam uṣṭratvaṃ śūdratvaṃ vopagacchati ||

aṅgirā api |

	ṣaṇmāsaṃ yo dvijo bhuṅkte śūdrasyānnaṃ vigarhitam |

	sa ca jīvan bhavec chūdro mṛtaś ca śvābhijāyate ||

annaṃ pakvam āmaṃ ca | yat tu sumantunoktam,

	gorasaṃ caiva saktūṃś ca tailaṃ piṇyākam eva ca |

	apūpān bhakṣayec chūdrāt yac cānyat payasā kṛtam ||

yad api hārītena,

	kandupakvaṃ snehapakvaṃ pāyasaṃ dadhi saktavaḥ |

	etāny aśūdrānnabhujo bhojyāni manur abravīt ||

—apūpādipacanārthaṃ parimaṇḍalatayā kṛtam ayomayaṃ pātraṃ kanduḥ, tatra pakvaṃ kandupakvam | snehena tailādidravyeṇa pakvaṃ senapakvam | aśūdrānnabhujo dvijasya — yad apy aṅgirasā,

	pātrāntaragataṃ grāhyaṃ śūdrāt svagṛham āgatam || iti |

— annam iti śeṣaḥ — yad api viṣṇupurāṇe,

	saṃprokṣya vidvān gṛhṇīyāc chūdrānnaṃ gṛham āgatam | 

iti, yat tu śaṅkhena,

	gṛhāt parārthe bhūmyarthe gavārtheṣu viśeṣataḥ |

	śrotriyeṇa tu bhoktavyaṃ śūdrāṇāṃ tu yamo 'bravīt ||

tad etat sarvam āpadviṣayam | evam agnivihīnasyānnam apy āpadviṣaya eva bhojyam, "agnihīnasya nānnam adyād anāpadi" iti yājñavalkyasmaraṇāt | saty apy adhikāre śrautasmārtādiparigraham akurvato vidhāne notsṛṣṭāgneś cānnam anāpadi na bhuñjītety arthaḥ | anenārthād agnihīnasyānnam āpady adyād ity uktaṃ bhavati | āpady api yativānaprasthayor annaṃ nadyāt | tathā ca ślokāpastambaḥ |

	dvāv evāśramiṇau bhojyau brahmacārī tathā gṛhī |

	muner annam abhojyaṃ syāt sarveṣāṃ liṅgināṃ tathā || iti |

bhojyau bhojyānnau | muniḥ vānaprastho yatiś ca | liṅginām avedoktaliṅginām ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ nityabhojane māṃsavyatiriktavarjyadravyaviṣayāṇi**

**atha nityabhojane varjanīyamāṃsadravyaviṣayāṇi **

**kānicid vacanāni likhyante **

tatra manuḥ |

	etad uktaṃ dvijātīnāṃ bhakṣyābhakṣyam aśeṣataḥ |

	māṃsasyātaḥ pravakṣyāmi vidhiṃ bhakṣaṇavarjane ||

māṃsasya bhakṣaṇe varjane ca vidhiṃ pravakṣyāmīty arthaḥ | tatra māṃsabhakṣaṇe prāpte vidhikathanaṃ niṣedhakathanena vinā na saṃbhavatīti prathamaṃ manūktam eva niṣedhavacanaṃ pradarśyate |

	nākṛtvā prāṇinām hiṃsāṃ māṃsam utpadyate kvacit |

	na ca prāṇivadhaḥ svargyas tasmān māṃsaṃ vivarjayet ||

	samutpattiṃ ca māṃsasya vadhabandhau ca dehinām |

	prasamīkṣya nivarteta sarvamāṃsasya bhakṣaṇāt || iti |

prāṇihiṃsā mā bhūd iti sarvasmād rāgaprāptamāṃsabhakṣaṇān nivarteta, na tu pratyavāyabhayād ity arthaḥ | atroktaṃ tenaiva |

	na māṃsabhakṣaṇe doṣo na madye na ca maithune |

	pravṛttir eṣā bhūtānāṃ nivṛttis tu mahāphalā || iti |

anena māṃsabhakṣaṇe pratyavāyābhāvāl lokavidveṣābhāvāc ca phalārthitvābhāve māṃsaṃ bhakṣayed iti vidhir arthād ukta iti mantavyam | nivṛttes tu mahāphalasādhanatvaṃ ca tenaivoktam |

	phalamūlāśanair medhyair munyannānāṃ ca bhojanaiḥ |

	na tat phalam avāpnoti yan māṃsaparivarjanāt || iti |

evam uktaphalārthinām api keṣucid viṣayeṣu māṃsaṃ bhakṣitavyam ity sa eva |

	prokṣitaṃ bhakṣayen māṃsaṃ brāhmaṇasya ca kāmyayā |

	yathāvidhi niyuktaś ca prāṇānām eva cātyaye ||

prokṣitaṃ bhakṣayen māṃsaṃ kratau paśvavayavabhūtaṃ hṛdayādimāṃsam iṣṭiśiṣṭaṃ bhakṣayet | brāhmaṇasya ca kāmyayā nimantritabrāhmaṇasyecchayā māṃsaṃ bhakṣayet | iṣṭaiḥ sahopabhujyatām iti svecchāpūrvakoktyanujñātaṃ śrāddhaśiṣṭaṃ māṃsaṃ śrāddhakartā bhakṣayed iti yāvat | yathāvidhi niyuktaś ca vidhivac chrāddhe nimantrito brāhmaṇapitrādyuddeśena tyaktaṃ māṃsaṃ bhakṣayet | prāṇānām eva cātyaye māṃsaṃ bhakṣayet | bheṣajatvena durbhikṣādāv annālābhena vā yatra māṃsabhakṣaṇam antareṇa prāṇadhāraṇam aśakyaṃ tathāvidhaviṣaye 'pi māṃsaṃ bhakṣayet | evaṃ ca prokṣitādiviṣayacatuṣṭayād anyatra phalārthināṃ māṃsabhakṣaṇaṃ varjanīyam | phalārthitvābhāve tu nāvaśyaṃ varjanīyam iti siddham | yat punas tenoktam,

	asaṃskṛtān paśūn mantrair nādyād vipraḥ kadācana |

iti tad api phalārthiviṣayam | 

	na māṃsabhakṣaṇe doṣo na madye na ca maithune |

iti vākyatrayaṃ yatra prātipadyena niṣedho na vidyate tadviṣayam | prātipadyena niṣedhavidhiṣu satsu puruṣasya nivṛttisiddhyarthaṃ niṣiddhakaraṇe doṣakalpanasyāvaśyakatvāt | tena parastrīgamane veśyāgamane vā nānāvidhadhoṣasadbhāvāt prātipadyena niṣiddhamāṃsabhakṣaṇe 'pi nānāvidhadoṣāḥ santy eva | ata eva śaṅkena prātipadyena niṣiddhamāṃsabhakṣaṇe prāyaścittam uktam: "viḍvarāhagrāmakukkuṭakumbhikabhakṣaṇe dvādaśarātraṃ payaḥ pibet" iti | viḍvarāhādimāṃsabhakṣaṇe niṣedho manunā prātipadyena darśitaḥ |

	kravyādān śakunīn sarvān tathā grāmanivāsinaḥ |

	anirdiṣṭāṃś caikaśaphān ṭiṭṭibhaṃ caiva varjayet ||

	kalaviṅkaṃ plavaṃ haṃsaṃ cakrāṅgaṃ grāmakukkuṭam |

	sārasaṃ rajjudālaṃ ca datyūhaṃ śukaśārike ||

	pratyudān jālapādāṃś ca koyaṣṭinakhaviṣkirān |

	nimajjataś ca matsyādān saunaṃ vallūram eva ca ||

	bakaṃ caiva valākāṃ ca kākolaṃ khañjarīṭakam |

	matsyādān viḍvarāhāṃś ca matsyān eva ca sarvaśaḥ || iti |

kravyaṃ māṃsam, tad attīti kravyādaḥ | ye kravyādāḥ śakunayas tān gṛdhrādīn varjayet | grāmavāsinaḥ śakunayaḥ pārāvataprabhṛtayaḥ, tān api varjayet | anirdiṣṭān ajñātān ajñātāvāntarajātiviśeṣān, mṛgapakṣiṇa iti śeṣaḥ, "ajñātāṃś ca mṛgadvijān" iti yājñavalkyasmaraṇāt | ekaśaphān aśvādīn varjayet | niṣṭhuraśabdabhāṣī pakṣiviśeṣaḥ ṭiṭṭibhaḥ | tathā ca vaijayantyām uktam: "ṭiṭṭibhas tu kaṭkkāṇaḥ(?)" iti | kalaviṅkaś caṭakaḥ | plavo jalakukkuṭaḥ | haṃsaḥ prasiddhaḥ | cakrāṅgaś cakravākaḥ | kukkuṭaḥ prasiddhaḥ | sārasaḥ puṣkarāhvayaḥ | sa ca dīrghagalajaṅgho nīlāṅgaḥ pakṣiviśeṣaḥ | rajjudālo vṛkṣakukkuṭaḥ | dātyūhaḥ kālakaṇṭakaḥ sa ca jalasamīpacaraḥ | śukaḥ prasiddhaḥ | tasya strī śārikā | cañcvā pratyudya bhakṣayantīti pratyudāḥ śyenādayaḥ | jālapādā jālākārapādāḥ | koyaṣṭiḥ kīdṛśa iti cintyaḥ | nakhair vikīrya bhakṣayantīti nakhaviṣkirāḥ cakorādayaḥ | nimajjataś ca matyādāḥ nimajjyanimajjya matsyān bhakṣayantīti tān | sūnā hiṃsāsthānam, tatra hatasya māṃsaṃ saunam | vallūraṃ śuṣkamāṃsam "uttaptaṃ śuṣkamāṃsaṃ syāt tad vallūraṃ triliṅgakam" ity amaraḥ | bakabalāke prasiddhe | kākolaḥ girikākaḥ | vṛddhakāko vā | yo meghaparyantam ākāśārohaṇaṃ līlayā karoti sa ca khañjarīṭaḥ | matsyādān, animajjto 'pi | viḍvarāhāḥ grāmasūkarāḥ | matsyān eva ca sarvaśaḥ sarvaprakārān matsyān varjayet | anantaroktasyāpavādam āha sa eva |

	pāṭhīnarohitāv ādyau niyuktau havyakavyayoḥ |

	rājīvāḥ siṃhatuṇḍāś ca saśalkāś caiva sarvaśaḥ || (MDh 5.16)

pāṭhīno bahudaṃṣṭro matsyaḥ, "sahasradaṃṣṭraḥ pāṭhīnaḥ" ity amaraḥ | rohito raktavarṇaḥ | etau pāṭhīnarohitau havyakavyayor niyuktau niveditau dattau nimantritenādyau bhakṣyāv ity arthaḥ | rājīvāḥ padmavarṇāḥ, rājimanto vā | siṃhatuṇḍāḥ siṃhamukhāḥ | saha śalkaiḥ śuktyākāraiḥ pṛṣṭhabhāgato vartante iti saśalkāḥ | eteṣu siṃhatuṇḍādayaḥ sarvaśaḥ nimantritair animantritaiś ca bhakṣyāḥ | saśalkānāṃ bhakṣyatvaṃ vedādhyayanahīnapuruṣābhiprāyeṇoktam,

	matsyān saśalkān sarvān vai vedādhyāyī vivarjayet |

iti yamasmaraṇāt | devalo 'pi prātipadyena niṣedham āha |

	ulūkakuraraśyenagṛddhrakukkuṭavāyasāḥ |

	cakorakokilau rajjudālakaś cāṣamadgukau ||

	pārāvatakapotau ca na bhakṣyāḥ pakṣiṇaḥ smṛtāḥ ||

ulūko ghūkaḥ | yo 'ntarikṣe caran jalāntarvartinaṃ matsyādikaṃ śyena iva nipatyādatte sa kuraraḥ | cakoraḥ candrikāsvādakaḥ | yaḥ śakunasūcakatvena prasiddho haritapītavarṇaḥ kharvakāya pakṣiviśeṣaḥ sa cāṣaḥ | madguḥ jalakākaḥ "madgus tu jalavāyasaḥ" it vaijayantyām | śeṣāḥ prasiddhāḥ | evaṃ yatra yatra prātipadyena pratiṣedhaḥ smaryate tatra niṣedhavidhim atikramya bhakṣaṇe kṛte pratyavāyo na māṃsamātrabhakṣaṇa ity anusaṃdheyam | ata eva śaṅkhenāpratiṣiddhānāṃ māṃsaṃ bhakṣyam iti darśayituṃ kecana pakṣimṛgāṇām apratiṣiddhānām upalakṣaṇatayoktāḥ |

	tittiriṃ ca mayūraṃ ca lāvakaṃ ca kapiñjalam |

	vārdhrīṇasaṃ vartikaṃ ca bhakṣyam aha yamaḥ sadā ||

lāvakaḥ svajātīyaiḥ saha kalahakārī pakṣiviśeṣaḥ | kapiñjalaḥ śaruḥ | sa ca citravarṇapakṣaḥ | "citrapakṣe śarukapiñjalau" iti vaijayantyām abhidhānāt | vārdhrīṇasaḥ khaḍgākhyo mṛgaḥ "gaṇḍake khaḍgakhaḍginau, vārdhrīṇaso gaṇotsāhaḥ" it tatraivābhidhānāt | vartikaḥ pakṣiviśeṣaḥ | śeṣāḥ prasiddhāḥ | vārdhrīṇasagrahaṇam apratiṣiddhapaśumṛgāṇāṃ pradarśanārtham | ata eva manuḥ |

	śvāvidhaṃ śalyakaṃ godhāṃ khaḍgakūrmaśaśāṃs tathā |

	bhakṣyān pañcanakheṣv āhur anuṣṭrāṃś caikatodataḥ ||

śvāvit śvabhakṣako vyāghraviśeṣaḥ | na tu śalyaḥ, paunaruktyāpatteḥ | śvāvicchabdaḥ śvabhakṣakavyāghraviśeṣe 'pi prasiddhaḥ | ata eva aparārkeṇa "sedhā śvāvit" iti vyākhyāya "sa ca śvabhakṣako vyāghraviśeṣaḥ" ity uktam | śalyakaḥ śalyaḥ, sa ca jalākāsannibhatanūruhaśālī mṛgaviśeṣaḥ | godhā vileśayā īṣannakulasadṛśī | itare prasiddhāḥ | anuṣṭrāṃś caikatodataḥ paśūnāṃ madhye uṣṭravyatiriktān | ekatodataḥ mahiṣameṣaprabhṛtīn bhakṣyān āhur iti saṃbandhaḥ | uṣṭragrahaṇaṃ gavādīnām api pradarśanārtham | ata eva devalaḥ |

	abhakṣyāḥ paśujātīnāṃ gokharoṣṭrāśvakuñjarāḥ |

	siṃho vyāghraś ca śarabhasarpājagarakās tathā ||

	ākhumūṣakamārjāranakulagrāmyasūkarāḥ |

	śvasṛgālavṛkadvīpigolāṅgūlakamarkaṭāḥ || iti |

vyāgha iti pūrvam uktatvāt dvīpiśabdo vyāghraviseṣaparaḥ | golāṅgūlo vānaraviśeṣaḥ | markaṭagrahaṇaṃ pañcanakhānām upalakṣaṇam | ata eva na bhakṣayed ity anuvṛttau manunoktam "sarvān pañcanakhāṃs tathā" iti | sarvān bhakṣyatvena pūrvoktaśvāvicchalyakagodhākhaḍgakūrmaśaśavyatiriktān ity anusaṃdheyam | śaṅkho 'pi bhakṣyamāṃsam āha |

	māhiṣaṃ tv ājam aurabhraṃ mārgaṃ rauravam eva ca |

	bhakṣyamāṃsaṃ samuddiṣṭaṃ yac ca vai pārṣataṃ bhavet ||

	varāhāṃś ca tathā bhakṣyān āhāraṇyanivāsinaḥ ||

urabhro meṣaḥ, tasya māṃsam aurabhram | mṛgo hariṇaḥ tasya māṃsaṃ mārgam | ruruḥ kṛṣṇasāraviśeṣaḥ "rurur mahān kṛṣṇasāraḥ" iti vaijayantyāṃ, tasya māṃsaṃ rauravam | pṛṣataḥ atisthūlabindupramāṇakaśuklavarṇatanūruhakṛtamaṇḍalaśateś citrato hariṇaviśeṣaḥ, tasya māṃsaṃ pārṣatam | tathāraṇynivāsino varāhān bhakṣyān āhety anvayaḥ | evam uktabhakṣymāṃsapratipādakavacanair bhakṣaṇīyeṣu bhakṣaṇamātreṇa pratyavāyo nāstīti gamyate, na tu bhakṣaṇāya prāṇivadhe kṛte 'pīti, prāṇivadham akṛtvā mśṃsārjanasaṃbhavāt (?), "na hiṃsyāt sarvā bhūtāni" it hiṃsāpratiṣedhāc ca,

	yo 'hiṃsakāni bhūtāni hinasty ātmasukheccayā |

	sa jīvaṃś ca mṛtaś caiva na kvacit sukham edhate ||

	sa vasen narake ghore dināni paśuromabhiḥ |

	saṃmitāni durācāro yo hanty avidhinā paśūn ||

iti manu-yājñavalkyasmaraṇāc ca | yat tu manunoktam,

	anumantā viśasitā nihantā krayavikrayī |

	saṃskartā codahartā ca khādakaś caiva ghātakāḥ ||

iti, tatra krayavikrayikhādakāder ghātakatvābhidhānaṃ hantṝṇāṃ kathaṃcit pretakabhūtasya na tūdāsīnasyeti mantavyam, udāsīnasya kathaṃcid api hananakartṛtvābhāvāt | ata eva devalaḥ |

	pañca pañcanakhā bhakṣyāḥ dharmataḥ parikīrtitāḥ |

	godhā kūrvaḥ śaśaḥ śvāvic chalyakaś ceti te smṛtāḥ ||

hiṃsām antareṇa vikrayādyair upādāya pañcanakhāḥ bhakṣyāḥ parikīrtitā ity arthaḥ | yady apy atra pañcagrahaṇam avadhāraṇārtham, tathāpi "śvavidhaṃ śalyakaṃ godhāṃ khaḍgakūrmaśaśāṃs tathā" iti mānave khaḍgamāṃsasya bhakṣyatvābhidhānam aviruddham, bhinnaviṣayatvāt | nityabhojanaviṣayaṃ devalavacanam | mānavaṃ tu śrāddhaviṣaayam,

	khaḍgamāṃsair bhaved annam akṣayyaṃ pitṛkarmaṇi |

iti khaḍgamāṃsasya śrāddhe phalaśrutidarśanāt ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ nityabhojane varjanīyamāṃsaviṣayāṇi**

**atha śrāddhe tṛptyatiśayahetubhūtadravyaviṣayāṇi **

**kānicid vacanāni likhyanta**

tatra manuḥ |

	havir yac cirarātrāya yac cānantyāya kalpate |

	pitṛbhyo vidhivad dattaṃ tat pravakṣyāmy aśeṣataḥ ||

yad dhaviḥ pitṛbhyo vidhivad dattaṃ cirarātrāya kalpate cilakālānusyūtapitṛtṛptaye, yac cānantyāya atyantavirakālānusyūtapitṛtṛptaye kalpate, tathābhūtahavir idānīṃ pravakṣyāmīty arthaḥ, tatra tāvat pratijñātaṃ krameṇa yac cirarātrāya kalpate tad āha sa eva |

	tilair vrīhiyavair māṣair adbhir mūlaphalena vā |

	dattena māsaṃ prīyante vidhivat pitaro nṛṇām ||

tilādicatuṣṭayagrahaṇaṃ grāmyauṣadhīnāṃ saptānām upalakṣaṇārtham | tatra grāmyābhir oṣadhībhiḥ māsaṃ prīyante | tāsāṃ puṣkalānām abhāve kiṃcid annasahitairavādibhir māsaṃ prīyanta ity arthaḥ | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ: "grāmyābhir oṣadhībhir māsaṃ tṛptiḥ, tadalābhe mūlaphalair adbhir vā sahānnenottarās tarpayanti" iti | uttarā mūlaphalāpaḥ, tāḥ sahaiva kiṃcid annena māsaṃ tarpayanti, na kevalā ity arthaḥ | mārkaṇḍeyo 'pi |

	godhūmair ikṣubhir mudgaiḥ satīnaiś caṇakair api |

	śrāddheṣu dattaiḥ prīyante māsam ekaṃ pitāmahāḥ ||

satīnāḥ kalāyāḥ "kalāyas tu satīnakaḥ" ity amaraḥ | caṇakaḥ cartulākāraś caṇakaḥ caṇakaśabdenaiva prasiddhaḥ harimanthkākhyaḥ, "caṇako harimanthakaḥ" iti tenaivābhidhānāt | godhūmādivikāraignyaiḥ (?) śrāddheṣu dattair ekaṃ māsaṃ prīyanta ity arthaḥ | ata eva "haritamudgakṛṣṇamāṣaśyāmākapriyaṅgugodhūmekṣuvikārāṃś ca dadyāt" iti pracetasoktam | dadyāt māsaparyantaṃ pitṛtṛptaye iti śeṣaḥ | evaṃ ca na sakṣād godhūmādayo deyāḥ, kiṃ tu tadvikārā maṇṭakādayaḥ | viṣṇur api: "sākaśyāmākanīvārapriyaṅgumudgair māsaṃ prīyante" iti, mārkaṇḍeyas tu māsaparyantaprītajanakāni śākāni prapañcayati |

	vidāryā cāvarūḍhaiś ca bisaiḥ śṛṅgāṭakais tathā |

	kecukaiś ca tathā kandaiḥ karkandhūbadarair api ||

	pālevatair ārukaiś cāpy akṣoṭaiḥ panasais tathā |

	kākolaiḥ kṣīrakākolais tathā piṇḍālukaiḥ śubhaiḥ ||

	lājābhiś ca sadhānābhiḥ trapuṣor vārubhir bhidaiḥ |

	sarṣapārājaśākābhyām iṅgudai rājajambubhiḥ ||

	priyālāmalakair mukhyauḥ phalgubhiś ca hy alābukaiḥ |

	vetrāṅkurais tālakandaiś cukrikākṣīrikāvacaiḥ ||

	mocaiḥ samocair lakucais tathā vai bījapūrakaiḥ |

	rāgaṣāḍavacoṣyaiś ca trijātakasamanvitaiḥ |

	dattais tu māsaṃ prīyante śrāddheṣu pitaro nṛṇām || iti |

vidārī kṛṣṇavarṇā, bhūkūśmāṇḍaphalam | bisaṃ padmakandoparisthitatantupuñjayuktaṃ bhakṣyāvayavaḥ | śṛṅgāṭakaṃ jalajaṃ trikaṇṭakam | kecukaḥ kharjūrākhyaṃ śākam | kandaḥ sūraṇaḥ | "arśoghnaḥ sūraṇaḥ kandaḥ" ity amaraḥ | badaraṃ badarīphalam | badaryavāntaraviśeṣaḥ karkandhūḥ tatphalaṃ karkandhūśabdenoktam | akṣoṭo girisaṃbhavaḥ pīluḥ | panasaḥ prasiddhaḥ | kākolakṣīrakākolau gauḍadeśe prasiddhau | urvāruḥ svādukarkaṭī | bhidaḥ tiktakarkaṭī | sarṣapaḥ prasiddhaḥ | sarṣapetistrīliṅgatayā nirdeśaḥ chāndasaḥ | rājaśākaṃ rājavṛkṣākhyaṃ śākaṃ kṛṣṇasarṣapa iti yāvat | iṅgudas tāpasataruḥ | rājajambūḥ jambūviśeṣaḥ | priyālo rājādanākhyo vṛkṣaḥ, "rājādanaṃ priyālaḥ syāt" ity amaraḥ | mukhyāny āmalakāni sthūlāmalakāni | phalgūni kṣudrāmalakāni | vetrāṅkuraḥ prasiddhaḥ | tālakandaḥ bhūmyantarnihitatālaprabhavam āragvadhaphalākāraṃ pāṇḍyadeśādau bhakṣyatvena prasiddhaṃ mūlam | cukrikā āmlikā tiṃtriṇī ciñcā iti yāvat | kṣīrikāphalādhyakṣam "rājādanapalādhyakṣe kṣīrakāyām" ity amaraḥ | mocā kadalī, "kadalī vāraṇavusā (?) rambhā mocāṃśumatphalā" iti tenaivābhidhānāt | lakuco likucaḥ | "lakuco likuco ḍahuḥ" ity amaraḥ | sa ca jambīraphalatulyakharvaphalavān gulmaviśeṣaḥ | bījapūro mātuluṅgaḥ "phalapūro bījapūro rucako mātuluṅgakaḥ" ity amaraḥ | padmaphalaṃ padmabījakośaḥ, karṇiketi yāvat | rāgaṣāḍavāḥ pānakaviśeṣāḥ | trijātakaṃ lavaṅgailāpatrāṇāṃ samāhāraḥ | śeṣāṇy atyantaprasiddhāni | matsyapurāṇe 'pi |

	annaṃ tu sadadhikṣīraṃ goghṛtaṃ śarkarānvitam |

	māsaṃ prīṇāti vai sarvān pitṝn ity āha keśavaḥ || iti |

dvimāsādisaṃvatsaragṛptihetubhūtāny āha manuḥ |

	dvau māsau matsyamāṃsena trīn māsān hāriṇena tu |

	aurabhreṇātha caturaḥ śākuneneha pañca vai ||

	chāgamāṃsena ṣaṇmāsān pārṣateneha sapta vai |

	aṣṭāv aiṇeyamāṃsena rauraveṇa navaiva tu ||

	daśamāsāṃs tu tṛpyanti varāhamahiṣāmiṣaiḥ |

	śaśakūrmayos tu māṃsena māsān ekādaśaiva tu ||

	saṃvatsaraṃ tu gavyena payasā pāyasena ca || iti |

hariṇaḥ kuraṅgaḥ, tasya māṃsaṃ hāriṇam | urabhro meṣaḥ, tasya māṃsam aurabhram | śakuniḥ pakṣī, tasya māṃsaṃ śākunam | pṛṣataś citramṛgaḥ tasya māṃsaṃ pārṣatam | eṇī mṛgī tasyā māṃsaṃ aiṇeyam | rurur mahān kṛṣṇasāraḥ tasya māṃsaṃ rauravam | payograhaṇaṃ payovikārāṇām upalakṣaṇam | ata eva viṣṇuḥ: "saṃvatsaraṃ tu payasā tadvikārair vā" iti | yady api pāyasenety atra payoviśeṣaḥ na śrutaḥ, tathāpi gavyapayaḥ saṃnidhānāt tatpayaḥ siddham iti gamyate | yat tu prīṇātīty anuvṛttau paiṭīnasinoktam "pāyasenaṃ tu ṣaṇmāsān" iti, tad agopayaḥsiddhapāyasaviṣayam | dvādaśasaṃvatsaraparyantatṛptikaradravyam āha manuḥ |

	vārdhrāṇasasya māṃsena tṛptir dvādaśavārṣikī | iti |

pitṝṇāṃ bhavatīti śeṣaḥ | vārdhrāṇaso 'tra pāribhāṣiko veditavyaḥ, na tu khaḍgamṛgaḥ, tasyātidīrghakālatṛptikaradravyeṣu manunaiva vakṣyamāṇatvāt | kaḥ punar asau pāribhāṣiko vārdhrāṇasa ity apekṣite viṣṇudharmottaram |

	tripibaṃ tv indriyakṣīṇaṃ yūthasyāgracaraṃ tathā |

	raktavarṇaṃ tu rājendra chāgaṃ vārdhrāṇasaṃ viduḥ || iti |

tribhiḥ mukhena karṇābhyāṃ ca pibatīti vyutpattyā tripibaḥ, atyantalambakarṇaḥ | yady api na karṇābhyāṃ pibati, tathāpi taṭākādigatodakapānasamaye karṇāv api lambitau mukhavaj jalasaṃsparśinau bhavata ity aupacārikas tripibaśabdo yuktaḥ | indriyakṣīṇaḥ saṃbhogākṣamaḥ | raktavarṇagrahaṇaṃ śvetavarṇasyāpi pradarśanārtham |

	tripibaṃ tv indriyakṣīṇaṃ śvetaṃ vṛddham ajāpatim |

	vārdhrāṇasaṃ tu taṃ prāhuḥ yājñikāḥ pitṛkarmaṇi ||

######### 257 MISSING

ttasyā vināśa iti | kāryabhūtāyās tṛpter nityatvāyogāt | tena nityavad atidīrghakālatṛptir vacobhaṅgyā jñāpyata iti mantavyam | ata eva pitṛgītāyāṃ gāthāyām (?) uktam |

	kālaśākaṃ mahāśalkaṃ māṃsaṃ vārdhrāṇasasya ca |

	viṣāṇavarjā ye khaḍgā āsūryaṃ tāṃs tu bhuñjmahe || iti |

sūryo yāvati kāle tiṣṭhati tāvantaṃ kālaṃ kālaśākādipadārthaṃ bhuñjmahe ity arthaḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ śrāddhakāṇḍe **

**pitṛtṛptyatiśayahetubhūtadravyaviṣayāṇi**

**evaṃ prasaktānuprasaktaṃ parisamāpyādhunā prakṛtasya **

**pūrvāhṇakṛtyasya śeṣam ucyate**

tatra mārkaṇḍeyaḥ |

	ahnaḥ ṣaṭsu muhūrteṣu gateṣu tv atha tān dvijān |

	pratyekaṃ preṣayet preṣyān pradāyāmalakodakam ||

dvādaśaghaṭikābhya ūrdhvaṃ nimantritabrāhmaṇānāṃ snānārthaṃ paricārakāṇāṃ hasteṣv āmalakakalkaṃ pradāya nimantritabrāhmaṇebhyaḥ pratyekaṃ dīyatām iti tān dvijān prati brāhmaṇān preṣayed ity arthaḥ | etad āmalakakalkadānaṃ pratiṣiddhatailāsu tithiṣu draṣṭavyam | tāsv apy amāvāsyāvyatiriktāsu deyam "dhātrīphalair amāvāsyāyāṃ na snāyāt" ity āmalakodakasnānasyāpy amāvāsyāyāṃ niṣedhāt | aniṣiddhatailāyāṃ tu dvitīyāditithau snānārthaṃ tailādi deyam ity āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	tailam udvartanaṃ snānaṃ dantadhāvanam eva ca |

	kṛttaromanakhebhyas tu dadyāt tebhyo 'pare 'hani ||

uttaredyuḥ pūrvāhṇe kṛttaromanakhebhyo nimantritebhyas tailādikaṃ snānasādhanaṃ dantadhāvanasādhanaṃ ca kāṣṭhādikaṃ dadyād ity arthaḥ | yat tu pracetasoktam,

	tailam udvartanaṃ snānaṃ dadyāt pūrvāhṇa eva tu \

	śrāddhabhugbhyo nakhaśmaśrucchedanṃ na tu kārayet ||

tatra nakhādicchedananiṣedho niṣiddhakṣurakarmatithiviṣayaḥ | tailādidāne veśeṣam āha devalaḥ |

	tailam utdvartanaṃ snānaṃ snāyīyaṃ ca pṛthagvidham |

	pātrair audumbarair dadyād vaiśvadaivikapūrvakam ||

udumbaraṃ tāmram | vṛddhaśātātapas tu kṛtyāntaram āha: "samūlān darbhān āharet" iti | pitṛkarmārtham iti śeṣaḥ | ata eva yamaḥ |

	samūlas tu bhaved darbhaḥ pitṝṇāṃ śrāddhakarmaṇi | iti |

darbhaḥ kuśaḥ | sa eva śrāddhakarmaṇi mukhyaḥ | tadabhāve kāśādikam āharaṇīyam, "kuśābhāve kuśasthāne kāśān dūrvāṃ vā dadyāt" iti viṣṇusmaraṇāt | kāśādyabhāve tu gobhilenoktam: "barhir upamūlalūnaṃ pitṛbhyas tadalābhe śūkatṛṇaśarabalvajavarjaṃ sarvatṛṇāni" iti | yady api barhiḥśabdas tṛṇamātre vartate | tathāpi tṛṇaviśeṣavihitakuśakāśadūrvāsv eva paryavasyati, tena tadalābha ity asya kuśakāśadūrvālābha ity artho 'vagantavyaḥ | upamūlalūnaṃ mūlasamīpe lūnam | śūkatṛṇaṃ śūkadhānyatṛṇam | śaraḥ puṇḍraḥ, sugandhitṛṇam iti yāvat | balvajāḥ muñjasadṛśāni tṛṇāni | "barhir upamūlalūnam" ity asya "samūlas tu bhaved darbhaḥ" it yamoktena saha vikalpo veditavyaḥ | barhir āharaṇavad yavādyāharaṇam api kartavyam, ata eva purāṇe 'bhihitam |

	upamūlaṃ kṛttamūlān kuśāṃs tatropakalpayet |

	yavāṃs tilān brusīḥ kāṃsyam apaḥśuddheḥ samāhṛtāḥ ||

	pārṇarājatatāmrāṇi pātrāṇi syuḥ samin madhu |

	puṣpadhūpasugandhādi kṣaumasūtraṃ ca mekṣaṇam || iti |

tatra śrāddhdeśa ity arthaḥ | brusīḥ nimantritabrāhmaṇānām upaveśanārthān āsanāni | "vratinām āsanaṃ brusī" ity amaraḥ | nimantritā api brahmacaryādivratagrahaṇād vratina iti tadarthāsane 'pi mukhya evāyaṃ śabdaḥ | kāṃsyaṃ kāṃsyamayaṃ bhājanam | pārṇaṃ parṇamayam | kṣaumasūtraṃ dukūlasūtram | mekṣaṇaṃ kāṣṭhamayī darvī | kāṃsyapārṇarājatatāmrabhājaneṣu yathāsāmarthyam upakalpanam | pratibrāhmaṇaṃ brusyupakalpanaṃ bhājanopakalpanaṃ ca | sugandhādīty atrādigrahaṇād akṣatadīpāñchādanādikaṃ gṛhyate | tilāḥ sati saṃbhave vanyā evopakalpanīyāḥ,

	jartilās tu tilāḥ proktāḥ kṛṣṇavarṇā vane bhavāḥ |

iti satyavratenābhidhānāt | evaṃrūpās tilāḥ śrāddhe grāhyatayā proktā ity arthaḥ | jartilā akṛṣṭabhūmau jātās tilāḥ,

	jartilāś caiva te jñeyā akṛṣṭotpāditās tu ye |

iti tenaivābhidhānāt | jartilānām asaṃbhave tu taditaratilā upakalpanīyāḥ | praśastānām alābhe guṇilopanyāyena jātimātraśālinām upādeyatvāt | yat tv āpastambenoktam,

	aṭavyāṃ ye samutpannā akṛṣṭaphalitās tathā |

	te vai śrāddhe pavitrāḥ syus tilās te na tilās tilāḥ ||

iti, na tilā iti "apaśavo vā anye go'śvebhyaḥ (?), asatraṃ vā etad yad achandomam" ityādivad arthavādamātram iti mantavyam | aparārkeṇa tu na tilās tilā ity etad anyathā vyākhyātam: "grāmyās tilā na tilā tilakāryakarā na bhavatīty arthaḥ" iti | tad asat, teṣām api śrāddhe jartilāsaṃbhave tilakāryakaratvāt | ata eva brahmāṇḍapurāṇe |

	yatis tridaṇḍī karakaṃ rājataṃ pātram eva ca |

	dauhitraḥ kutapaḥ kālaḥ chāgaḥ kṛṣṇājinaṃ tathā ||

	gaurāḥ kṛṣṇās tathāraṇyās tathaiva trividhās tilāḥ |

	pitṝṇāṃ tṛptaye sṛṣṭā daśaite brahmaṇā svayam || iti |

tridaṇḍīti yater viśeṣaṇam | rājatam iti pātrasya | kutapa iti kālasya | gaurās tilāḥ kṣṛṇās tilāḥ āraṇyās tilā iti guṇānuraktarūpeṇa trayaḥ padārthaḥ | evaṃ ca daśasaṃkhyā ghaṭate dauhitrapadaṃ vṛddhaśātātapena vyākhyātam |

	duhitraṃ khaḍgaśṛṅgaṃ tu lalāṭe yat tad ucyate |

	tasya śṛṅgasya yat pātraṃ dauhitram iti kīrtitam ||

kutapapadaṃ tu smṛtyantare vyākhyātam |

	ahno muhūrtā vikhyātāḥ daśa pañca ca sarvadā |

	tatrāṣṭamo muhūrto yaḥ sa kālaḥ kutapaḥ smṛtaḥ || iti |

prakṛtam ucyate; brusīṣu viśeṣam āha manuḥ: "kutapaṃ cāsane dadyāt" iti | kutapaśabdasyānekārthāḥ smṛtyantare darśitāḥ |

	madhyāhnaḥ khaḍgapātraṃ ca tathā nepālakambalam |

	rūpyaṃ darbhās tilā gāvo dauhitraś cāṣṭamaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

	pāpaṃ kutsitam ity āhuḥ tasya santāpakāriṇaḥ |

	aṣṭāv ete yatas tasmāt kutpā iti viśrutāḥ || iti |

kutapaśabdārtheṣv aṣṭasu nepāladeśaprabhavameṣāsilomanirmitakambalalakṣaṇaḥ kutapo manunoktaḥ, tasyaivānanākhye kārye yogyatamatvāt | tadasaṃbhave kambalamātram api pīṭhādyapekṣayā praśastam | āsanopakalpanaṃ bhojanārthopaveśanasthāneṣu kāryam | upakṛptāsaneṣu darbhāstaraṇaṃ ca kāryam,

	āsaneṣu sadarbheṣu vivikeṣūpaveśayet |

iti pūrvopakḷpteṣv āsaneṣūpaveśanavidhānāt | śuddhair āhartṛbhiḥ samāhṛtā ity apāṃ viśeṣaṇaṃ niṣiddhānām apām upakalpanaviṣedhajñāpanārtham | tena,

	durgandhi phenalaṃ varjyaṃ tathā vai palvalodakam |

	na labhed yatra gaus tṛptiṃ naktaṃ yac caiva gṛhyate ||

	yac ca sarvāya notsṛṣṭaṃ yac cābhojyanipānajam |

	tad varjyaṃ salilaṃ tāta sadaiva pitṛkarmaṇi ||

ityādivacananiṣiddhaṃ salilaṃ nopakalpayet | yac ca sarvāya notsṛṣṭaṃ sarvaprāṇyupajīvanārthaṃ kūpādikartṛbhir yan notsṛṣṭaṃ tad api varjyam | nipānaṃ kūpasamīpe kṛtaḥ paśvādīnām udakapānārtho jalāśayaḥ | kāṃśyapārṇarājatatāmraprātrāṇy arghyodakadhāraṇārthāni sarvāṇy upakalpyāni | bhojanārthāni ca mahānti | pārṇabhajanaṃ palāśaparṇavyatiriktaparṇakṛtaṃ bhojanārthaṃ nopakalpanīyam,

	na mṛnmayāni kurvīta bhojane daivapitryayoḥ |

	palāśebhyo vinā na syuḥ pārṇapātrāṇi bhojane ||

iti atra pratiṣedhāt | bhojane iti viśeṣitatvāt, arghyapātre tu nāyaṃ pratiṣedhaḥ | ata eva vaijavāpenoktam |

	khādiraudumbarāṇy arghyapātrāṇi śrāddhakarmaṇi |

	apy aśmamṛnmayāni syur api parṇapuṭās tathā || iti |

puṣpeṣūpakalpanīyāni brahmāṇḍapurāṇe darśitāni |

	śuklāḥ sumanasaḥ śreṣṭhāḥ tathā padmotpalāni ca |

	gandharūpopapannāni yāni cānyāni kṛtsnaśaḥ ||

sumanasaḥ puṣpāṇi | mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe 'pi |

	jātyaś ca sadā dātavyā sallikāḥ śvetayūdhikāḥ |

	jalodbhavāni sarvāṇi kusumāni ca campakam ||

jātyo mālatyaḥ | "sumanā mālatī jātiḥ" ity amaraḥ | śvetayūdhikā hemapuṣpikāvyatiriktagaṇikā, "gaṇikā yūdhikāmbaṣṭhā sā pītā hemapuṣpikā" iti tenaivābhidhānāt | varjyāny api kusumāni brahmāṇḍapurāṇe darśitāni |

	japādikusumaṃ bhaṇḍī rūpikā sakuraṇṭakā |

	puṣpāṇi varjanīyāni śrāddhakarmaṇi nityaśaḥ ||

japā rudrapuṣpam | "rudrapuṣpaṃ japā" ity amaraḥ | ādigrahaṇena japākusumavad raktānāṃ karavīrādikusumānāṃ varjanīyatvam uktam | bhaṇḍī mañjiṣṭhā | 

	mañjiṣṭhā vikasā jiṅgī samaṅgā kālameṣikā | 

	maṇḍūkaparṇī bhaṇḍīrī bhaṇḍī yojanavally api ||

ity amaraḥ | rūpikā prasiddhā | kuraṇṭakaḥ pītapuṣpo 'mlānaḥ | 

	almānas tu mahāsahā |

	tatra śoṇe kuravakas tatra pīte kuraṇṭakaḥ ||

ity amaraḥ | bhaṇḍyādīnāṃ puṣpāṇi varjyāni | śaṅkho 'pi varjyān āha |

	ugragandhīny agandhīni caityavṛkṣodbhavāni ca |

	puṣpāṇi varjanīyāni raktavarṇāni yāni ca ||

caityavṛkṣaḥ śmaśānavṛkṣaḥ | raktapuṣpeṣu pratiprasavaḥ tenaiva darśitaḥ |

	jalodbhavāni deyāni raktāny api viśeṣataḥ | iti |

viṣṇunāpi saha pratiprasavena varjyāny uktāni: "na kaṇṭakijaṃ dadyāt kaṇḍakijam api śuklasugandhi yat tad dadyāt" iti | yat tv aṅgirasoktam: "na jātikusumāni na kadalīpatram" iti, atra kadalīpatraṃ bhojanapātratayā prāptaṃ niṣidhyate | jātikusumaniṣedho na nityaḥ, nityaniṣedhe "jātyaś ca sarvā dātavyāḥ" iti mārkaṇḍeyavacanasyānirviṣayatvāpatteḥ | yad api kratunoktam,

	asurāṇāṃ kule jātā jātiḥ pūrvaparigrahe |

	tasyā darśanamātreṇa nirāśāḥ pitaro gatāḥ || iti |

pūrvaparigrahe pūrvajanmani dehaparigrahāvasare | yady api "trīṇi ha vai yajñasyodarāṇi gāyatrī bṛhaty anuṣṭup, atra hy evāvapanti, ata evodvapanti" ity atra vartamānāpadeśatayārthavādasarūpe vākye 'rthavādatvanirvāhārthaṃ gāyatryādiṣv āvāpodvāpavidhikalpanavad atrāpi nindārthavādarūpe vākye niṣedhavidhiḥ kalpyate | tathāpi pākṣika evāyam api pratiṣedha iti na mārkaṇḍeyavacanaṃ nirviṣayam, kiṃ tv aniṣiddhapuṣpāntarālābhaviṣayam | pratiṣedhavacanadvayaṃ tu tallābhaviṣayam iti mantavyam | matsyo 'pi varjyān āha |

	padvabilvārkaduttūrapāribhadrāṭarūpakāḥ |

	na deyāḥ pitṛkāryeṣu payaś caivāvikaṃ tathā||

duttūraḥ kanakāhvayaḥ | pāribhadro mandāraḥ raktapuṣpastabakayuktaḥ (?) | aṭarūpaḥ siṃhāsyaḥ "vṛṣo 'ṭarūpaḥ siṃhāsyo vāsako vājidantakaḥ" ity amarasiṃhenābhidhānāt | smṛtyarthasāre tu tulasy api varjyetu uktam | tatra mūlaṃ cintyam, prasiddhasmṛtisamuccayeṣu tulasīniṣedhasyādarśanāt | dhūpadravyeṣūpakalpanīyāni viṣṇudharmottare darśitāni |

	dūpeṣu guggulo deyas tathā candanasārajaḥ |

	agarus tv atha karpūraḥ turuṣkaḥ tvak tathaiva ca ||

turuṣkaḥ sallakīvṛkṣatvagādinā saṃpāditaṃ dhūpadravyam | tvak lavaṅgākhyaṃ dhūpadravyam | marīcir api dhūpadravāṇy āha |

	candanāgaruṇī cobhe tamālośarīpadmakam (?) | iti |

uśarīṃ vīraṇākhyagandhatṛṇamūlam | "syād vīraṇaṃ vīrataraṃ mūle 'syośīram astryām" ity amaraḥ | tamālapadmake svaśabdenaiva prasiddhe | viṣṇunā tu varjyadhūpadravyam uktam: "jīvajaṃ ca sarvaṃ na dhūpārtham" iti | jīvajaṃ mṛgaviśeṣādirūpaprāṇijaṃ kastūryādikaṃ dhūpārthaṃ na grāhyam ity arthaḥ | anulepanārtheṣu sugandhidravyeṣūpakalpanīyāni marīcinoktāni |

	karpūrakuṅkumopetaṃ sugandhi haricandanam |

	daivike 'py atha vā pitrye gandhadāne praśasyate ||

viṣṇunāpi: "candanakuṅkumakarpūrāgarupadmakāny anulepanārthāni" iti | dīpārthasnehadraveṣūpakalpanīyāny āha marīciḥ |

	ghṛtād vā tilatailād vā nānyadravyāt tu dīpakam | iti |

anyadravyam atra vasāmedorūpaṃ vivakṣitam, na punar eraṇḍakusumbhāgasībījādisaṃbhavaṃ snehadravyam, ata āha śaṅkhaḥ |

	ghṛtena dīpo dātavyas tv atha vā hy oṣadhīrasaiḥ |

	vasāmedodbhavaṃ dīpaṃ prayatnena vivarjayet ||

vasā pākādinā vibhakto māṃsasnehaḥ | medo hṛdayakamalācchādako māṃsaviśeṣaḥ, pākādinā vibhaktaḥ tadīyasneho 'tra medaḥśabdena lakṣyate | medaḥśabdo 'kārānto 'py asti, medinītyādiṣu darśanāt | ācchādaneṣu phalaviśeṣārtham upakalpanīyāni smṛtyantare darśitāni |

	ācchādanaṃ tu yo dadyād ahataṃ śrāddhakarmaṇi |

	āyuḥ prākāmyam aiśvaryaṃ rūpaṃ ca labhate śubham ||

	kauśeyakṣaumakārpāsaṃ dukūlam ahataṃ tathā |

	śrāddheṣv etāni yo dadyāt kāmān āpnoti puṣkalān || iti |

kauśeyaṃ krimikoṣotthatantujam | kṣaumam atasītvaksaṃbhavatantunirmitam | dukūlam atisūkṣmaṃ vastaṃ prasiddham | ahataṃ kāśyapena nirūpitam |

	ahataṃ yat tv anirmuktam uktaṃ vāsaḥ svayaṃbhuvā || iti |

etat tu na śrāddhe deyam, yato 'nantaram āha sa eva |

	śastaṃ tan māṅgalikyeṣu tāvatkālaṃ na sarvadā | iti |

māṅgalikyaṃ vivāhādikam | śrāddhe deyaṃ tv ahataṃ pracetasoktam |

	īṣaddhautaṃ navaṃ śvetaṃ sadaśaṃ yan na dhāritam |

	ahataṃ tad vijānīyāt sarvakarmasu pāvanam || iti |

īṣaddhautaṃ svenaiveti śeṣaḥ | ata eva vṛddhamanuḥ |

	svayaṃdhautena kartavyāḥ kriyā dharmyā vipaścitā |

	na tu nejakadhautena ..................... || iti |

nejako rajakaḥ | svayaṃgrahaṇād eva nejakanivṛttau siddhāyām api punar nejakapratiṣedho 'nyenāpi brāhmaṇādinā dhautena kriyā kāryeti jñāpanārthaḥ | kṣaumasūtropakalpanaṃ vastrālābhe yajñopavītasthāne dānārtham it mantavyam | mekṣaṇaṃ tu homasādhanatvād upakalpanīyatayoktam, tena yajñiyavṛkṣasaṃbhavaṃ grāhyam | evaṃ dharbhādimekṣaṇāntaṃ sarvam upakalpya karmāṅgasnānaṃ ca tantreṇa kṛtvā śuklaṃ vastraṃ ca paridadhyāt,

	snāto 'dhikārī bhavati daive pitrye ca karmaṇi |

	śrāddhakṛc chuklavāsāḥ syāt ................... || \
iti smaraṇāt ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ śrāddhadinapūrvāhṇakṛtyaśeṣaḥ**

**atha śrāddhadināparāhṇakṛtyam**

tatra mārkaṇḍeyaḥ |

	snātaḥ snātān samāhūtān svāgatenārcayet pṛthak | iti |

snātān dvijān preṣyaiḥ samāhūtān aparāhṇe svagṛham āgatān svāgatenārcayet pṛthak utthāya kṛtāñjaliḥ pṛthak pṛthak svāgatam iti brūyād ity arthaḥ | tathā ca śaṅkhaḥ: "prayato 'parāhṇe śuciḥ śuklavāsā darbhahastaḥ svāgatam iti brūyāt" iti | prayataḥ śucir iti padadvayaṃ bāhyābhyantararūpadvividhaśuddhiyukto yathā syād ity evamartham | aparāhṇaśabdo 'tra dvedhā vibhaktasyāhna āvartanād uparitanabhāge prayuktaḥ, evaṃbhūta evāparāhṇaḥ śrāddhaviṣaye grāhya ity aparāhṇanirṇaye prāg eva samarthitatvāt | atrāpi śayāhnavyatiriktāparāhṇo grāhyaḥ,

	ūrdhvaṃ muhūrtāt kutapāt yan muhūrtacatuṣṭayam |

	muhūrtapañcakaṃ hy etat svadhābhavanam iṣyate ||

iti smṛtyantrānurodhāt | susvāgatam iti brāhmaṇaiḥ prativacanaṃ kartavyam, praśnasyottarāpekṣitatvāt | yamo 'pi |

	tataḥ snātvā nivṛttebhyaḥ pratyutthāya kṛtāñjaliḥ |

	pādyam ācamanīyaṃ ca saṃprayacched yathākramam || \
pratyutthāya kṛtāñjaliḥ svāgatam ity uktvā mārgabhavopahatiśuddhyarthaṃ pādaprakṣālaṇārtham udakam ācamanārtham udakaṃ ca krameṇa prayacched ity arthaḥ | tata ūrdhvaṃ yad yat pitryam anuṣṭhīyate tat tad adakṣiṇaṃ prācīnāvītinā cāśrāddhasamāpter anuṣṭheyam | tathā ca manuḥ |

	prācīnāvītinā sarvam apasavyam atandriṇā |

	pitryam ā nidhanāt kāryaṃ vidhivad dharbhapāṇinā ||

apasavyam apradakṣiṇam ā nidhanād ā śrāddhasamāpteḥ | pitryagrahaṇād apitrye vaiśvadaivike karmaṇi yajñopavītinā pradakṣiṇaṃ ca sarvaṃ kāryam iti dyotitam | svāgatapratyutthānādau tu yajñopavītinā kāryam ityādi sāmānyadharma eva, teṣāṃ śreṣṭhopacāratvena śrāddhāṅgatvābhāvāt | brahmāṇḍapurāṇe 'pi daivike paitṛke ca viśeṣa uktaḥ|

	udaṅmukhas tu devānāṃ pitṝṇāṃ dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ |

	pradadyāt pārvaṇaśrāddhe daivapūrvaṃ vidhānataḥ || iti |

kātyāyano 'pi viśeṣam āha |

	dakṣiṇaṃ pātayej jānuṃ devān paricaran sadā |

	pātayed itaraṃ jānuṃ pitṝn paricaran sadā ||

bodhāyano 'pi |

	pradakṣiṇaṃ tu devānāṃ pitṝṇām apradakṣiṇam |

	devānām ṛjavo darbhāḥ pitṝṇāṃ dviguṇās tathā ||

dviguṇāḥ madhyabhaṅgena dviguṇīkṛtyety arthaḥ | tathā ca śaunakaḥ: "darbhān dviguṇabh (?) ugrān āsanaṃ pradāpayet" iti | āsanagrahaṇaṃ darbhasādhyapitṛkarmopalakṣaṇārtham | daive pitrye ca sādhāraṇadharmāḥ brahmāṇḍapurāṇe darśitāḥ |

	nāprokṣitaṃ spṛśet kiṃcid daive pitrye tathā punaḥ |

	uccāvacāḥ śrāddhadharmāḥ sādhāraṇyāt prakīrtitāḥ ||

uccāvacā anekaprakārāḥ śrāddhadeśasaṃskāragomayānulepanapariśrayaṇādayaḥ | samāgatabrāhmaṇeṣv ācamanārthavārisamarpaṇānantaraṃ yat kartavyaṃ tad āha śaṅkhaḥ |

	saṃmārjitopalipte tu dvāri kurvīta maṇḍalam | iti |

dvāri dvārasamīpe gṛhasyāṅgaṇapradeśa iti yāvat | tathā ca matsyapurāṇe |

	................................... bhavanāsyāgrato bhuvi |

	gomayenopaliptāyāṃ gomūtreṇa tu maṇḍalam || iti |

kartavyam iti śeṣaḥ | gomūtreṇa gomayasahitena | kevalena vakṣyamāṇodakpravaṇādisiddhyasaṃbhavāt | gomayasahitena kathaṃ kartavyam ity apekṣite śaṅkhaḥ |

	udakplavam udīcyaṃ syāt dakṣiṇaṃ dakṣiṇaplavam | iti | 

udīcyaṃ maṇḍalam udakplavam udakpravaṇam | dakṣiṇaṃ maṇḍalaṃ dakṣiṇaplavaṃ dakṣiṇāpravaṇaṃ yathā bhavati tathoktakrameṇa kartavyam ity arthaḥ | maṇḍalakaraṇānantaraṃ kartavyam āha sa eva |

	uttare 'kṣatasaṃyuktān pūrvāgrān vinyaset kuśān |

	dakṣiṇe dakṣiṇāgrāṃs tu satilān vinyased dvijaḥ || iti |

atrāpy uktakrameṇa kartavyam | akṣatagrahaṇaṃ tu puṣpāṇām api pradarśanārtham | ata eva matsyapurāṇe |

	akṣatābhiḥ sapuṣpābhis tad abhyarcyāpasavyavat |

	viprāṇāṃ kṣālayet pādāv abhivandya punaḥ punaḥ ||

apasavyavat pradakṣiṇam, udīcyamaṇḍale prathamaṃ puṣpākṣatābhir arcanaṃ paścād dakṣiṇamaṇḍala iti yāvat | maṇḍalakaraṇaṃ kuśādinyasanaṃ pādaprakṣālanaṃ ca padārthānusamayena kāryam, na tu kāṇḍānusamayena | padārthānusamaye his sarvapadārthānāṃ pradhānapratyāsattir avaiṣamyeṇa bhavati, na kāṇḍānusamaye | tena padārthānusamayenānuṣṭhānam utsargasiddhaṃ bhavati | vacanabalāt kvacit kāṇḍānusamayenānuṣṭhānam upariṣṭād vakṣyate | pādaprakṣālaṇe viśeṣo brahmasiddhāntanirukte darśitaḥ |

	pādyaṃ caiva tathaivāghyaṃ daiva ādau prayojayet |

	śaṃ no devīti mantreṇa pādyaṃ caiva pradāpayet ||

pādyārghyayor daivapūrvakatvābhidhānaṃ nimantraṇādīnāṃ sarvānuṣṭheyānāṃ pradarśanārtham | "śaṃ no devī" iti mantrānte purūravārdravasaṃjñikā viśvedevā idaṃ vaḥ pādyam ity uktvā vaiśvadaivikabrāhmaṇapādayoḥ pādyodakaṃ prakṣipya tatpādaprakṣālanaṃ kuryāt | evaṃ pitrarthabrāhmaṇapādaprakṣālanaṃ "śaṃ no devī" iti mantrānte pitaram uktagotra devadattaśarmann idaṃ te pādyaṃ pitāmahām uktagotra yajñadattaśarmann idaṃ te pādyaṃ pratipitāmahām uktagotra viṣṇumitraśarmann idaṃ te pādyam iti tu viśeṣaḥ | pādyādisamarpaṇe pitṝṇāṃ gotraṃ nāma ca vaktavam,

	nāma gotraṃ pitṝṇāṃ tu prāpakaṃ havyakavyayoḥ |

iti matsenābhidhānāt | havyakavyagrahaṇaṃ samarpyāṇāṃ pādyādīnām api pradarśanārtham | ata eva aśvalāyenārghyasamarpaṇe "pitar idaṃ te arghyaṃ pitāmahedaṃ te arghyaṃ prapitāmahedaṃ te arghyam" ity uktam | evaṃ pādaprakṣālanaṃ svayam eva kuryāt,

	pādaprakṣālanaṃ kuryāt svayam eva vinītavat |

iti yamasmaraṇāt | pādaprakṣālanānantaraṃ kartavyam āha kratuḥ |

	darbhapāṇir dvir ācamya laghuvāsā jitendriyaḥ |

	pariśrite śucau deśe gomayenopalepite ||

	dakṣiṇāpravaṇe samyag ācāntān prayatān śucīn |

	āsaneṣu sadarbheṣu vivikeṣūpaveśayet || iti |

vivikteṣu parasparam asaṃspṛṣṭeṣu deśeṣu | upaveśane kramam āha viṣṇuḥ: "viprān svāgatān svācāntān yathābhūyovidyaṃ kuśottareṣv āsaneṣūpaveśayet" iti | āsaneṣu kambalapīḍhādiṣu (?) kuśottareṣu pūrvam evoparinihitakuśeṣu yathābhūyovidyaṃ vidyātāratamyānusāreṇa vaiśvadevabrāhmaṇapaṅktau ca prathamadvitīyānusāreṇopaveśayed ity arthaḥ | pūrvopakḷpteṣv asatsu smṛtyantare 'bhihitam |

	tatrāsanāni deyāni tilāś caiva kuśaiḥ (?) saha |

	pṛthak pṛthag āsaneṣu tilatailena dīpikāḥ || iti |

sthāpanīyā iti śeṣaḥ | tatra śrāddhadeśe dīpikāsthāpanānantaraṃ bhojanapātrasthāpanasthāneṣu nīvārādipiṣṭaiś caturaśrāṇi maṇḍalāni kuryāt | tathā ca tatraiva |

	maṇḍalāni tu kāryāṇi nīvāraiś caṇakaiḥ śubhaiḥ |

	gauramṛttikayā vātha praṇītenātha bhasmanā ||

praṇītena maṇḍalārthaṃ śubhacūrṇatayā nirmitena | pāṣāṇacūrṇena tu na maṇḍalāni kāryāṇi,

	pāṣāṇacūrṇasaṃkīrṇam āhṛtaṃ tatra varjayet |

iti tatraivābhidhānāt | āhṛtam āpāditam ity arthaḥ | maṇḍalakaraṇānantaraṃ viprān āsaneṣu pūrvoktaprakāreṇopaveśayet | etad api tatraivānantaram uktam |

	pāṇipādamukhārdrāś ca svācāntāḥ susamāhitāḥ |

	teṣv āsaneṣu saṃsthāpyāḥ viprās tena krameṇa tu ||

yena krameṇopaveśane (?) kṛte mānyānatikramaḥ tena krameṇety arthaḥ | ata eva paiṭhīnasiḥ |

	vidyātapo'dhikānāṃ vai prathamāsanam ucyate |

	ekapaṅktyupaviṣṭānāṃ bhojanādi samaṃ smṛtam || iti |

hārīto 'pi |

	saṃtiṣṭhamāneṣv arhatsu yo 'narho 'grāsanaṃ śrayet |

	gṛhṇāti sa malaṃ paṅkter āyuṣā ca vihīyate ||

tasmān mānyānatikrameṇaivāsanaviśeṣaṃ saṃśrayed ity abhiprāyaḥ | pūrvopakḷpteṣv āsaneṣu vipropaveśanapakṣe tūpaviṣṭeṣu dīpikāsthāpanaṃ maṇḍalakaraṇaṃ ca pūrvoktaprakāreṇa kāryam | āsaneṣūpaveśanaprakāram āha yamaḥ: "āsanaṃ (?) saṃspṛśan apasavyena pāṇinā dakṣiṇena brāhmaṇam upasaṃgṛhya samādhvam iti copaveśayet" iti | āsyatām ity uktvā vopaveśayet,

	āsyatām iti tān brūyād āsanaṃ saṃspṛśann api |

iti smṛtyantare 'bhidhānāt | upasaṃgrahaṇasthāne jānvārambhaṇam, pitrarthabrāhmaṇānām upaveśane mantraṃ cāha dharmaḥ |

	jānvārabhya tato devān upaveśya tataḥ pitṝn |

	samastābhir vyāhṛtibhir āsaneṣūpaveśayet ||

jānvārabhya daivikabrāhmaṇān atrāsyatām ity āsaneṣūpaveśya paitṛkabrāhmaṇān jānvārambhaṇapūrvakaṃ "bhūr buvaḥ svaḥ" ity uktvātrāsyatām ity upaveśayed ity arthaḥ | atra purāṇam |

	viprau tu prāṅmukhau devyau dvau tu pūrvaṃ niveśayet |

	uttarābhimukhān viprān trīn pitṛbhyaś ca sarvadā || iti |

daivikau viprau prāṅmukhau sarvadā niveśayet | pitrarthān viprān sarvadā uadaṅmukhān niveśayed ity arthaḥ | dvau trīn iti smṛtyantaroktabrāhmaṇasaṃkhyopalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva yājñavalkyaḥ |

	dvau daive prāk trayaḥ pitrye udag ekaikam eva vā |

	mātāmahānām apy evaṃ tantraṃ vā vaiśvadaivikam ||

prāk prāṅmukhāv upaveśanīyau | udak udaṅmukhā upaveśanīyāḥ | mātāmahānām apy evam ity asyāyam arthaḥ: mātāmahārthabrāhmaṇānām api yathoktasaṃkhyāvikalpo vakṣyamāṇanirdeśasiddho veditavya ity anusaṃdheya iti | tantraṃ vā vaisvadaivikam ity atra vāśabdārthaḥ pratiyogipakṣāntarapradarśanamukhena marīcinā spaṣṭīkṛtaḥ |

	tathā mātāmahaśrāddhaṃ vaiśvadevasamanvitam |

	kurvīta bhaktisaṃpannas tantraṃ vā vaiśvadaivikam || iti |

vaiśvadevasamanvitaṃ mātāmahaśrāddhaṃ bhaktisaṃpannaḥ āvṛtaṃ kurvītety arthaḥ | atra prāptāprāptavivekena vaisvadevam āvṛtaṃ kurvītety uktaṃ bhavati | vaiśvdevetarāṅgopetapradhānāvṛtter nyāyat eva siddhatvāt, vaisvadeve tu tantrāvṛttī pūrvam asiddhe idānīm eva pratipādanīye | etac ca vākyam evaṃ vyākhyeyam, anyathā tantraṃ vā vaiśvadaivikam iti pakṣāntarābhidhānāghaṭanāt | tathā hi pūrvavākye āvṛttipakṣe anukte pakṣāntaratayā tantrābhidhānam anupapannam eva | tantraṃ vā vaiśvadaivikam ity asyāyam arthaḥ: vaiśvadaivikakarmānuṣṭhānaṃ pitṛmātamahaśrāddhadvayārthaṃ tantreṇa vā kartavyaṃ sakṛd vā kartavyam iti | ayaṃ tu tantrānuṣṭhānapakṣaḥ sāṅgayoḥ pitṛmātāmahaśrāddhayoḥ ekaprayogavidhiyojyatve bhavitum arhati, na bhinnaprayogavidhiprayojyatve, "bhinnaprayogavidhiprayojyeṣu padārtheṣ na tantratā" iti tantracintādhyāye pratipaditatvāt | tataś ca tantrapakṣoktyaiva pitṛmātāmahaśrāddhayor ekaprayogavidhiprayojyatvam apy uktam | ekaprayogavidhiprayojyatvaṃ caikādhikārāpūrvasādhakatve bhavati, ekādhikārāpūrvasādhakatvam apy asmād eva vākyād anayor jñāyate | etena caikādhikārāpūrvasādhakatvam anayoḥ pākṣikam iti vāśabdāt jñāyate | tena bhinnādhikārāpūrvasādhakatvam apy astīti vāśabdād evāvagantavyam | tataś ca prathamaṃ paitṛkaśrāddhaṃ saṃkalpaprabhṛti brāhmaṇavisarjanāntaṃ kāryam ity asmād eva vākyāt jñāyate | na ca vācyaṃ bhaktisaṃpanna it vacanāt bhaktyabhāve mātāmahaśrāddhaṃ na kartavyam iti,

	pitaro yatra pūjyante tatra mātāmahā dhruvam |

	aviśeṣeṇa kartavyaṃ viśeṣān narakaṃ vrajet ||

iti smaraṇāt | ata eva śrāddhadvaye 'pi yathāsāmarthyam avaiṣamyeṇa viprasaṃkhyādikaṃ purāṇe darśitam | 

	pañcabhiḥ pañcabhir vipraiḥ dvābhyāṃ dvābhyām athāpi vā |

	śrāddhadvayaṃ tribhir vā syād ekaikenātha vā punaḥ ||

sāṅgapradhānasya pṛthak pṛthag anuṣṭhānapakṣe yadā pitrye śrāddhe dvau viprau daive, pitrye trīn viprān upaveśayet tadā mātāmahaśrāddhe tathaivopaveśayet | yadā tu pitrye śrāddhe ekaṃ vipraṃ daive pitrye caikaṃ vipram upaveśayet, tadā mātāmahaśrāddhe tathaivopavesayet | yadā tu śrāddhadvayasya sahānuṣṭhānapakṣaḥ tadā vaiśvadaivikabrāhmaṇadvayālābhe ekam eva brāhmaṇaṃ śrāddhadvayavaiśvadevārtham upaveśya tadarthapariśiṣṭam annaṃ viśvān devān uddiśya sakṛd eva tyājyam, yadā tu śrāddhadvayārtham ekasyaiva brāhmaṇasya lābhaḥ tadāvargadvayārtham upaveśya śrāddhadvayāṅgabhūtavaiśvadaivikārtham annaṃ pātre samuddhṛtya vaiśvadaivikabrāhmaṇasthāne vidhāya pūrvavat tyājyam | na tu pitryaśrāddhe mātāmahaśrāddhe brāhmaṇasaṃkhyādinā vaiṣamyaṃ sarvathā kāryam iti vacanasya tātparyārthaḥ pratyetavyaḥ | evaṃ śrāddhadvaye upavesanāyoktasaṃkhyānusāreṇaiva nimantraṇakāle brāhmaṇanimantraṇaṃ kāryam, tathā ca vṛddhavasiṣṭho 'pi |

	śrāddhadvayaṃ kariṣyaṃs tu daśa vā caturo 'pi vā |

	trīn vā nimantrayed viprān dvāv ekaṃ brahmavādinam || iti |

upaveśanāyodyuktān brāhmaṇān praty āha yamaḥ |

	dakṣiṇāsaṃsthā āsīraṇn aspṛśantaḥ parasparam | iti |

dakṣiṇāsaṃsthā ity asya na dikṣiṇāsaṃsthāparatvam, kiṃ tu prāksaṃsthāparatvam avaseyam | prāksaṃsthatve 'bhidhitsite 'pi dakṣiṇāsaṃsthety uktiḥ pitrarthabrāhmaṇaviṣayatāṃ dyotayituṃ kṛtā | ata eva smṛtyantaram |

	paścārdhāt samupakramya prācyāṃ niṣṭhā yathā bhavet |

	dakṣiṇāsaṃsthatā hy eṣā pitṝṇāṃ śrāddhakarmaṇi || iti |

niṣṭhā samāptiḥ | vaisvadevikabrāhmaṇāṃs tu praty āha bodhāyanaḥ: "pradakṣiṇaṃ tu daivānām" iti | daivānāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ dakṣiṇādikprakramam udagapargaṃ (?) ca yathā bhavati tathā āsīrann ity arthaḥ | ubhayārthabrāhmaṇān prati smṛtyantare 'bhihitam |

	pavitrapāṇayaḥ sarve te ca maunavratānvitāḥ |

	ucchiṣṭocchiṣṭasaṃsparśaṃ varjayantaḥ parasparam || iti |

te viprāḥ sarve devārthāḥ pitrarthāś ca pavitrapāṇayo maunavratānvitāḥ prasādasaṃbhavaṃ parasparam ucchiṣṭocchiṣṭasaṃsparśaṃ varjayantaḥ ā bhojanasamāpter varterann ity arthaḥ | caśabdāc chrāddhakartāpi maunavratānvito varteteti gamyate | maunavratānvayasya kvacid apavādam āha yamaḥ |

	brahmodyāś ca kathāḥ kuryuḥ pitṝṇām etad īpsitam | iti |

paiṭhīnasir apy upaveśanāyodyuktabrāhmaṇān praty āha |

	nāniyukto 'grāsanaṃ gacchet paṅktyā harati duṣkṛtam | iti |

atrāsyatām iti śrāddhakartrā na niyukto yo 'sāv aniyuktaḥ | agrāsanaṃ prathamāsanam | anupaviṣṭadaśāyām api parasparasaṃsparśo yathā na bhavati tathā vartitavyam ity āha gautamaḥ |

	parasparśe bhavet pāpam ekapaṅktiniyogataḥ |

	hīnavṛttādipaṅktau tu yuktaṃ tasmād dvivecanam || iti |

atra yamaḥ |

	bhikṣuko brahmacārī vā bhojanārtham upasthitaḥ |

	upaviṣṭeṣv anuprāptaḥ kāmaṃ tam api bhojayet || iti |

bhikṣuko yatiḥ | tathā ca chāgaleyaḥ |

	pūjayec chrāddhakāle 'pi yatiṃ sabrahmacāriṇam |

	viprān uddharate pāpāt pitṝn mātṛgaṇān api ||

vṛddhaśātātapo 'pi |

	ātithyarahite śrāddhe bhuñjate ye budhā dvijāḥ |

	vṛthā tenānnapākena kākayoniṃ vrajanti te || iti |

ātithyarahite atithilakṣaṇalakṣitaviprāgamane 'pi tatpūjārahite | tasmād upaviṣṭabrāhmaṇaiḥ saha saty avakāśe tatsamīpe bhikṣuko brahmacārī atithiś ca pitrarthaviprānupraveśenaiva  bhojayitavyaḥ | tathā ca purāṇe nimantritabrāhmaṇabhojanaṃ vidhāyābhihitam |

	śeṣān vittānusāreṇa bhojayed anyaveśmani | iti |

śeṣān nimantritavyatiriktān atithiprabhṛtīn | etac cātithibhojanam atithilakṣaṇalakṣite āgate sati draṣṭavyam, na punaḥ "kākayoniṃ vrajanti te" it doṣaśravaṇāt kalpayitvāpy atithiḥ kartavyaḥ | yas tv atithilakṣaṇahīno bhojanayācanādinā śrāddhavighnaṃ karoti tasya doṣam āha hārītaḥ |

	caturṇāṃ duṣkṛtaṃ harati brāhmaṇo vighnakārakaḥ |

	annasyānnapateḥ paṅkter bhojanākāṅkṣiṇāṃ tathā || iti |

bhojanākāṅkṣiṇaḥ kṛte srāddhe bhojanākāṅkṣiṇaḥ | śrāddhakartur bāndhavā iti yāvat |

**iti smrticandrikāyāṃ nimantritabrāhmaṇopaveśanam**

**athāvāntarasaṃkalpādikṛtyam**

tatra purāṇam |

	śrāddhabhūmau gayāṃ dhyātvā dhyātvā devaṃ gadādharam |

	tābhyāṃ caiva namaskṛtya tataḥ śrāddhaṃ pravartayet ||

śrāddhāvāntarasaṃkalpaṃ kuryād ity arthaḥ | atrāvāntarasaṃkalpaḥ upaviṣṭabrāhmaṇānujñālābhārtham, tathā ca tatraivoktam |

	ubhau hastau samau kṛtvā jānubhyām antare sthitau |

	sapraśrayaś copaviṣṭān sarvān pṛcchet dvijottamān ||

namaskārāñjalikaraṇād ubhau hastau samau jānvor antare yathā sthitau syātāṃ tathā kṛtvā sapraśrayaḥ namaskārāñjalibandhanādivinayasaṃpanno nimantritān upaviṣṭān dvijottamān sarvān pṛcched ity anvayaḥ | kathaṃ pṛcchet kathaṃ ca tair uttaraṃ deyam ity apekṣite tatraivoktam |

	śrāddhaṃ kariṣye ity evaṃ pṛcched viprān samāhitaḥ |

	kuruṣveti ca tair ukto dadyād darbhāsanaṃ tadā || iti |

darbhāsanadānāt pūrvam "devatābhyaḥ pitṛbhyaś ca" iti mantraḥ trir āvartanīyaḥ | tathā ca brahmāṇḍapurāṇe |

	evatābhyaḥ pitṛbhyaś ca tathā yogibhya eva ca |

	namaḥ svadhāyai svāhāyai nityam eva bhavatv iti ||

	ādyāsane tu śrāddhasya trir āvṛttaṃ japet sadā |

	paṭhyamānam idaṃ śrutvā śrāddhakāla upasthite ||

	pitaraḥ kṣipram āyānti rākṣasāḥ pradravanti ca ||

caśabdād asurāḥ piśācāḥ pradravantīti sūcitam | rākṣasādīnām apanuttaye kartavyāntaram āha nigamaḥ: "apahatā iti tilān vikiret" iti | 

	apahatā asurā rakṣāṃsi piśācā ye kṣayanti pṛthivīm anu |

	anyatreto gacchantu yat traiṣāṃ (?) gataṃ manaḥ ||

iti mantraliṅgād asurādīnām apahatyartham anena mantreṇa tilavikiraṇaṃ kartavyam iti gamyate | śrāddhe daivapūrvakaṃ sarvam anuṣṭhānaṃ rākṣasādyapanuttaye kartavyam ity āha kratuḥ |

	sadaivaṃ bhojayec chrāddhaṃ tatpūrvaṃ ca pravartayet |

	anyathā hy avalumpanti sadaivāsurarākṣasāḥ ||

sadaivaṃ śrāddhaṃ vaiśvadaivikakarmopetam | sadaiva sarvadaiva | manur api |

	devakāryād dvijātīnāṃ pitṛkāryaṃ viśiṣyate |

	daivaṃ hia pitṛkāryasya pūrvam āpyāyanaṃ smṛtam ||

	teṣām ārakṣabhūtaṃ tu daivaṃ pūrvaṃ niyojayet |

	rakṣāṃsi vipralumpanti śrāddham ārakṣavarjitam || iti |

devakāryāt pitṛkāryaṃ viśiṣyate, devakāryasyāṅgatvāt pitṛkāryasya pradhānatvād ity abhiprāyaḥ | pūram āpyāyanaṃ daivaṃ karma pūrvānuṣṭheyaṃ pitṛkāryasyopabṛṃhakam upakāri tadaṅgam iti yāvat | evaṃ ca kuruṣvety anujñānantaraṃ "devatābhyaḥ pitṛbhyaś ca" iti mantram uktvā "apahatāḥ" iti mantreṇa śrāddhabhūmau tilān vikīrya prathamaṃ (?) vaiśvadaivikabrāhmaṇāsanārthaṃ darbhāsanaṃ dadyād ity anuṣṭhānakramo veditavyaḥ | darbhāsanadānaṃ ca brāhmanahaste apa āsicya kāryam,

	pāṇiprakṣālanaṃ datvā viṣṭarārthān kuśān api |

	āvāhayed anujñāto viśve devāsa ity ṛcā ||

iti yājñavalkyasmaraṇāt | viṣṭarārthān kuśān āsanārthān kuśān | yady api pāṇiprakṣālanārtham udakaṃ brāhmaṇahaste datvā viṣṭarārthān kuśān api tatraiva datvā āvāhayed iti śabdabalāt pratibhāti | tathāpi viṣṭarārthān kuśān āsane datveti viṣṭarārthapadasāmarthyād arthaḥ pratyetavyaḥ | ata eva pracetāḥ |

	darbhāṃś caivāsane dadyān na tu pāṇau kadācana | iti |

yat tu tenoktam,

	devānām ṛjavo darbhāḥ pradātavyāḥ pṛthak pṛthak |

	dharmo 'sīty atha mantreṇa gṛhṇīyus te tu tān kuśān || iti |

tasyāyam arthaḥ: pūrvopakḷptāsaneṣūpaviṣṭā āsanāntarān ākāṅkṣā api dharmo 'sīti mantram uccārya tān kuśān apy āsanārthatayā manasā svīkuryuḥ, na tu pāṇineti | ato na pūrvāparavirodhaḥ | devasvāmināpy avirodhārtham evam uktam: "pāṇau dharmadānapratiṣedha āsanāstarṇārthadarbhaviṣayaḥ, mantreṇa grahaṇavidhānasāmarthyād yājñavalkyavacanāc ca viṣṭarārthā darbhāḥ pāṇāv eva deyāḥ" iti, tad ayuktam, āsanāstaraṇārthadarbhāṇām āsane prakṣeptavyānāṃ haste dānāprasaktes tatra pratiṣedhānavakāśāt,

	āsane cāsanaṃ dadyād vāme vā dakṣiṇe 'pi vā |

iti viṣṭarārthadarbhāṇām āsane nidhānavidhāyakādipurāṇavacanaviruddhatvāc ca | atra vāma iti pitrarthabrāhmaṇāsanadānaviṣayam | dakṣiṇam iti devārthabrāhmaṇāsanadānaviṣayam | tathā cānantaram uktaṃ tatraiva |

	pitṛkarmaṇi vāme vai daivakarmaṇi dakṣiṇe | iti |

vāme āsanasya vāmabhāge | dakṣiṇe dakṣiṇabhāge | dauvikakarmaṇi yavasahitaṃ darbhāsanaṃ dadyāt, "devānāṃ sayavā darbhāḥ" iti kāṭhake 'bhidhānāt | āsanasya dakṣiṇe bhāge purūravārdravasaṃjñakānāṃ viśveṣāṃ devānām idam āsanam iti darbhāsanaṃ dadyāt | tathā ca ślokasaṃgrahakāraḥ |

	akṣayyāsanayoḥ ṣaṣṭhī dvitīyāvāhane smṛtā |

	annadāne caturthī syāt śeṣāḥ saṃbuddhayaḥ smṛtāḥ || iti |

darbhāsanadānānantaraṃ gadyasaṃgrahakāraḥ: "tataḥ punar apo datvā daive kṣaṇaḥ kriyatām iti kartā, oṃ tatheti vipro brūyāt | prāpnotu bhavān iti kartā punar brūyāt | prāpnavānīti vipraḥ punar brūyād iti | etat tu nimantraṇaṃ brāhmaṇahastam aṅguṣṭhavyatiriktaṃ gṛhītvā kartavyam,

	niraṅguṣṭhaṃ gṛhītvā tu viśvān devān samāhvayet |

iti purāṇe 'bhidhānāt | niraṅguṣṭhaṃ gṛhītvā nimantraṇe kṛte saty anantaraṃ viśvān devān samāhvayed ity arthaḥ | āvāhanaprakāram āha yamaḥ |

	yavahastas tato devān vijñāpyāvāhanaṃ prati |

	āvāhayed anujñāto viśvedevāsa ity ṛcā ||

	viśvedevāḥ śṛṇutemaṃ mantraṃ japtvā tato 'kṣatān |

	oṣadhaya iti mantreṇa vikiret tu pradakṣiṇam || iti |

śrāddhakartā gṛhītayavaḥ purūravārdravasaṃjñakān viśvān devān āvāhayiṣyāmīti viśeṣanāmnā sāmānyanāmnā ca devānām āvāhanaṃ vaiśvadevabrāhmaṇebhyo vijñāpya tair āvahayety anujñāto "viśvedevasa āgata" ity anayā ṛcā viśvān devān brāhmaṇeṣv āvāhya yavān brāhmaṇasya dakṣiṇapade savyapāde dakṣiṇajānuni savyajānuni dakṣiṇe 'ṃse savye 'ṃse śirasi ca samāropya brāhmaṇeṣu viśvān devān āgatān dhyātvā "viśve devāḥ śṛṇuta" iti mantraṃ japitvā pradakṣiṇaṃ dakṣiṇapādādimastakāntam "oṣadhayaḥ pratimodadhvam" iti mantreṇākṣatān vikiret āropayed ity arthaḥ | evam ukto yavākṣatāropaprakāraḥ pracetasā puṣpāropaṇam udāhṛtya darśitam |

	pādaprabhṛti mūrdhāntaṃ devānāṃ puṣpapūjanam | iti |

anujñāpanānujñānaprakāraḥ kātyāyanena sāmānyanāmnā darśitaḥ: "viśvān devān āvāhayiṣyāmīti pṛcchaty āvāhayety anujānāti" iti | viśeṣanāmnānujñāpanaprakāras tu "purūravārdravasaṃjñakān" ity evaṃrūpaḥ svayam ūhyaḥ | 

	kratur dakṣo vausḥ satyaḥ kālaḥ kāmas tathaiva ca |

	dhuriś ca rocanaś caiva tathā caiva purūravaḥ ||

	ārdravaś ca daśaite tu viśve devāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ||

śrāddheṣu vibhajyeti śeṣaḥ | tathā ca śaṅkhaḥ |

	iṣṭiśrāddhe kratur dakṣaḥ saṃkīrtyau vaiśvadaivike |

	nāndīmukhe satyavasū kāmye tu dhurilocanau ||

	purūravārdravau caive pārvaṇe samudāhṛtau |

	naimittke kālakāmāv evaṃ sarvatra kīrtayet || iti |

iṣṭiśrāddhaṃ yāgādikarmāṅgam, śrautasmārtakarmaṇām ādhānasomayāgapuṃsavanasīmantādīnām ādau tadaṅgatvenānuṣṭhīyamānaṃ śrāddham iti yāvat |

	niṣekakāle some ca sīmantonnayane tathā |

	jñeyaṃ puṃsavane śrāddhaṃ karmāṅgaṃ vṛddhivat kṛtam ||

iti karmāṅgaśrāddhalakṣaṇam abhidadhatā pāraskareṇaiva vṛddhivat kṛtam ity abhidhānāt karmāṅgaśrāddhaṃ vṛddhiśrāddhād anyad iti darsitam | nāndīmukhaṃ nāndīmukhasaṃjñakapitṛdevatākaṃ vṛddhisrāddham iti yāvat,

	evaṃ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya vṛddhau nāndīmukhān pitṝn |

	yajeta ......................... ||

iti yājñavalkyena vṛddhisrāddhe nāndīmukhasaṃjñakapitṝṇāṃ devatātvena vidhānāt | vṛddhiśrāddhaṃ ca vṛddhavasiṣṭhena nirūpitam |

	putrajanmavivāhādau vṛddhiśrāddham udāhṛtam | iti |

putrajanmavivāhādau kriyamāṇam ābhyudayikaṃ śrāddhaṃ vṛddhiśrāddham iti vyapadiśyata ity arthaḥ | ādiśabdena garbhādhānapuṃsavanasīmantavyatiriktānām annaprāśanacūḍākaraṇādisaṃskārakarmaṇāṃ saṃgrahaṇam, garbhādhānapuṃsavanasīmanteṣu kriyamāṇābhyudayikaśrāddhasya karmāṅgaśrāddhakoṭipraviṣṭatvāt | kāmyaṃ phalakāmanayānuṣṭheyaṃ mahalayādiśrāddham,

	putrān āyus tathārogyam auśvaryam atulaṃ tathā |

	prāpnoti pañcame datvā śrāddhaṃ kāmāṃś ca puṣkalān ||

iti pañcamapakṣe kanyāgate sūrye mahālayākhyaśrāddhasya putrādikāmyaphalasādhakatvasmaraṇāt | pārvaṇaśrāddhaṃ sarvaśrāddhaprakṛtibhūtam amāvāsyāśrāddham | tathā ca śātātapaḥ |

	darśaśrāddhaṃ tu yat proktaṃ pārvaṇaṃ tat parkīrtitam | iti |

	ekoddiṣṭaṃ tu yac chrāddhaṃ tan naimittikam ucyate |

itivacanān naimittikapadenātraikoddiṣṭaśrāddham uktam iti yady api pratibhāti, tathāpi tadvacanottarārdhe,

	tad apy adaivaṃ kartavyam ayugmān āśayed dvijān |
