iti pūrvārdhoktaikoddiṣṭaśrāddhe vaiśvadaivikaniṣedhena tatra kālakāmasaṃjñayā viśveṣāṃ devānāṃ nirdeśaḥ kārya iti vidhyasaṃbhavāt yogarūḍhyā pratīyamānam ekoddiṣṭaṃ hitvā nimitte bhavaṃ naimittikam iti yogam āśritya naimittikapadena navānnalābhādinimitte sati pitṛbhyo bhaktyā kriyamāṇaṃ śrāddham uktam ity avagantavyam | atha vā, naimittikapadenaikoddiṣṭābhidhāyakena sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ lakṣaṇayā nirdiśyate, sapiṇḍīkaraṇe ekoddiṣṭasyāpi sadbhāvāt | evaṃ ca, sapiṇḍīkaraṇe viśveṣāṃ devānām āvāhanārthaṃ kālakāmasaṃjñayā nirdeśaḥ kāryaḥ | "evaṃ sarvatra kīrtayet" evam uktarītyā sarvaśrāddheṣu nāmagrahaṇasthāne kīrtayed ity arthaḥ | ādipurāṇe viśeṣanāmāni darśitāni |

	viśvedevau kratur dakṣaḥ sarvāsv iṣṭiṣu kīrtitau |

	nityaṃ nāndīmukhaśrāddhe vasusatyau ca paitṛke ||

	navānnalambhane devau kālakāmau sadaiva hi |

	api kanyāgate sūrye śrāddhe ca dhurilocanau ||

	purūravārdravau caiva viśvedevau ca pārvaṇe || iti |

sarvāsv iṣṭiṣu sarveṣu karmāṅgaśrāddheṣu navānnalambhane paitṛke navannalābharūpanimitte sati, navānnabhojanopakramāt pūrvaṃ pitṛbhaktyā navānnena kriyamāṇaśrāddhavat | tac ca nimittādhikāreṇa kriyamāṇānāṃ viśvedevasamanvitānāṃ śrāddhānām upalakṣaṇārtham | kanyāgate sūrye śrāddhe putrādiphalakāmanayā kriyamāṇamahālayākhya ity arthaḥ | evaṃ ca sarvakāmyaśrāddhopalakṣaṇatayoktam | pārvaṇe amāvāsyāyāṃ kriyamāṇe pārvaṇaśrāddhe iti | kratudakṣasatyādīnāṃ ca dakṣaprajāpater duhitari viśvākhyāyāṃ lokaviśrutāyām utpattiḥ samabhūd ity utpattim api jñātvā āvāhanaṃ kāryam | ata evaiṣām utpattiḥ purāṇe 'bhihitā |

	dakṣasya duhitā sādhvī viśvā nāma pariśrutā |

	tasyāḥ putrā mahātmāno viśve devā iti śrutāḥ ||

evam uktotpattir āvāhanasamaye jñātavyety abhiprāyaḥ | ata eva kratudakṣādisaṃjñāṃ dakṣaduhitur utpattiṃ ca ye na viduḥ teṣām anukalpam āha śaṅkhaḥ |

	nāma caiva tathotpattiṃ na vidur ye dvijātayaḥ |

	ślokam etaṃ paṭheyus te brāhmaṇānāṃ samīpagāḥ ||

	āgacchantu mahābhāgā viśvedevā mahābalāḥ |

	ye hy atra vihitāḥ śrāddhe sāvadhānā bhavantu te || iti |

āgacchantu mahābhāgā iti mantraṃ vaiśvadaivikabrāhmaṇasamīpasthāḥ "viśve devāḥ śṛṇutemam" iti mantrajapānantaraṃ japeyur ity arthaḥ | tathā ca purāṇam |

	tathā mantraṃ japen maunī viśvedevāsa āgata |

	viśvedevāḥ śṛṇuteti dvitīyaṃ tadanantaram ||

	tṛtīyaṃ tu japen mantram āgacchantv ity ataḥ param || iti |

viśvedevāsa ity anayā ṛcā prathamam āvāhya tadanantaraṃ viśvedevāḥ śṛṇuteti mantraṃ japed ity anvayaḥ | yady api karmāṅgaśrāddhādiṣu na kvāpi daśa viśvedevā devatātvena smṛtipurāṇābhyām abhihitāḥ, kiṃ tu dvai dvāv ekaikasmin śrāddhe devatātvenokto (?) | tathāpy āvāhanādau purūravārdravasaṃjñakān viśvān devān āvāhayiṣyāmīty evaṃ bahuvacanāntatayaiva prayogaḥ kāryaḥ "viśvān devān āvāhayiṣyāmīti niraṅguṣṭhaṃ gṛhītvā viśvān devān samāhvayet" ityādismṛtipurāṇeṣu bahuvacanāntatayaiva prayogadarśanāt | yathā ekasmin pitari pitāmahe prapitāmahe vā āvāhanādisarvopacāreṣu pitaraḥ pitāmahāḥ prapitāmahā idaṃ va āsanam ityādibahuvacanānto 'pi prayoga pūjārthaṃ yathā nānupapannaḥ tathā dvayor api pūjārthaṃ bahuvacanāntaprayogo yukta eva | vaiśvadaivikabrāhmaṇānām ekatve 'pi na pratibrāhmaṇam āvāhanāvṛttiḥ, sakṛdāvāhanenaivānekabrāhmaṇādhiṣṭhānadevatādhyāsasaṃbhavāt | āvāhanād ūrdhvaṃ tu pratibrāhmaṇaṃ devatādhyāsāt brāhmaṇabhede sati tadupādhito devatāyā api bhedo bhavati, tenāvāhanottarakāle yad yad devatārādhanaṃ kriyate yavāropaṇādi saṃnipatyopakārakaṃ tatpuroḍāśapradānādivat pratibrāhmaṇam āvartanīyam, saṃnipatyopakārakeṣv āvṛttiṃ vinā brāhmaṇāntare kāryāsiddheḥ | "viśvedevāḥ śṛṇutemam" iti mantrajapas tv āvāhanottarakāle kriyamāṇo 'pi nāvartate, sakṛj japenaiva japasādhyādṛṣṭasiddheḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyām avāntarasaṃkalpādivaiśvadaivikāvāhanāntakṛtyam**

**atha vaiśvadaivikārcanavidhiḥ**

tatra yājñavalkyaḥ |

	yavair anvavakīryātha bhājane sapavitrake |

	śan no devyā apaḥ kṣiptvā yavosīti yavāṃs tathā || iti |

ayam arthaḥ: vaiśvadaivikabrāhmaṇayoḥ pādādyaṅgeṣu yavān samāropya "viśvedevāḥ śṛṇuta" ityādikaṃ japitvā arghyabhājane dve uttāne nidhāya tatraikaikasmin bhājane dvidarbham ekaikaṃ pavitraṃ prāgagram udagagraṃ vā nidhāya "śan no devīr abhiṣṭaye" ity ṛcā pratipātraṃ jalaṃ niṣicya,

	yavo'si dhānyarāj tvaṃ vāruṇo mudhusaṃyutaḥ (?) |

	nirṇodaḥ sarvapāpānāṃ patitram ṛṣibhiḥ kṛtam ||

iti mantreṇa yavān pratipātraṃ prakṣipet | tathānyad api gandhādikaṃ kṣiped iti | atrādyapādasyārtho matsyapurāṇe spaṣṭam uktaḥ |

	viśvān devān yavaiḥ puṣpair abhyarcyāsanapūrvakam |

	pūrayet pātrayugmaṃ tu sthāpy darbhapavitrake || iti |

pracetasā tv antyapādatrayasyārthaḥ spaṣṭam uktaḥ |

	ekaikasyāpi viprasya arghyaṃ pātre vinikṣipet |

	yavosīti yavān kṣiptvā gandhapuṣpaiḥ supūjitam ||

arghyam arghyārthaṃ jalam, tad ekaikasya viprasya ekaikasmin pātre mantrāvṛttyā vinikṣipet, tadaiva yavān kṣiptvā gandhapuṣyaiḥ supūjitaṃ kuryād ity arthaḥ | arghyapātre viśeṣam āha kātyāyanaḥ: "sauvarṇarājataudumbarakhaḍgamaṇimayānām anyatameṣu yāni vidyante patrapuṭādiṣu vā" iti | vaijavāpo 'pi |

	rājatāni praśastāni pitrye haimāi daivike |

	api vā tāmrapātrāṇi daive pitrye 'rghyakarmaṇi ||

uttarārdhe 'pi praśastānīty anuṣajyate | rājatāni tu pātrāṇi daive ninditāni, tathā ca rājataṃ pātram adhikṛtya matsyenoktam |

	śivanetrodbhavaṃ yasmād atas tat pitṛvallabham |

	amaṅgalaṃ tad yatnena devakāryeṣu varjitam ||

śivanetrodbhavaṃ śivanetrrajalaprabhavam, tathā ca śrutiḥ: "so 'rodīd yad arodīt tad rudrasya rudratvaṃ yad aśrv aśīyata tad rajataṃ hiraṇyam abhavat" iti | amaṅgalaṃ tad ity atrāśruprabhavatvād ity abhiprāyo 'vaseyaḥ | arghyapātrāntardhāyakapavitre pratyarghyapātraṃ bhedena kārye iti caturviṃśatimate 'bhihitam: 

	dve dve śalāke devānāṃ pātre kṛtvā payaḥ kṣipet | iti | 

darbhādiṣu sāgreṣu śalākāśabdo vartate | dve dve iti vīpsayā pratipātraṃ dve dve śalāke nidhātavye iti darśitam | pavitrakaraṇaprakāram āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	pavitre stha iti mantreṇa dve pavitre ca kārayet |

	anantargarbhe kuśacchinne kauśe prādeśasaṃmite ||

kuśachinne kuśam antardhāya chinne kauśe kuśamaye pavitre stha iti mantreṇa "pavitre stho vaṣṇavī (?) | vāyur vāṃ manasā punātu" iti mantreṇa | yajñapārśvo 'pi |

	oṣadhim antare kṛtvāṅguṣṭhāṅgulivarvaṇoḥ |

	chindyāt prādeśamātraṃ tu pavitraṃ viṣṇudaivatam ||

	na nakhena na kāṣṭhena na lohena na mṛnmayāt |

	nakhena tu bhaved vyādhiḥ kāṣṭhenārtho na sidhyati ||

	āyasena bhaven mṛtyuḥ mṛnmaye kalaho dhruvam || iti |

gandhapuṣpaiḥ supūjitakaraṇāntaraṃ gārgyaḥ |

	svāheti caiva devānāṃ homakarmaṇy udāharet |

homaśabdo 'tra tyāgasadbhāvasāmānyād dāne vartate | tataś cāyam arthaḥ: devānām arghyadānakarmaṇi kariṣyamāṇatayā prastute devebhyo 'rghyaṃ nivedayituṃ svāhety udāharet | "svāhārghyam" ity uccārya viprasamīpe arghyapātraṃ sthāpayed ity arthaḥ | sthāpanānantaraṃ yājñavalkyaḥ |

	yā divyā iti mantreṇa hasteṣv arghyaṃ vinikṣipet | iti |

"yā divyā āpas suhavā bhavantu" iti mantreṇa mantrānte purūravārdravasaṃjñikā viśvedevā idaṃ vo arghyam ity uktvā vaiśvadaivikabrāhmaṇasyaikasya haste dakṣiṇe arghyapavitreṇāntarhite ekapātrastham udakaṃ kṛtsnaṃ dadyād ity arthaḥ,

	datvā haste pavitraṃ tu hasteṣv arghyaṃ vinikṣipet |

iti gārgyasmaraṇāt | yady apy atropakramopasaṃhāragatavacanayor virodhaḥ pratibhāti | tathāpy anupajātavirodhitvād upakramānurodhenaivopasaṃhārasya varṇanaṃ kāryam iti nyāyena bahuvacanam atra ślokasiddhyarthaṃ prayuktam iti varṇayitavyam | evaṃ ca yājñavalkyavacane 'pi "hasteṣv arghyaṃ vinikṣipet" ity atra hasteṣv api bahuvacanaṃ ślokasiddhyarthaṃ kṛtam, hastasyādhikaraṇatvapratipādanamātre tu tātparyam iti mantavyam | brāhmaṇahasteṣv arghyasecanānantaraṃ yājñavalkyaḥ |

	datvodakaṃ gandhamālyaṃ dhūpadānaṃ sadīpakam | iti |

gandhamālyadhūpadīpadānāni pratyekamudakam ādau datvā kāryāṇīty arthaḥ | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "bhikṣādānam appūrvaṃ dadātṣu caivam" (GDh 5.18–19) iti | āpaḥ pūrvaṃ dattā yasmād bhikṣādānāt tad appūrvam, dadātiṣu bhikṣāto vastvantaradāneṣv apy evam appūrvaṃ dānaṃ kāryam | vaiśvadaivikadāneṣu samarpaṇāya prayoktavyā mantrā brahmapurāṇe darśitaḥ |

	idaṃ vaḥ pādyam arghyaṃ ca puṣpadānavilepanam |

	ayaṃ dīpaprakāśaś ca viśvedevāḥ samarpyate || iti |

viśevedevā idaṃ vaḥ pādyaṃ viśve devā idaṃ vo arghyaṃ iti napuṃsakaliṅganirdeśena pādyādikam, viśve devā eṣa vo dhūpaḥ viśve devā ayaṃ vo dīpaprakāśe iti pulliṅganirdeśena dhūpādiḥ samarpyate viśvebhyo devebhyaḥ samarpaṇīyam ity arthaḥ | gandhadānādāv evaṃ prayogaḥ: brāhmaṇahaste udakaṃ ninīya purūravārdravasaṃjñakā viśvedevā ayaṃ vo gandha iti gandhaṃ brāhmaṇahaste dadyāt | pūrvavad udakaṃ ninīya purūravārdravasaṃjñakaviśvedevā idaṃ vo mālyaṃ iti mālyaṃ dadyāt | pūrvavad udakaṃ ninīya pūrvavat teṣāṃ nāma gṛhītvā ayaṃ vo dhūma iti dhūpārpaṇam, pūrvavad udakaṃ ninīya devatānāma gṛhītvā ayaṃ vo dīpa iti dīpārpaṇam, punar āpo datvā nāma gṛhītvā idaṃ va ācchadanam iti vastratanmūlyayajñopavīteṣu yathālābham ekaṃ dadyāt | arcanaṃ sarvaṃ saṃpūrṇam astv iti kartā brūyāt | astu saṃpūrṇam iti vipro brūyāt | saṃkalpasiddhir astv iti bhavanto bruvantv iti kartā brūyāt | astu saṃkalpasiddhir iti bhavanto brūyāt | āsanādau sarvatra svāsanaṃ svarghyaṃ sugandhaḥ sumālyaṃ sudhūpaḥ sudīpaḥ svācchādanam iti vipro brūyāt | etat sarvaṃ gadyasaṃgrahakāreṇoktam | devapitrarcanārthaṃ yāni gandhapuṣpadhūpadīpācchādanāny upādeyāni varjyāni ca yāni prāgupakalpyadravyakathanāvasare kathitānītīha noktāni | tenopakalpyadravyakathanāvasaroktaṇīhopadeyāni ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ vaisvadaivikārcanavidhiḥ**

**atha paitṛkārcanavidhiḥ**

tatra devalaḥ |

	dvijātayo yathāproktā niyatāḥ syur udaṅmukhāḥ |

	pūjayed yajamānas tu vidhivad dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ ||

yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	apasavyaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā pitṝṇām apradakṣiṇam | iti |

vaiśvadevārtham upavītatvena sthitaṃ yajñasūtraṃ tato vaiśvadaivikārcanānantaram apasavyaṃ prācīnāvītaṃ kṛtvā pitṝṇām upacārabhūtāsanādipadārthān apradakṣiṇaṃ kuryād ity arthaḥ | yady api vaiśvadaivikāsanadānānantaraṃ paitrṛkāsanadānaṃ vaiśvadaivikāvāhanānantaraṃ paitṛkāvāhanam ity evaṃ padārthānusamayenaivāsanāvāhanārghyagandhupuṣpadhūpadīpācchādanākhyāḥ padārthāḥ vaisvadaivikāḥ paitṛkāś ca anuṣṭheyāḥ, na tu vaiśvadaivikāsanādyācchādanāntapadārthakāṇḍād ūrdhvaṃ paitṛkāsanādipadārthānāṃ padārthānusamayenānuṣṭhānam, anyāyyatvāt | tathāpy atra vaiśvadaivikapadārthānāṃ kāṇḍānusamayenānuṣṭhānasya vācanikatvāt tathaivānuṣṭhānaṃ kāryam, vācanikatvaṃ ca "apasavyaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā" ityādinā vacanena vaiśvadevikārcanapadārthakāṇḍād ūrdhvaṃ paitṛkārcanavidhānāt siddham | kathaṃ punaḥ paitṛkārcanam ity apekṣite sa evāha |

	dviguṇāṃs tu kuśān datvā uśantas tvety ṛcā pitṝn |

	āvāhya tadanujñāto japed āyantu nas tataḥ ||

dviguṇān tilān, "pitṝṇāṃ dviguṇāṃs tilaiḥ" it smaraṇāt | kuśān tripañcādiviṣamasaṃkhyākān "pitrye 'yugmāṃs tathaiv ca" it smaraṇāt | datvā āsanasya vāmabhāge,

	pradadyād āsane darbhān na tu pāṇau kadācana |

	pitṛkarmaṇi vāme syāt |

iti smaraṇāt | āsanadānāt pūrvaṃ paścāc ca brāhmaṇahaste apām āsecanaṃ kāryam "apaḥ pradāya darbhaān dviguṇān āsanaṃ pradāyāpaḥ pradadyāt" iti śaunakasmaraṇāt | "pitṝn āvāhayet" ity atra pitṛśabdena kartur atītāḥ pūrvapuruṣāḥ pitṛpitāmahaprapitāmahā uktāḥ, teṣāṃ śrāddhakarmaṇi haviḥpratyuddeśyatayā devatātvena āvāhyatvāt | tathā ca āpastambaḥ: "athaitan manuḥ śrāddhaśabdaṃ karma provāca prajātiḥśreyasāya tatra pitaro devatā brāhmaṇas tv āhavanīyārthe" iti | śrāddhaśabdaṃ karma śrāddhanāmadheyaṃ karma | prajāniḥśreyasāya putrapautrādisaṃtatiśreyaḥprāptyartham | tatra śrāddhanāmadheye karmaṇi | pitaro devatāḥ śrāddhakartuḥ pitṛpitāmahaprapitāmahā lokāntaragatāḥ saṃpradānatvena haviḥpratyuddeśyāḥ, na tu brāhmaṇāḥ saṃpradānatvena haviḥpratyuddeśyāḥ | kiṃ tv āhavanīyārthe devatoddeśena tyaktasya haviṣaḥ prakṣepyamāṇasya dhāraṇarūpe āhavanīyakārye kevalaṃ vartanta ity arthaḥ | tatkarye vartanaṃ ca "brāhmaṇasya haste hotavyam" itivad atra vacanābhāvān na hastadvārā, kiṃ tu,

	dvau daive pitṛkṛtye trīn ekaikam ubhayatra vā |

	bhojayet | (MDh 3.125)

iti vacanāt, tyaktānnaprāśanadvāreti gamyate | pitṛkṛtye yajamānasya pitṛpitāmahaprapitāmahān uddiśya tyaktānnabojanakṛtye | ata eva brahmapurāṇe |

	pitṝn pitāmahān yakṣye bhojanena yathākramam |

	prapitāmahān vai sarvāṃś ca tatpitṝṃś cānupūrvaśaḥ ||

tatpitṝn prapitāmahasya pitṛpitamahaprapitāmahān | piṇḍadānasamaye hastalagnena lepanena yakṣye ity arthaḥ | vaijavāpināpi yajamānasya pitṛpitāmahaprapitāmahānāṃ śrāddhadevatātvam abhidhāya suspaṣṭaṃ teṣām evāvāhanam uktam: "tiṣṭhan pitṝn āvāhayiṣye" ity āmantrya "uśantas tvā ity anayā yajamānasya pitaraṃ pitāmahaṃ prapitāmahaṃ nāmabhir āvāhya" iti | purāṇe 'pi śrāddhakartuḥ pūrvapuruṣāṇām eva śrāddhadevatatvam abhisaṃdhāya suspaṣṭaṃ teṣām eva kavyabhāgitvam uktam |

	yā tu piṇḍakriyā tatra brāhmaṇānāṃ tu bhojanam |

	yajamānasya pūrveṣāṃ tat tu gacchati nānyathā ||

tatra śrāddhakarmaṇi yā piṇḍakriyā ādyapiṇḍakriyā pitṛsaṃbandhinī kṛtā "brāhmaṇānāṃtu bhojanam, yathāsukhaṃ juṣadhvam" iti yad yad annaṃ brāhmaṇabhojanāya niveditaṃ tad dvividham annaṃ yajamānasya pūrveṣāṃ śrāddhakartuḥ pitṛpitāmahaprapitāmahānām upabhhogāya gacchati nānyathā nānyeṣām upabhogāya gacchatīty arthaḥ | kathaṃ punaḥ sarveṣāṃ puruṣāṇāṃ prātisvikaśaubhāśubhakarmavaśena svarganarakādigatānāṃ dūrasthakavyabhoktṛtvasāmarthyarahitānām upabhogāya netṛpuruṣaśūnyam acetanam annādi dravraṃ (?) gacchatīty anupapattinirākaraṇārtham uktaṃ tatraiva |

	yathā goṣu praṇaṣṭeṣu vatso vindati mātaram |

	evaṃ śrāddhe 'nnam uddiṣṭaṃ mantraḥ pāpayate pitṝn ||

mantro mantrasāmarthyam | mantrasāmartham api brāhmaṇabhojanādinā naṣṭam annaṃ kathaṃ prāpayatīty anupapattinirākaraṇāya matsyenoktam |

	nāma gotraṃ pitṝṇāṃ tu prāpakaṃ havyakavyayoḥ |

	nāmamantrās tathādeśāḥ bhavāntaragātān api ||

	prāṇinaḥ prīṇayanty ete tadāhāratvam āgatān |

	devo yadi pitā jātaḥ śubhakarmaniyogataḥ ||

	tasyānnam amṛtaṃ bhūtvā divyatve 'py anugacchati |

	devatve bhogyarūpeṇa paśutve tu tṛṇaṃ bhavet ||

	śrāddhānnaṃ vāyurūpeṇa nāgatve 'py upagacchati |

	pānaṃ bhavati yakṣatve gṛdhratve tu tathāmiṣam ||

	danujatve tathā māṃsaṃ pretatve rudhirodakam |

	mānuṣye tv annapānādi nānābhogakaraṃ tathā ||

	ratiśaktiḥ striyaḥ kāntā bhojyaṃ bhojanaśaktitā |

	dānaśaktiḥ savibhavā rūpam ārogyam eva ca ||

	śrāddhapuṣpam idaṃ proktaṃ phalaṃ brahmasamāgamaḥ | iti |

nāmāni devadattayajñadattādīni | mantrāḥ "pṛthivī te pātram" ityādayaḥ | ādeśāḥ "idam annādikam amuṣmai bhavatu" ityevamādayo nirdeśāḥ | tadāhāratvam āgatān tattajjātyucitāhāratvaṃ prāptān | tasyānnaṃ tadtaduddeśena tyaktam annam amṛtaṃ bhūtvā yatrāsau sthitaḥ tatra mantrasāmarthāt tattadbhogayogyaṃ dravyāntaraṃ bhūtvānugacchati bhogasādhanaṃ bhavati | divyatve divisthitatve devatve | bhogyarūpeṇa divo 'nyatra lokāntare vartamāne devatve sthite devocitabhogyarūpeṇa | idaṃ svakarmānusāriśarīrocitānnādirūpeṇa bhogasādhanatvaṃ śrāddhakarmaṇaḥ puṣpam avāntaraphalam | brahmasamāgamo brahmalokaprāptiḥ paramaphalaṃ proktam ity arthaḥ | atrāvāntaraphalaprāptiḥ kālādiviśeṣalābhe bhavati | tathā ca hārītaḥ |

	kāle nyāyāgataṃ pātre vidhinā pratipaditam |

	prāpnoty annaṃ yathādattaṃ jantur yatrāvatiṣṭhate || iti |

paramaphalaprāptis tu gayādideśaviśeṣalābhe bhavati,

	yannāmnā pātayet piṇḍaṃ taṃ nayed brahma śāśvatam |

iti gayādideśaveśeṣakṛtasya śrāddhasya phalatvena śravaṇāt | śāśvataṃ brahma nayet brahmaṇā saha brahmaprāptyāpādakaṃ brahmalokaṃ nayed ity arthaḥ | evam āpastambādivacanaiḥ śrāddhakarmaṇi na brāhmaṇa uddeśyaḥ | kiṃ tu śrāddakartuḥ pitṛpitāmahaprapitāmahā lokāntaragatā uddeśyā iti siddham | teṣūddeśyapitrādiṣu vasvādirūpatayā uddeśārthaṃ yathākramaṃ vasvādibuddhiḥ karyety āha śātātapaḥ |

	vasavaḥ pitaro jñeyāḥ rudrāḥ jñeyāḥ pitāmahāḥ |

	prapitāmahās tathādityā ity eṣā vaidikī śrutiḥ ||

evaṃ jñātvā śrāddhe kṛte vasvādīnām api prītir bhavatīty āha paiṭhīnasiḥ: "vasavaḥ pitaro rudrāḥ pitāmahā ādityāḥ prapitāmahā ya evaṃ vidvān pitṝn yajate vasavo rudrā ādityāś cāsya prītā bhavanti" iti | pitrādiṣv eva vasvādirūpam anusaṃdhāyānuṣṭhitena śrāddhena prītā vasvādayaḥ śrāddhajanitaprītiśālitvena śrāddhadevatābhūtapitrādikalpāḥ putrādidattānnanidānakasyāmṛtādyannapānāntasya prāptiṃ nāmagotramantrādivastusāmarthyena kurvatāṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ pitṝn śubhāśubhakarmārabdhaśarīrāntaragatān prīṇayantīty arthaḥ | tena putrādibhir avaśyaṃ nāmagotramantrādyuccāraṇavad vasvādirūpeṇa pitrādayo dhyātavyāḥ | tathāha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	vasurudrāditisutāḥ pitaraḥ śrāddhadevatāḥ |

	prīṇayanti manuṣyāṇāṃ pitṝn śrāddhena tarpitāḥ ||

aditisutā ādityāḥ | evaṃ ca āpastambādivacanānāṃ śātātapādivacanānāṃ ca na parasparavirodhaḥ | tena śrāddhakartuḥ pūrvapuruṣā eva lokāntaragatāḥ śrāddhadevatā iti siddham | yat tu devalenoktam,

	vasavaḥ pitaro jñeyāḥ rudrā jñeyāḥ pitāmahāḥ |

	prapitāmahās tathādityāḥ śrutir eṣā sanātanī ||

	pretān uddiśya yat karma kriyate mānuṣair iha |

	tuṣyanti pitaras tena na pretāḥ pitaraḥ smṛtāḥ || iti |

ayam arthaḥ: mānuṣaiḥ putrādibhir iha manuṣaloke yac chrāddākhyaṃ karma pretān paralokagatān pitrādīn śrāddhe uddheśyabhūtān vasvādirūpeṇa dhyātān uddiśya kriyate tena tathākṛtena karmaṇā tasmin karmaṇi vasvādirūpeṇa dhyātvoddiṣṭāḥ pitaraḥ pitrādayas tuṣyanti na punaḥ svarūpeṇoddiṣṭāḥ yato na pretāḥ paralokagatāḥ svarūpamātreṇa śrāddhadevatābhūtāḥ pitaraḥ smṛtā iti | ataḥ anenāpi saha āpastambādivacanānāṃ na virodhaḥ | evaṃ nirūpitaṃ śrāddhakartuḥ pitrādīnāṃ devatātvaṃ mātṛpitāmahyādisahitānām eva na tu kevalānām ity āha śātātapaḥ |

	ekamūrtitvam āyāti sapiṇḍīkaraṇe kṛte |

	patnī patipitṝṇāṃ tu tattadaṃśeṣu bhāginī ||

etad vacanaṃ pitrādidaivatye śrāddhe tatpatnīnāṃ sahabhāvena devatātvaṃ bodhayati | tataś ca sapatnīkāḥ pitaro devatā ity eṣo 'rtha ukto bhavati | evaṃ ca pārvaṇādiśrāddhe pitrādīnāṃ sapatnīkānāṃ ca tṛptir bhavati na punaḥ kevalānām iti mantavyam | ata eva bṛhaspatiḥ |

	svena bhrtrā samaṃ śrāddhe mātā bhuṅkte sudhāmayam |

	pitāmahī ca svenaiva svenaiva prapitāmahī || iti |

evam eva vasvādirūpeṇa mātāmahādīnām api śrāddhadevatātvaṃ tatpatnīnāṃ ca sahabhāvena devatātvam avagantavyam, "mātāmahānām ity evam" iti yājñavalkyādibhir uktatvāt | evaṃ nirūpitaśrāddhadevatāvāhane viśeṣaḥ purāṇe darśitaḥ |

	apasavyaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā tilān ādāya saṃyataḥ |

	pitṛn āvāhayāmīti pṛcched viprān udaṅmukhān ||

	āvāhayety anujñāta uśantas tvety ṛcā pitṝn |

	tataḥ kṣiptvāpasavyaṃ ca pitṝn dhyāyan samāhitaḥ ||

	japed āyantu na iti mantraṃ samyag aśeṣataḥ || iti |

uśantas tvety ṛcā ptṝn ityāder ayam arthaḥ: uśantas tvety ṛcā pitṛpitāmahaprapitāmahān āvāhya anantaram apradakṣiṇaṃ pūrvopāttāṃs tilān "namo vaḥ pitaraḥ" iti mantreṇa śiraḥprabhṛti pādāntaṃ kṣiptvā pitṝn dhyāyan "āyantu naḥ" iti mantraṃ japed iti | tathā pracetāḥ |

	śiraḥprabhṛti pādāntaṃ namo va iti paitṛke |

paitṛke karmaṇi "namo vaḥ pitaraḥ" iti mantreṇa śiraḥprabhṛti pādāntam apradakṣiṇaṃ puṣpatilādibhiḥ pūjanaṃ kuryād ity arthaḥ | vaijavāpenāpy āvāhane viśeṣo darśitaḥ: "tiṣṭhan pitṝn āvāhayiṣyāmīty āmantryośantas tvety anayā yajamānasya pitaraṃ pitāmahaṃ prapitāmahaṃ nāmabhir āvāhya 'āyantu naḥ pitaraḥ' iti japtvā" iti | nāmabhiḥ dvitīyādivibhaktyantaiḥ | tathā ca ślokasaṅgrahakāraḥ |

	akṣayyāsanayoḥ ṣaṣṭhī dvitīyāvāhane tathā |

	annadāne caturthī syāc cheṣāḥ saṃbuddhayaḥ smṛtāḥ || iti |

etāsu ṣaṣṭhyādivibhaktiṣu sarvatra ekavacanabahuvacanayor vikalpa eva smṛtipurāṇagṛhyādiṣu pitṛpitāmahaprapitāmahādiśabdānāṃ kvacid ekavacanāntatayā kvacid bahuvacanāntatayā ca tatra tatra praayogadarśanāt | evaṃ cāsanadānāvāhanayor evaṃ prayogaḥ: prācīnāvītī udaṅmukhatayā prathamopaviṣṭaviprahaste jalaṃ ninīya kuśāsanayugmān mathyabhaṅgato dviguṇīkṛtān satilān gṛhītvā dakṣināmukha āsīno 'smatpitur vasurūpasyāmukagotrasyāmukaśarmaṇaḥ sapatnīkasyedam āsanam iti viprasyāsanasya vāmabhāge pūrvagṛhītāt satilān kuśān nikṣipya viprahaste punar jalaṃ ninayet | evam anantaropaviṣṭabrāhmaṇahaste tadanantaropaviṣṭabrāhmaṇahaste ca jalaninayanādi punarjalaninayanāntaṃ kuryāt | pitāmahasya rudrarūpasya prapitāmahasyādityarūpasyeti viśeṣaḥ | evam eva mātāmahasthānasthavipratrayahasteṣu jaladānādi kuryāt | mātāmahasya vasurūpasya mātuḥ pitāmahasya rudrarūpasya matuḥ prapitāmahasyādityarūpasyeti viseṣaḥ | evaṃ ṣaṭsu vipreṣu padārthānusamayenāsanaṃ datvānantaraṃ prativipraṃ nimantraṇaṃ pūrvaprakaraṇoktaprakāreṇa kuryat | daive kṣaṇaḥ kriyatām ityādivākyasthadaivapadasthāne śrāddhe iti saptamyantapadaṃ ṣaṭsu vipreṣu prayoktavyam | oṃ tathetyādikaṃ tu pūrvaprakaraṇoktaprakāreṇaiva prayoktavyam | ṣaṣṭhaṃ vipraṃ nimantryātha tilān ādāya prācīnāvītī dakṣiṇābhimukhas tiṣṭhann asmatpitṛpitāmahaprapitāmahān vasurudrādityarūpān āvāhayiṣye ity udaṅmukhatayāsīnān brāhmaṇān pṛṣṭvā āvāhayety anujñātaḥ " uśantas tvā havāmahe" ity ṛcam uktvā ṛgante 'smatpitaraṃ vasurūpam amukagotram amukaśarmāṇaṃ sapatnīkam asmatpitāmahaṃ rudrarūpam amukagotram amukaśarmāṇaṃ sapatnīkam āvāhayāmīti prathame vipre pitaram, dvitīya pitāmaham, gṛtīye prapitāmaham, āvāhya "namo vaḥ pitaraḥ" iti mantreṇa śirasi savyāṃse dakṣiṇāṃse savyajānuni dakṣiṇajānuni savyapāde dakṣiṇapāde ca prativipraṃ tilān āropya prathame vipre pitaraṃ vasurūpaṃ sapatnīkam, dvitīya pitāmahaṃ rudrarūpaṃ sapatnīkam, tṛtīye prapitāmaham ādityarūpaṃ sapatnīkaṃ dhyāyan "āyantu naḥ pitaraḥ" ityādikām ṛcaṃ sakṛj japet | evaṃ mātāmahādyāvāhanaṃ kuryāt | tatrāyaṃ viśeṣaḥ: asmanmātmahamātuḥpitāmahamātuḥprapitāmahān vasurudrādityarūpān āvāhiṣye iti mātāmahādisthānasthān viprān pṛcchet | uśantas tveti mantrānte mātāmahaṃ vasurūpam amukagotram amukaśarmāṇaṃ sapatnīkam, evaṃ mātuḥpitāmahaṃ sapatnīkaṃ rudrarūpam amukagotram amukaśarmāṇam, evaṃ mātuḥprapitāmaham ādityarūpam amukagotram amukaśarmāṇaṃ sapatnīkam āvāhayāmīti prathame vipre mātāmaham, dvitīye mātuḥpitāmaham, tṛtīye mātuḥprapitāmaham āvāhya prativipram ekaikaṃ dhyāyan "āyantu naḥ" iti japet | 'uśantas tvā, āyantu naḥ" iti mantradvayagatapitṛśabdasthāne mātāmahaśabdaḥ na prayoktavyaḥ | "na pitā vardhate" iti śrutyā janakaikaniṣṭhapitṛśabdavyatiriktapitṛśabdohapratiṣedhāt | "āyantu naḥ pitaraḥ" iti japānantaraṃ kartavyam uktaṃ purāṇe |

	japed āyantu na iti mantraṃ samyag aśeṣataḥ |

	rakṣārthaṃ pitṛsatrasya triḥkṛtvaḥ sarvatodiśam ||

	tilāṃs tu prakṣipen mantrair uccāryāpahatā iti ||

"apahatā asurā rakṣāṃsi (?) piśācā ye kṣayanti pṛthivīm anu | anyatreto gacchantu yatraiṣāṃ gataṃ manaḥ" iti mantram uccārya sarvatodiśaṃ brāhmaṇān paritas trivāram apradakṣiṇaṃ tilān prakṣiped ity arthaḥ | pitṛsatraṃ pitṛyāgaḥ, śrāddham iti yāvat ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ paitṛkārcanavidhāvāhanāntopacāravidhiḥ (?)**

**athārghyādyupacāravidhiḥ **

atra purāṇam |

	sauvarṇarājatāmbhojamaṇipātrāṇy athāpi vā |

	arghārthaṃ saṃskaroty eva śubhapatrapuṭādi vā ||

arghārtham arghyodakasthāpanārthaṃ darbheṣv āsādanaprokṣaṇābhyāṃ sauvarṇādiṣu yathālābham anyatamāni pātrāṇi saṃskuryād evety arthaḥ | patrapuṭādīty ādiśabdena camasādikaṃ gṛhyate | ata eva viṣṇuḥ: "dakṣiṇāgreṣu darbheṣu camaseṣu dakṣināpavargeṣu triṣu pavitrāntarhiteṣu apa āsiṃcet 'śaṃ no devīḥ' " iti | dakṣiṇāgreṣu darbheṣu dakṣiṇāpavargatayāsāditeṣu camasādyarghyapātreṣu triṣu pavitrāntarhiteṣu śaṃ no devīr iti mantreṇa pratipātram apo ninayed ity arthaḥ | pracetā api: "yajñiyavṛkṣacamaseṣu pavitrāntarhiteṣv ekaikasmin apa āsiñcet" iti | śaunako 'pi: "taijasāśmamayamṛnmayeṣu pātreṣv ekadravyeṣv anekadravyeṣu vā darbhāntarhiteṣv apaḥ pradāya saṃ no devīr abhiṣṭaye ity anumantritān tilān āvapati, 'tilosi pitṛdevatyo gosavao devanirmitaḥ | patnavadbhiḥ pṛktaḥ svadhayā pitṛn imān lokān prīṇayāhi naḥ svadhā namaḥ' " iti | taijasaṃ kāṃsyādimayam | aśmamayaṃ marakatādimaṇimayam | ekadravyeṣu kāṃsyarājatatāmrādīnām anyatemeṣu | anekadravyeṣu kāṃsyādinānādravyamayeṣu vā | darbhāntarhiteṣu pavitrāntarhiteṣu | | śaṃ no devīr iti mantreṇāpo ninīyānumantritāsu pūrvoktamantreṇa nītāsv apsu tilo 'sīti mantreṇa tilān prakṣiped ity arthaḥ | pātreṣv iti bahuvacanaṃ triṣv evāvatiṣṭhate, prakṛtibhūte tridevatāke śrāddhe pratidaivatam ekaikapātravidhiparatvāt | ata eva pracetasā "trīṇy evodapātrāṇi" ity uktam | pitrādīnāṃ trayāṇām ekaikasyānekabrāhmaṇaniyogaje sarveṣām ekabrāhmaṇaniyojane 'pi śrāddhasya tridevatākatvāt trīṇy evodapātrāṇi na tu brāhmaṇasaṃkhyayā saṃkhyātānīty arthaḥ | ata eva tilais tathety adhikṛtya vaijāvāpenoktam |

	nītvā pitṝṇāṃ trīṇy eva kuryāt pātrāṇi dharmavit |

	ekasmin vā bahuṣu vā brāhmaṇeṣu yathāvidhi || iti |

tilair nītvā tilān arghyodakeṣu prakṣiped ity arthaḥ | arghyodakasaṃskārārthaṃ pavitrakaraṇaprakāram āha sa eva |

	kuśau samāvaśīrṇāgrāv anantargarbhakau kuśaiḥ |

	chinatti tat pavitraṃ syāc chrāddhe karmaṇi sarvadā || iti |

kuśāv iti yugmasaṃkhyā vaiśvadaivakārghyapātrapavitraviṣayā | paitṛkārghyapātrapavitraviṣaye anucitatvāt | ata eva caturviṃśatimate paitṛkārghyapavitre ayugmasaṃkhyā darśitā |

	tisras tisraḥ śalākās tu pitṛpātreṣu pārvaṇe | iti |

śalākāḥ śalākāsaṃnibhā darbhāḥ, acchinnāgrā iti yāvat | arghyapātreṣu tilaprakṣepānantaraṃ brahmapurāṇe kartavyam uktam |

	arghyāḥ puṣpaiś ca gandhaiś ca tāḥ prapūjyāś ca śāstravat | iti |

arghyā arghyārthā yā āpaḥ tilamiśrās tāḥ gandhaiḥ puṣpaiś ca prapūjyāḥ | tāsu gandhapuṣpāṇi prakṣiped ity arthaḥ | gandhādiprakṣepānantaraṃ śaunakaḥ: "tāḥ pratigrāhayiṣyaṃś ca svadhārghyāḥ" iti | tāḥ arghyārthā apaḥ brāhmaṇaiḥ pratigrāhayiṣyan svadhārghyā iti mantreṇa brāhmaṇānāṃ puraḥ sthāpayed ity arthaḥ | sthāpanānantaraṃ paiṭhīnasiḥ: "tato brāhmaṇahasteṣūdakapūrvaṃ darbhān pradāyodakapūrvam arghyodakaṃ dadāti yā divyā āpaḥ ity ṛcaitat te arghyodakam ity apa upaspṛśed ity evam evetarayoḥ" iti | arghyasthāpanānantaraṃ brāhmaṇahasteṣu prathamam apo ninīyārghyapavitradarbhān dakṣiṇāgratayā kṣiptvā punar apo ninīya "yā divyā āpaḥ" iti mantram uktvā mantrānte "asmatpitar amukagotra amukaśarman vasurūpasapatnīkaitat te arghyodakam" iti dakṣiṇahaste pitṛtīrthenārghyaṃ datvāpa upaspṛśet | evam evetarayoḥ pitāmahaprapitāmahayor api brāhmanahaste arghyaṃ dadyād ity arthaḥ | asmat pitāmaha amukagotra amukaśarman rudrarūpa sapatnīka, asmatpitāmahāsityarūpeti tu viśeṣaḥ | kātyāyanena "yā divyā āpaḥ" iti mantraṃ kṛtsnaṃ paṭhitvārghyasamarpaṇam uktam: "sapavitreṣu hasteṣu 'yā divyā āpaḥ payasā saṃbabhūvuḥ yā antarikṣa uta pārthivīryāḥ | hiraṇyavarṇā yajñiyās tā na āpaḥ śaṃsyonā suhavā bhavantu' iti | pitaras te arghyaṃ pitāmahaitat te arghyaṃ prapitāmahaitat te arghyam iti brāhmaṇāñ jaleṣu pātrāṇi ninīya pitṛbhyo 'kṣayyam astṝit (?) śeṣaṃ darbheṣv avanejayati iti" pātrāṇi pātrasthodakānīty arthaḥ | dharmeṇa gotragrahaṇaṃ ca kāryam ity uktam: "yā divyā āpaḥ iti pātraṃ pānibhyām uddhṛtya nāma gotraṃ ca gṛhītvā sapavitre haste 'rghyaṃ dadyāt" iti | pāṇibhyām uddhṛtena pātreṇa dadyād iti gamyate | pracetā api |

	apradakṣiṇam eteṣām ekaikaṃ tu pitṛkramāt |

	saṃbodhya gotranāmabhyām eṣa te 'rghyam itīrayet ||

eteṣāṃ pitṛpitāmahaprapitāmahānāṃ pitṛkramāt pitrādikramād ekaikaṃ gotranāmabhyāṃ saṃbodhya eṣa te 'rghyam ity uktvā ekaikaṃ brāhmaṇam ekaikenārghyeṇārcayed ity arthaḥ | tathā cāha gautamaḥ: "pūrvavat pṛthag ekaikam ekaikenārcayet kramāt" iti | etat "trīn pitrye" ity uktabrāhmaṇasaṃkhyāpakṣābhiprāyeṇoktam | "trīn trīn" ity uktabrāhmaṇasaṃkhyāpakṣe tu trīn brāhmaṇān ekaikenārghyeṇārcayet | ata eva paiṭhīnasinā "hasteṣu" ityādy uktam | na ca vācyam "trīn pitrye" iti pakṣa eva hasteṣv ity upapadyate, triṣu pitṛvargabrāhmaṇeṣu dakṣiṇahastatrayasaṃbhavād iti | yatas tena "pitṛsthānasthabrāhmaṇārcana eva hasteṣu" ity uktvā "evam itarayoḥ" ity abhidhānāt | tasmāt trīn trīn pitrye iti pakṣe pitṛsthānasthabrāhmaṇadakṣiṇahasteṣv apām āsecanādyarghyaninayanāntaṃ sakṛt kuryāt | tathā pitāmahasthānasthabrāhmaṇahasteṣu caivaṃ ninayet, "evam itarayoḥ" ity abhidhānāt | evaṃ mātāmahādīnām arghyapātrāsādānādi (?) brāhmaṇahasteṣv arghyadānāntaṃ yathoktaṃ nāmagotrasahitaṃ padārthānusamayena kuryāt, "mātāmahānām apy evam" ity atideśasmaraṇāt | pitrādibrāhmaṇahasteṣv arghyadānānantaraṃ yājñavalkyaḥ |

	datvārghyaṃ saṃsravāṃs teṣāṃ pātre kṛtvā vidhānataḥ |

	pitṛbhyaḥ sthānam asīti nyubjaṃ pātraṃ karoty adhaḥ ||

teṣāṃ prativipraṃ dattānām arghyāṇāṃ saṃsravān viprahastebhyaḥ anyeṣu pātreṣu galitān pitṛpātre saṃbhṛtya tat patram "pitṛbhyaḥ sthānam asi" iti mantreṇa nyubjam adhobaliṃ adhaḥkaroti bhūmyāṃ nidadhyāt na pātrāder uparīty arthaḥ | tathā ca pracetāḥ |

	prathame pitṛpātre tu sarvān saṃbhṛtya saṃsravān |

	pitṛbhyaḥ sthānam asīty uktvā kuryād bhūmāv adhomukham ||

atra gobhilenokto viśeṣaḥ: "nyubjaṃ kuryāt pavitravat" iti | brāhmaṇahasteṣu nikṣiptāni pavitrāṇy ādāya pitṛpātre nidhāya taiḥ saha bhūmau nyubjaṃ kuryād ity arthaḥ | kātyāyanenātra viśeṣa uktaḥ: "kuśavatyāṃ bhūmau adhomukhaṃ kuryāt tasyopari ca kuśam" iti | nidadhyād iti śeṣaḥ | matsyenāpi: 

	datvā saṃsravam āditaḥ |

	pitṛpātre nidhāyātha nyubjam uttarato nyaset || iti |

āditaḥ prathamam arghyaṃ datvā pitṛpātre saṃsravaṃ nidhāya tat pātraṃ brāhmaṇādhyāsitadeśād uttarataḥ kiṃcid dūre adhomukhaṃ nidadhyād ity arthaḥ | atriṇāpi pitṛpātraṃ prakṛtya viśeṣa uktaḥ: "gandhādibhis tad abhyarcya" iti | ādiśabdena puṣpāṇi gṛhyante | "gandhamālyais tad abhyarcya" iti śaunakasmaraṇāt | evaṃ nyubjakaraṇam anityam,

	apasavyaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā piṇḍapārśve samāhitaḥ |

	kṣiptvā darbhapavitrāṇi mocayet saṃsravāṃs tataḥ ||

ity atrivacane svadhāvācanakālaparyantaṃ saṃsravodakadhāraṇadarśanāt | dhāraṇaṃ ca pitṛpātrasyottānatayā sthāpane (?) sati bhavati na tu nyubhatayā sthāpane | tasmād uttānatayā sthāpanapakṣo 'pi gamyate | asmin pakṣe pitṛpātrasya pitāmahādipātreṇāpidhānaṃ kāryam | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ |

	paitṛkaṃ prathamaṃ pātraṃ tasmin paitāmahaṃ nyaset |

	prapitāmahaṃ tato nyasya noddharen na ca cālayet ||

pitṛpātraṃ pitāmahapātre 'pidhāya prapitāmahapātreṇa pidadhyād ity arthaḥ | (prapitāmahapātrābhāve 'nyena kenacit pātreṇa pidadyād ity arthaḥ | ) (??) adhomukhatayā uttānatayā vā nyastasya pātrasyānyathākaraṇe kātyāyanena doṣo darśitaḥ |

	spṛṣṭam uddhṛtam anyatra nītam udghāṭitaṃ tathā |

	pātraṃ dṛṣṭvā vrajanty āśu pitaraḥ prasravanti ca ||

udghāṭitaṃ pidhāyakapitāmahādipātrāpasāraṇena vivṛtam ity arthaḥ | ata eva uśanāḥ |

	uttānaṃ vivṛtaṃ vāpi pitṛpātraṃ yadā bhavet |

	abhojyaṃ tad bhaved annaṃ kruddhaiḥ pitṛgaṇair gataiḥ || iti |

nyubjaṃ kṛtaṃ pitṛpātraṃ yadottānaṃ bhavet | uttānatayā sthāpitaṃ pātrāntareṇa pihitaṃ pitṛpātraṃ yadā vā vivṛtaṃ bhaved iti pūrvārdhasyārthaḥ | nyubjaṃ pātraṃ kṛtvāha vaijavāpaḥ |

	tasyopari kuśān datvā pradadyād devapūrvakam |

	gandhapuṣpāṇi dhūpaṃ ca dīpaṃ vastropavītake ||

tasyopari kuśān datvā tasya nyubjakṛtapitṛpātrasyopari kuśagandhapuṣpāṇi datvā vaisvadaivikabrāhmaṇapūrvakaṃ gandhādi dadyād ity arthaḥ | anena gandhadānaṃ vaisvadaivikabrāhmaṇeṣu kṛtvā paitṛkabrāhmaṇeṣu kāryam ity ucyate | evam eva puṣpadānādy api | tataś ca vaisvadaivikabrāhmaṇārcanaṃ ca padārthānusamayena sahaiva kāryam iti vacobhaṅgyābhihitam | evaṃ ca vaiśvadaive yājñavalkyena kāṇḍānurūpasamayakrama uktaḥ, tena saha anenoktapadārthānusamayarūpakramasya vikalpo veditavyaḥ | na cāyaṃ vikalpo gandhadānaprabhṛty eva na punaḥ prāg apīti vācyam, arthavaiśamāpatteḥ, "devāṃś ca pitṝṃś cāvāhayiṣye ity anujñāpya" ityādinā gandhādidānāt prāg eva sahānuṣṭhānasya paiṭhīnasinā smṛtatvāc ca | viṣṇunāpi gandhādidānam uktam: "anulepanavastrālaṃkaraṇapuṣpadhūpair yathāśakti viprān samabhyarcya" iti | anulepanādīni pitrādidevatoddeśena viprebhyo dadyād ity arthaḥ | ata eva paiṭhīnasiḥ: "gandhān pitṛgotranāma gṛhītvāpaḥ spṛśed evam itarayor dhūpadīpamālyācchādanam evam" iti | pitrarthabrāhmaṇahaste 'po ninīya gandhān candanakuṅkumakarpūrādīn ādāya asmatpitaro 'mukagotrā amukaśarmāṇo vasurudrādityarūpāḥ sapatnīkā amī vo gandhā iti brāhmaṇhasta eva gandhān datvā udakaṃ spṛśet | evam evetaryoḥ pitāmahaprapitāmahayor gandhasamarpaṇam | rudrarūpeti pitāmahe, prapitāmahe ādityarūpeti viśeṣaḥ | puṣpadhūpadīpamālyācchādanādidānaṃ caivaṃ gandhadānavad eva kāryam ity arthaḥ | tathā ca brahmapurāṇam |

	idaṃ vaḥ puṣpam ity uktvā puṣpāṇi ca nivedayet |

	ayaṃ vo dhūpa ity uktvā dhūpaṃ saumyaṃ nivedayet ||

	idaṃ vo mālyam ity uktvā dadyān mālyaṃ suśobhanam || iti |

evam anayā rītyā idaṃ vo jyotir ity uktvā dīpaṃ nivedayet | idaṃ va ācchādanam ity uktvā vastraṃ nivedayed ityādi dvayam evohyam | ata evohaprakārapradarśanārthaṃ devalenoktam |

	idaṃ jyotir iti jyotiḥ sujyotir iti te 'pi ca | iti |

idaṃ vo jyotir iti jyotir nivedayet | sujyotir iti te viprā bhrūyur ity arthaḥ | "sujyotir iti te 'pi ca" iti caśabdāt svāsanam astu svarghyaṃ sugandhāḥ supuṣpāṇi sudhūpaḥ sudīpaḥ svācchādanam ity āsanādiṣu yathāliṅgaṃ prativacanāni viprā brūyur iti sūcitam iti mantavyam | ata eva gṛhyasaṃgrahakāreṇaitāni prativacanāny uktāni | kīdṛśā gandhā deyā ity apekṣite brahmapurāṇam |

	śvetacandanakarpūrakuṅkumāni śubhāni tu |

	vilepanārthaṃ dadyāt tu yac cānyat pitṛvallabham || iti |

lepanaṃ ca viprāḥ svayaṃ kuryuḥ śrāddhakartā vā | tatra śrāddhakartrā vilepanapakṣe viśeṣam āha vyāsaḥ |

	vipavitrakaro gandhair gandhadvāreti pūjayet | iti |

gandhadvāreti mantreṇa tadante nāmagotragrahaṇapūrvakam amī vo gandhā ity uktvā brāhmaṇahaste gandhān pradāya tair gandhaiḥ pūjayet | vipavitrakaro vipralalāṭe gandhaṃ vilepayed ity arthaḥ | svayaṃ vilepanapakṣe 'pi gandhadvāreti mantro 'sti, gandhadāne karaṇamantratvāt | vipavitrakaratvalakṣaṇadharma eva na vidyate | ata eva śrāddhakartrā vilepanapakṣa eva sapavitrakareṇa vilepane kṛte vṛddhaśātātapena doṣo darśitaḥ |

	pavitraṃ tu kare kṛtvā yaḥ samālabhate dvijān |

	rākṣasānāṃ bhavec chrāddhaṃ virāśāḥ pitaro gatāḥ ||

samālambhanaṃ gandhair vilepanam | pakṣadvayasādhāraṇadoṣo devalena darśitaḥ |

	yajñopavītaṃ viprāṇāṃ skandhān naivāvatārayet |

	gandhādipūjāsiddhyarthaṃ daive pitrye ca karmaṇi ||

viprāṇāṃ yajñopavītaṃ gandhādyanulepanasiddhyartham anulepako nāvatārayed ity arthaḥ | skandhād avatāryānulepane kṛte śaṅkhena doṣa uktaḥ |

	upavītaṃ kaṭau kṛtvā kuryād gātrānulepanam |

	ekavāsāś ca yo 'śnīyāt nirāśāḥ pitaro gatāḥ ||

kratunā tu lalāṭe vartulatayā puṇḍre kṛte doṣa uktaḥ |

	lalāṭe puṇḍrakaṃ dṛṣṭvā skandhe mālāṃ tathaiva ca |

	nirāśāḥ pitaro yānti dṛṣṭvā tu vṛṣalīpatim ||

iti doṣasmṛtibalena kalpyasya niṣedhasya kḷptordhvapuṇḍravidhyavādhena (?) kalpyatvād vartulapuṇḍraviṣayam etat | skandhe mālādhāraṇe doṣasmaraṇāt śirasy eva vipreṇa mālā dharyā | tatrāpi śikhāyām eva,

	na niyuktaḥ śikhāvarjaṃ mālāṃ śirasi veṣṭayet |

iti vṛddhamanusmaraṇāt | niyuktaḥ śrāddhe nimantrito vipraḥ | mālyaṃ ca vihitapuṣpamayaṃ deyam | kāni punar vihitāni puṣpāṇīty apekṣite brahmapurāṇe |

	śaulkāḥ sumanasaḥ śreṣṭhāḥ tathā padmotpalāni ca |

	gandhadhūpopannāni yāni cānyāni kṛtsnaśaḥ || iti |

viṣṇus tu puṣpadāne mantram āha: "puṣpāvatīr iti puṣpam" iti | dadyād iti purvavākyaśrutam ihānuṣajyate | 

	oṣadhayaḥ pratimodadhvaṃ puṣpāvatīḥ supipplāḥ | 

	ayaṃ vo garbhaṛtviyaḥ pratnaṃ sadhastham āsadat || 

iti mantrasya madhyamapratīkopādānam etat puṣpāvatīr iti | mantrānte nāmagotragrahaṇapūrvakam idaṃ vaḥ puṣpam iti puṣpaṃ deyam | dhūpadravye viśeṣaḥ śaṅkhenoktaḥ |

	dhūpārthe guggulaṃ dadyāt ghṛtayuktaṃ maghūtkaṭam | iti |

vyāsas tu dhūpadāne mantram āha: "dhūpaṃ ca dhūr asīty uktvā" iti | "dhūr asi dhūr va dhūrvantam" iti yajurvedamantram uktvā dhūpaṃ dadyād ity arthaḥ | purāṇe tu mantrāntaram uktam |

	vanaspatiraso divyo gandhāḍhyaḥ sumanoharaḥ |

	ādhreyaḥ sarvadevānāṃ dhūpo 'yaṃ pratigṛhyatām || iti |

dhūr asīty anena sahāsya vikalpo veditavyaḥ | atrāpi mantrānte nāmagotragrahaṇapūrvakam ayaṃ vo dhūpa iti dhūpo deyaḥ | hastavātaprāpito dhūpo na vipreṇa sevyaḥ tasya niṣedhāt | śātātapaḥ |

	hastavātāhataṃ dhūpaṃ ye pibanti dvijottamāḥ |

	vṛthā bhavati tac chrāddhaṃ tasmāt taṃ parivarjayet || 

dīpe tu viśeṣam āha marīciḥ |

	ghṛtād vā tilatailād vā nānyad dravyāt tu dīpakam | iti |

ācchādane mantram ācchādanābhāve tatpratinidhiṃ cāha śātātapaḥ: "yuvā suvāsā iti vastraṃ dadyāt tadabhāve yajñopavītam" iti | atrāpi mantrānte nāmagotragrahaṇapūrvakam idaṃ va ācchādanam idaṃ vo yajñopavītam iti vā uktvā ācchādanaṃ yajñopavītaṃ vā deyam | anyāny api grāhyavarjanīyagandhapuṣpadhūpadīpācchādanaviṣayāṇi smṛtyantaravacanāni santi, tāni cāsmābhiḥ śrāddhāṅgadravyopakalpanaprakaraṇe likhitānīhāpy anusaṃdheyāni | evaṃ mātāmahādīnām api gandhapuṣpādidānaṃ nāmagotrasahitaṃ padārthānusamayena kāryam, "mātāmahānām apy evam" ity atideśasmaraṇāt | mātuḥprapitāmahācchādanānantaram arcanaṃ pūrṇam astv iti kartā brūyāt | astv iti viprā brūyuḥ | saṃkalpasiddhir astv iti bhavanto bruvantv iti kartā vadet | astu saṃkalpasiddhir iti viprā vadeyuḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyām arghyādyupacāravidhiḥ**

**athāgnaukaraṇavidhiḥ**

tatra kātyāyanaḥ |

	gandhān brahmāṇasāt (?) kṛtvā puṣpāṇy ṛtubhavāni ca |

	dhūpaṃ caivānupūrveṇa agnau kuryād ataḥ param ||

ṛtubhavāni puṣpāṇi svodbhavakālatvena prasiddhavasantādikālaprabhavāni | caśabdo 'nuktasamuccayārthaḥ | evaṃ cāyam arthaḥ: gandhapuṣpālaṃkāradhūpācchādanāni brāhmaṇārthāni kṛtvānantaram agnaukaraṇākhyaṃ karma kuryād iti | kathaṃ kuryād ity apekṣite hārītaḥ: "athoddhṛtānnaḥ paṅktimūrdhani sarvān prcchaty agnau kariṣye" iti | nigamo 'pi: "annam uddhṛtyābhighāryāgnau kariṣya iti pṛcchati" iti | viṣṇupurāṇe 'pi |

	agnau kariṣya ity uktvā tair uktaḥ kriyatām iti |

	gṛhyoktenaiva vidhinā hutvā pātreṣu dāpayet ||

hutvā hutaśeṣaṃ pitṛbrāhmaṇabhājaneṣu dadyād ity arthaḥ | gṛhyoktenaivety evakāro na dharmaśāstrādyuktavidhinivṛttyarthaḥ, dharmaśāstroktavidher  gṛhyoktavidheś ca parasparāpekṣatvāt | tenātraivakāraḥ purāṇoktavidhinivṛttyarthaḥ | ata eva gṛhyoktavidhānenāgnaukaraṇaṃ kāryam ity abhidhāya tasminn eva purāṇe gṛhyeṣv anukto vidhir darśitaḥ |

	juhuyād vyañjanakṣāravarjam annaṃ tato naraḥ |

	anujñāto dvijais tais tu triḥkṛtvo bharatarṣabha || iti |

vyañjanakṣāravarjam annaṃ haviṣyam annm ity arthaḥ | yat tu purāṇāntare,

	puṣpāṇāṃ ca phalānāṃ ca bhakṣyāṇāṃ ca prayatnataḥ |

	agram uddhṛtya sarveṣāṃ juhuyāj jātavedasi ||

iti pitrarthapākasiddhalavanādisaṃspṛṣṭāhaviṣyahomasmaraṇaṃ tad yeṣāṃ gṛhye 'gnaukaraṇahomāntaram ahaviṣyahomāntaram amantrakaṃ kāryam iti vidhīyate tadviṣayam | ato na pūrvoktavirodhaḥ | jātavedasi uṣṇabhasmagatāgnāv ity arthaḥ | tathā ca āpastambenāgnaukaranāṅgatayoktam: "na kṣāralavaṇahomo vidyate tathāvarānnasaṃsṛṣṭasyāhaviṣyasya homaḥ | udīcīnam uṣṇaṃ bhasmāpohya tasmin juhuyāt tad dhutam ahutaṃ cāgnau bhavati" iti | pāraskaro 'py agnaukaraṇam āha |

	datvā gandhādi dhūpāṃś ca sarpiṣmad dhavir uddharet |

	paitṛkair abhyanujñāto juhoti pitṛyajñavat || iti |

paitṛkaid (?) brāhmaṇair iti śeṣaḥ,

	agnau kuryād anujñāto brāhmaṇo brāhmaṇaiḥ saha |

iti manusmaraṇāt | brāhmaṇaiḥ paitṛkaiḥ sarvaiḥ saha yugapad anujñāta ity arthaḥ | pitṛyajñavj juhotīty asyārtho hārītena prapañcitaḥ: "kuruṣvety anujñātaḥ pūrvoddhṛte 'gnau sakṛd ācchinnair upamūlalūnaiḥ paristīrṇe samit tantreṇa prāṅmukho mekṣaṇenāhutidvayaṃ hutvā mekṣaṇam agnāv eva kuryāt" iti | pūrvoddhṛte 'gnau paristaraṇāt pūrvam evodbodhite 'gnau mūlasamīpapradeśe sakṛd ekayatnena chinnair darbhaiḥ paristīrṇe samit tantreṇa prāṅmukho mekṣaṇena āhutidvayārtham ekām eva samidham ādāya mekṣaṇena yajñiyakāṣṭhakṛtena āhutidvayaṃ hutvā agnāv eva mekṣaṇaṃ prakṣiped ity arthaḥ | samit tantreṇety anena na pitṛyajñadharma uktaḥ, pitṛyajñe samidādhānasyābhāvāt | kiṃ tv iha dharmāntaram upadiṣṭam | tena suyajño 'py upadiṣṭadharmābhyāṃ sahātidiṣṭadharmān āha: "parsamūhya paryukṣya paristīrya dakṣiṇaṃ jānv ācya yajñopavītī prāṅāsīno (?) mekṣaṇena juhoti" iti | atra parisamūhanaparyukṣaṇe upadiṣṭe | "juhuyāt pitṛyajñavat" ity atideśataḥ prāptau homamantrau madālasayā darśitau |

	agnaye kavyavāhanāya svāheti prathamāhutiḥ |

	somāya vai pitṛmate svāhety anyā tathā bhavet ||

vaiśabdaḥ pādapūraṇārthatvāt sa prayogakāle na prayojyaḥ | gobilena tu viparītakrameṇa purastāt svāhākārau homamantrau agnaukaraṇam adhikṛtyoktau: "mekṣaṇenopaghātaṃ juhuyāt svāhā somāya pitṛmate iti prathamām, svāhāgnaye kavyavāhanāyeti dvitīyām, ata ūrdhvaṃ prācīnāvītī" iti | homāntaraṃ prācīnāvītīty abhidhānād arthād dhome yajñopavītīty eveti gamyate | mekṣaṇenopaghātaṃ mekṣaṇenāvadāya juhotīty arthaḥ | purāṇe tv āhutitrayapakṣaḥ svadhānamo'ntair mantrair uktaḥ |

	antar nidhāya samidhaṃ juhuyāj jātavedasi |

	agnaye kavyavāhanāya svadhā nama iti bruvan ||

	somāya ca pitṛmate svadhā nama iti bruvan |

	ity ete homamantrās tu trayāṇām anupūrvaśaḥ ||

	uttarato 'gnaye nityaṃ somāyeti ca dakṣiṇe |

	etayor antare nityaṃ juhuyād vai vivasvataḥ || iti |

atra nidheyāyāḥ samidho grāhyāgrāhatvanirūpaṇārtham uktaṃ tatraiva |

	palāśaphalgunyagrodhaplakṣāśvatthavikaṅkatāḥ |

	udumbaraśamībilvacandanā yajñiyāś ca ye ||

	panaso devadāruś ca sālaś ca khadiras tathā |

	samidarthe praśastāḥ syur ete vṛkṣā viśeṣataḥ ||

	grāhyāḥ kaṇṭakinaś caiva yajñiyā ye ca kecana |

	śleṣmātako naktamālaḥ kapitthaḥ śālmalis tathā ||

	nīpo vibhītakaś caiva śrāddhakarmaṇi garhitāḥ |

	ciribilvas tathā ṭaṅkas tindukāmrātakau tathā ||

	tilbakaḥ kovidāraś ca ete śrāddhavigarhitāḥ ||

phalguḥ kākodumbarikā | emasuktāhutisaṃkhyāvikalpo (?) vyapadeśād eva siddhaḥ | prakṛtau piṇḍapitṛyajñe pakṣadvayam apy uktam | tathā āpastambaḥ piṇḍapitṛyajñam adhikṛtyāha: "adhvaryur upavītī dakṣiṇaṃ jānv ācya mekṣaṇe upastīrya tenāvadāyābhighārya somāya pitṛpītāya svadhā nama iti dakṣiṇāgnau juhoti | yamāyāṅgirasvate pitṛmate svadhā nama iti dvitīyām, agnaye kavyavāhanāya svadhā nama it trtīyāṃ ye mekṣaṇe taṇḍulās tān hutvā tūṇīṃ mekṣaṇam ādadhāti na yamāya juhotīty eke" iti | svadhānamo'ntamantrāṇāṃ svāhārāntamantraiḥ saha vikalpo 'pi pūrvavad atideśata eva siddhāḥ, prakṛtau dvividhamantrāṇām abhidhānāt | tatra svadhānamo'ntā mantrā āpastambenoktā darśitāḥ | svāhāntamantrās tu piṇḍapitṛyajñe sāṅkhyāyanenoktāḥ: "dakṣiṇaṃ jānv ācya yajñopavītī prāṅāsīno mekṣaṇena juhoty agnaye kavyavāhanāya svāhā somāya yamāyāṅgirasvate (?) pitṛmate svāhā" iti | somāyety atra pitṛmate svāhety anuṣajyate | ato 'gnaye svāhā somāya svāheti viśeṣavihitāv api mantrāv atideśato 'gnaukaraṇe (?) sthaḥ, prakṛtāv evaṃvidhayor api mantrayor upadeśāt | tathā ca piṇḍapitṛyajñam adhikṛtya vaijāvāpaḥ: "ājyam āsicyodvāsya yajñopavītīty anvāhāryapacane mekṣaṇena dve āhutī juhoty agnaya iti pūrvāṃ somāyety uttarām" iti | anvāhāryapacano dakṣiṇāgniḥ | evaṃ piṇḍapitṛyajñahome yajñopavītitvam "upavītaṃ devānām" iti śrutyā daivaikadharmatvenāvagataṃ bruvāṇā āpastambasāṅkhyāyanavaijavāpakalpasūtrakārāḥ piṇḍapitṛyajñe homātmakaṃ pradhānaṃ daivikam iti manyante | kātyāyano 'py evam eva manyate | yad āha |

	agnaukaraṇahomas tu kartavya upavītinā |

	prāṅmukhenaiva devebhyo juhotīti śrutiśruteḥ || iti |

ayam arthaḥ: agnaukaraṇahomaprakṛtibhūtapiṇḍapitṛyajñahomavidhāyakasrutau "sa udvāsyāgnau dve āhutī juhiti devebhyaḥ" iti śruteḥ tadbalāt prakṛtidaivikadharmavat tadvikṛtibhūāgnaukaraṇahomo 'py upavītitvādidaivikadharmeṇa kartavya iti | atra "dve āhutī juhoti" iti vihitahomadvaye "somāya pitṛmate svāhāgnaye kavyavāhanāya svāhā" iti mantravarṇe devatātvenāvagatayoḥ somāgnyoḥ cāturmāsyāntargatapitṛyajñavākyaśeṣādiṣu kvacit pitṛrūpeṇa kvacid devarūpeṇa vyapadeśadarśanād iha kiṃ pitṛrūpayor devatātvam uta devarūpayor iti saṃdehe devebhyo (?) ity anuvādasarūparthavādadarśanād iha devarūpayor eva devatātvam iti gamyata ity abhiprāyeṇa devebhyo juhotīti śrutiśruter ity uktam | na tu sākṣād devarūpayor eva devatātvam iti śrutau śrūyat ity abhiprāyeṇeti mantavyam | ata evānantaram aparitoāt pakṣāntaram uktaṃ tenaiva |

	apasavyena vā kāryo dakṣinābhimukhena vā |

	nirūpya havir anyasmā anyasmai na hi hūyate || iti |

asyārthaḥ: piṇḍapitṛyajñe "pitṛbhyo juṣṭaṃ nirvapāmi" iti mantreṇa sakṛd eva homārthaṃ pitṛdevatārthaṃ ca nirvāpaḥ kriyate | tataś ca nirvāpamantrasāmarthyāt pitṛrūpayor eva somāgnyor homadevatātvam iti gamyate | devarūpayos tu devatātve devebhya iti vākyaseṣabalād āśriyamāṇe anyasmai niruptam anyasmai hūyata ity ayuktaṃ syāt | tasmāt pitṛūpayor eva devatātvaṃ tena prakṛtibhūto homaḥ prācīnāvītinā dakṣiṇābhimukhena ca kriyate iti vikṛtibhūtāgnaukaraṇahomo 'pi prācīnāvītinā dakṣiṇāmukhena ca kārya iti | ayam eva pakṣaḥ śreyān iti manyamāna āśvalāyanaḥ svamatatvena piṇḍapitṛyajñahomaṃ paitṛkadharmakaṃ paramatatvena daivikadharmakam āha: "prācīnāvītīdhmam upasamādhāya mekṣaṇenāvadāyāvadānasaṃpadā juhuyāt somāya pitṛmate svadhā namo 'gnaye kavyavāhanāya svadhā nama iti svāhākāreṇa vāgnipūrvaṃ yajñopavītī" iti | evaṃ prakṛtibhūtapiṇḍapitṛyajñasyobhayavidhatvena vikalpitadharkatvāt tadvikṛtibhūtāgnaukaraṇahomo 'py atideśata eva vikalpitadharmaka iti yajñopavītinā prācīnāvītinā vā kāryaḥ | tatra āśvalāyanagṛhyānusāriṇāṃ paitṛkadharmakaḥ kāryaḥ | tathā ca tenaiva svakṛtagṛhye 'bhihitam: "uddhṛtya ghṛtāktam annam anujñāpayaty agnau kariṣye karavai karavāṇīti vā | pratyabhyanujñā kriyatāṃ kuruṣva kurviti vā | athāgnau juhoti yathoktaṃ purastāt" iti | kātyāyanagṛhye tu: "uddhṛtya ghṛtākam annaṃ pṛcchtyāgnau (?) kariṣya iti kuruṣvety anujñātaḥ piṇḍapitṛyajñavad dhutvā" ity uktam, tatra yady api piṇḍapitṛyajñaśabdena piṇḍaiḥ sādhyaḥ pitṛyajñaḥ piṇḍapitṛyajña iti vyutpattyā piṇḍadānātmakapitṛyajñasyaiva nāmadheyam, na tu homātmakapiṇḍapitṛyajñasyeti pratibhāti, tathāpi piṇḍādānātmakapitṛyajñasya homātmakapitṛyajñasya ca daṇḍina itivallakṣaṇayā nāmadheyam, cāturmāsyeṣu prathamaparvaṇi kriyamāṇānām āgneyādisaptayāgānāṃ vaiśvadevayāgasya ca vaiśvadevanāmadheyavat | evaṃ ca piṇḍadānaṃ homaś cātra pradhānam, na tu piṇḍadānam eva pradhānaṃ homo 'ṅgam | yata evaṃ homo 'pi pradhānam, ata evoktam āpastambena: "yadi jīvapitā dadyād ā homāt kṛtvā viramet" iti | yadi tu homo 'ṅgam, tadā piṇḍadānākhyapradhānanivṛttau prayojakapradhānasyābhāvād aṅgabhūtahomasyāpi nivṛtteḥ "ā homāt kṛtvā viramet" it sūtram atyantānupapannaṃ syāt | tato jñāyate homātmako 'pi pitṛyajñaḥ pradhānabhūta iti | evaṃ ca pitṛyajñavad dhutvā, ity asyāyam arthaḥ: homātmakapiṇḍapiṛyajñavad agnaukaraṇaṃ kuryād iti | evaṃ vadatas tasya svakīyasmṛtau |

	prāṅmukhenaiva devebhyo juhotīti śrutiśruteḥ |

	nirupya havir anyasmā anyasmai na hi hūyate ||

ity etābhyām uktadaivikapaitṛkadharmapiṇḍapitṛyajñavad ity abhiprāyaḥ prayetavyaḥ, piṇḍapitṛyajñavidhāyakasūtraviśeṣānukteḥ | baijavāpagṛhya: "yajñopavīty agnau akravāṇītyāmantryagnaukaraṇam" ity abhidhānāt svasūtroktapiṇḍapitṛyajñavad agnaukaraṇahomo daivikadharmavān iti sphuṭam | yat tu yājñavalkyena piṇḍapitṛyajñam anuktvaivoktam,

	oṃ kuruṣvety anujñāto hutvāgnau pitṛyajñavat |

iti, yac ca pāraskareṇa,

	paitṛkair abhyanujñāto juhoti pitṛyajñavat | 

iti, atra sarvatra daivikadharmakapitṛyajñavad ity artho grāhyaḥ "daivikadharmakapitṛyajñavat" it bahubhiḥ sūtrakārair uktatvāt | na ca bahubhir uktatvam aprayojakam iti vācyam "bhūyasāṃ syāt sadharmatvam" iti jaimininā prayojakatvasyābhidhānāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> bhūyasām api matam "nirūpya havir anyasmā anyasmai na hi hūyate" iti nyāyaviruddhatvād aprayojakam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span>, te khalv āpastambādayo 'py evaṃ manyante yathā darśayogenaikadevatāsaṃbandhitvena nirupteṣu śūrparūpaikasthānagateṣu prokṣitavyeṣu "agnaye vo juṣṭaṃ prokṣāmi" iti prokṣaṇamantrastho va ity ayaṃ śabdaḥ keṣucit paryavasyati na sarveṣu vartate | yathā ca teṣv eva vrīhiṣu "indrāgnibhyāṃ vo juṣṭaṃ prokṣāmi" iti prokṣaṇamantrastho va ity ayaṃ śabdaḥ keṣucit paryavasyati na sarveṣu vartate | tathā sthālīrūpaikasthānagateṣu vrīhiṣu "pitṛbhyo vo juṣṭaṃ nirvapāmi" iti nirvāpamantrastho va ity ayaṃ śabdaḥ keṣucit paryavasyati na sarveṣu vrīhiṣu vartate iti na sthālisthaṃ sarvaṃ pitṛbhyo niruptaṃ kiṃ tu tadardham, tena pitṛbhyo niruptaṃ pitṛmadantasomādibhyo hūyate ato na bhūyasāṃ mataṃ nyāyaviruddham iti sarvam anavdyam | tūṣṇīm eva sarvanirvāpapakṣe tu nyāyāvirodhaḥ sutarām | so 'pi pakṣa āpastambenoktaḥ: "mṛṇmaye nirvapati pitṛbhyo vo juṣṭaṃ nirvapāmīti tūṣṇīṃ vā" iti | bhedena nirvāpapakṣe dūrotsārito nyāyavirodhaḥ | ayaṃ tu pakṣo vatsenoktaḥ: " pavitrāntarhite caruṃ nirvapati trir yajñopavītī dakṣiṇena hastena triḥ prācīnāvītī savyena hastena yajñopavītī mekṣaṇena juhuyāt somāya pitṛmate svadhā namo yamāyāṅgirasvate pitṛmate svadhā namo 'gnaye kavyavāhanāya svadhā namaḥ" | tasmāt smṛtiṣu pitṛyajñaśabdena daivikadharmapitṛyajñābhidhānaṃ yuktam | yat tu manunoktam,

	apasavyam agnau kṛtvā sarvam āvṛtparikramam | 

tad āśvalāyanaśākhīyaviṣayam,

	svāhā svadhā namaḥ savyam apasavyaṃ tathaiv ca |

	āhutīnāṃ tu yā saṃkhyā sāvagamyā svasūtrataḥ ||

iti kātyāyanasmaraṇāt | evaṃ ca yā āpastambenoktāhutīnāṃ trayodaśasṃkhyā sā āpastambasūtriṇāmity avagantavyam | āpastambena dharmaśāstrasūtre: "uddhriyatām agnau ca kriyatām ity āmantrayate | kāmam uddhriyatāṃ kāmam agnau ca kriyatām ity atisṛṣṭam uddharej juhuyāc ca" ity agnaukaraṇavidhānād āhutisaṃkhyā yady api vaktavyā | tathāpi svakṛtagṛhyasūtra anūditamantravidhānmukhenārthād āhutīnāṃ trayodaśasaṃkhyā darśite 'pi tatra saṃkhyā nokteti mantavyam | atisṛṣṭo 'abhyanujñātaḥ | evaṃ coddharaṇapraśnādikaṃ kṛtvānnam uddhṛtyāgner upasamādhānādyājyabhāgāntaṃ kuryāt, āpastambīyagṛhyoktakrameṇa vakṣyamāṇatattatpradhānahomasādhāraṇatayā prācyāṅgakalāpasya vihitatvāt | ājyabhāgānte, "yan me mātā" ityādimantrair juhuyāt | tathā ca āpastambīyagṛhyam: "annasyottarābhir juhoty ājyāhutīr uttarāḥ" iti | uddhṛtasyānnasya kiṃcit kiṃcid avadānadharmeṇāvadāya darvyāṃ nidhāya "yan me mātā pralulobha carati, yās tiṣṭhanti" iti dvābhyāṃ ṛgbhyāṃ amuṣmai svāhety antābhyāṃ amuṣmā ity atra caturthyantatayā pitur nāma gṛhītvā dve āhutī juhoti | evam eva "yan me pitāmahī pralulobha carati antardadhe parvataiḥ" iti dvābhyām ṛgbhyām amuṣmai svāhety antābhyāṃ amuṣmā ity atra caturtyantatayā pitāmahasya nāma gṛhītvā dve āhutī juhoti | evam eva "yan me pitāmahī pralulobha carati, antardadhe parvataiḥ" iti dvābhyām ṛgbhyām amuṣmai svāhetyantābhyām amuṣmā ity atra caturthyantatayā pitāmahasya nām gṛhītvā dve āhitī juhoti | evam eva "yan me prapitāmahī pralulobha carati, antardadha ṛtubhiḥ" iti dvābhyām amuṣmai svāhetyantābhyāṃ amuṣmā ity atra caturthyantatayā prapitāmahasya nām gṛhītvā dve śhutī juhoti | "yan me mātāmahī pralulobha carati, yās tiṣṭhanti" iti dvābhyāṃ mātāmahāya dve āhutī juhoti | "yan me mātuḥpitāmahī pralulobha carati, antardadhe parvataiḥ" iti dvābhyāṃ mātuḥpitāmahāya dve āhutī juhoti | iti dvābhyāṃ mātuḥprapitāmahāya dve āhutī juhoti | atra prathamamantre yan me mātāmahī pralulobha carat .................... tan me reto mātāmaho vṛṅktām ity ūhaḥ kāryaḥ | dvitīye mantre antar anyaṃ mātāmahād vadha ity ūhaḥ | mantradvaye 'py amuṣmā ity atra mātāmahasya caturtyantatayā nāmagrahaṇaṃ kāryam | tṛtīye mantre yan me mātuḥ pitāmahī pralulobha carat .............. tan me mātuḥ pitāmaho vṛṅktām ity ūhaḥ | caturthe mantre matuḥ pitāmahād vadha ity ūhaḥ | mantradvaye 'py amuṣmā ity atra mātuḥ pitāmahanāmagrahaṇaṃ kāryam | pañcame mantre yan me mātuḥ prapitāmahī pralulobha carati ............ tan me mātuḥ prapitāmaho vṛkktām ity ūhaḥ | ṣaṣṭhe mantre antar anyaṃ mātuḥ prapitāmahād vadha ity ūhaḥ | mantradvaye 'py amuṣmā ity atra mātuḥ prapitamahanāmagrahaṇaṃ kāryam,

	yojyāḥ pitrādiśabdānāṃ sthāne mātāmahādikāḥ |

	annahome tathā sparśe jalapiṇḍādidānake ||

	yan me mātāmahītyādi tatrodāharaṇam bhavet ||

iti gṛhyabhāṣyārthasaṃgrahakāreṇoktatvāt | sparśe "eṣa te tata madhumān ūrmiḥ saraḥ svān" (?) ityādimantratrayeṇa brāhmaṇabhojanārthānnasparśe | tataḥ pūrvavad avadāya "ye ceha pitaraḥ" ity ṛcā ekām āhitiṃ juhoti evam annāhutīr hutvā ṣaḍājyāhutīr juhoti — tatra "svāhā pitre" iti purastāt svāhāhutiṃ juhoti | upariṣṭāt svāhākāreṇa dvitīyām | etābhyām eva mantrābhyāṃ tṛtīyāṃ caturthīm āhutiṃ hutvā svadhā svāheti pañcamīṃ juhoty agnaye kavyavāhanāya svāheti ṣaṣṭhīṃ tataḥ sviṣṭakṛtaṃ hutvā bhakṣyabhojyasarvavidhāhviṣyānnāt kiṃcid ādāyodīcīnaṃ bhasmāpohya tasminn uṣṇe bhasmani tūṣṇīṃ juhoti | tato lepayoḥ prastaravat tūṣṇīṃ barhir aktvāgnau praharatītyādi pariṣecanāntaṃ pāścātyāṅgakalāpam āgneyasthālīpākoktaṃ kṛtvā hutaśeṣaṃ brāhmaṇabhojanapātreṣu nidadhyāt | etat sarvaṃ tadbhāṣyārthasaṃgrahakāreṇoktam |

	agnīndhanādi pratipadya karma kṛtvājyabhāgāntam athāvadāya |

	yan meti mantraiḥ pratimantram agnau kuryus tathā saptabhir annahomān ||

	svāhādimantrair api sarpiṣā syur homās tataḥ sviṣṭakṛtaṃ ca hutvā |

	bhasmāpy apohyāhavirannahomo lepeṣu darvyoś ca samañjanādi |

	śeṣaṃ ca kṛtvā pariṣecanāntaṃ pātreṣu dadyād dhutaśeṣam annam || iti |

saptabhir annahomā ity anūhitamantrābhiprāyoktam, ūhitamantrasāhitye trayodaśasaṃkhyāsaṃpatteḥ saptabhir ity ayogāt | evam etad agnaukaraṇaṃ prācīnāvītinā kāryam, paitṛkatvāt | tathā ca āpastambena svakṛtagṛhyaśāstrādāv uktam: "aparapakṣe pitryāṇi prācīnāvītinā prasavyaṃ dakṣiṇatopavargaḥ" iti | tatrāpi yad apaitṛkam āghārasamindhanādikaṃ tat yajñopavītinā kāryam, ata eva bhāṣyārthasaṃgrahakāreṇoktam |

	āghāradārvagnimukhājyabhāgapradakṣiṇānuvrajaneṣu tadvat |

	āghārayoḥ sviṣṭakṛti pradiṣṭaṃ yajñopavītaṃ hi kapardinaḥ syāt ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyām agnaukaraṇavidhiḥ**

**athobhayavidhāgnaukaraṇārthāgninirṇayaḥ**

tatra yājñavalkyaḥ |

	karma smārtaṃ vivāhāgnau kurvīta pratyahaṃ gṛhī |

	dāyakālāhṛte vāpi śrautaṃ vaitānikāgniṣu ||

smārtaṃ karma aupāsanahomavaiśvadevakaraṇāgnaukaraṇādikam | vivāhāgnau vivahakālotpannaupāsanāgnau | dāyakālāhṛte dāyakāle vaiśyādikulād āhṛtyotpādite aupāsanāgnau kurvītety arthaḥ | sarvādhāne aupāsanāsaṃbhave tv āpastamboktāgnaukaraṇahomasya lopaḥ, na tu vaitānikāgnāv anuṣṭhānam, "śrautaṃ vaitānikāgniṣu" ity abhidhānāt | na tu laukike, devatāder ivāgner api pratinidhyabhāvāt | ata eva sarvādhānenaupāsanāsaṃbhave dhūrtasvāminoktam: "śrāddham ūrdhvaṃ homāt kartavyaṃ brāhmaṇas tv āhavanīyārthe iti tasyāpi pradhānatvāt" iti | tasyāpi homād ūrdhvaṃ kriyamāṇasyānnapradānalakṣaṇśrāddhasyāpīty arthaḥ | pitṛyajñadharmakāgnaukaraṇasya tu sarvādhānenaupāsanābhāve 'pi na nivṛttiḥ "karma smārthaṃ vivāhagnau" ityādinopadiṣṭaupāsanāgnyabhāve 'pi "pitṛyajñavat" ity atideśataḥprātadakṣiṇāgneḥ saṃbhavād dakṣiṇāgnāv anuṣṭhānam | anenaivābhiprāyeṇa mārkaṇḍeyenoktam |

	āhitāgnis tu juhuyād dakṣināgnau samāhitaḥ | iti |

āpastamboktāgnaukaraṇe tu piṇḍapitṛyajñātideśābhāvān na dakṣiṇāgniprāptir iti sarvādhāne dhūrtasvāmyuktāgnaukaraṇābhāva eva yuktaḥ | pūrvoktābhiprāyeṇa vāyupurāṇe 'py uktam |

	āhṛtya dakṣiṇāgniṃ tu homārthaṃ vai prayatnataḥ |

	agnyarthaṃ laukikaṃ vāpi juhuyāt karmasiddhaye || iti |

asyārthaḥ: agnaukaraṇahomārthaṃ gṛhyāgnyabhāve dakṣiṇāgniṃ laukikaṃ vāpy āhṛtya svīkṛtya homakarmasiddhaye juhuyād iti | agnyartham ity anena gṛhyāgnibhāve (?) tu nāgnyantarasvīkāra ity arthād uktam | tatra dakṣināgnipakṣasya pravāsādinā asaṃbhave laukikāgnipakxaḥ, tasyopadeśātideśarūpapramāṇadvayāvagatasya dakṣināgnibhādakatvenāgatyāśrayaṇiyatvāt | ata eva prayatnato dakṣināgnim āhṛtyety uktam | yat tu smṛtyantaram |

	sāgnir agnāv anagnis tu dvijapāṇāv athāpsu vā |

	kuryād agnau kriyāṃ nityaṃ laukike neti nitścitam || iti |

tasyāyam arthaḥ: agnimān puruṣaḥ aupāsanāgnau dakṣiṇāgnau vā pūrvoktavyasthayāgnaukaraṇaṃ kuryāt | dāyāt prāg asvīkṛtaupāsanatayā chinnāgnitayā vā bhāryāvidhuratayā vā yo 'gnir ahitaḥ sa dvijapāṇāv apsu vāgnaukaraṇaṃ kuryāt, na jātu laukikāgnau kuryād iti | tataś ca na vāyupurāṇavacanavirodhaḥ | śrautāgninā sāgnikasyāpy anignikavat kvacid viṣaye dvijapāṇāv agnaukaraṇaṃ kāryam | tathā ca smṛtyantaram |

	haste 'gnaukaraṇam kuryād agnau vā sāgniko dvijaḥ | iti |

atrāgniśabdena na gṛhyāgnir ucyate, tasmin vidyamāne hastapakṣanavakāśāt | tena śrautāgnir ucyate laukiko vā | sāgnikaśabdena sarvādhāny evocyate | tataś cāyam arthaḥ: sarvādhānenaupāsanāgnyabhāve pitṛyajñadharmakāgnaukaraṇaṃ dakṣiṇāgnau, tadasaṃnidhāne laukikāgnau dvijapāṇau vā kuryād iti | tatrāpi pravāsādinā dakṣiṇāgnyabhāve laukikāgnihastapakṣau pūrvoktanyāyavad avagantavyau | laukikāgnes tādṛśaviśeṣānavagamāt pāṇinā saha samavikalpa eva | yady api nyāyato 'gneḥ pratinidhyabhāvaḥ, tathāpi na pratinidhinyāyenātra dakṣiṇāgnyāder upādānam | kiṃ tu gṛhyāgnyabhāvena tatsādhyakarmaṇo 'nanuṣṭhāne prāpte vacanenāgṛhyāgnyādāv api gṛhyāgnisādhyaṃ karma vidhīyata iti na kaścid doṣaḥ | evaṃ cānāhitāgner aupāsanavad āhitāgner apy ardhādhāninaḥ ubhayavidhāgnaukaraṇahomaḥ aupāsana eva | sarvādhānenaupāsanarahitasyāhitāgner āpastamboktāgnaukaraṇābhāva eva | piṇḍapitṛyajñadharmakāgnaukaraṇasya tu dakṣiṇāgau, tadasaṃnidhau laukikāgnau dvujapāṇau vānuṣṭhānam | anagnikasya dvijapāṇāv apsu vā ubhayavidham agnaukaraṇam iti siddham | anāhitāgner aupāsanavad āhitāgner ardhādhānenaupāsanavataḥ pravāsādinā kathaṃcid aupāsanāsaṃnidhāne dvijapāṇāv apsu vāgnaukaraṇaṃ kartavyam | tathā ca viṣṇudharmottare mārkaṇḍeyaḥ |

	anāhitāgniś caupasade 'gnyabhāve dvije 'psu vā | iti |

aupasado gṛhyāgniḥ | anāhitāgniś ceti caśabda āhitāgneḥ samuccayārthaḥ | tataś cāyam arthaḥ: anāhitāgnir āhitāgniś cārdhādhānenaupāsanavān gṛhyāgnisaṃnidhau tatrauvāgnaukaraṇaṃ kuryāt | agnyabhāve gṛhyāgnyasaṃnidhāne 'psu dvijapāṇau vāgnaukaraṇaṃ kuryād iti | atrāpsv iti pakṣasya viṣayaviśeṣaḥ kātyāyanena darśitaḥ |

	agnaukaraṇahomaṃ tu kuryād apsv iti yan matam |

	sa yadāpāṃ samīpe syāt śrāddhaṃ jñeyo vidhis tadā ||

evaṃ cāpāṃ samīpād anyatra yadā śrāddhaṃ tadaiva dvijapāṇāv iti pakṣo grāhyaḥ | ayaṃ ca viṣayavibhāgaḥ "anagnis tu dvijapāṇāv athāpsu vā" ity atrāpi draṣṭavyaḥ, viṣṇudharmottare mārkaṇḍeya ity uktasmṛtyantaravivakṣāyāṃ kāraṇābhāvāt | yat tu manunoktam,

	agnyabhāve tu viprasya pāṇāv evopasādayet |

iti, tat bhāryāparigrahāt pūrvam anuṣṭheyanityanaimittikaśrāddhaviṣayam | ayam eva viṣayo jātūkarṇena spaṣṭīkṛtaḥ |

	agnyabhāve tu viprasya pāṇau dadyāt tu dakṣiṇe |

	agnyabhāvaḥ smṛtas tāvad yāvad bhāryāṃ na vindati || iti |

dakṣiṇe pāṇau dadyāt ubhayavidhāgnaukaraṇāhutyartham annam iti śeṣaḥ | yas tu gṛhyapariśiṣṭakāreṇoktam |

	anvaṣṭakyaṃ ca pūrvedyur māsi māsy atha pārvaṇam |

	kāmyam abhyudaye 'ṣṭamyām ekoddiṣṭam athāṣṭamam ||

	caturṣv ādyeṣu sāgnīnām agnau homo vidhīyate |

	pitryabrāhmaṇahaste syād uttareṣu caturṣv api ||

iti, "hemantaśiśirayorś caturṇām aparapakṣāṇām aṣṭamīṣv aṣṭakāḥ" iti vihitāny aṣṭakāśrāddhāni | tatra aṣṭakāśrāddhadinād uttaradine navamyāṃ kriyamāṇaṃ śrāddham anvaṣṭakyam, pūrve 'hni saptamyāṃ kriyamāṇaṃ śrāddhaṃ pūrvedyur iti padena lakṣaṇayoktam | pratimāsaṃ kriyamāṇam āparapakṣikaṃ śrāddhaṃ māsi māsīty anenoktam | pārvaṇaṃ sarvaśrāddhaprakṛtibhūtaṃ darśaśrāddham | kāmyaṃ putrādikāmanayā kriyamāṇaṃ śrāddham | ābhyudayikaṃ śrāddham abhyudayapadenoktam | aṣṭakākhyaṃ śrāddham āṣṭamyām iti padenoktam | ekoddiṣṭam iti padena sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ lakṣaṇayoktam, sapiṇḍīkaraṇe ekoddiṣṭasyāpi sadbhāvāt | eṣāṃ madhye ādyeṣu caturṣu sāgnikānām agnāv evāgnaukaraṇahomaḥ | uttareṣu tu sāgnīnāṃ pitryabrāhmaṇahasta eveti tasyārthaḥ | tad etat yeṣāṃ gṛhyapariśiṣṭaṃ teṣām eva vyavasthāpakaṃ na sarveṣām | ato na pūrvoktavyavasthāvirodha iti sarvam anavadyam | yadā tu pāṇihomapakṣaḥ tadaikasyaiva viprasya pāṇau homo na sarvaviprāṇām ity āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	pitrye yaḥ paṅktimūrdhanyaḥ tasya pāṇāv anagnikaḥ |

	hutvā mantravad anyeṣāṃ tūṣṇīṃ pātreṣu nikṣipet || iti |

pitryaprathamabrāhmaṇapāṇau homo 'yaṃ na nityaḥ,

	daivaviprakare 'nagniḥ kṛtvāgnaukaraṇaṃ dvijaḥ |

iti yamena vaiśvadaivikabrāhmaṇapāṇāv agnaukaraṇahomavidhānāt | evaṃ ca vrīhiyavavat pitryavaiśvadaivikabrāhmaṇapāṇyor vikalpo veditavyaḥ | daivavipraharahomapakṣe 'pi hutaśeṣaṃ pitryabrāhmaṇabhojanapātreṣv eva nikṣipet | tathā ca vāyupurāṇam |

	hutvā daivakare 'nagniḥ śeṣaṃ pitrye nivedayet |

	na hi smṛtāḥ śeṣabhājo viśvedevāḥ purāṇagaiḥ ||

daivaviprkarād anyatra pitṛviprapāṇyagnau home 'pi hutaśeṣabhājo viśvedevā na bhavantīti jñāpayituṃ na hi smṛtāḥ śeṣabhājo viśvedevā iti sāmānyenoktam | yata eva sāmānyena śeṣabhājo viśvedevā na bhavantīti ata eva viśeṣeṇa purāṇāntare śeṣadānaṃ pratiṣidhyate |

	agnaukaraṇaśeṣaṃ tu na dadyād vaiśvadaivike | iti |

agnaukaraṇahomaṃ vaiśvadaivikabrāhmaṇapāṇau kurvann apy ekabrāhmaṇapāṇāv eva kuryāt, guṇānurodhena pradhānānāvṛtter agnitvenaikaviprapāṇāv evānuṣṭheyatvāt | tad etad uktaṃ vāyupurāṇe |

	vaiśvadaive yadaikasmin bhaveyuḥ dvyādayo dvijāḥ |

	tadaikapāṇau hotavyaṃ syād vidhir vihitas tathā ||

yadaikasmin vaiśvadaivikabrāhmaṇabhojanakarmaṇi dvau catvāraḥ ṣaḍ ity evaṃ yugmasaṃkhyayā dvyādayo viprā daivikatvena bhaveyuḥ tadaikasya prathamopaviṣṭasya viprasya pāṇau hotavyaṃ tatrāhutividhir vihitaḥ syād anuṣṭhito bhaved ity arthaḥ | evaṃ brāhmaṇapāṇāv agnaukaraṇahomaṃ kariṣye karavai karavāṇīti vā brāhmaṇānujñāpanam, tathāstv iti brāhmaṇaiḥ prativacanaṃ bhaved ity āha śaunakaḥ: "anagnikaś ced ādyaṃ gṛhītvā bhatsv evāgnaukaraṇahomaṃ kuryāc cet | ādyaṃ ghṛtāktam annam | pūrvavat brāhmaṇānujñāpanam iti śeṣaḥ | tathāstv iti brāhmaṇānāṃ prativacanam iti śeṣaḥ | yat tu smṛtyarthasāre 'bhihitam: "pāṇihome tv idhmamekṣaṇaviprānujñā na santi" iti, tatra viprānujñābhāvoktir etadvacanādarśananibandhanety upekṣaṇīyā | mekṣaṇābhāvoktir api cintyā, mekṣaṇakāryasya vidhyadarśanāt | yac ca tatraivābhihitaṃ "parismūhanaparyukṣaṇe sthaḥ" iti, tad ap cintyam, tayor dṛṣṭakāryasya dhūlyapagamāder atrābhāvāt, niyamādṛṣṭamātrasyāprayojakatvāt | yasya tv adṛṣṭasaṃskāraḥ kāryaṃ paristaraṇasya tad atrāsti | tathā ca yamaḥ |

	agnaukaraṇavat tatra homo daivakare bhavet |

	paryastadarbhān āstīrya yato hy agnisamo hi saḥ || iti |

daivakaro vaiśvadaivikabrāhmaṇapāṇiḥ | paryastadarbhāḥ paritaḥ sarvato nyasnīyadarbhāḥ paristaraṇadarbhā iti yāvat | daivakaragrahaṇaṃ pitryabrāhmaṇakarasyāpy upalakṣaṇārtham | brāhmaṇapāṇau hutaṃ tadānīya tadānīm eva brāhmaṇena na bhhoktavyam, api tu bhojanakāle | tathā ca bahvṛcagṛhyapariśiṣṭam |

	annaṃ pāṇitale dattaṃ pūrvam aśnanty abuddhayaḥ |

	pitaras tena tṛpyanti śeṣānnaṃ na labhanti te ||

	yac ca pāṇitale dattaṃ yac cānyad upakalpitam |

	ekībhāvena bhoktavyaṃ pṛthagbhāvo na vidyate ||

śeṣānnaṃ viprabhojanārthaṃ saṃpāditam annam | pitryabrāhmaṇapāṇitalād anyatra pitṛyajñavad agnaukaraṇam | pitṛkaśrāddhe mātāmahaśrāddhe ca vaiśvadaivikaṃ tantram, dravyadevatāvad adhikaraṇakārakaikyasyāpi saṃpratipannatvāt | pitryabrāhmaṇapāṇitale kriyamāṇaṃ tu mātāmahabrāhmaṇapāṇitale 'py āvṛttyā kāryam, adhikaraṇakārakaikyasyāsaṃpratipannatvāt | ata eva kātyāyanaḥ |

	mātāmahasya bhede 'pi kuryāt tantre ca sāgnikaḥ | iti |

ayam arthaḥ: mātāmahasya brāhmaṇapāṇau pṛthag agnaukaraṇaṃ kuryāt | etac ca vaiśvadaivikabhedapakṣe tantrapakṣe ca samānam iti | yasmin viṣaye sāgnikasya pāṇau agnaukaraṇam uktaṃ tasmin viṣaye idaṃ vacanaṃ draṣṭavyam ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyām ubhavavidhāgnaukaraṇārthāgninirṇayaḥ **

**atha pariveṣaṇavidhiḥ**

tatrādāv amatrāṇi sati saṃbhave śreṣṭhāni saṃpādyāni | daive sauvarṇāni śreṣṭhāni | pitrye rājatāni | tathā ca śreṣṭhānīty anuvṛttāv atriḥ |

	bhojane hemarūpyāṇi daive pitrye yathākramam | iti |

eteṣām alābhe viṣṇuḥ: "taijasāni pātrāṇi dadyāt" iti | taijasāni kāṃsyatāmrādīni | teṣām alābhe pālāśaparṇanirmitāni,

	pālāśebhyo vinā na syuḥ parṇapātrāṇi bhojane |

ity atriṇābhidhānāt | parṇapātrapakṣe 'pi ghṛtādidravyadhāraṇārthaṃ taijasāni sati saṃbhave saṃpādyāni, "ghṛtādidāne taijasāni pātrāṇi" iti viṣṇusmaraṇāt | teṣām abhāve pālāśaparṇanirmitapatrapuṭāni ghṛtādidhāraṇārthāni bhavanti na kadācin mṛnmayapātrāṇi,

	na mṛnmayāni kurvīta bhojane daivapitryayoḥ |

ity atrismaraṇāt | yathāsaṃbhavalabdhānāṃ caiteṣāṃ pātrāṇāṃ dviḥ prakṣālanaṃ kāryam, tatrādāv apo ninīye hastena nirmṛjya prakṣālanam, anantaraṃ jalenaiva | tathā ca brahmāṇḍapurāṇam |

	prakṣālya hastapātrādi paścād adbhir vidhānavat |

	prakṣālanaṃ jalaṃ darbhaiḥ tilair miśraṃ kṣipec chucau ||

hastapātrādīti madhyamapadalopī samāsaḥ | hastanirmṛṣṭaṃ pātrādi prakṣālyety arthaḥ | pātraśabdena talam uktam, ādiśabdena ghṛtāder dhāraṇārthāni gṛhyante | pātraprakṣālanānantaraṃ yājñavalkyaḥ |

	hutaśeṣaṃ pradadyāt tu bhājaneṣu samāhitaḥ |

	yathālābhopapanneṣu raupyeṣu tu viśeṣataḥ ||

bhājaneṣu pitryabrāhmaṇārthabhājaneṣv ity arthaḥ, raupyeṣu tu viśeṣata iti pitryakarmaṇi praśastaraupyasamabhivyāhārāt | śaunakena tu spaṣṭam uktam |

	hutvāgnau pariśiṣṭaṃ tu pitṛpātreṣv anantaram |

	nivedyaivāpasavyena pariveṣaṇam ācaret ||

apasavyeneti pūrveṇaiva saṃbadhyate, na punar uttareṇa,

	apasavyena kartavyaṃ pitryaṃ kṛtyaṃ viśeṣataḥ |

	annadānād ṛte sarvam evaṃ mātāmaheṣv api ||

iti kārṣṇājinismaraṇāt | annadānam annaprakṣepaḥ pariveṣaṇam iti yāvat | evaṃ ca śrāddhakartrā pariveṣaṇaṃ kāryam ity arthād uktam | uktaṃ ca sākṣān manunā |

	pāṇibhyām upasaṃgṛhya svayam annasya bandhukam |

	viprāntike pitṝn dhyāyan śanair upari nikṣipet ||

annasya bandhukam annena pūrṇaṃ pariveṣaṇapātram iti yāvat | pāṇibhyām upasaṃgṛhya viprabhojanapātre śanair nikṣipet | pitṝn dhyāyann iti pitryavipraviṣayam, daivavipraviṣaye annam ity uktatvāt | yat tu vāyupurāṇe 'bhihitam,

	pariveṣaṇaṃ praśastaṃ syād bhāryayā pitṛtṛptaye |

	pitṛdevamanuṣyāṇāṃ strīsāhāyyaṃ yataḥ smṛtam ||

iti, tatra praśastam ity atra paricārakakartṛkapariveṣaṇād iti śeṣo draṣṭavyaḥ | svayaṃkartṛkapariveṣaṇāpekṣayā prāśastyāsaṃbhavāt | ata evānantaram uktaṃ tatraiva |

	phalasyānantatā proktā svayaṃ tu pariveṣaṇe | iti |

evaṃ ca svayaṃ patnī anye vā niyatāḥ śūdravyatiriktāḥ pariveśaṇaṃ kartum arhantīty avagantavyam | patny apy asavarṇā na pariveṣaṇārhā | ata eva nārāyaṇenoktam |

	yad dhavyaṃ yat pavitraṃ ca yat pitryaṃ yat sukhāvaham |

	dvijātibhyaḥ savarṇāyā nāryā hastena dīyate || iti |

hastena hastadvayenety arthaḥ,

	ubhābhyām api hastābhyām āhṛtya pariveṣayet |

iti matsyenoktatvāt | hastadvayenāpi na sākṣād deyam, kiṃ tu darvyādidvārā,

	hastadattās ye snehalavaṇavyañjanādayaḥ |

	dātāraṃ nopatiṣṭhanti bhoktā bhuñjīta kilbiṣam ||

iti vṛddhaśātātapena sākṣād dhatadattasya doṣahetutvasmaraṇāt | darvyādikaṃ ca sati saṃbhave suvarṇādimayaṃ grāhyam,

	sauvarṇarājatābhyāṃ vā khaḍgenodumbareṇa vā |

	dattam akṣayyatāṃ yāti phalgupātreṇa vā punaḥ ||

iti hārītasmaraṇāt | khaḍgena khaḍgamṛgaśṛṅgakṛtadarvyādinā | phalgupātreṇa kākodumbarikākhyavṛkṣadārukṛtadarvyādinā | purāṇe tu pariveṣaṇasādhanāni niṣiddhāni darśitāni |

	nāpavitreṇa hastena naikena na vinā kuśam |

	nāyasenāyase naiva śrāddhe tu pariveṣayet ||

apavitreṇa durlepasaṃsargādinā apavitreṇa | āyasena ayomayadarvyādinā | āyase ayomayapātre 'pi naiva pariveṣayet | aniṣiddhadarvyādyasaṃbhave 'pi tatraivoktam |

	tasmād antaritaṃ deyaṃ parṇenātha tṛṇena vā | iti |

yasmād āhṛtya hastena dānaṃ niṣiddhaṃ tasmād aniṣiddhadarvyādyasaṃbhave parṇādinā prāntaritaṃ kṛtvā deyam ity arthaḥ | bhoktāraṃ dvijaṃ praty āha vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	ubhayor hastayor muktaṃ pitṛbhyo 'nnaṃ niveditam |

	tad annaṃ saṃpratīcchanti asurā duṣṭacetasaḥ ||

	tasmād aśūnyaṃ hastena kuryād annam upasthitam |

	bhājanaṃ tu samālabhya tiṣṭhed occheṣaṇād dvijaḥ || iti |

pariveṣaṇopakramaprabhṛti bhuktaśiṣṭasya bhājanād bahiṣkaraṇaparyantaṃ vāmahastena bhājanam aparityajann eva varteta | kaṇḍūyanarthaṃ vāmahastavyāpārasamaye dakṣiṇahastena bhajanaṃ samālabhya varteteti tātparyarthaḥ | pariveṣaṇārambhaprakāram āha śaunakaḥ |

	pākaṃ sarvam upānīya saṃvedya ca pṛthak pṛthak |

	vidhinā daivapūrvaṃ tu pariveṣaṇam ācaret || iti |

saṃvedya bhoktṝṇāṃ saṃviditaṃ kṛtvety arthaḥ,

	bhakṣyabhojyaguṇān uktvā bhojayed brāhmaṇān śanaiḥ |

iti bṛhaspatismaraṇāt | pākaṃ sarvam ity asyārtho manunā prapañcitaḥ |

	bhakṣyaṃ bhojyaṃ ca vividhaṃ mūlāni ca phalāni ca |

	hṛdyāni caiva māṃsāni pānāni surabhīṇi ca ||

	upānīya ca tat sarvaṃ śanakaiḥ susamāhitaḥ |

	pariveṣayet tu prayato guṇān sarvān pracodayan ||

pracodayan prakhyāpayann ity arthaḥ | devapūrvaṃ pariveṣeyed iti vidher arthavādaḥ purāṇe darśitaḥ |

	tapyamānās tapas tīvraṃ preṣitā brahmaśāsanāt |

	viśvedevās tu rakṣārthaṃ pitṛyajñeṣu sarvadā ||

	ataḥ pūrvaṃ pradātavyaṃ tebhyo 'nnaṃ pitṛkarmaṇi | iti |

pradātavyaṃ bhājaneṣu prakṣeptavyam | devapūrvaṃ pariveṣaṇam ācared iti vadan pariveṣaṇārthaṃ prathamam ājyenopastaraṇaṃ daivapūrvaṃ kṛtvā annaṃ datvā evam eva pāyasādi sarvaṃ pṛthak pṛthak pariveṣaṇīyam iti darśayati | anyāny api pariveṣaṇīyāny āha manuḥ |

	guṇān sākṣād bhujikriyānirvartakān na tu grāhakatayā guṇabhūtān sūpaśākamadhvādīn bhūmau nihiteṣu svalpabhājaneṣu prakṣipet na pradhānānnārthamahābhājane nihiteṣv ity arthaḥ | tathā ca hārītaḥ: "bhūmāv eva nidadhyān nopary upari pātrāṇi" iti | asyārthaḥ: yāny uparipātrāṇi mahābhājanopari nidheyāni ghṛtādyādhārabhūtāni svalpapātrāṇi tāny atra bhūmāv eva nidadhyāt na mahābhājanasyoparīti | mahābhājanam apy atra pūrvoktapiṣṭakādiracitaparitakākhyacaturaśramaṇḍalopari nidhāya pāyasāpūpādi vividham annaṃ prakṣipet | na tu yantrikāder upari nidhāyeti "bhūtalān noddharet pātram" ityādivacanasiddhaṃ boddhavyam | śrāddhārthaṃ yad yat pākādinopakalpitaṃ tat sarvaṃ kiṃcit kiṃcid ādāyāvaśyaṃ pariveṣaṇīyam | ata eva pracetasoktam: "sarvaṃ ca prakṛtaṃ datvā pātram ālabhya japet" iti | japyam āha paiṭhīnasiḥ: "pṛthivī te pātraṃ dyaur apidhānaṃ brāhmaṇasya mukhe juhomi svadhā" iti | japānantaraṃ kātyāyanaḥ: "vaiṣṇavy arcā yajuṣā cāṅguṣṭham anne 'vagrāhya" iti | kā punar atra vaiṣṇavī ṛk, kasya vāṅguṣṭham ity apekṣite yājñavalkyaḥ |

	idaṃ viṣṇur iti tv anne dvijāṅguṣṭhaṃ niveśayet | iti |

yamas tu sārthavādam aṅguṣṭhaniveśanavidhiṃ vadan atra viniyuktayajurmantrasvarūpam āha |

	aṅguṣṭhamātro bhagavān viṣṇuḥ paryaṭate mahīm |

	rākṣasāṇāṃ vadhārthāya ko 'lpavān prahariṣyati ||

	tasmāc chrāddeṣu sarveṣu aṅguṣṭhagrahaṇaṃ smṛtam |

	viṣṇo havyaṃ ca kavyaṃ ca brūyād rakṣeti ca kramāt ||

brūyāt daive pitrye cānna iti śeṣaḥ | atra daive 'nne aṅguṣṭhaniveśanāt prāg viṣṇo havyaṃ rakṣeti yajur brūyāt | pitrye 'nne tu viṣṇo kavyaṃ rakṣeti yajur brūyād iti | atraivaṃ vṛddhācārānusārī prayogaḥ: yajñopavītī dakṣiṇaṃ jānv ācya udaṅmukhaḥ prathamaṃ devatārthapariviṣṭam annam abhyukṣaṇenāvokṣya pātram ālabhya "pṛthivī te pātram" iti japādyaṅguṣṭhaniveśanāntaṃ kṛtvā prācīnāvītī savyaṃ jānv ācya dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ pitryaṃ pariviṣṭam annam abhyukṣaṇenāvokṣya pātram ālambhya japādyaṅguṣṭhaniveśanāntaṃ kuryāt | evaṃ mātāmahādipātrasthāneṣu abhyukṣaṇāvokṣaṇādyaṅguṣṭhaniveṣanāntaṃ kāryam | abhyukṣaṇāvokṣaṇādyaṅguṣṭhaniveśanāntaṃ daive pitrye ca brāhmaṇān ekatve pratibrāhmaṇapātraṃ kāryam,

	ekaikasyātha viprasya gṛhītvāṅguṣṭham ādarāt |

iti brahmāṇḍapurāṇe 'bhidhānāt | sarvabhājanastheṣv anneṣu aṅguṣṭhaniveśanānantaraṃ caturviṃśatimate 'bhihitam |

	pātrālambhaṃ dvijaḥ kuryād idaṃ vo 'nnam iti bruvan | iti |

ayam arthaḥ: pariviṣṭānnādhārabhūtapātrālambhanaṃ vāmahastena kṛtvānnyatyāgāt pātram anutsṛjann eva "viśvedevā idaṃ vo 'nnam" ity uccārayann annatyāgaṃ kuryād iti | viṣṇus tv annatyāgāt prāk smartavyam āha: "namo viśvebhyo devebhyaḥ ity annam ādau prāṅmukhayor nivedayet | pitre pitāmahāya prapitāmahāya ca nāmagotrābhyām udaṅmukheṣu" iti | caśabdāt prapitāmahāya ca nivedayed ity āha | viśvebhyo devebhyaḥ pitre pitāmahāya ceti caturthyā viśveṣāṃ devānāṃ pitrādeś ca devatātvaṃ pradarśyate | viśvedevā devatā pitrādayo devateti smṛtvā nivedanārtham, prākmukhayor udaṅmukheṣv iti saptamyā brāhmaṇānām āhavanīyārthatvaṃ pradarśyate | āhavanīyārthe brāhmaṇa iti smṛtvā nivedanārtham | etad uktaṃ bhavati: pariviṣṭānnatyāgāt pūrvam amukanāmānau viśvedevā devatā idam annaṃ haviḥ brāhmaṇa āhavanīyārthe ityādi smṛtvā namaḥ śabdoccāraṇapūrvakam annaṃ nivedayed iti | tathā pitāmukagotro 'mukaśarmā devatā idam annaṃ havir brāhmaṇa āhavanīyārthe pitāmaho 'mukagotro 'mukaśarmā devatā idam annaṃ havir brāhmaṇa āhavanīyārthe ityādi smṛtvā namaḥ śabdoccāraṇapūrvakaṃ nivedayed iti | evaṃ ca śrāddhākhyaṃ karma homātmakam ity avagamyate | tataś ca nivedayed ity anena homātmakaṃ karma kuryād iti vacobhaṅgyā dyotyate | ata eva śrāddhākhyaṃ karma homātmakam | ata eva brahmapurāṇe: "etad vo annam ity uktvā viśvān devāṃś ca yajet" ity uktam | homayāgayor atyalpabhedatvād dhomātmake śrāddhe anāsthayā yajed ity uktir yujyate | ahomātmakatve tu yajed ity uktir atyantāsamañjasā syāt | tenātra śrāddhākhyaṃ karma homātmakam ity avagamyate, "brāhmaṇa āhavanīyārthae" ity smaraṇāt | anantaraṃ brāhmaṇādhyāsitāṃ bhūmiṃ gayārūpāṃ dhyātvā brāhmaṇaṃ ca gadhādhararūpaṃ dhyātvānnaṃ nivedayet,

	śrāddhabhūmau gayāṃ dhyātvā dhyātvā devaṃ gadādharam |

	tābhyāṃ caiva namaskṛtya tataḥ śrāddhaṃ pravartayet ||

iti purāṇe 'bhidhānāt | vaiśvadevānnatyāgaprakāram āha atriḥ |

	hastena muktam annādyam idam annam udīrayet |

	svāheti ca tataḥ kuryāt svasattāvinivartanam ||

ayam arthaḥ: pariveṣakahastena nirmuktaṃ pariviṣṭam annādyaṃ purovartitvād idam annam iti pradeyahavirnirdeśārthaṃ devatoddeśakaśabdoccāraṇānantaram udīrayet | tata idam annam ity udīraṇānantaraṃ svāheti havirdānaprakāśakaṃ śabdam udīrayet | tataḥ svāhāśabdodīraṇānantaraṃ svasattāvinivartanaṃ kuryāt | svaśabdenātra svatvaṃ nirdiśyate | svatvasya sadbhāvaḥ svasattā tasyā vinivartanaṃ nivartakaṃ karma yan mānasaṃ na mameti buddhirūpaṃ svatvatyāgākhyaṃ tat kuryād iti | pitrādibhyo 'nnatyāgaprakāram api sa evāha |

	gotrasambandhanāmāni idam annaṃ tataḥ svadhā |

	pitṛkarmaṇy udīryātha svasattāṃ vinivartayet ||

ayam arthaḥ: pitṛpitāmahādikramād ekaikaṃ devatātvenoddiṣṭaṃ pitre amukagotrāyāmukaśarmaṇe pitāmahāyāmukagotrāyāmukaśarmaṇe ityādigotrasaṃbandhanāmāni caturthyantāny udīrya tataḥ pradeyahavirdravyanirdeśakam idam annam ity udīrya tataḥ kuryād dānaprakāśakaṃ svadhāśabdam udīrya svasattāṃ vinivartayet | svatvadhvaṃsakaraṃ na mameti buddhirūpaṃ mānasaṃ karma kuryād iti | evaṃ viṣṇutrivacanavihitānnatyāgaprakāra eva vyaktīkaraṇārthaṃ prayogasaukaryārthaṃ ca punaḥ prapañcenocyate | mātuḥ prapitāmahārthe 'nne aṅguṣṭhaniveśanānantaraṃ vaiśvadaivikabrāhmaṇasaṃnidhāv udaṅmukha upaviśyopavītī dakṣiṇaṃ jānv ācya dakṣiṇahastena yavasahitam udakam ādāya savyahastena pātram ālabhya purūravārdravasaṃjñikā viśvedevā devatā idam annaṃ havir brāhmaṇa āhavanīyārthe iyaṃ bhūr gayā ayaṃ bhoktā brāhmaṇo gadādharaḥ purūravārdravasaṃjñikebhyo viśvebhyo devebhya idaṃ pariviṣṭam annam ā tṛpteḥ parivekṣyamāṇaṃ ca svāhā namo na mamety uktvā bhājanasamīpe yavasahitam udakaṃ ninīya bhaktyā praṇāmaṃ kuryāt | vaiśvadaivikabrāhmaṇānekatve tattadbhājane pariviṣṭam annam evaṃ tyajet | tataḥ pitryabrāhmaṇasaṃnidhau dakṣiṇāmukha upaviśya savyaṃ jānv ācya prācīnāvītī hastena tilān udakaṃ cādāya vāmahastena pātram ālabhya asmatpitāmukagotro 'mukaśarmā vasurūpaḥ sapatnīko devatedam annaṃ havir ityādi brāhmaṇo gadādhara ityantaṃ pūrvavad uktvā asmatpitre 'mukagotrāyāmukaśarmaṇe vasurūpāya sapatnīkāya pariviṣṭam annam ā tṛpteḥ parivekṣyayāṇaṃ (?) ca svadhā namo na mamety uktvā bhājanasamīpe tilasahitam udakaṃ ninīya bhaktyā praṇamaṃ kuryāt | brāhmaṇānekatve tattadbrāhmaṇabhājane pariviṣṭam annam evaṃ tyajet | pitāmahādibhyo 'py evam evānnatyāgaḥ | asmatpitāmaho 'mukagotro 'mukaśarmā rudrarūpaḥ sapatnīkaḥ ............ asmatpitāmahāyāmukagotrāyāmukaśarmaṇe rudrarūpāyeti pitāmahīyānnatyāge viśeṣaḥ | asmatprapitāmaho 'mukagotro 'mukaśarmādityarūpaḥ sapatnīkaḥ ......... prapitāmahāyāmukagotrāyāmukaśarmaṇe ādityarūpāyeti prapitāmahīyānnatyāge viśeṣaḥ | asmanmātāmaho 'mukagotro 'mukaśarmā vasurūpaḥ sapatnīkaḥ .............. mātāmahāyāmukagotrāyāmukaśarmaṇe vasurūpāyetyādiviśeṣaḥ | mātuḥ pitāmahīyānnatyāge viśeṣaḥ mātuḥ prapitāmahīyānnatyāge viśeṣaś ca svayam ūhyaḥ | mātuḥ pitāmahādisthāne 'pi brāhmaṇānekatve pūrvoktaprakāreṇānnatyāgāvṛttiḥ | yadā tu pitrādīnām eka eva brāhmaṇas tadā yāvanta uddeśyās tāvato bhāgān ekasmin bhājane pariviṣṭasyānnāder buddhyā kṛtvā ekaikaṃ bhāgam ekaikaṃ pitrādikam uddiśya tyajet | yadā tv atithir bhojanārtham upaviṣṭas tadā taṃ gandhapuṣpādibhir arcayitvā pitṛbhyo 'nnatyāgānantaraṃ asmai brāhmaṇāya viṣṇurūpāya śivarūpāya vā idam annam ā tṛpteḥ parivekṣyamāṇaṃ ca namo na mameti pariviṣṭam annaṃ tyajet | atra viṣṇupurāṇam |

	pitā pitāmahaś caiva tathaiva prapitāmahaḥ |

	tṛptiṃ prayāntu te bhaktyā yan mayaitad ihāhṛtam ||

	mātāmahas tṛptim upaitu tasya tathā pitā tasya pitā va yo 'nyaḥ |

	viśve ca devāḥ paramāṃ prayāntu tṛptiṃ praṇaśyantu ca yātudhānāḥ ||

	yajñeśvaro havyasamastakavyabhoktāvyayātmā harir īśvaro 'tra |

	tatsaṃnidhānād apayāntu sadyaḥ rakṣāṃsy aśeṣāṇy asurāś ca sarve ||

evam uktapaurāṇikaślokajapānantaraṃ laghuyamaḥ |

	annahīnaṃ kriyāhīnaṃ mantrahīnaṃ ca yad bhavet |

	sarvam acchidram ity uktvā tato yatnena bhojayet ||

acchidraṃ jāyatām ity adhyāhāreṇācchidrabhāṣaṇavākyaṃ pūraṇīyam, sākāṅkṣatvāt | bodhāyanena tu acchidraṃ jāyatām ity evoktam | yady api laghuyamavacanād acchidrabhāṣaṇānantaram eva bhojanapratīter āpośanahasteṣu brāhmaṇeṣu satsv acchidrabhāṣaṇaṃ kāryam iti pratibhāti, tathāpi prāg evāpośanataḥ kāryaṃ na paścāt | tathāha pracetāḥ |

	āpośanakarāgrāṇām acchidrasya ca bhāṣaṇāt |

	nirāśāḥ pitaro yānti devaiḥ saha na saṃśayaḥ ||

kiṃ tarhi āpośanadānānantaraṃ kartavyam ity ukte sa evāha |

	āpośanaṃ pradāyātha sāvitrīṃ trir japed atha |

	madhu vātā iti tyṛcaṃ (?) madhv ity eva trikaṃ tathā ||

madhv ity etāvat trir āvartanīyam iti caturthapādasyārthaḥ | vyāhṛtīr japitvā sāvitrīṃ japet, "savyāhṛtikāṃ gāyatrīm" it yājñavalkyasmaraṇāt | āpośanadānavidhānān nityabhojanāśritaniyamāḥ paryukṣaṇādayaḥ prāṇāhutyantā bhoktṝṇām atrāpi santīti gamyate | ata eva kasyacid bhojananiyamasyātra pratiṣedharthaṃ tadanuṣṭhāne doṣam āha bharadvājaḥ |

	pitṝṇām annam ādāya baliṃ yas tu prayacchati |

	steyena brahmahā tena suvarṇasteyakṛd bhavet ||

pitṝṇām annaṃ devapitrarthaṃ pariviṣṭam annam | ata eva sāmānyenoktam atriṇā |

	datte vāpy atha vādatte bhūmau yo nikṣiped balim |

	tad annaṃ niṣphalaṃ yāti nirāśaiḥ pitṛbhir gataiḥ ||

baliṃ nityabhojananiyamavidhipūrvakaṃ balim,

	bhojanāt kiṃcid annāgraṃ dharmarājāya vai balim |

	datvātha citraguptāya prayataś cedam uccaret ||

iti vihitam iti yāvat | vyāhṛtyādijapānantaraṃ yājñavalkyaḥ: "japtvā yathāsukhaṃ vācyam" iti | yathāsukham iti padam aparipūrṇatvād anvitābhidhānāt padāntaram apekṣate | tena juṣadhvam iti padam adhyāhāryam | ata eva,

	juṣadhvam iti te coktāḥ samyag vidhṛtabhājanāḥ |

	kṛtamaunāḥ samaśnīyur āpośanād anantaram ||

iti vyāsenoktam | āpośanād anantaram amṛtopastaraṇam asīti mantreṇāpaḥ pītvā tadanantaram ity arthaḥ | prāṇāhutayas tv aśanakriyāyām anupraviṣṭā iti tāsāṃ karaṇe 'pi samaśnīyur āposanād anantaram ity asya na kaścid virodhaḥ | bhoktum upakrānteṣu brāhmaṇeṣu śraddhakartuḥ kartavyam āha kātyāyanaḥ: "aśnatsu japed vyāhṛtipūrvāṃ gāyatrīṃ sapraṇavāṃ sakṛt trir vā rakṣoghnīḥ pitryamantrān puruṣasūktam apratiratham anyāni ca pavitrāṇi" iti | rakṣoghnīḥ "kṛṇuṣva pājaḥ prasitiṃ (?) na pṛthvīm" ityadyā ṛcaḥ | pitryamantrāḥ: "udīratām avare" ityādayaḥ | apratirathaḥ: "āśuḥ śiśānaḥ" iti sūktam | manur api |

	svādhyāyaṃ śrāvayet pitrye dharmaśāstrāṇi caiva hi |

	ākhyānānītihāsāṃś ca purāṇāny akhilāni ca ||

śrāvayed yajñopavītīti śeṣaḥ,

	apasavyena kartavyaṃ sarvaṃ śrāddhaṃ yathāvidhi |

	sūktastotrajapaṃ muktvā viprāṇāṃ ca visarjanam ||

iti jamadagnismaraṇāt | sūktastotragrahaṇaṃ bhuñjāneṣu vipreṣu yad yaj japyaṃ tasya sarvasyopalakṣaṇārtham | bṛhaspatis tu mantrādijapād anyad api kartavyam āha |

	bhakṣyabhojyaguṇān uktvā bhojayed brāhmaṇān śanaiḥ | iti |

bhoktāraṃ bhojayitāraṃ ca praty āha vṛddhaśātātapaḥ |

	apekṣitaṃ yācitavyaṃ śrāddhārtham upakalpitam |

	na yācate dvijo mūḍhaḥ sa bhavet pitṛghātakaḥ ||

	apekṣitaṃ yo na dadyāc chrāddhārtham upakalpitam |

	kṛpaṇo mandabuddhiś ca sa śraddhaphalaṃ labhet ||

na kevalaṃ śrāddhaphalālābhaḥ api tu kaṣṭatamajanmapāptir api | tathā ca nigamaḥ |

	apekṣitaṃ na dadyād yaḥ śrāddhārtham upakalpitam |

	atha kṛcchāsu ghorāsu tiryagyoniṣu jāyate ||

yat tu vāyupurāṇe 'bhihitam,

	yācate yadi dātāraṃ brāhmaṇo jñānavarjitaḥ |

	pitaras tasya ruṣyanti dātur bhoktur na saṃśayaḥ ||

yac ca yamena,

	kṛcchradvādaśarātreṇa mucyante karmiṇas tataḥ |

	tasmād vidvān naiva dadyān na yācen na tu dāpayet || iti |

tat śrāddhārtham anupakalpitavastuviṣayam, sāmānyenābhidhānāt | śrāddhārtham upakalpitānnādiviṣaye 'py atyantādhikaṃ dātā na dadyāt | bhoktā ca na pratigṛhṇīyāt | tathā ca śaṅkhalikhitau: "nātyadhikaṃ dadyān na pratigṛhṇīyāt" iti | atyadhikānnasyāparigrahaṇārthaṃ pūrvapariviṣṭaṃ prabhūtam atrāsti | kim anyeneti bhoktrā na vaktavyam, kiṃ tu hastasaṃjñayā sūcanīyam | tathā tāv eva: "annapānādi na prabhūtam iti brūyur anyatra hastasaṃjñāyāḥ" iti | nigamo 'pi |

	nānnapānādikaṃ śrāddhe vārayen mukhataḥ kvacit |

	aniṣṭatvād bahutvād vā vāraṇaṃ hastasaṃjñayā ||

evaṃ yācanam api na mukhataḥ kuryāt, maunabhaṅgaprasaṅgāt | tena tad api hastasaṃjñayā kāryam | evaṃ dātrāpi punardānasamaye atyadhikadānaṃ na bhaviṣyatīti jñāpanārtham īṣad dadāmīti mukhato na vaktavyam | kiṃ tu tūṣṇīṃ kiṃcit pradarśya pratiṣedhasūcakahastasaṅketābhāve 'bhyanujñāsūcakahastasaṅkete vā deyam | yad āha yamaḥ,

	yāvad dhaviṣyaṃ bhavati yāvad iṣṭaṃ pradīyate |

	tāvad aśnanti pitaro yāvan nāha dadāmy aham || iti |

pariviṣṭānneṣu yan niravaśeṣatayā bhuktaṃ yac ca bhoktuṃ punaḥ punar gṛhyate tat tasyeṣṭam ity anumāya tad ānīya pradarśya pratiṣedhasūcanābhāve deyam | tathā ca sa eva |

	yad yad roceta viprebhyas tad dadyād avimatsaraḥ | iti |

matsaragrahaṇaṃ doṣāntarāṇām upalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva brahmāṇḍapurāṇam |

	na cāśru pātayej jātu na śuktāṃ giram īrayet |

	na codvīkṣeta bhuñjānaṃ na ca kurvīta matsaram ||

	na dīno na ca vā kruddho na caivānyamanā naraḥ |

	ekāgram ādhāya manaḥ śrāddhaṃ kuryāt sadā budhaḥ || iti |

śuktāṃ niṣṭhurām | kārṣṇyājinir api |

	kuryād athāpariśrānto dambhāhaṅkāravarjitaḥ |

	krodhaṃ lobhaṃ tathā mohaṃ varjayec chrāddhakarmaṇi || iti |

samāneṣu svasya śraiṣṭhyasiddhaye paramaśreṣṭhāni bhakṣyabhojyāni dadyād ity āha sa eva |

	bhakṣyabhojyāni coṣyāṇi peyalehyayutāni ca |
