	sarvaśreṣṭhāni yo dadyāt sarvaśreṣṭho bhaven naraḥ ||

datteṣu bhakṣyādiṣu ā tṛpteḥ svecchayā na kiṃcid avaśeṣayet | tathā ca sumantuḥ |

	akrodhano rasān samyag adyād yady asya rocate |

	ā tṛpter bhojanaṃ teṣāṃ kāmato nāvaśeṣaṇam ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ pariveṣaṇavidhiḥ**

**athānyāny api nimantritabrāhmaṇaviṣayāṇi **

**kānicid vacanāni likhyante**

tathā ca pracetāḥ |

	pītvāpośanam aśnīyāt pātradattam agarhitam |

	sarvendriyāṇāṃ cāpalyaṃ na kuryāt pāṇipādayoḥ ||

indriyādiṣu cāpalyaṃ bhojanārthavyāpārād abhyadhikavyāpāraḥ | tasmiṃs tu kṛte bhuktam annaṃ na pitṝn prīṇātīty āha hārītaḥ |

	uddhṛtya pāṇī vihasan sakrodho vismayānvitaḥ |

	śrāddhakāle tu yat bhuṅkte na tat prīṇāti vai pitṝn ||

bodhāyano 'pi |

	pādena pādam ākramya yo bhuṅkte 'nāpadi dvijaḥ |

	naivāsau bhojyate śrāddhe nirāśāḥ pitaro gatāḥ ||

vāgvyāpāraḥ sarvo 'pi na kāryaḥ | yad āha nigamaḥ: "tūṣṇīṃ bhuñjīrann avilokamānā anuddhṛtya pātram" iti | avilokayamānāḥ diśa iti śeṣaḥ | manur api |

	atyuṣṇaṃ sarvam annaṃ syād aśnīraṃś caiva vāgyatāḥ |

	na ca dvijātayo brūyuḥ dātrā pṛṣṭān havirguṇān ||

aśnīraṃś caivety evaśabdena ekapaṅktyupaviṣṭabrāhmaṇeṣu bhuñjāneṣu kathaṃcid anyonyasparśane saty api bhojanoparamo naiva kārya ity āha | ata eva śaṅkhaḥ |

	śrāddhapaṅktau tu bhuñjāno brāhmaṇo brāhmaṇaṃ spṛśet |

	tad annam atyajan bhuktvā gāyatryaṣṭaśataṃ japet ||

vāgyamanavidhānād eva havirguṇavacananiṣedhasiddhau punarniṣedho hastasaṅketenāpy atatsūcanārthaḥ | ato hastasaṅketenāpi havirguṇakathane doṣam āha atriḥ |

	huṅkāreṇāpi yo brūyād dhastād vāpi guṇān vadet |

	bhūtalāñ coddharet pātraṃ muñced dhastena vāpi tat ||

	prauḍhapādo bahiḥkakṣo bahirjānukaro 'tha vā |

	aṅguṣṭhena vināśnāti mukhaśabdena vā punaḥ ||

	pītāvaśiṣṭatoyādi punar uddhṛtya vā pibet |

	khāditārthaṃ punaḥ khādet modakādi phalāni vā ||

	mukhena vā dhamed annaṃ niṣṭhīvet bhājane 'tha vā |

	ittham aśnan dvijaḥ śrāddhaṃ hatvā gacchaty adhogatim ||

prauḍhapāda āsanādhyāropitapādaḥ | bahiḥkaṣa uttaravāsobahirbhūtakakṣadvayaḥ | bhūtalāt pātroddharaṇe doṣo 'nnādyādhāramahābhājanaviṣayaḥ | pānādyādhāralaghupātrasya "punar uddhṛtya vā pibet" ity anenoddhārābhyanujñāvagamāt | yat tu devalenoktam,

	annapānakaśītodaṃ dadadbhir avalokitaḥ |

	vaktavye kāreṇe saṃjñāṃ kurvan bhuñjīta pāṇinā || iti |

apekṣānusāreṇānnapānaśītalavāryādidātṛbhir apekṣāṃ jñātum avalokitaḥ kṣutpipāsādilakṣaṇe apekṣādeḥ kāraṇe vaktavye pāṇinā saṃjñāṃ saṅketam apekṣādisūcakaṃ kurvan bhuñjīteti tasyārthaḥ pratyetavyaḥ | na tu svādutvādihavirguṇarūpe apekṣākāraṇe saṃjñāṃ kurvann iti, evaṃvidhārthaparigrahe pūrvoktavacanavirodhāpatteḥ | annapānadātrā tu havirguṇapraśno 'tyarthaṃ doṣatvān na kārya ity āha śaṅkhaḥ |

	śrāddhe niyuktān bhuñjānān na pṛcchel lavaṇādiṣu |

	ucchiṣṭāḥ pitaro yānti pṛcchato nātra saṃśayaḥ ||

	dātuḥ patati bāhur vai jihvā bhoktuś ca bhidyate | iti |

lavaṇādiṣu nyūnādhikyābhāvena haviṣaḥ sādguṇyaṃ punar api pradānārthaṃ na pṛcchet | na ca pṛṣṭvā samyaktvena jñānaṃ dadyāt, "dātuḥ patati bāhuḥ" iti doṣasravaṇāt | "jihvā bhoktuś ca bhidyate" iti nindābalād dhaviḥsādguṇṇaṃ (?) saṅketenāpi bhoktā. na sūcayed iti niṣedhavidhir gamyate | pādukayor upaviṣṭapīṭhe vā pādau nidhāya na nimantritā aśnīyur ity āha viṣṇuḥ: "aśnīyur brāhmaṇā na sopānatkāḥ na pīṭhopari nihitapādāḥ" iti | atra dvitīyaniṣedhātikrameṇa yo bhuṅkte tasya doṣam āha vṛddhaśātātapaḥ |

	āsane pādam āropya yo bhuṅkte dvijasattamaḥ |

	hanti daivaṃ ca pitryaṃ ca tad annaṃ ca prajāḥ paśūn ||

niṣedhāntaram āha pracetāḥ |

	na spṛśed vāmahastena bhuñjāno 'nnaṃ kadācana |

	na pādau na śiro bastiṃ (?) na padā bhajanaṃ spṛśet ||

nigamo 'pi |

	māṃsāpūpaphalekṣvādi dantacchedaṃ na bhakṣayet |

	grāsaśeṣaṃ na pātre 'syet pītaśeṣaṃ na no pibet (?) ||

dantacchedaṃ na bhakṣayet hastena māṃsādi dhṛtvā svalpaṃ svalpaṃ dantaiś chitvā na bhakṣayet grāsaśeṣaṃ āsyārpitagrāsaśeṣaṃ punar bhājane nāsyet na kṣipet | uśanāpi |

	bhājanaṃ tu na niḥśeṣaṃ kuryāt prājñaḥ kathaṃcana |

	anyatra dhadhnah kṣīrād vā kṣaudrāt saktubhya eva ca ||

iti, yat tu jamadagninoktam "na nindeyur nāvaśeṣayeyuḥ" iti, tad adhikāvaśeṣaviṣayam | yato 'nantaram āha sa eva: "alpaṃ punar utsraṣṭavyaṃ tasyāsaṃskṛtapramītānāṃ bhāgadheyatvāt" iti | pracetā api varjanīyam āha |

	dantacchedaṃ hastapānaṃ varjayec cātibhojanam | iti |

hastapānaṃ hastena peyādipānaṃ varjayet | apit tu lughupātreṇa (?) kuryāt | atibhojanaṃ tṛptau satyām api bhojanam ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ nimantritabhoktṛviṣayāṇi **

**athāgnivikiraṇādividhiḥ **

	tṛptiṃ bhudhvānnam ādāya satilaṃ pūrvavaj japet |

	tṛptiṃ pṛcchet ....................... || iti |

pūrvavaj japed ityāder arthaḥ kātyāyanena prapañcitaḥ: "gāyatrīṃ madhu madhv iti ca japitvā tṛpyāḥ stha iti pṛcchati" iti | evaṃ pṛṣṭāḥ te viprāḥ tṛptāḥ smaḥ, it brūyuḥ,

	tṛptāḥ stha iti pṛṣṭās te brūyus tṛptāḥ sma ity api |

iti vyāsasmaraṇāt | tṛptāḥ smaḥ ity ukte anantaraṃ brāhmaṇḍapurāṇam |

	prokṣya bhūmim athādbhis tu bhūmau pitṛparāyaṇaḥ |

	tato vikiraṇaṃ kuryād vidhidṛṣṭena karmaṇā ||

kiṃ punar vidhidṛṣṭaṃ karmety apekṣite manuḥ |

	sārvavarṇikam annādyaṃ saṃnīyāplāvya vāriṇā |

	samustṛjed bhuktavatām agrato vikiran bhuvi ||

sarve viprabhuktānnavyañjanavarṇāḥ prakārā yasminn annādye tatsārvavarṇikam annādyaṃ saṃnīya yad yad annaṃ viprair upabhuktaṃ tatas tata ekadeśam avadāyāvadāya kvacit pātre ekīkṛtyety arthaḥ | matsyapurāṇe |

	bhuktavatsu tatas teṣu bhājane vāntike nṛpa |

	sārvavarṇikam annādyaṃ saṃnīyāplāvya vāriṇā ||

	samutsṛjed bhuktavatām agrato vikired bhuvi ||

āplāvya avokṣyety arthaḥ | samutsṛjet vinikṣipet, "ye agnīti bhuvi kṣipet" iti pracetasābhidhānāt | ye agnīti mantraḥ kātyāyanena darśitaḥ:

	ye agnidagdhā ye anagnidagdhā ye vā jātāḥ kule mama |

	bhūmau dattena piṇḍena tṛptā yāntu parāṃ gatim || iti |

yady api bhūmau datteneti mantravarṇāt vidhāyakasarvavacaneṣu bhuvītyabhidhānāc ca na darbhāstaraṇamātrāstīti pratibhāti | tathāpi "darbheṣu vikiraś yaḥ" iti manuvacane darbhasattvānuvādadarśanād darbhān āstīrya tatra vikiro deya iti vidhiḥ kalpyate | tena darbhāstṛtabhūmau vikiro deyaḥ na kevalāyām iti mantavyam | sārvavarṇikānnoddaraṇādi sarvaṃ prācīnāvītinā kāryam, sūktādijapavyatirikte śrāddhakarmaṇi prācīnāvītitvābhidhānāt | vikiranikṣepasthāne vikṣepāt pūrvaṃ piṇḍadānoktaprakāreṇa tūṣṇīṃ satilaṃ vāri kṣiptvā vikirasyopari punaḥ satilaṃ vāri nikṣeptavyam,

	udaṅmukhānāṃ viprāṇāṃ puraḥ sodakaṃ tataḥ |

	annaṃ tu kiret bhaktyā ............ ||

iti mārkaṇḍeyenoktatvāt | annaṃ vikīryānantaram upavītī bhūtvācāmet, anācamane doṣasmaraṇāt | tathā ca marīciḥ |

	śrāddheṣu vikiraṃ datvā yo nācāmen matibhramāt |

	pitaras tasya ṣaṇmāsaṃ bhavanty ucchiṣṭabhojinaḥ ||

tadanantaraṃ brāhmaṇāṃś cācamayet | tathā ca madālasāvākyam |

	............................................ prakīrya bhuvi sarvataḥ |

	tadanvācamanārthāya dadyād āpaḥ sakṛt sakṛt ||

tadanu annavikiraṇāt paścād ācamanārthāya nityabhojananiyameṣu uktaṃ "amṛtāpidhānam asi" iti mantrapūrvakaṃ yad gaṇḍūṣaṃ tadarthaṃ vaisvadaivikaviprapūrvakaṃ prativipraṃ sakṛt sakṛd apo ninayed ity arthaḥ | gaṇḍūṣakaraṇaṃ ca viprair hastalepaprakṣālanam akṛtvaiva kāryam iti sūcayituṃ sakṛt sakṛd adyād ity uktam | evaṃ ca yathā hastaprakṣālanaṃ krtvā gaṇḍūṣakaraṇe nityabhojane puruṣārthavidhyatikramāt puruṣadoṣaḥ, tathātra śrāddhārthavidhyatikramāc chrāddhasya vaiguṇyaṃ bhavati | tathāha marīciḥ |

	hastau prakṣālya gaṇḍūṣaṃ yaḥ pibed avicakṣaṇaḥ |

	āsuraṃ tad bhavec chrāddhaṃ pitṝṇāṃ nopatiṣṭhate || iti |

gaṇḍūṣaṃ yaḥ pibed bhojane virate "amṛtāpidhānam asi" iti mantreṇāpo yaḥ pibed ity arthaḥ | gaṇḍūṣarthodakadānānantaraṃ viṣṇuḥ: "udaṅmukheṣv ācamanam ādau dadyāt prāṅmukheṣu tataḥ prokṣaṇam iti śrāddhaśeṣaṃ prokṣya darbhapāṇiḥ sarvaṃ kurvīta" iti | paitṛkabrāhmaṇeṣu prathamaṃ hastaprakṣālanapūrvakācamanārtham apo datvā paścād vaiśvadaivikabrāhmaṇeṣu datvā "suprokṣitam" iti mantreṇa śraddhadeśaṃ prokṣya darbhapāṇiḥ sarvam uparitanaṃ karma kuryād ity arthaḥ | evaṃbhūtahastaprakṣālanapūrvakācamanakramavidhiṃ hetuvan nigadārthavādasahitam āha śātātapaḥ |

	viśvedevaniviṣṭānāṃ caramaṃ hastadhāvanam |

	visarjanaṃ ca nirdiṣṭaṃ teṣu rakṣā yataḥ sthirā || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyām annavikiraṇādividhiḥ**

**atha piṇḍadānavidhiḥ**

tatra manuḥ |

	piṇḍanirvāpaṇaṃ kecit purastād eva kurvate | iti |

brāhmaṇabhojanāt purastāt teṣām arcanānantaram agnaukaraṇānantaraṃ vā piṇḍanirvāpaṇaṃ kecit kurvata ity arthaḥ | evam eva smṛtyantareṣu bhojanāt purastāt piṇḍanirvāpaṇasya kāladvayadarśanāt | kecid iti vacanād apare brāhmaṇabhojanāt parastād ācamanāt prāg ūrdhvaṃ vā (brāhmaṇavisarjanād pūrvaṃ vā) (?) piṇḍanirvapaṇam kurvata ity avagamyate, smṛtyantareṣu brāhmaṇabhojanād ūrdhvam eva kaladvayadarśanāt | atra yathāsvaśākhaṃ vyavasthā | tathā ca smṛtyantaram |

	munibhir bhinnakāleṣu piṇḍadānaṃ tu yat smṛtam |

	tat svaśākhāmayaṃ yatra tatra kuyād vicakṣaṇaḥ ||

tat bhinnakālexu smṛtaṃ piṇḍadānaṃ yasmin kāle kṛtaṃ svaśākhāyām anumatam anugṛhītaṃ bhavati tasmin kāle kuryād ity arthaḥ | brāhmaṇabhojanāt purastāt parastād veti pakṣadvaye vyavasthām āha lokākṣiḥ |

	apraśasteṣu yāgeṣu pūrvaṃ piṇḍāvanejanam |

	bhojanasya praśastaṃ tu paścād evopakalpayet ||

apraśasteṣu yāgeṣu sapiṇḍīkaraṇākhyaśrāddhāt pūrvaṃ vihitaśrāddheṣu | avanejanam avācīnapāṇinā nirvapaṇam | bhojanasya nimantritabrāhmaṇabhojanasya | praśastaṃ sapiṇḍīkaraṇādiśraddhexu kriyamāṇaṃ bhojanat paścād eva yathākālam upakalpayet | evaṃ ca pārvaṇaśrāddhe bhojanāt paścād eva svaśākhānumate kāle piṇḍaṃ dadyāt | tatra āśvalāyanaśākhināṃ brāhmaṇabhojanād ūrdhvaṃ teṣv ācānteṣu piṇḍadānakālaḥ | tathā āśvalāyanaḥ: "bhuktavatsv ācānteṣu piṇḍaṃ nidadhyād anācānteṣv eke" iti | tatra anācānteṣv eke iti iti pakṣasya saukaryāt svagṛhyānuktakālaviśeṣair apy ayam eva pakṣo grāhyaḥ | yājñavalkyas tu piṇḍadānaprakāram āha |

	sarvam annam upādāya satilaṃ dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ |

	ucchiṣṭasaṃnidhau piṇḍān dadyāt tu pitṛyajñavat ||

śrāddhārthapākasiddhaṃ sarvaprakāram annaṃ stokaṃ stokam uddhṛtya kvacit pātre samavadāya tadannamayān piṇḍān svaśākhāvihitapiṇḍapitṛyajñavidhānena smṛtikāropadiṣṭena satilatvadakṣiṇāmukhatvādiviśeṣasahitenocchiṣṭasaṃnidhau dadyād ity arthaḥ | nanūcchiṣṭasaṃdhir aśucir deśo bhavatīti tatra kathaṃ piṇḍadānaṃ vidhīyata ity āśaṅkyāha atriḥ |

	pitṝṇām āsanasthād agratisraṣv aratniṣu |

	ucchiṣṭasaṃnidhānaṃ tan nocchiṣṭāsanasaṃnidhau ||

ucchiṣṭasaṃparkarahitāsannadeśopalakṣaṇārthaṃ triṣv aratniṣv ity uktam | tena nātra tryaratniniyamaḥ | ata eva jātūkarṇyaḥ |

	vyāyāmamātraṃ samutsṛjya piṇḍāṃs tatra pradāpayet | iti |

pāraskaro 'pi |

	pātrāṇāṃ bāhumātreṇa piṇḍadānaṃ vidhīyate | iti |

pātrāṇām ucchiṣṭāśanavad amātrāṇām ādhārasthānāt | bāhumātreṇa bāhumātram utsṛjed ity arthaḥ | vyāso 'pi |

	aratnimātram utsṛjya piṇḍāṃs tatra pradāpayet |

	yatropaspṛśatāṃ vāpi prāpnuvanti na bindavaḥ || iti |

kārṣṇājinir api piṇḍapitṛyajñavidhānena kriyamāṇe piṇḍadāne viśeṣam āha |

	annaṃ pātre samuddhṛtya sarvasya prakṛtasya tu |

	śeṣānnapraśnapūrvaṃ tu dadyāt piṇḍān krameṇa tu || iti |

śeṣam annaṃ piṇḍārtham uddhṛtāc cheṣaṃ sarvaṃ prakṛtam annam | tasya evaṃvidhaśeṣānnasya praśnaḥ tatpūrvakaṃ piṇḍān dadyāt | śeṣam apy astikaṃ kriyatām ity evaṃvidhaṃ praśnaṃ kṛtvā tadanuguṇaṃ viprāṇām uttaraṃ ca śrutvā paścāt piṇḍadānavidhiṃ kuryād iti yāvat | kiṃ punas tadanuguṇam uttaraṃ viprair vaktavyam ity apekṣite tatsūcanārtham uśanasoktam: "tair anujñātaḥ śeṣam iṣṭebhyo dadyāt svayaṃ vā bhuñjīta" iti | iṣṭebhyo dadyād iṣṭān bhojayet svayaṃ vā bhuñjītety arthaḥ | vāśabdo 'tra caśabdārthe draṣṭavyaḥ, "bhuñjīta pitṛsevitam" iti yājñavalkyena nityavad bhojanavidhānāt | yata eva pitṛsevitāvaśiṣṭabhojanaṃ nityam ata evaikādśyām upavāsasiddhaye pitṛsevitaśeṣabhojanasthāne pratyāmnāyaḥ smaryate |

	upavāso yadā nityaḥ śrāddhaṃ naimittikaṃ bhavet |

	upavāsaṃ tadā kuryād āghrāya pitṛsevitam || iti |

yat punar auśanasavacanagatavāśabdasya prasiddhārthatvam abhisaṃdhyābhihitaṃ devasvāminā: "bhuñjīta pitṛsevitam ity etan na naiyamikam" iti, evaṃ ca svayaṃ bhuñjītety auśanasavacasthavāśabdena pitṛsevitaśeṣabhojanasya pākṣikatvāvagater bhuñjīta pitṛsevitam ity etad yājñavalkīyaṃ vidhānaṃ na naiyamikaṃ na nityam iti tadīyagrahthasyārthaḥ — tad etac cintyam, yājñavalkīyaṃ ca vacanaṃ nityam, pratyāmnāyavacanasya darśitatvāt,

	śrāddhaṃ kṛtvā tu yo vipro na bhuṅkte tu kadācana |

	devā havir na gṛhṇanti kavyāni pitaras tathā ||

iti devalena pitṛsevitaśeṣabhojanākaraṇe doṣasmaraṇāc ca | evaṃ ceṣṭaiḥ saha bhujyatām ity abhyanujñārūpam uttaraṃ viprair deyam ity uśanasā sūcitam iti mantavyam | devalo 'pi pitṛyajñavidhānena piṇḍadāne viśeṣam āha |

	tataḥ sarvāśanaṃ pātre gṛhītvā vidhivat svayam |

	teṣām uccheṣaṇasthāne tena pātreṇa nikṣipet ||

teṣāṃ bhuktavatāṃ brāhmaṇānām uccheṣaṇasthāne ucchiṣṭasaṃnidhāv ity arthaḥ | pātreṇa nikṣepo naiyamiko na bhavati | yad āha marīciḥ |

	pātrāṇāṃ khaḍgapātreṇa piṇḍadānaṃ vidhīyate |

	rājataudumbarābhyāṃ vā hastenaivātha vā punaḥ ||

hasteneti pakṣaḥ śreyān ity artham evakāraḥ kṛtaḥ, na punar avadhāraṇārthaḥ | tathātve pūrvāparavirodho devavacanavirodhaś ca syāt | piṇḍanirvāpaṇasthāne prathamaṃ yat kartavyaṃ tad brahmāṇḍapurāṇe darśitam |

	savyottarābhyāṃ pāṇibhyāṃ kuryād ullekhanaṃ dvijaḥ |

	pragharṣaṇaṃ tataḥ kuryāc chrāddhakarmaṇy atandritaḥ ||

	khaṇḍanaṃ preṣaṇaṃ caiva tathaivollekhanakriyā |

	sakṛd eva pitṝṇāṃ syād devānāṃ tu trir ucyate ||

khaṇḍanaṃ barhirādecchedanam (?) | peṣaṇaṃ bhūmigharṣaṇādikam | ullekhanakriyā piṇḍanirvāpaṇalekhākaraṇam | kenollekhanaṃ kāryam ity apekṣāyām uktaṃ tatraiva |

	vajreṇa vā kuśair vāpi ullikhet tu mahīm dvijaḥ | iti |

vajreṇa sphyenety arthaḥ | "vajro vai sphyaḥ" it śruteḥ | pāraskareṇa tu sphyaśabdenaivoktam |

	karābhyām ullikhet sphyena kuśair vāpi mahīṃ dvijaḥ | iti |

karābhyāṃ gṛhītena sphyena gṛhītaiḥ kuśair vā mahīṃ likhed ity arthaḥ | atra mantram āha kātyāyanaḥ: "ullikhyāpahatāḥ" iti | "apahatā asurā rakṣāṃsi piśācā vediṣadaḥ" iti mantreṇollikhyety anvayaḥ | anena mantreṇa spyenollekhanaṃ pitṛyajñavad ity anena prāptam | ullekhanānantaram ullikhitadeśam avokṣet, "spyena teṣām ullikhed apahatā asurā rakṣāṃsi piśācā vediṣada iti tām avokṣya" iti āśvalāyanena piṇḍapitṛyajñadharmakathane 'bhidhānāt | rekhāṃ dakṣiṇāprācīm ullikhet, "sarvakarmaṇi tāṃ diśam" it paribhāṣāyāṃ tenaivoktatvāt | avokṣitadeśe kuśān āstṛṇuyāt, "kṣipet kuśāṃs tatra ca dakṣiṇāgrān" iti purāṇe 'bhidhānāt | idam api piṇḍapitṛyajñavad ity anenaiva prāptam, sakṛdācchinnair avastīryeti piṇḍapitṛyajñe vihitatvāt | evaṃ ca dakṣiṇāgratvamātram eva paurāṇiko viśeṣaḥ | kuśālābhe viṣṇudharmottare 'bhihitam |

	piṇḍanirvapaṇaṃ kāryaṃ kuśālābhe vicakṣaṇaiḥ |

	kāśeṣu rājadūrvāsu pavitre parame smṛte ||

rājadūrvāsu atidīrghadūrvāsu | kuśāstaraṇe viśeṣo vāyupurāṇe darśitaḥ |

	sakṛd evāstared darbhān piṇḍārthaṃ dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ |

	prāgdakṣiṇāgrān  niyataḥ || iti |

evaṃ ca dakṣiṇāgratayā saha dakṣiṇāprāgagratāyā vikalpo veditavyaḥ | darbhāstaraṇānantaraṃ sumantuḥ |

	asāv avaneniṅkṣveti puruṣaṃ puruṣaṃ prati |

	tris trir ekena hastena vidadhītāvanejanam ||

asāv ity atra pitrādīnāṃ gotrasahitanāmagrahaṇaṃ saṃbodhanarūpeṇa kṛtvā avaneniṅkṣveti vaktavyam,

	piṇḍodakapradānaṃ tu nityanaimittikeṣv api |

	ālabhya nāma gotreṇa kartavyaṃ sarvadaiva hi || 

iti vyāsasmaraṇāt | ālabhya pitrādīn saṃbodhyety arthaḥ | ekena hastenety añjalinivṛttyartham uktam | tathā ca sumantuḥ |

	śrāddhe secanakāle tu pāṇinaikena dīyate |

	tarpaṇe tūbhayaṃ kuryād eṣa eva vidhiḥ sadā || iti |

ekena pāṇinā savyetareṇa,

	apasavyena hastena nirvaped udakaṃ bhuvi |

iti manusmaraṇāt | apasavyahaste pradeśaviśeṣo madālasayoktaḥ |

	pitṛtīrthena toyaṃ ca dadyāt tebhyaḥ samāhitaḥ | iti |

tebhyaḥ pitṛbhyaḥ | caśabdāt satilaṃ toyaṃ pratyetavyam | tathā ca uśanasoktam: "tilamiśritodakenāsicya darbhāstīrṇāyāṃ bhūmau piṇḍān (?) dadyāt" iti | kātyāyanas tv avanejanam udapātreṇa kartavyam ity āha: "udapātreṇāvanejayaty asāv avaneniṅkṣveti yajamānasya pitṛprabhṛtīṃs trīn" iti | āśvalāyanas tv avanejane mantrāntaram āha: "prācīnāvītī rekhaṃ trir udakenopanayec chundantāṃ pitaraḥ śundhantāṃ pitāmahāḥ śundhantāṃ prapitāmahāḥ" iti | kātyāyanas tv avanejanānantaraṃ barhirāstraṇaṃ kāryam ity āha: "upamūlaṃ ca sakṛd ācchinnaṃ rekhāyāṃ kṛtvā yathavaniktaṃ piṇḍān dadāti" iti | avanejanabarhirāstaraṇayoḥ paurvāparyavikalpe yathāsvaśākhaṃ vyavasthā | evam evāvaneniṅkṣva śundhantāṃ pitara ityādimantrāṇām api yathāsvaśākhaṃ vyavasthā | evam evāvanejanakaraṇabhūtahastodapātrayor api | yathāvaniktaṃ piṇḍadāne mantrān āha kātyāyanaḥ: "asāv etat te iti, ye ca tvām (?) anv iti caike" iti | asāv ity atra pitrādīnāṃ saṃbodhanarūpeṇa gotrasahitanāmagrahaṇaṃ kṛtvā etat te iti vaktavyam,

	piṇḍodakapradānaṃ tu nityanaimittikeṣv api |

	ālabhya nāma gotreṇa kartavyaṃ sarvadaiva hi ||

iti vyāsasmaraṇāt | evaṃ ca amukagotrāmukaśarmann etat te iti piṇḍadānamantra unneyaḥ | "ye ca tvām anu it caike" iti pakṣe mantratraye 'py etat te ity asmād anantaram "ye ca tvām anu" iti mantraśeṣo draṣṭavyaḥ | āśvalāyanas tv anyathā piṇḍadānamantrān āha: "etat te 'sau, ye ca tvām anu" iti | atrāpi asāv ity atra saṃbodhanarūpeṇa pitrādīnāṃ gotrasahitanāmagrahaṇaṃ kartavyam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanv</span> etat te ity atraitad iti kathaṃ napuṃsakaliṅganirdeśaḥ, piṇḍasyaitac chabdābhidheyatvāt tasya ca puṃliṅgatvāt (?) | ata eva gobhilena: "asāv eṣa te piṇḍo ye ca tvām anu" ity uktam | atra kecid etat te piṇḍarūpam annam ity adhyāhāraḥ kārya ity āhuḥ, tad ayuktam | agatyādhyāhāra āśrayaṇīyaḥ | asti cātra gatiḥ "kruddhasya piṇḍaṃ patati" iti vṛddhaprayogadarśanāt | napuṃsakaliṅgo 'pi bhūriprayogasiddhaḥ piṇḍaśabdo 'sti | tena piṇḍadānamantre 'pi etat piṇḍaṃ tavety adhyāhāraṃ vinaivārtho 'vagantavyaḥ | avanejanādikaṃ ca sarvaṃ pitṛyajñavad ity anenaiva prāptam | satilatvamātraṃ tu viśeṣaḥ | piṇḍe 'pi satilatvarūpo viśeṣo madālasayoktaḥ |

	satilena tato 'nnena piṇḍāṃs trīn eva putrakaḥ |

	pitṝn uddiśya darbheṣu dadyād ucchiṣṭasaṃnidhau ||

pitṝn yajamānasya janakādīn ity arthaḥ | tathā ca kārṣṇājiniḥ |

	teṣāṃ lokāntarasthānāṃ bāndhavair nāmagotrataḥ |

	apasavyena darbheṣu piṇḍā deyās trayas tu vai ||

teṣāṃ pitṛpitāmahaprapitāmahānām | apasavyena dakṣiṇahastena | lokāntarasthānām ity atra mṛtānām iti jñāpayitum āha sa eva |

	nānā tu jātaya iha tiryagyoniṣu jatiṣu |

	piṇḍabhājo bhavanty ete tāsu tāsu ca yoniṣu ||

iha ihaloka ity arthaḥ | anena piṇḍadānarūpaśrāddhe 'pi yajamānasya pūrvapuruṣā eva devatāḥ na vasvādaya iti gamyate | evaṃ ca yad yuktaṃ smṛtyantare,

	prathamo varuṇo devaḥ prajāpatis tathāparaḥ |

	tṛtīyo 'gniḥ smṛtaḥ piṇḍa eva piṇḍavidhiḥ smṛtaḥ ||

iti, tat na varuṇādīnāṃ devatātvapratipādanaparam, kiṃ tu yathā vasurudrādityatvarūpāḥ pitaraḥ śrāddhadevatā iti yājñavalkyenānnatyāgādau vasvādirūpeṇa pitradayo dhyātavyāḥ ity evaṃparatayoktam, tathā piṇḍadāne varuṇādirūpeṇa pitradayo dhyātavyāḥ ity evaṃparatayoktam it mantavyam | tena yathānnatyāge vasvādirūpān sapatnīkān pitrādīn caturthyantena pitrādipadena gotranamasahitenoddiśyānnatyāgaḥ kriyate tathaitat te iti mantroccāraṇānantaraṃ varuṇādirūpān sapatnīkān pitrādīn uddiśya piṇḍatyāgaḥ kartavyaḥ | atha vā āvāhanādau annatyāgaparyante piṇḍanirvāpaṇādau ca sarvatrātmānam aniruddhatvena pradyumnasaṃkarṣaṇavasudevarūpeṇa pitṛpitāmahaprapitāmahāṃś ca yathākrameṇa dhyatvā āvāhanādikaṃ kuryāt | tathā ca bhaviṣyatpurāṇe |

	aniruddhaḥ svayaṃ devaḥ pradyumnas tu pitā smṛtaḥ |

	saṅkarṣaṇas tajjanako vāsudevas tu tatpitā ||

svayaṃ śrāddhakartā aniruddho devaḥ | śrāddhakartuḥ pitā pradyumnaḥ smṛtaḥ | tajjanakaḥ śrāddhakartṛpitṛjanakaḥ saṅkarṣaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ | tatpitā śrāddhakartṛpitṛjanakapitā vasudevaḥ smṛta ity arthaḥ | piṇḍadātā piṇḍadānasamaye savyaṃ jānv ācya piṇḍadānaṃ kuryād iti vāyupurāṇe 'bhihitam |

	madhusarpistilayutān trīn piṇḍān nirvaped budhaḥ |

	jānu kṛtvā tathā savyaṃ bhūmau pitṛparāyaṇaḥ ||

savyaṃ jānu bhūmau kṛtvā savyaṃ jānv ācyety arthaḥ | etat pitṛyajñavad ity anenaiva siddham | trīn piṇḍān iti vadan mātrādīnāṃ pṛthakpiṇḍanirvāpaṇābhāvaṃ darśayati | tena sapatnīkasya pitrāder ekaikaḥ piṇḍo nirvapaṇīyaḥ | piṇḍapramāṇam āha vyāsaḥ |

	dvihāyanasya vatsasya viśaty āsye yathāsukham |

	tathā kuryāt pramāṇaṃ tu piṇḍānāṃ vyāsabhāṣitam ||

dvihāyano dvivarṣo vatsaḥ | pramāṇāntarāṇy āha aṅgirāḥ |

	kapitthabilvamātrān vā piṇḍān dadyād vidhānataḥ |

	kukkuṭāṇḍapramāṇān vā yadi vāmalakaiḥ samān ||

	badareṇa samān vāpi dadyāc chrāddhāsamanvitaḥ || iti |

āmalake tu viśeṣam āha marīciḥ |

	ārdrāmalakamātrāṃs tu piṇḍān kurvīta pārvaṇe |

amāvāsyākhye pārvaṇe | piṇḍapitṛyajñānantaram,

	pitṛyajñaṃ tu nirvartya vipraś candrakṣaye 'gnimān |

	piṇḍānvāhāryakaṃ śrāddhaṃ kuryān māsānumāsikam ||

iti vacanena yad vihitaṃ tad idam amāvāsyārūpaparvasaṃbandhalakṣaṇapravṛttinimittena yogena rūḍhyā vā pārvaṇaśabdenocyate | tathā ca śātātapaḥ |

	darśaśrāddhaṃ ca yat proktaṃ pārvaṇaṃ tat prakīrtitam | iti |

tatra brāhmaṇanimantranādisarvadharmāṇām āmnānāt śrāddhāntarāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ prakṛtibhūtaṃ tad ity avagantavyam, tadvikṛtibhūtam itarad ekoddiṣṭādiśrāddham | evaṃ ca pārvaṇagrahaṇam antareṇa ārdrāmalakapramāṇasya prakaraṇād eva pārvaṇārthatve labdhe pārvaṇagrahaṇaṃ vispaṣṭārtham | eteṣu pramāṇeṣu śaktyanusāreṇa vyavasthā kalpyā | pramāṇāntaram api brahmāṇḍapurāṇe vacobhaṅgyā darśitam |

	trīn piṇḍān ānupūrveṇa sāṅguṣṭhamuṣṭibandhanāt | iti |

sāṅguṣṭhamuṣṭigrāhyapramāṇakāt kiṃcid abhyadhikānīty arthaḥ | ānupūrvyeṇa dakṣiṇāpavargatvadakṣiṇāprāgapavargatvādiviruddhānupūrvyeṇa | pitṛyajñavd ity atideśena piṇḍānāṃ dakṣiṇāpavargatvasya dakṣināprāgapavargatvasya vā prāptatvāt | piṇḍanirvāpaṇānantaraṃ manuḥ |

	nyupya piṇḍān pitṛbhyas tu prayato vidhipūrvakam |

	teṣu darbheṣu taṃ hastaṃ nimṛjyāl lepabhāginām ||

prapitāmahapitṛpitāmahaprapitāmahāḥ lepabhāginaḥ | "lepabhājaś caturthādyāḥ" iti matsyenābhidhānāt | lepanirmārjanamantram āha viṣṇuḥ: "atra pitaro mādayadhvam iti darbhamūleṣu karāvagharṣaṇm" iti | karāvagharṣaṇaṃ hastalepanirmārjanam | karāvagharṣaṇānantaraṃ kātyāyanaḥ: "atra pitara ity uktvā udaṅṅ āste ātamanād ātmānam āvṛtyāmī madanta iti japati" iti | dakṣiṇam ātmānam āvṛtya ātamanāt prāṇāyāmena vāyupīḍāvadhi udaṅmukha āsīta | tataḥ yathāśakyam anucchvsann evābhiparyāvṛtya "amī madanta" it japitvā prāṇān mocayet iti | karmapradīpe viśeṣa uktaḥ |

	vāmenāvartanaṃ kecid udagantaṃ pracakṣate |

	āvṛtya prāṇān āyamya pitṝn dhyāyan yathārhataḥ ||

	japaṃs tenaiva cāvṛtya tataḥ prāṇān pramocayet ||

vāmenāvartanaṃ savyenāvartanam | udagantaṃ yāvad āvartanenodaṅmukho bhavati tāvad āvartanaṃ kāryaṃ nādhikāvartanam iti gautamādivyatiriktā munayaḥ pracakṣate,

	sarvaṃ gautamaśāṇdilyau śāṇḍilyāyana eva ca ||

iti tatraivābhidhānāt | japan amī madanteti tenaivāvṛtya vāmenaiva dakṣiṇāmukhāntam āvṛtya prāṇān mocayed ucchvased ity arthaḥ | viṣṇus tu nyuptapṇḍānumantraṇādivādodaśādānāntam āśvalāyanoktapitṛyajñānusāreṇāha: "datvā ca piṇḍān nivṛtān anumantryītāta pitaro mādayadhvaṃ yathābhāgam āvṛṣāyadhvam" iti | tataḥ savyāvṛdudaṅmukhaḥ parāvṛtya yathāśakti prāṇānāṃ nirodhāntaṃ kṛtvā paryāvṛtyāmī madantety anumantrya śeāvaghrāṇaṃ kṛtvā śundhantāṃ pitara iti pūrvadudakaṃ (?) ninīya piṇḍopari tato 'sāv abhyaṅkṣvety abhyañjanaṃ dadyād aṅkṣvety añjanam atha vastram abhāve daśām ūrṇāṃ vā 'etad vaḥ pitaro vāso mānotonyat  (?) pitaro yuṅdhvam' iti | piṇḍān uptvā śeṣāvaghrāṇaṃ pātrasthaśeṣābhighrāṇaṃ pūrvavad udakaninayanaṃ tilamiśrodakāvanejanaṃ tato 'vanejanānantaram asāv abhyaṅkṣya iti mantreṇābhyañjanaṃ piṇḍopari pratipiṇḍaṃ dadyāt asāv ity atra saṃbodhanarūpeṇa pitrādīnāṃ nāmagrahaṇam, asāv aṅkṣyeti mantreṇa piṇḍopari pratipiṇḍam añjanaṃ dadyād etad iti mantreṇa pratipiṇḍaṃ yathālābhaṃ daśādikaṃ dadyāt | yat tu śaṅkhenoktam,

	kṣumāsūtraṃ pradātavyaṃ kārpāsam atha vā navam |

	daśāṃ vivarjayet prājño yady apy ahatavatrajām ||| iti |

kṣumā atasī | atra yady api nityavad daśāpratiṣedhaḥ pratibhāti (?), tathāpi pūrvoktasmṛtau daśāyā vidhānāt ṣoḍaśigrahaṇāgrahaṇavad vikalpo 'nusaṃdheyaḥ | vastrābhāve purāṇe 'py uktam |

	sūtrāṇy ūrṇā daśā vāpi patir loma pradāpayet | iti |

patiḥ yajamānaḥ | lomapradānapakṣaḥ pūrvavayasi na bhavati tad āha kātyāyanaḥ: "etad vaḥ pitaraḥ, iti sūtrāṇi praipiṇḍaṃ vayasy uttare yajamānasya lomāni vā" iti | uttare vayasi pañcāśadvarṣād ūrdhvam ity arthaḥ | vāśabdād uttare vayasi lomapakṣaḥ pakṣāntarāṇy api | etat sarvaṃ "pitṛyajñavat" ity anena prāptam | avanejane tu pitṛyajñād viśeṣam āha vyāghraḥ |

	adbhiḥ prakṣālya tat pātraṃ pratipiṇḍaṃ tu pūrvavat |

	kṛtvāvanejanaṃ kuryāt piṇḍapātram adhobilam || iti |

pūrvavat piṇḍapradānāt pūrvaṃ vihitāvanejanavat | evaṃ ca dvitīyāvanejanam api piṇḍapātraprakṣālanodakena kāryam, na tu pitṛyajñavad udakāntareṇa | ata eva,

	pātranirṇejanenaiva punaḥ pratyavanejayet |

iti purāṇe evakāraḥ kṛtaḥ | etad va iti mantreṇa daśādānānantaraṃ pitṛyajñād viśeṣam āha vyāghraḥ |

	gandhapuṣpāṇi dhūpaṃ ca dīpaṃ caiva nivedayet |

	etad vaḥ pitaro vāsodaśāṃ datvā pṛthak pṛthak ||

etad va iti mantreṇa pratipiṇḍaṃ vāsaso daśāṃ datvā gandhadikam api pratipiṇḍaṃ dadyād ity arthaḥ | yat tu viṣṇunoktam: "piṇḍanirvāpaṇaṃ kṛtvārghyapuṣpadhūpānulepanānnādyabhakṣyabhojyāni nivedayet | udapātraṃ madhughṛtanilaiḥ saṃyuktaṃ ceti" iti tat, piṇḍanirvāpaṇānantaram arghyādiviśeṣaprātyartham | anyathā,

	nyupya piṇḍān pitṛbhyas tu prayato vidhipūrvakam |

	teṣu darbheṣu taṃ hastaṃ nimṛjyāl lepabhāginām ||

iti manūpadiṣṭayuktatarakramavirodhāpatteḥ | tenārghādipradarśanmātrārthaṃ viṣṇuvacanam, na tu piṇḍanirvāpaṇānantaryapratipādanārtham apīti na vyāghroktānantaryaparipanthīti (?) mantavyam | yat tu matsyapurāṇe 'bhihitam,

	gandhadhūpādikaṃ dadyāt kṛtvā pratyavanejanam |

iti, tat pratyavanejanāt pūrvaṃ na gandhādidānam ity evaṃparam | na tu pratyavanejanānantaram eva gandhādidānaṃ kartavyam ity evaṃparam | "prakṛteḥ pūrvoktatvā apūrvam ante syāt" iti nyāyenāvanejanānantaram abhyañjanādidānaṃ tadanantaraṃ gandhādidānam iti nyāyamūlakakramābhidāyakaprāguktavyāghravacanavirodhāpatteḥ | ataḥ etad api na vyāghroktānantaryaparipanthi | yata eva pratyavanejanagandhādidānayoḥ parasparakramaparaṃ na matsyapurāṇavacanam | ata eva viṣṇunā prakṛtibhūtapiṇḍapitṛyajñakrama evātroktaḥ: "śundhantāṃ pitara iti pūrvavad udakaninayanaṃ piṇḍopari tato 'sāv abhyaṅkṣvety abhyañjanaṃ dadyāt" iti | tasmād vyāghravacanāvagatakrameṇa daśāṃ datvānantaraṃ gandhādinā piṇḍārcanaṃ kāryam iti siddham | piṇḍārcanaṃ prakṛtya purāṇe |

	yat kiṃcit pacyate gehe bhakṣyaṃ bhojyam agarhitam |

	anivedya na bhoktavyaṃ piṇḍamūle kathaṃcana ||

tena sarvasmād ādāya piṇḍārcane upahāro deya ity abhiprāyaḥ | piṇḍārcanānantaraṃ kartavyam āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	dhūpadīpair mālyagandhaiḥ tadā vastrāñjanādinā |

	samabhayarcyodapātraṃ tu teṣām upari nikṣipet ||

dhūpadīpa ityādipāṭhakramo nātra vivakṣitaḥ ślokasiddhipartvāt | tataś cāyam arthaḥ: abhyañjanāñjanavastragandhamālyadhūpadīpasārvavarṇikānnopahāraiḥ piṇḍān samabhyarcya teṣāṃ piṇḍānām upari pātrapūrṇam udakaṃ tenaiva pātreṇa ninayed iti | udapātraninayanānantaraṃ viṣṇuḥ: "athainān upatiṣṭhate 'namo vaḥ pitaraḥ' ityādinā 'mano 'nvāhuvāmahe' ity ṛgantena | athaitān piṇḍāṃś cālayet 'pareta naḥ pitaraḥ saumyā gambhīrebhiḥ pathibhiḥ pūrvebhiḥ datvāathātmbhyaṃ draviṇeha bhadraṃ rayiṃ ca naḥ sarvavīrān niyachata" iti | namo vaḥ pitara ityādinā mantreṇa āśvalāyanapaṭhiteneti śeṣaḥ | āśvalāyanoktapitṛyajñakalpānusāritvād viṣṇusmṛteḥ | mano 'nvāhuvāmaha iti tyṛcaḥ (?) ante yasya namo vaḥ pitara ityādimantrasya asau mano 'nvāhuvāmaha iti tyṛcāntaḥ | tenātra namaskārāñjaliṃ badhvā upasthānaṃ kartavyam, mantraliṅgānuguṇyāt | ata eva namaskārāñjalim āśritya niyamamātram uktaṃ brāhmaṇapurāṇe |

	savyottarābhyāṃ pāṇibhyāṃ vaden mantram imaṃ sadā |

	namo vaḥ pitara iṣa iti samyag atandritaḥ ||

"namo vaḥ pitaraḥ" iti samyag vadataḥ savyottarābhyāṃ pāṇibhyāṃ dakṣiṇapāṇim uttānaṃ kṛtvā tadupari savyapāṇinā adhomukhena namaskārāñjaliṃ badhvā "namo vaḥ pitara iṣe" itīdam āśvalāyanoktaṃ mantraṃ vaded ity arthaḥ | piṇḍavālanānantaraṃ "agne tad adya" ity etayā ṛcā agnaukaraṇāgniṃ pratigacchet | "yad antarikṣam" ity etayarcā gārhapatyaṃ pratigacchet | tathā ca piṇḍapitṛyajñakalpe āśvalāyanenoktam: "agniṃ pratyeyād agni tam adyāśvaṃ na stomaiḥ" iti | gārhapatyam "yad antarikṣaṃ pṛthivīm uta dyāṃ yan mātaraṃ pitaraṃ vā jihiṃsi ma agnir mā tasmād enaso gārhapatyaḥ pra muñcatu duritā yāni cakṛma karotu mām anenasam" iti | evam uktam ullekhanādyagnismīpagamanāntaṃ piṇḍadānavidhānaṃ mātāmahādyarthapiṇḍadāne 'py avagantavyam,

	mātāmahānām apy evaṃ dadyād ācamanaṃ tataḥ |

iti yājñavalkyenoktatvāt | yathā pitrādīnāṃ vipranimantraṇāditadvisarjanāntaśrāddhakalpaḥ evaṃ mātāmahādīnām api vipranimantraṇādi kṛtsnaśrāddhakalpo jñeya ity arthaḥ | mātāmahādīnām apy evaṃ pitrādīnām iva piṇḍadānaṃ kuryād iti | tathā ca madālasāvākyam |

	tadvan mātāmahānāṃ ca dadyāt piṇḍān yathāvidhi | iti |

tadvat pitṛvad ity arthaḥ | yady apy asmin vākye pitṛvargasya piṇḍadānavidhānam uktvā tadvad ity anena mātāmahavargasya piṇḍadānābhidhānāt pitṛvargārthapiṇḍadānavidhiṃ samāpya mātāmahavargārthapiṇḍadānaṃ bhinnatantratayā kāryam iti pratibhāt | tathāpi kṛtsnaśrāddhānuṣṭhānaṃ samānatantratayā vargadvayasyeti "tantraṃ vā vaiśvadaivikam" ity atraivoktatvāt piṇḍadānam api samānatantratayaiva vargadvayasya kāryam | ata eva purāṇe samānatantreṇānuṣṭhānam uktam |

	upamūlāt samāstīrya darbhānucchiṣṭasaṃnidhau |

	kṛtvāvanejanaṃ dadyāt trīn trīn piṇḍān yathākramam ||

upamūlāt mūlasamīpāt trīn iti vīpsayā vargadvayasya samānatantreṇa piṇḍanirvapaṇam ity uktam | 

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ piṇḍadānavidhiḥ**

**atha pitṛyajñadharmakapiṇḍadānaprayogaḥ**

athopadeśātideśasaṃkalanatayā saṃpannaḥ piṇḍadānaprayoga ucyate | śrāddhārthapākasiddhāt sarvavidhād annāt ṣaṭpiṇḍaparyāptaṃ kiṃcid abhyadhikam annaṃ pātrāntare samuddhṛtya śeṣam apy asti kiṃ kriyatām iti pṛṣṭvā iṣṭaiḥ saṃhopabhujyatām ity evaṃvidham anujñārūpam uttaraṃ vipradattaṃ śrutvā anantaraṃ sphyena darbhair vā "apahatā asurā rakṣāṃsi piśācā vediṣadaḥ" iti mantreṇa savyottarābhyāṃ pāṇibhyāṃ piṇḍasthāne dakṣiṇāprācīm ekāṃ rekhāṃ kṛtvā tato dakṣiṇato dvitīyāṃ rekhāṃ prathamarekhāvat kuryāt | tato rekhādvayasamīpabhūmāv uddhananaṃ kṛtvā tūṣṇīṃ dvir abhyukṣya sakṛdācchinnam upamūlalūnaṃ barhir dakṣiṇāprāgagraṃ dakṣiṇāgraṃ vā pṛthak pṛthag rekhādvaye saṃstīrya dakṣiṇena hastena pitṛtīrthena prathamarekhāgatabarhiṣi piṇḍasthāne "śundhantāṃ pitaraḥ śundhantāṃ pitāmahāḥ śundhantāṃ prapitāmahāḥ" iti tribhir mantrais tilamiśram udakaṃ ninīya dvitīyarekhāgatabarhiṣi piṇḍasthāneṣu "śundhantāṃ mātāmahāḥ śundhantāṃ mātuḥpitāmahāḥ śundhantāṃ mātuḥprapitāmahāḥ" iti mantrair tilamiśram udakaṃ ninayet | atha vā prathamarekhāyām "pitar amukagorāmukaśarman avaneniṅkṣva, pitāmahāmukagotrāmukaśarmann avaneniṅkṣva, prapitāmahāmukagorāmukaśarmann avaneniṅkṣva" iti mantrair ninayet | dvitīyarekhāyāṃ "mātāmahāmukagotrāmukaśarmann avaneniṅkṣva, matuḥpitāmahāmukagotrāmukaśarmann avaneniṅkṣva, mātuḥprapitāmahāmukagotrāmukaśarmann avaneniṅkṣva" it mantrair ninayet | tato dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ savyaṃ jānv ācya ghṛtamadhutilamiśram annaṃ pūrvaprakaraṇoktārdrāmalakādyanyatamapramāṇakaṃ piṇḍaṃ kṛtvā "etat te pitar amukagotrāmukaśarman ye ca tvām anu" ity uktvā pitre 'mukagotrāyām amukaśarmaṇe vasurūpāya sapatnīkāyedam annaṃ na mamety uktvā prathamapiṇḍasthāne avācīnapāṇinā prakṣipet | etat te pitāmahāmukagotrāmukaśarman ye ca tvam anv ity uktvā pitāmahāyāmukagotrāyāmukaśarmaṇe prajāpatirūpāya sapatnīkāyedam annaṃ na mamety uktvā dvitīyasthāne dvitīyapiṇḍaṃ prakṣipet | evam etat te prapitāmaha amukagotrāmukaśarman ye ca tvām anv ity uktvā prapitāmahāyāmukagotrāyāmukaśarmaṇe 'gnirūpāya sapatnīkāyedam annam ity uktvā tṛtīyasthāne trtīyaṃ piṇḍaṃ prakṣipet | ete ca piṇḍāḥ dakṣiṇāpavargā dakṣiṇāprāgapavargā vā barhiḥstaraṇānusāreṇa kāryāḥ | tato dvitīyarekhāyām evam eva piṇḍasthānexu piṇḍān prakṣipet | etat te mātāmaha amukagotrāmukaśarman ye ca tvām anu ity uktvā mātāmahāyāmukagotrāyāmukaśarmaṇe varuṇarūpāya sapatnīkāyedaṃ na mameti prathamapiṇḍe viśeṣaḥ | mātuḥpitāmahamātuḥprapitāmahayoḥ prajāpatyagnirūpābhyām idaṃ na mameti piṇḍān prakṣipet | ete ca piṇḍaḥ dakṣiṇāvapargāḥ dakṣiṇāprāgapavargā vā barhiḥstaraṇānusāreṇa kāryāḥ | evam āśvalāyanamatānusāreṇa piṇḍadānamantrā darśitāḥ | kātyāyanādimatānusāreṇa piṇḍadānmantrāḥ pūrvaprakaraṇ eva darśitāḥ | tanmatānusāribhir ihāpy anusaṃdheyāḥ | evaṃ piṇḍān datvā rekhāyām āstīrṇe barhiṣi "atra pitaro mādayadhvam" ity etāvanmātreṇa hastalepanirmārjanaṃ kṛtvā "atra pitaro mādayadhvaṃ yathābhāgam āvṛṣāyadhvam" ity uktvā, apradakṣiṇāvartanenodaṅmukho bhūtvā yathāśakty anucchvasann āsitvābhiṣaryāvṛtya "amī madanta pitaro yathābhāgam āvṛṣāyīṣatha" iti ṣaṭpiṇḍān sakṛd eva anumantrya ucchvaset | tatas tūṣṇīṃ piṇḍapātrasthaśeṣam avaghrāya prakṣālanodakena "śundhantām pitaraḥ" ityādibhiḥ ṣaḍbhir mantraiḥ pitaḥ amukagotra amukaśarman avaneniṅkṣva ityādibhiḥ ṣaḍbhir mantraiḥ ṣaṭsu piṇḍeṣu pūrvavad avanejanaṃ krtvā piṇḍapātram adhomukhaṃ kuryāt | tato 'mukagotra amukaśarman abhyaṅkṣveti yathānāmadheyaṃ ṣaṭsu piṇḍeṣu tailaṃ datvā amukaśarman aṅkṣvety yathānāmadheyaṃ ṣaṭsu piṇḍeṣu añjanaṃ dadyāt | "etad vaḥ pitaro vāso mānotonyat pitaro yuṅdhvam" itimantreṇa vāsodaśādikaṃ ṣaṭpiṇḍeṣu dadyāt | tatas tūṣṇīm arghyagandhamālyadhūpadīpasārvavarṇikānnopahārair madhughṛtatilasahitodapātreṇa pratipiṇḍam arcanaṃ kuryāt | tataḥ pātrapūrṇam udakaṃ tenaiva pātreṇa sarveṣāṃ piṇḍānām upari ninayet | dakṣiṇaṃ pāṇim uttānaṃ kṛtvā tadupari savyapāṇinādhomukhena namaskārāñjaliṃ badhvā "namo vaḥ pitara iṣe namo vaḥ pitara ūrje namo vaḥ pitaraḥ śuṣmāya namo vaḥ pitaro ghorāya namo vaḥ pitaro jīvāya namo vaḥ pitaro rasāya svadhā vaḥ pitaro namo vaḥ pitaro nama etā yuṣmākaṃ pitara imā asmākaṃ vo jīvanta iha santaḥ syāma mano 'nvāhuvāmahe nārāśaṃsena somena pitṝṇāṃ ca manvabhiḥ" iti tisṛbhi ṛgbiś ca sarvān piṇḍān sakṛd evopatiṣṭhet | tataḥ "pareta pitaraḥ somyāso gambhīrebhiḥ pathibhiḥ pūrvebhiḥ | datvāyāsmabhyaṃ draviṇeha bhadraṃ rayiṃ ca na smarvavīraṃ niyacchata" iti mantreṇa piṇḍāṃś cālayet | tataḥ "agne tam adyāśvaṃ na stomaiḥ kratuṃ na bhadraṃ hṛdi spṛśam | ṛddhāmāta ohaiḥ" ity etararcāgnaukaraṇāgniṃ pratigacchet | "yad antarikṣaṃ pṛthivīm uta dyāṃ yan mātaraṃ pitaraṃ vā jihiṃsima | agnir mā tasmād enaso gārhapatyaḥ pramuñcatu duritā yāni cakṛma karotu mām anenasam" iti mantreṇa gārhapatyaṃ pratigacchet | evam abhyañjanādikam āśvalāyanamatānusāreṇoktam | yeṣāṃ svagṛhye prakārāntaram anuktaṃ teṣām āśvalāyanokatam abhyañjanādikam anuṣṭheyam, viṣṇusmṛtiparigraheṇa smārtatayā sarvasādhāraṇatvāt ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ pitṛyajñadharmakapiṇḍadānaprayogaḥ **

**athānyāny api piṇḍadānaviṣayāṇi kānicid vacanāni likhyante**

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	sarvasmāt prakṛtād annāt piṇḍān madhutilānvitāt |

	pitṛmātāmahādīnāṃ dadyād gṛhyavidhānataḥ ||

etad uktaṃ bhavati | āpastambādigṛhyeṣu yatra pitṛyajñavidhānād vidhyantareṇa piṇḍadām uktaṃ tadgṛhyānusāriṇāṃ taduktavidhyantareṇaiva pitrādibhyo mātāmahādibhyaś ca piṇḍadānaṃ kāryam iti | yasya ca ravasya (?) gṛhye vidhānāntaraṃ nopadiśyate piṇḍapitṛyajñavidhānaṃ vā nirdiśyate tenaiva piṇḍapitṛyajñakalpena piṇḍadānaṃ kāryaṃ nānyeneti mantavyam | gṛhyoktavidhānāntareṣūdāharaṇārtham āpastambagṛhyoktaṃ vidhyantaraṃ pradarśyate tatra hy evam abhihitam: "bhuktavato 'nuvrajya pradakṣiṇīkṛtya dvaidhaṃ dakṣiṇāgrān darbhān saṃstīrya teṣūttarair apo datvottaraiḥ dakṣināpavargān piṇḍān datvā pūrvavad uttarair apo datvottarair upasthāyodapātreṇa triḥ prasavyaṃ pariṣicya nyubjya pātrāṇy uttaraṃ yajur anavānaṃ (?) tryavarārdham āvartayitvā prokṣya pātrāṇi dvaṃdvam abhyupāhṛtya" iti | asyārtho vivicyate | "bhuktavato 'nuvrajya pradakṣiṇīkṛtya" ity anena brāhmaṇabhojanātmakaṃ pradhānam anuvrajanapradakṣiṇīkaraṇāntapāścātyāṅgajātasahitaṃ (?) parisamāpyānantaraṃ piṇḍapradānātmakaṃ pradhānaṃ sāṅgam anuṣṭhātavyam | na punar brāhmaṇabhojanātmakaṃ pradhānam aparisamāpya anantaram ity uktam | tataś ca svakīyasthānaṃ prati gateṣu vipreṣu piṇḍanirvāpaṇam anuṣṭheyam, na tu bhuktavtsv ācānteṣu anācānteṣu tiṣṭhatsu vipreṣv avagantavyam | dvaidhaṃ dakṣiṇāgrān darbhān saṃstīrya dvidhābhūtaṃ yathā bhavati dakṣiṇāgrān darbhān anupahatadeśasya pūrvabhāge paścādbhāge ca pṛthak pṛthak saṃstīrya teṣūttarair apo datvā teṣu dvidhā saṃstīrṇeṣu darbheṣu uttaraiḥ "mārjayantāṃ mama pitaraḥ" ityādibhir mantraiḥ ekasmin piṇḍasthāne ekaikena mantreṇāpo ninayet | pūrvabhāgasthadarbheṣu prathamapiṇḍasthāne "mārjayantām pitaraḥ" iti mantreṇāpo ninayet | dvitīyatṛtīyapiṇḍasthānayoḥ "mārjayantāṃ pitāmahāḥ prapitāmahāḥ" iti mantrābhyām apo ninayet | paścādbhāgasthadarbheṣu prathamapiṇḍasthāne "mārjayantāṃ mātaraḥ" iti mantreṇa, dvitīyatṛtīyapiṇḍasthānayoḥ "mārjayantāṃ pitāmahyaḥ prapitāmahyaḥ" iti apo ninayet | uttarair eva dakṣiṇāpavargān piṇḍān datvā "etat te tatāsau ye ca tvām anu" ityādibhir mantraiḥ ekasmin piṇḍasthāne ekaikena mantreṇa ekaikapiṇḍaṃ pitrādīn uddiśya tyāgapūrvaṃ nivaped ity arthaḥ | tatra pūrvabhāgasthadarbheṣūdakaninayanakrameṇa "etat te tatāsau ye ca tvām anu" iti mantreṇa prathamapiṇḍasya nivapanam | evaṃ pitāmahaprapitāmahapiṇḍayor nivapanam | paścādbhāgasthadarbheṣu "etat te mātar asau yāś ca tvām anu" iti mantreṇa prathamapīṇḍasya | evaṃ pitāmahīprapitāmahyoḥ piṇḍayor nivapanam | "strībhyaś ca piṇḍā iha paścimāḥ syuḥ" iti gṛhyabhāṣyārthasaṃgrahakāreṇābhidhānāt paścādbhāgasthadarbheṣu strīṇāṃ piṇḍanivapanam ity avagantavyam | ṣaṭsv api piṇḍamantreṣu asāv ity atra saṃbodhanarūpeṇa pitṛpitāmahaprapitāmahānāṃ mātṛpitāmahīprapitāmahīnāṃ ca nāmagrahaṇaṃ kartavyam,

	arghyadāne ca saṃkalpe piṇḍadāne tathākṣaye |

	gotrasaṃbandhanāmāni yathāvat praipādayet ||

iti pāraskarasmaraṇāt | piṇḍāś ca viprabhojanāvaśiṣṭasarvaprakārānnamayā madhutilānvitā na deyāḥ | "sarvasmāt prakṛtād annāt" ityāder āpastambenānibaddhatvād odanamātreṇaiva piṇḍadānaṃ kāryam ity āhuḥ | pūrvavad uttarair apo datvā piṇḍanirvapaṇāt pūrvodakaninayanavad darbheṣv eva piṇḍasamīpe uttaraiḥ "etat te tatāsau" ityādibhyaḥ ṣaḍbhyo mantrebhyaḥ parastāt paṭhitaiḥ "mārjayantāṃ pitaraḥ" ityādibhir eva mantrair apo ninayed ity arthaḥ | pūrvoktodakaninayane paścāduktodakaninayane ca tilamiśram udakaṃ grāhyam iti kecid vadanti | uttarair upasthāya "ye ca vo 'tra" ityadibhir mantair upasthāyety arthaḥ | "ye ca vo 'tra ye cāsmāsv āśaṃsante te ca vahantāṃ tṛpyantu bhavantaḥ tṛpyata tṛpyata tṛpyata" ity etair mantraiḥ pitṛvargārthapiṇḍopasthānam | "yāś ca vo 'tra yāś cāsmāsv āśaṃsante tāś ca vahantāṃ tṛpyantu bhavatyaḥ tṛpyata tṛpyata tṛpyata" ity etair mantraiḥ mātṛvargārthapiṇḍopasthānaṃ kāryam iti mantraliṅgād avagantavyam | uttarayodapātreṇa triḥ prasavyaṃ pariṣicya (?) uttarayā "putrān pautrān" ity ṛcā ubhayeṣāṃ piṇḍān pariṣicyety arthaḥ | nyubjya pātrāṇi nyubjya adhomukhatayā sthāpayitvertha (?) | uttaraṃ yajuranavānaṃ (?) tryavrārdham āvartayitvā "tṛpyata tṛpyata tṛpyata" ity ekaṃ yajus trivāraṃ japtvānyapakṣāvalambanenānucchvasvan āvartyety arthaḥ | prokṣya pātrāṇi dvaṃdvam abhyudāhṛtya nyubjīkṛtāni pātrāṇi prokṣya dve pātre yugapad uddhatyānyatra sthāpayed ity arthaḥ | evam uktāpastambagṛhyavidhānato gṛhyāntroktavidhānato vā yathāsvagṛhyaṃ piṇḍān dadyāt | gṛhyoktavidhāne 'pi mātāmahādīnāṃ piṇḍanivapanaṃ kāryam,

	pitṛmātāmahādīnāṃ dadyād gṛhyavidhānataḥ |

ity etasminn eva prakaraṇe bṛhaspativacanena darśitatvāt | tatra āpastambagṛhyavidhānato mātāmahādīnāṃ pṛthakpiṇḍanivapanaṃ kāryaṃ vikṛteḥ prakṛtivat kartavyatvāt | vikṛtitvaṃ ca mātāmahādiśrāddhasya bhāṣyārthasaṃgrahakāreṇoktam |

	mātāmahāder apy evaṃ śrāddhaṃ kuryāt prayatnataḥ | iti |

tataś ca tadgṛhyānusāriṇām evaṃ mātāmahādyarthapiṇḍadānaprayogaḥ | mātṛvargārthadarbhasaṃstaraṇaṃ vidhāya tataḥ paścād bhāge mātāmahavargārthadarbhasaṃstaraṇaṃ kṛtvā tataḥ paścādbhāge mātāmahīvargārthadarbhasaṃstaraṇaṃ kuryāt | mātṛvargārtham apo datvā mātāmahavargārtham apo dadyāt | "mārjayantāṃ mātāmahāḥ" ityādimantrā ūhyāḥ | mātāmahavargārtham apo datvā mātāmahīvargārtham apo dadyāt "mārjayantāṃ mātāmahyaḥ" iti mantrā ūhyāḥ | mātṛvargārthapiṇḍān datvā mātāmahavargārthapiṇḍān dadyāt "etat te mātāmaha amukagotra amukaśarman ye ca tvām anu" iti piṇḍadānamāntrā ūhyāḥ | mātāmahavargārthapiṇḍān datvā mātāmahīvargārthapiṇḍān dadyāt | "etat te mātāmahī amukagotre amukanāmni yāś ca tvām anu" iti piṇḍadānamantrā ūhyāḥ | mātṛvargārthapiṇḍasamīpe punar apo datvā mātāmahavargārthapiṇḍasamīpe (?) punar apo dadyāt | tadanantaraṃ mātāmahīvargapiṇḍasamīpe punar apo ninayet | ninayanamantrāṇām ūhaḥ pūrvavad eva kāryaḥ | mātṛvargārthapiṇḍān upasthāya pitṛvargārthapiṇḍopasthānamantrair eva mātāmahavargārthapiṇḍopasthānaṃ kāryam | tato mātṛvargārthapiṇḍopasthānamantrair eva mātāmahīvargārthapiṇḍopasthānaṃ kāryam | "putrān pautrān" ity etayarcā dvādaśapiṇḍānāṃ yugapat triḥ prasavyaṃ pariṣecanaṃ kāryam, śeṣaṃ yajurāvartanādi sādhāraṇatayā sakṛd eva kāryam, "mārjayantāṃ mātāmahāḥ" ity ūho bhāṣyārthasaṃgrahakāreṇa sūcitaḥ |

	yojyaḥ pitrādiśabdānām sthāne mātamahādikaḥ |

	annahome tathā sparśe jalapiṇḍādidānake ||

	yan me mātāmahītyādi tatrodāharaṇaṃ bhavet || iti |

annahome "yan me mātā pralulobha caranty ananuvratā" ityadibhiḥ mantraiḥ agnaukarānnahome | sparśe "eṣa te tata madhumāṃ ūrmiḥ sarasvān" ityādibhir mantraiḥ brāhmaṇabhojanārthānnasparśe | jalapiṇḍādidānake "marjayantāṃ pitaraḥ" ityādijaladānamantre, "etat te tatāsau ye ca tvām anu" ityādipiṇḍadānamantre ca pitrādiśabdānāṃ sthāne mātāmahādiśabdo yojyaḥ prayojya ity arthaḥ | yan me mātāmahītyādi tatrodāharaṇaṃ bhaved ity asyāyam arthaḥ: tatra pitrādiśabdasthāne mātāmahādiśabdayojanam | "yan me mātā pralulobha caraty ananuvratā tan me retaḥ pitā vṛṅktām" iti mantreṇa mātāmahārtham annahome kartavye mantragatamātṛpadasthāne mātāmahīpadaprakṣepeṇa yan me mātāmahīty evaṃ saṃpanna ūhaḥ, tathā etanmantragatapitṛpadasthāne mātāmahapadaprakṣepeṇa tan me reto mātāmaho vṛṅktām ity evaṃ saṃpanna ūhaś (?) codāharaṇaṃ bhaved iti | nāmājñāne piṇḍadānaṃ prakṛtya gṛhyāntaraṃ "yadi nāmāni na vidyāt svadhā pitṛbhyaḥ pṛthivīṣadbhyaḥ iti prathamapiṇḍaṃ dadyāt svadhā pitṛbhyo 'ntarikṣasadbhya iti dvitīyam, svadhā pitṛbhyo dviṣadbhya iti tṛtīyam" iti | ete mantrāḥ mātāmahādyarthapiṇḍadānamantre 'pi nāmājñānaviṣaye prayojyāḥ | gotrājñāne 'py āha vyāghrapāt: "gotranāśe tu kaśyapaḥ" iti | gotrājñāne kaśyapagotragrahaṇaṃ kartavyam, kaśyapagotrasya sarvasādhāraṇatvāt | tathā ca śrutiḥ: "tasmād āhuḥ sarvāḥ prajāḥ kaśyapaḥ" iti | evaṃ ca mātāmahādigotrājñāne 'pi kāśyapagotragrahaṇaṃ kartavyam ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ piṇḍadānaviṣayāṇi**

**atha brāhmaṇabhojanātmakapradhānapāścātyāṅgaviṣayāṇi**

tatra matsyaḥ |

	athācānteṣu cācamya vāri dadyāt sakṛt sakṛt || iti |

brāhmaṇeṣv ācānteṣu svayam apy ācānto bhuktavad brāhmaṇadakṣiṇahasteṣu sakṛt sakṛd apo dadyād ity arthaḥ | etad anācānteṣu vipreṣu piṇḍadānapakṣe draṣṭavyam | ācānteṣu piṇḍadānapakṣe ācamya piṇḍaṃ dadyāt tato viprahasteṣu sakṛt sakṛd apo dadyāt | teṣāṃ pavitrapāṇitvāya darbhāś ca deyāḥ, bhojanasamayapavitrāṇām ucchiṣṭatvena tyaktatvāt | padmapurāṇē 'pi |

	ācānteṣūdakaṃ dadyāt puṣpāṇi sayavāni ca | iti |

'vaiśvadaivikabrāhmaṇahasteṣv iti śeṣaḥ, sayavāni cety abhidhānāt | paitṛkabrāhmaṇahasteṣu tu yavasthāne tilā deyāḥ, arghyādau tathā darśanāt | sayavāni ceti caśabdāt punar apy udakaṃ deyam iti sūcyate | hasteṣu dattānāṃ yavādīnāṃ darbhāṇām iva dhāraṇaprayojanakāryābhāvāt kṛtakāryatvena kvacit śucau deśe prakṣepaṇaṃ viprāḥ kuryuḥ | prakṣepaṇānantaraṃ punaḥ matyaḥ |

	ācānteṣu punar dadyāj jalapuṣpākṣatodakam |

	datvāśīḥ pratigṛhṇīyāt dvijebhyaḥ prāṅmukho budhaḥ ||

punaḥśabdena padmapurānoktaṃ sayavapuṣpaṃ jalaṃ prathamaṃ deyam iti sūcitam | jalapuṣpākṣatodakaṃ dadyāt prathamaṃ jalaṃ dadyāt sākṣatapuṣpaṃ pradāya punar api jalaṃ dadyād ity arthaḥ | āśīḥ pratigṛhṇīyād āśiṣaḥ pratigṛhṇīyād ity arthaḥ | kāḥ punar āśiṣaḥ kathaṃ ca tāsāṃ pratigrahaḥ, pratigṛhya kiṃ kartavyam ity apekṣite tenaivānantaram uktam |

	aghorāḥ pitaraḥ santu santv ity ukte punar dvijaiḥ |

	gotraṃ tathā vardhatāṃ nas tathety uktaś ca taiḥ punaḥ ||

	dātāro no 'bhivardhantāṃ vedāḥ santatir eva ca |

	śraddhā ca no mā vyapagāt bahudeyaṃ ca no 'stv iti ||

	etāḥ satyāśiṣaḥ santu santv ity uktaś ca taiḥ punaḥ |

	svastivācanakaṃ kuryāt ................... || iti |

aghorāḥ pitaraḥ santv iti śrāddhakartrā vartavyam | śivāḥ pitaraḥ santv iti tasyārthaḥ | santv ity ukte punar dvijaiḥ santv adhorāḥ pitara ity ukte gotraṃ vardhatāṃ na iti kartrā vaktavyam | tathety uktaś ca taiḥ punaḥ tair dvijaiḥ vardhatāṃ gotram ity uktāḥ kartā dātāro no 'bhivardhantāṃ ityādiślokaṃ paṭhitvā etāḥ satyā āśiṣaḥ santv iti brūyāt | santv ity uktaś ca taiḥ punaḥ svastivācanaṃ kuryāt | tair dvijaiḥ santv etāḥ satyā āśiṣa ity uktaḥ kartā dvijaidattam (?) akṣatapuṣpaṃ śirasā pratigṛhya svastivācanaṃ kuryāt | kātyāyanagṛhye tu dātāra ityādikaṃ noktam | aghorāḥ pitaraḥ santv ity ukte gotraṃ no vardhatām ity etāvanmātram uktam | yady apy āśīḥpratigrahānantaram eva svastivācanaṃ kāryam iti matsyavacanamātrāt pratibhāti | tathāpy āśiṣaṃ parigṛhyānantaraṃ bhojanapātrāṇi cālayitvā svastivācanaṃ kuryāt | anyathā doṣaśravaṇāt | tathā ca nārāyaṇaḥ |

	acālayitvā tatpātraṃ svasti kurvanti ye dvijāḥ |

	nirāśāḥ pitaras teṣāṃ śaptvā yānti yathāgatam ||

bṛhaspatir api |

	bhājaneṣu ca tiṣṭhatsu svasti kurvanti ye dvijāḥ |

	tad dattam asurair bhuktaṃ nirāśāḥ pitaro gatāḥ ||

tasmāt svastivācanāt prāk pātracālanam avaśyaṃ kāryam ity abhiprāyaḥ pātracālanakartṛviṣaye vidhipratiṣedhau jātūkarṇyena darśitau |

	pātrāṇy uccālayec chrāddhe svayaṃ śiṣyo 'tha vā sutaḥ |

	na strībhir na ca bālena nāsajātyā kathaṃcana ||

svastivācanaprakāras tu pāraskareṇa darśitaḥ: "svastīti bhagavan brūhīti vācanam" iti | akrodakaṃ datvā svastivācanam iti kātyāyanenokto viśeṣaḥ | atraivaṃ prayogaḥ: yajñopavītī vaiśvadaivikahaste udakaṃ datvā purūravārdravasaṃjñikebhyo viśvebhyo devebhyaḥ svastīti bhagavan brūhīti kartā brūyāt | vipreṇa ca tebhyaḥ svastīti vaktavyam | prācīnāvītī pitryabrāhmaṇahasteṣūdakaṃ datvā pitṛbhyaḥ pitāmahebhyaḥ prapitāmahebhyaḥ amukagotrebhyaḥ amukaśarmabhyaḥ svastīti bhagavan brūhīti kartā brūyāt | vipreṇa ca tebhyaḥ svastīti vaktavyam | evaṃ mātāmahādibrāhmaṇahasteṣūdakaṃ datvā mātāmahamātuḥpitāmahamātuḥprapitāmahebhyo 'mukagotrebhyo 'mukaśarmabhyaḥ svastīti bhagavan brūhīti kartā brūyāt | vipreṇa ca tebhyaḥ svastīti vaktavyam | svastivācanānantaraṃ yājñavalkyaḥ: "tataḥ kuryād akṣayyodakam eva ca" iti | tataḥ svastivācanānantaram akṣayyodakaṃ kuryāt | akṣayyam astv ity uktvā viprahaste jalaṃ ninayed ity arthaḥ | pitryaviprahaste tu satilaṃ jalaṃ ninayet, akṣayyam astv iti ca tilodakaṃ datveti kātyāyanenoktatvāt | astv akṣayyam iti viprair vācyam | tathā ca mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇam |

	pitṝṇāṃ nāmagotreṇa jalaṃ deyam anantaram |

	brāhmaṇānāṃ dvijair vācyam akṣayyam idam astv iti ||

brāhmaṇānāṃ hasteṣv iti śeṣaḥ | atraivaṃ prayogaḥ: purūravārdravasaṃjñakānāṃ viśveṣāṃ devānām akṣayyam astv iti vaiśvadaivikabrāhmaṇahasteṣu kevalaṃ jalaṃ yajñopavītī ninayet | pitṛpitāmahaprapitāmahānām amukagotrāṇām amukaśarmaṇāṃ sapatnīkānām akṣayyam astv iti pitryabrāhmaṇahasteṣu satilaṃ jalaṃ prācīnāvītī ninayet | evaṃ mātāmahādīnām amukagotrāṇām amukaśarmaṇāṃ sapatnīkānāṃ akṣayyam astv iti mātāmahādibrāhmaṇahasteṣu satilaṃ jalaṃ ninayet | vaiśvadaivādidvijaiḥ tatpradānānantaram akṣayyam idam astv iti vaktavyam | akṣayyodakadānānantaraṃ dakṣiṇāṃ dadyāt | tathā ca matyaḥ |

	akṣayyodakam eva ca |

	satilaṃ nāmagotreṇa dadyāc chaktyā ca dakṣiṇām || iti |

satilam akṣayyodakaṃ pitrādināmagotreṇa dadyāt | tadanantaraṃ śaktyanusāreṇa dakṣiṇāṃ dadyād ity arthaḥ | atra deyavastūni nirdiśya vyāsa āha |

	gobhūhiraṇyavāsāṃsi navyāni śayanāni ca |

	dadyād yad iṣṭaṃ viprāṇām ātmanaḥ pitur eva ca ||

	vittaśāṭhyena rahitaḥ pitṛbhyaḥ prītim ācaran || iti |

vittaśāṭhyena rahito gavādikaṃ pitṛbhyo dadyāt | teṣāṃ prītim ācarann ity anvayaḥ | pāraskaro 'pi: "hiraṇyaṃ viśvebhyo devebhyo rajataṃ pitṛbhyo 'nyac ca gokṛṣṇājinādikaṃ yāvac chaknuyāt" iti | vāyupurāṇe |

	loke śreṣṭhatamaṃ yat tu ātmanaś cāpi yat priyam |

	sarvaṃ pitṝṇāṃ dātavyaṃ teṣām evākṣayārthinā ||

pitṝṇāṃ pitṛbhya ity arthaḥ | pitṛbhyo dakṣiṇādāne prakāram āha jamadagniḥ |

	satilaṃ nāmagotreṇa dadyāc chaktyā ca dakṣināṃ |

	hiraṇyaratnavāsāṃsi harmyāṇi śayanāni ca || iti |

hiraṇyādi dravyaṃ tilopetaṃ pitṛbhyo gotranāmasahitebhyaḥ pratipadayāmīti saṃkalpya paitṛkabrāhmaṇānāṃ bhuktavatāṃ samarpayed ity arthaḥ, "brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā tu dadyāc chaktyā ca dakṣiṇām" ityuktatvāt | yat tu vāyuprāṇe 'bhihitam,

	yad yad iṣṭatamaṃ loke yac cānyad vidyate gṛhe |

	tat tad guṇavate deyaṃ tadaivākṣayam icchatā ||

iti, tat devebhyaḥ pitṛbhyaś ca saṃkalpitaṃ dakṣiṇādravyam, na bhakṣyabhojyādikam | bhakṣyabhojyaṃ tu bhoktṛviprebhyaḥ samaṃ deyam | dakṣiṇādidravyam api bhoktṛvipraguṇānusāreṇa viṣamaṃ deyam ity evaṃparam, na tu guṇavantaṃ brāhmaṇam uddiśya deyaparam ity avagantavyam | pāraspakaraḥ |

	ekapaṅktyupaviṣṭānāṃ viprāṇāṃ śrāddhakarmaṇi |

	bhakṣybhojyaṃ samaṃ deyaṃ dakṣiṇā tv anusārataḥ || iti |

samaṃ deyaṃ guṇatāratamyanibandhanavaiṣamyaṃ hitvā deyam ity arthaḥ | dakṣiṇādau tāratamyanibandhanavaiṣamye kṛte 'pi na doṣaḥ | anusārataḥ nimantritavipraguṇānusāreṇety arthaḥ | evaṃ cetthaṃ dakṣiṇādānaprayogaḥ: yajñopavītī purūravārdravasaṃjñikebhyo viśvebhyo devebhyo hiraṇyādidakṣiṇāṃ pratipādayāmīti saṃkalpya vaiśvadaivikabrāhmaṇahaste samarpayet | tataḥ prācīnāvītī pitṛpitāmahaprapitāmahebhyo 'mukagorebhyo 'mukaśarmabhyaḥ sapatnīkebhyaḥ rajatādidakṣiṇāṃ pratipādayāmīti saṃkalpya pitṛvargārthaviprahaste samarpayet | evaṃ mātāmahādibhyaḥ samarpayet | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> yadi pitrādyuddeśena dravyatyāgaḥ na punar brāhmaṇoddeśena, kathaṃ tarhi brāhmaṇānāṃ dakṣiṇādravye svāmyam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span>: yathā darśapūrṇamāsayor dakṣiṇādāne "brāhmaṇā ayaṃ va odanaḥ" ity uktvā yajamānena odane samarpite brāhmaṇoddeśena odanatyāgābhāve 'pi ṛtvijāṃ karmakartvenaiva odanasvāmyam utpadyate, tathehāpi hiraṇyarajatādisarmarpaṇe tatra svāmyaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ karmakartvenaiva sidhyati | yathā vā — pratiṣṭhādau prātiṣṭhāpyadevatāyai saṃkalpitavastrābharaṇādiṣu ācāryasya svāmyam "pratiṣṭhānte tu sarvam upakaraṇam ācāryo gṛhṇāti" iti vacanānugṛhītakarakaratvenaiva bhavati, tathehāpi "brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā tu dadyāc chaktyā ca dakṣiṇām" ityanugṛhītena karmakartvena brāhmaṇānāṃ pitrādyuddeśena saṃkalpitarajatādau svāmyaṃ saṃpadyata iti na kaścid virodhaḥ | atha vā brāhmaṇoddeśena tyāgād evātrāpi brāhmaṇānāṃ svāmyaṃ bhaviṣyati,

	ācāntebhyo dvijebhyas tu prayacched atha dakṣiṇām | iti |

devalena dvijān uddiśya dakṣiṇā deyety abhihitam |

	dakṣiṇāṃ pitṛviprebhyo dadyāt pūrvaṃ tato dvayoḥ | iti |

dvayor vaiśvadaivikaviprayor iti yāvat | dvayor iti ṣaṣṭhī pitṛviprebhya iti caturthīsamabhivyāgārāt caturthyarthe draṣṭavyā | evām cāyam arthaḥ: pūrvaṃ pitṛviprebhyo dakṣiṇāṃ datvā paścād vaiśvadaivikabrāhmaṇābhyāṃ dadyād iti | asmin pakṣe dakṣiṇādānasyāpaitṛkatvāt pitṛviprebhyo 'pi yajñopavīty eva dadyāt | ata eva jamadagniḥ |

	sarvaṃ karmāpasavyena dakṣiṇādānavarjitam | iti |

yat punas tenoktam,

	apasavyaṃ tu tatrāpi matsyo bhagavān hi mene | 

iti, tat pitṝn uddhiśya dakṣiṇādānapakṣe draṣṭavyam | bṛhaspatis tu animantritaviprebhyo 'pi dakṣiṇādānam āha |

	jñātayo bāndhavā niḥsvās tathā vātithayo 'pare |

	pradadyād dakṣiṇāṃ teṣāṃ sarveṣām anurūpataḥ || iti |

jñātayaḥ pitṛsaṃbandhāḥ | bāndhavā mātṛsaṃbandhāḥ | dakṣiṇādānānantaraṃ yājñavalkyaḥ |

	datvā tu dakṣiṇāṃ śaktyā svadhākāram udāharet | iti |

dakṣiṇādānānantaraṃ svadhāṃ vācayiṣye iti viprān anujñāpayed ity arthaḥ | atrir api |

	vācayiṣye svadhāṃ praśnam itthaṃ kuryād dvijātiṣu | iti |

svadhāṃ vācayiṣye itītthaṃ svadhāpraśnaṃ dvijātiṣv āsīneṣv eva kuryād ity arthaḥ | tato dvijātayaḥ vācyatām ity anujñāṃ dadyuḥ,

	vācyatām ity anujñāṃ tu prītā dadyuḥ samāhitāḥ |

iti tenaivānantaram abhidhānāt | evam anujñātaḥ kiṃ kuryād ity apekṣite yājñavalkyaḥ |

	vācyatām ity anujñātaḥ prakṛtebhyaḥ svadhocyatām | iti |

anenedam uktam: pitṛbhya pitāmahebhyaḥ prapitāmahebhyo mātāmahebhyo mātuḥpitāmahebhyo mātuḥprapitāmahebhyaḥ sapatnīkebhyaḥ svadhocyatām iti kartā brūyād iti | astu svadheti viprā brūyuḥ | tataḥ kartā kamaṇḍalunā piṇḍasamīpabhūmau jalaṃ siñcet | kātyāyanas tu darbhān āstīrya tasyāṃ bhūmau samantrakaṃ secanaṃ kāryam ity āha: "sapavitrān kuśān āstīrya svadhāṃ vācayiṣye iti pṛcchati vācyatām ity ukte pitṛbhyaḥ pitāmahebhyaḥ prapitāmahebhyāh svadhocyataṃ  astu svadhety ucyamāne ūrjaṃ vahantīr ity apo niṣiñcet sapavitreṣu kuśeṣu" iti | sapavitreṣu arghyasaṃskārārthapavitrasahiteṣu | sapavitreṣv iti vadan nyubjīkṛtārghyapātram uttānaṃ kṛtvā tatra pavitrāṇi grāhyāṇy asmin kāla iti sūcayati | ata eva saṃgrahakāraḥ |

	yājñavalkyo visargāt prāk pātram uttānam icchati |

	yamo visarjanaṃ kṛtvā gṛhyakartāpi śaunakaḥ ||

	prītipraśṇāt tu devānāṃ pūrvaṃ kātyāyanādayaḥ || iti |

visarjanāt prāg vipravisarjanāt pūrvam, devānāṃ prītipraśnāt pūrvaṃ viśvedevāḥ prīyantām ity abhidhānāt pūrvam, svadhāvācanakāle ity arthaḥ | atra yathāsvagṛhyaṃ vyavasthā,

	sarveṣām api pakṣāṇāṃ svasvagṛhyāt tu gṛhyate |

iti smaraṇāt | svasvagṛhyoktapakṣasyābhāve tu svecchaiva pakṣaviśeṣagrahaṇe niyāmikā,

	svagṛhyoktasya cābhāve grahaṇaṃ svecchayā bhavet |

ity api smaraṇāt | sapavitrakuśavatyāṃ bhūmau udakadhārāniṣecanānantaraṃ svadhā saṃpadyatām iti kartā brūyāt | vipraiś ca saṃpadyatāṃ svadhā iti svadhākārātmikā pitṝṇām āśīr vaktavyā | tathā ca atriḥ |

	astu svadheti taiḥ prokte niṣicyodīrya nityaśaḥ |

	svadhākāraḥ parā proktā pitṛṣv āśīḥ svayaṃbhuvā ||

	āyuḥputradanārogyaśāntyarthaṃ vācayed dvijān || iti |

tair viprair astu svadhety ukte kartā "ṛce tvā ruce tvā samithsravanti (?) saritaḥ" ityādikam "svadhāṃ duhānā amṛtasya dhārām" ityantaṃ mantraṃ sāmarthyarūpaliṅgād evātra prāptam udīryodakadhārāṃ niṣicya svayaṃbhuvā brahmaṇā proktā pitṛsvadhākārātmikā parā utkṛṣṭā yā āśīs tām āyurādiphalasiddhyarthaṃ dvijān vācayed ity arthaḥ | svadhāvācanānantaraṃ yājñavalkyaḥ |

	viśvedevāś ca prīyantāṃ vipraiś cokte idaṃ japet | iti |

viśvedevāḥ prīyantām iti pūrvaṃ śrāddhakartā, paścāt prīyantāṃ viśvedevā iti vaiśvadaivikavipraiś cokte, caśabdāt pitaraḥ prīyantām iti pūrvaṃ kartā, paścāt prīyantāṃ pitara iti pitryavipraiś cokte idaṃ vakṣyamāṇaṃ japet "dātāro no 'bhivardhantām" ityādikam āśīḥprārthanāvākyavṛndaṃ kartā paṭhed ity arthaḥ | atra saṃgrahakāraḥ |

	dātāra iti yājñoktyā pādārthaḥ prārthanā smṛtā |

	tāṃ suraprītisaṃpraśnān prāk pracetanās tu manyate ||

	pāraskaraḥ svasti vācyaṃ kṛtvāśīr grahaṇaṃ jagau |

	visarjiteṣu vipreṣu bahiṣṭheṣu manur jagau ||

	yāny atra kālabhedena karmāṇi munayo jaguḥ |

	svasvagṛhyānusāreṇa vikalpas teṣu yujyate |

	na gṛhyādismṛtir yeṣāṃ śrāddhādāv upalabhyate ||

	kartum arhanti te kṛtsnaṃ yasya kasya muner iti ||

vaikalpikeṣu svagṛhyādyuktapakṣābhāve yasya kasyacid ekasya muneḥ pakṣaṃ svecchānuguṇaṃ kuryād ity arthaḥ | viśvedevāḥ prīyantām ity uktvā vaiśvadaivikabrāhmaṇapāṇau apo datvā pitaraḥ prīyantām ity uktvā paitṛkabrāhmaṇapāṇau apo datvā anantaraṃ sarvabrāhmaṇapāṇiṣu sapuṣpāḥ sākṣatās cāpo dadyāt | tathā ca atriḥ |

	viprapāṇau tu datvāpaḥ sapuṣpāḥ sākṣatās tataḥ | iti |

apo dadyād iti śeṣaḥ | atra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	vāje vāja iti procya brāhmaṇāṃs tān visarjayet |

	viprān pradakṣiṇīkṛtya pitṛbhyaḥ prārthayed varān ||

tān pāṇidhṛtapuṣpākṣatān visarjayet | svasthānaṃ prati gamanārthaṃ āsanebhya utthāpayet,

	vāje vāja ity utthāpya kṛtvā caitān pradakṣiṇam |

iti mārkaṇḍeyasmaraṇāt | utthāpane ca sākṣādviprahastagrahaṇaṃ na kuryāt, kiṃ tu hastasaṃsṛṣṭadarbhadvārā,

	vāje vāje iti japan kuśāgreṇa visarjayet |

iti matsyenābhidhānāt | kuśāgreṇa kuśena hastasparśanaṃ kṛtvety arthaḥ | agreṇa tu hastasparśane kriyamāṇe ekadā ekasyaiva hastasaṃsparśo na bahūnām | tataś ca "tṛptā yāta" iti bahuvacanam "aditiḥ pāśān" itivad avivakṣitaṃ syāt | evaṃ ca kuśena yāvatāṃ hastasaṃsparśanaṃ yugapat kartuṃ śakyaṃ tāvatāṃ sakṛn mantroccāraṇam, yāteti bahuvacanato bahuvipravisarjanalakṣaṇakāryasya sakṛduccāraṇād eva siddheḥ | asaṃbhave mantrāvṛttiḥ | vinotthānaṃ viprāṇāṃ yānaṃ ca saṃbhavatīty arthād uttiṣṭhatety api yātety anenaivoktaṃ bhavati | viprāṇām utthāpanenaiva tatrāvāhitadevapitṝṇām apy utthāpanaṃ siddham iti smṛtiṣu tat pṛthanṅoktam (?) | tathāpi tasya spaṣṭānusaṃdhānārthaṃ darbheṇa saṃsparśanāt pūrvam uttiṣṭhata pitaro viśvair devaiḥ sahety uktvā vipravisarjanaṃ kāryam | evaṃ ca dvijavisarjanasaṃpātāyātaṃ pitrādivisarjanaṃ nāhatyānuṣṭheyam iti na visarjane prācīnāvītinā bhavitavyam | ata eva "upavītī visarjanam" it śaunakenoktam | vipravisarjane kramaḥ purāṇe darśitaḥ |

	paścād visarjayed devān pūrvaṃ paitāmahān dvijān |

	mātāmahānām apy evaṃ saha devaiḥ kramaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

devān vaiśvadaivikadvijān | paitāmahān pitrādisthāneṣūpaviṣṭān | viprotthāpanānantaraṃ kātyāyanaḥ: "āmā vājasya, ity anuvrajya pradakṣiṇīkṛtya" iti | pradakṣiṇīkaraṇānantara dātāra ityādiślokadvayena pitṛsakāśād varayācanaṃ kāryam | tathā ca matsyaḥ |

	visṛjya brāhmaṇāṃs tāṃs tu teṣāṃ kṛtvā pradakṣiṇam |

	dakṣiṇāṃ diśam ākāṃkṣan pitṝn yāceta mānavaḥ ||

	dātāro no 'bhivardhantāṃ vedāḥ santatir eva ca |

	śraddhā ca no mā vyagamad bahu deyaṃ ca no 'stu ||

	annaṃ ca no bahu bhaved atithīṃś ca labhemahi |

	yācitāraś ca naḥ santu mā ca yāciṣma kaṃcana || iti |

dakṣiṇāṃ diśam ākāṃkṣan dakṣiṇābhimukhaḥ ślokadvayena pratīyamānān varān ślokadvayapādenaiva pitṝn yāceta n viprān ity arthaḥ | bṛhaspatir api |

	viprān pradakṣiṇīkṛtya pitṛbhyaḥ prārthayed varān | iti |

varayācanānantaraṃ vṛddhaśātātapaḥ |

	evam astv iti tair vācyaṃ mūrdhnā grāhyaṃ ca tena tat | iti |

taiḥ bhūtapūrvagatyā pitradhiṣṭhānabhūtair viprair evam astv iti vācyam, sākṣāt pitṛbhir evam astv iti vacanāsaṃbhavāt | evam astv ity uktvā taiḥ svahastagataṃ puṣpākṣataṃ pradeyam | tena śrāddhakartrā ca tatpuṣpākṣataṃ mūrdhnā grāhyam | evam āśīr grahaṇānantaraṃ sa evāha |

	tataḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā punas teṣāṃ kṛtāñjaliḥ |

	uktvā caiva priyāṃ vācaṃ praṇipatya prasādayet || iti |

priyāṃ vācam: "dhanyā vayaṃ yuṣmadanugraheṇa pitṝṇām anṛṇā jātāḥ" ityevamādikām | prasādanārthaṃ yad vaktavyaṃ tad āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	adya me saphalaṃ janma bhavatpādābhivandanāt |

	adya me vaṃśajāḥ sarve yātā vo 'nugrahād divam ||

	patraśākādidānena kleśitā yuyam īdṛśāḥ |

	tatkleśajātaṃ citte tu vismṛtya kṣantum arhatha || iti |

evaṃ prasādyānantaraṃ sarvaṃ saṃpūrṇam astv iti viprāḥ prārthayitavyāḥ | tathā ca viṣṇuḥ |

	mantrahīnaṃ kriyāhīnaṃ bhaktihīnaṃ dvijottamāḥ |

	śrāddhaṃ saṃpūrṇatāṃ yātu prasādād bhavatāṃ mama || iti |

viprair api sarvaṃ saṃpūrṇam astv ity uktvā havirguṇastutiḥ kartavyā,

	śrāddhāvasāne kartavyā dvijair annaguṇastutiḥ |

iti vṛddhavasiṣṭhasmaraṇāt | tato viprān svasthānagamanārthaṃ visarjayet | tathā ca purāṇam |

	visarjayet prītimataḥ saṃmānyābhyarcya tāṃs tataḥ | iti |

mārkaṇḍeyo 'pi |

	jānubhyām avanīṃ gatvā praṇipatya visarjayet | iti |

madālasāvākyam api |

	vasarjayet priyāṇy uktvā praṇipatya ca bhaktitaḥ |

	ādvāram anugaccheta āgacchetānumoditaḥ || iti |

anumodito brāhmaṇair iti śeṣaḥ |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ brāhmabhojanātmakapradhānapāś cātyāṅgaviṣayāṇi**

**atha piṇḍapratipattyādiviṣayāṇi**

**samāptaṃ ca pārvaṇaśrāddhavidhānam**

**atha yathāśakti pārvaṇānuṣṭhānavidhiḥ**

tatra śātātapaḥ |

	yathā kathaṃcin nityāni kuryād indukṣayādiṣu |

	pātradravyādisaṃpatsu sarvakāmaphalaṃ labhet ||

amāvāsyādikāleṣu coditāni nityādhikārāṇi pārvaṇaśrāddhādīni pātradravyādisaṃpattyalābhe 'pi yathā kathaṃcit kuryāt yathāśakti kuryād iti pūrvārdhasyārthaḥ | tatra pātrāsaṃpattau devalenoktam |

	ekenāpi ca vipreṇa ṣaṭpiṇḍaṃ śrāddham ācaret |

	ṣaḍarghyān dāpayet tasmai ṣaḍbhyo dadyāt tathāsanam ||

	pitā bhuṅkte dvijakare mukhe bhuṅkte pitāmahaḥ |

	prapitāmahas tu tālau ca kaṇṭhe mātāmahaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

	pramātāmahas tu hṛdaye vṛddho nābhau tu saṃsthitaḥ || iti |

vṛddhaḥ pramātāmahasya pitā | atra vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	yady ekaṃ bhojayec chrāddhe daivaṃ tatra kathaṃ bhavet |

	annaṃ pātre samuddhṛtya sarvasya prakṛtasya ca ||

	devatāyatane kṛtvā tataḥ śrāddhaṃ pravartayet |

	prāsyed agnau tad annaṃ tu dadyād vā brahmacāriṇe || iti |

devatāyatanaṃ vaiśvadaivikabrāhmaṇopaveśanasthānam | tatra brāhmaṇārcanāt pūrvaṃ sthaṇḍile viśvān devān āvāhyāsanakalpanādidhūpadīpācchādanāntam ārādhanaṃ kṛtvā paścāt pitrartham upaviṣṭaṃ brāhmaṇam abhyarcya annapariveṣaṇakāle prakṛtasya śrāddhārthaṃ saṃpāditasya sarvasya saṃbandhi kiṃcid annaṃ pātre samuddhṛtyābhghāryārādhitasthāne purato nidhāyānnatyāgakāle pūrvam etad annaṃ viśvān devān uddiśya tyaktvānantaraṃ śrāddhaṃ pravartayet | pitṝn uddiśya brāhmaṇasya purataḥ pariviṣṭam annaṃ tyajed ity arthaḥ | ekasyāpi brāhmaṇasyālābhe devalenoktam |

	pātrābhāve paraṃ kṛtvā pitṛyajñavidhiṃ naraḥ |

	nirdiśyāpy annam uddhṛtya yatra pātraṃ tato gatiḥ ||

	nidhāya vā darbhavaṭūn āsaneṣu samāhitaḥ |

	praiṣānupraiṣasaṃyuktaṃ vidhānaṃ pratipādayet ||

	pātrābhāve kṣiped agnau gave dadyād athāpsu vā |

	na tu prāptasya lopo 'sti paitṛkasya viśeṣataḥ ||

asyārthaḥ: pātrābhāve 'nukalpatayoktaviprasyābhāve pitṛyajñavidhiṃ piṇḍapitṛyajñadharmakam agnaukaraṇaṃ paraṃ kevalaṃ (?) kṛtvā amāvāsyāyām (?) annaṃ bhājanādāv uddhṛtya nirdiśya caturthyantaśabdena devān pitṝn uddiśya uddhṛtam annaṃ tyaktvā yatrātyantānatidūre pātralakṣaṇānvito vipro 'sti, tatra nītvā tasmai tad annaṃ samarpayet | yad vā: pitṛyajñadharmakam agnaukaraṇaṃ kṛtvā darbhavaṭūn kuśamayān viprapratinidhīn vaṭūn atyantālpaparimāṇān āsaneṣu saṃsthāpya daive kṣaṇaḥ kriyatāṃ śrāddhe kṣaṇaḥ kriyatām ityādipraiṣasaṃyuktam oṃ tathetyādyanupraiṣasaṃyuktaṃ kṛtsnaṃ śrāddhavidhānaṃ kṛtvā devapitrarthaṃ tyaktam annaṃ pūrvavat pātralaṇayuktaviprebhyaḥ (?) pratipādayet samarpayet | atidūrasthe tu pātre pakṣadvaye 'pi tyaktam annam agnau kṣipet | atha vā gave bakṣaṇārthaṃ prayacchet | nadyādyudake vā kṣipet | na tu pātrābhāvamātreṇa karmaṇo lopaḥ kārya iti | pakvadravyasaṃpādanāsaṃbhave tu sumantuḥ |

	pākābhāve 'dhikāraḥ syād viprādīnāṃ narādhipa |

	apatnīnāṃ mahābāho videśagamanādibhiḥ ||

	sadā caiva tu śūdrāṇām āmaśrāddhaṃ vidur budhāḥ |

	ātmano deśakālābhyāṃ viṣame samupāgate ||

	āpady anagnau tīrthe ca pravāse patnyasaṃbhave |

	candrasūryagrahe caiva dadyād āmaṃ viśeṣataḥ || iti |

viprādīnāṃ traivarṇikādīnāṃ patnīrahitānāṃ videśagamanādibhiś ca kāraṇaiḥ pākasaṃpādanāsaṃbhave āmaśrāddhe adhikāraḥ syāt | candrasūryagrahe 'pi yasya pākāsaṃbhavaḥ sa āmaṃ dadyāt | yasya vā bhoktur brāhmaṇasyālābhaḥ so 'py āmaṃ dadyāt | śūdras tu sarvaśrāddheṣu pārvaṇavidhānenāmam eva dadyāt | tathā ca markaṇḍeyaḥ |

	sarvaṃ śrāddhaṃ tathā kāryaṃ śūdreṇāpy evam eva tu |

	mantravarjaṃ tu śūdrasya sarvam evaṃ vidhīyate ||

evam eva pārvaṇavidhinaiva | tathā ca pracetāḥ |

	strī (?) śūdraḥ svapacaś caiva jātakarmaṇi cāpy atha |

	āmaśrāddhaṃ tadā kuryād vidhinā pārvaṇena tu ||

svayaṃ pavatīti svapacaḥ | vāyupurāṇe |

	na pakvaṃ bhojayed viprān sacchūdro 'pi kadācana |

	bhojayet tv aśnatāṃ pāpaṃ tasyāpi prabhavet satām ||

satāṃ śūdrānnabhojane bhoktṛṇāṃ śūdrasya ca pāpaṃ bhavet | kaḥ punaḥ sacchūdra ity apekṣite vyāghraḥ |

	saṃskṛtānāṃ tu śūdrāyāṃ brahmavīryasamudbhavaḥ |

	svakarmanirataś caiva sacchūdraḥ saṃprakīrtitaḥ ||

uśanasā tu labdhakrītādipakvānnasadbhāve 'py āmaśrāddham eva dvijaiḥ kāryam ity uktam |

	apatnīkaḥ pravāsī ca yasya bhāryā rajasvalā |

	siddhānnena na kurvīta āmaṃ tasya vidhīyate ||

siddhānnena kāryāntarārthaṃ yathā kathaṃcit siddhānena | apatnīkādigrahaṇaṃ pākasāmagryādirahitapuruṣopalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva jamadagniḥ |

	na bhaved yasya sāmagrī dārā vā gṛham eva vā |

	āmaśrāddhaṃ prakurvīta vṛddho bālaś ca yo bhavet ||

pākasāmagrīsadbhāve kasyacid āmaśrāddhaṃ kartavyam ity āha sa eva |

	yāvat syān nāgnisaṃyuktaḥ utsannāgnir athāpi vā |

	āmaśrāddhaṃ tadā kuryād dhaste 'gnaukaraṇaṃ bhavet ||

pakvena śrāddhaṃ kvacid āvaśyakam ity āha hārītaḥ |

	śrāddhavighne dvijātīnām āmaśrāddhaṃ prakīrtitam |

	amāvāsyādyaniyataṃ māsasaṃvatsarād ṛte ||

anena māsikam ābdikaṃ ca śrāddham avaśyaṃ pakvānnena kāryam iti vacobhaṅgyoktam iti mantavyam | yat punar jamadganinoktam,

	śrāddhajñaḥ śraddhayā śrāddhaṃ śrāddhakāle yathāvidhi |

	pakvena vāśritenāpi nūnaṃ kuryāt pituḥ sutaḥ ||

iti, tat māsike sāmvatsarike 'pi sarvathā pakvānnāsiddhau āmadravyavidhānārtham iti na pūrvoktajamadagnivacanena gatārtham | āmaśrāddhe viśeṣam āha vyāsaḥ |

	āmaṃ tad anu kaunteya dadyād annaṃ caturguṇam |

	siddhānne tu vidhir yaḥ syād āmaśrāddhe 'py asau vidhiḥ ||

	āvāhanādi sarvaṃ syāt piṇḍadānaṃ ca bhārata |

	dadyād yac ca dvijātibhyaḥ śṛtaṃ vāśṛtam eva vā ||

	tenāgnaukaraṇaṃ kuryāt piṇḍāṃs tenaiva nirvapet ||

annam āmarūpaṃ puruṣāpekṣayā caturguṇaṃ dadyād ity arthaḥ | agnaukaraṇm atra pāṇāv eva,

	āmaśrāddhaṃ yadā kuryād vidhijñaḥ śrāddhas tadā |

	haste 'ganukaraṇaṃ kuryād brāhmaṇaḥ svavidhānataḥ ||

iti tenaivoktatvāt | ṣaṭtriṃśanmate 'pi |

	āmaśrāddhaṃ yadā kuryāt piṇḍadānaṃkathaṃ bhaet |

	gṛhapākāt samuddhṛtya saktubhiḥ pāyasena vā || iti |

piṇḍadānaṃ bhaved iti śeṣaḥ | āmadravyagṛhapākasaktupāyaseṣu yathālābhaṃ vyavasthā | eta cāmaśrāddhaṃ pūrvāhne kāryam, "āmaśrāddhaṃ tu pūrvāhne" iti śātātapasmaraṇāt | yat tu tenaivoktam

	madhyāhnāt parato yat tu kutapaḥ samudāhṛtaḥ |

	āmamātreṇa tatraiva pitṝṇāṃ dattam akṣayam ||

iti, tat śrāddhakartuḥ āmaśrāddhaviṣayam ity aparārkeṇa sādhitam | āmadravyāsaṃbhave tu vyāsenoktam |

	dravyābhāve dvijābhāve pravāse putrajanmani |

	hemaśrāddhaṃ prakurvīta yasya bhāryā rajasvalā ||

atrāpy āmaśrāddhaviśeṣo yathāsaṃbhavam anusaṃdheyaḥ | āmaśrāddhe hemaśrāddhe ca bhojanaprayuktāpośanakarmādīnāṃ "yathāsukhaṃ jupadhvaṃ tṛptāḥ stha" ityādīnāṃ ca dvārakāryalopān nivṛttir avagantavyā | keṣucin mantreṣūho 'py evvam avagantavyaḥ | tathā ca marīciḥ |

	āvāhane svadhākāre mantrā ūhyā visarjane |

	annakarmaṇy anūhāḥ syur āmaśrāddhavidhiḥ smṛtaḥ ||

āvāhane āvāhanamantre | "pitṝn haviṣe attave" ity atra attava iti padasthāne svīkartavya ity ūhaḥ kāryaḥ | svadhākāre "namo vaḥ pitara iṣe" ityādmantre iṣa iti padasthāne āmadravyāyety ūhaḥ kartavyaḥ | visarjane vipravisarjanamantre "vāje vāje" ityadike tṛptā iti padasthāne uddhṛtya āmena tarpayanta ity ūhaḥ kāryaḥ | annakarmaṇi brāhmaṇāṅguṣṭhaniveśanādau "viṣṇo havyaṃ rakṣasva" ityādayo mantrā anūhyāḥ syuḥ | āmaśrāddhavidhiḥ smṛtaḥ ity āmaśrāddhagrahaṇaṃ hemaśrāddopalakṣaṇārtham | hemadravyālābhe 'pi smṛtyantaroktam |

	tṛṇāni vā gave dadyāt piṇḍān vāthāpi nirvapet |

	tilodakaiḥ pitṝn vātha tarpayet snānapūrvakam ||

	agninā vā dahet kakṣaṃ śrāddhakāle samāgate ||

	tasmiṃś copavased ahni japed vā śrāddhasaṃhitām || iti |

atrāpi yathāsaṃbhavaṃ vyavasthā | aṅgasaṃpādanāsaṃbhave 'pi smṛthantaroktam |

	aṅgāni pitṛyajñasya yadā kartuṃ na śaknuyāt |

	sa yadā vācayed viprān sakalā siddhir astv iti ||

pitṛyajñasya śrāddhasya sakalā siddhiḥ sakalāṅgasiddhir astv iti bhavanto bruvantu iti prārthaneti | nimantritān viprān sakalāṅgasiddhir asya śrāddhasyāstv iti vācayed ity arthaḥ | vismṛtapārvaṇānuṣṭhānāsaṃbhave tu vyāsenoktam |

	tyaktāgneḥ pārvaṇaṃ naiva naikoddiṣṭaṃ sapiṇḍanam |

	atyakāgnes tu piṇḍoktis tasmāt saṃkalpya bhojayet ||

ayam arthaḥ: tyaktāgner avidhinotsṛṣṭāgneḥ pārvaṇaikoddiṣṭasapiṇḍīkaraṇātmakaśrāddhakarmaṇi naivādhikāraḥ | piṇḍoktiḥ śrāddhaṃ kartavyam ityuktiḥ atyaktāgneḥ tyaktāgnivyatiriktasyaiva atyaktāger eva śrāddhādhikāra iti yāvat | tasmāt tyaktāgnir eva saṃkalpya bhojayet | saṃkalpavidhānena śrāddhaṃ kuryād iti | saṃkalpavidhānasya pārvaṇavidhānāt ko bheda ity apekṣite sa evāha |

	saṃkalpaṃ tu yadā kuryān na kuryāt pātrapūraṇam |

	nāvāhanāgnaukaraṇaṃ piṇḍāṃś caiva na dāpayet ||

pātrapūraṇam arghyadānam | āvāhanasya samantrakasya niṣedhaḥ, na tv āvāhanamātrasya tadabhāve devapitṛsāṃnidhyābhāvāt | tataś cāvāhanamantram anuktvaiva purūravārdravasaṃjñakān viśvān devān āvāhayāmīty etāvanmātram uktvā devāvāhanaṃ kāryam | pitrādyāvāhane 'py evam eva | piṇḍāṃś caivety atra caivaśabdena ucchiṣṭapiṇḍasyāpi niṣedhaḥ | ata eva smṛtyantare,

	saṃkalpaṃ tu yadā śrāddhaṃ na kuryāt pātrapūraṇam |

	vikiraṃ ca na dātavyam |

iti spaṣṭam uktam | evam anukalpānuṣṭhāne 'pi śāṭhyābhāve sati mukhyakalpānuṣṭhānaphalaṃ bhavati | tathā ca smṛtyantaram |

	śrāddhānukalpaṃ yaḥ kuryāj jātyavasthādyapekṣayā |

	śrāddhāṃśe sarvam āpnoti mukhyakalpaphalaṃ naraḥ || iti |

śrāddhāṃśe śrāddhapradhānāṃśe brāhmaṇabhojanamātre piṇḍapradānamātre 'pi vā kṛte, aṅgāṃśe yathāśakti katipayānuṣṭhāne 'pi kṛta ity arthaḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ yathāśaktipārvaṇānuṣṭhānavidhiḥ **

**atha mṛtāhaśrāddhavidhiḥ**

evaṃ pratimāsaṃ kartavyaṃ pārvaṇaśrāddham uktam | atha pratisaṃvatsaraṃ kartavyaṃ sāṃvatsarikaśrāddham ucyate |

atra lokākṣiḥ |

	śrāddhaṃ kuryād avaśyaṃ tu pramītapitṛkaḥ svayam |

	indukṣaye māsi māsi vṛddhau pratyabdam eva ca ||

svayaṃgrahaṇam ādarārthaṃ na punaḥ putraśiṣyartvigādinivṛttyartham, yajamānasya pitaḥ asāv etat te tata ity anyakartṛkapiṇḍanirvapaṇadarśanāt | asāv etat te tata iti mantreṇa yajamānasya pitre ṛtvigādiḥ piṇḍān dadyād iti | tatrāmukagotrāmukaśarmann etat te tata iti mantram uktvāmukagotrāyāmukaśarmaṇe yajamānasya pitre asāv etat te, ity ayaṃ piṇḍo na yajamānayajamānasya | smṛtyantare yajamānasyety uktyā barhiṣi piṇḍasthāpanam iti viśeṣo 'vagantavyaḥ | etac cānyakartṛkatvaṃ yajamānasyāsāmarthye gurutarakāryāntaravyagratvena kālātipattiviṣaye vā draṣṭavyam | pratyabdaṃ śrāddhaṃ kathaṃ kartavyam ity apekṣite jātūkarṇaḥ |

	pituḥ pitṛgaṇasthasya kuryāt pārvaṇavat sutaḥ |

	pratyabdaṃ pratimāsaṃ ca vidhir jñeyaḥ sanātanaḥ ||

pitṛgaṇasthaḥ sapiṇḍitaḥ tasya pratyabdaṃ pratimāsaṃ ca pārvaṇavad ābdikaṃ māsikaṃ ca śrāddhaṃ suto mṛtāhe kuryād ity arthaḥ | etad uktaṃ bhavati: yathā amāvāsyāśrāddhe arghyadānādau pitṛpitāmahaprapitāmahānāṃ trayāṇām uddeśaḥ tathā pitur ābdikaśrāddhe 'pi trayāṇām uddeśaḥ kāryaḥ | iti |

	darśavat syāt trayoddeśaḥ sapiṇḍīkaraṇe kṛte | iti |

pratimāsaṃ ceti tāvat | "tāny eva tu punaḥ kuryāt" iti vacanāt sapiṇḍīkaraṇād ūrdhvam api prathamasaṃvatsare kriyamāṇānumāsikeṣu pārvaṇavat tridevatākaṃ kuryād iti vidhānārtham uktam iti mantavyam | na ca vācyam,

	pitaro yatra pūjyante tatra mātāmahā dhruvam |

iti vacanāt, pitṛmṛtāhe (?) mātāmahādīnām api śrāddhaṃ kāryam iti | yad āha pāraskaraḥ |

	pitur gatasya devatvam aurasasya tripūruṣam | iti |

devatvaṃ gatasya sapiṇḍīkaraṇena pitṛtvaṃ prāptasya | tripuruṣagrahaṇaṃ ṣaṭpuruṣanivṛttyartham | tena mṛtāhe mātamahaśrāddhaṃ na kāryam | kātyāyano 'pi |

	karṣūsamanvitaṃ muktvā tadādyaṃ śrāddhaṣoḍaśam |

	pratyābdikam aśeṣeṣu piṇḍāḥ syuḥ ṣaḍ iti sthitiḥ || iti |

karṣūsamanvitaṃ sapiṇḍīkaraṇam | anenārthāt karṣūsamanvitādiṣi mātāmahaśrāddhaṃ na vidyata ity uktam | saṃgrahakāras tu pitṛmṛtāhe mātāmahādiśrāddhaṃ na kāryam iti nyāyenaivopapādayati |

	yājñavalkyena kālas tu amāvāsyādinoditaḥ |

	aviśeṣeṇa pitryasya tathā mātāmahasya ca ||

	yugapac ca sa vijñeyo vacanād vakṣyamāṇakāt |

	kālabhedena tantraṃ syād deśabhedena caiva hi ||

	tasmāt tantravidhānāt tu yaugapadyaṃ pratīyate |

	amāvāsyādikāleṣu tad jñeyaṃ na mṛte 'hani ||

	amāvāsyādikāleṣu kālaikatvāt sahakriyā |

	mṛtāhani tu tadbhedān na yujyeta sahakriyā || iti |

prathamaślokasyāyam arthaḥ: amāvāsyādinā

	amāvāsyāṣṭakā vṛddhiḥ kṛṣṇapakṣo 'yanadvayam |

ityādivacanena śrāddhakālaḥ aviśeṣeṇa sāmānyena pitryasya pitṛśrāddhasya mātāmahasaṃbandhiśrāddhasya ca yājñavalkyenodita iti | yugapac ca sa vijñeya iti pādasyāyam arthaḥ: sa yājñavalkyenoditaḥ kālaḥ piṇḍapitṛyajñadarśaśrāddhayor iva na bhāgakrameṇa | kiṃ tu pitṛśrāddhamātāmahaśrāddhayor yugapad (?) ekadā bhāgakramam antareṇaiva jñeya iti | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> kālavidhāyake pūrvoktavacane yugapadādipadābhāvāt katham evam avagatir ity āśaṅkyoktam "vacanād vakṣyamāṇakāt" iti | asyāyam arthaḥ: yady api na kālavidhāyakāt pūrvoktavacanād evam avagatiḥ tathāpi,

	mātāmahānām apy evaṃ tantraṃ vā vaiśvadaivikam |

ity asminn eva śrāddhaprakaraṇe vakṣyamāṇād vacanād evam avagatir bhaviṣyatīti | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanv</span> asmād api vacanāt kathaṃ yaugapadyāvagatir ity āśaṅkya kālabhedenetyādinā samarthayate spaṣṭārtho 'yaṃ śloka iti | evaṃ ca yatra paitṛkasya mātāmahaśrāddhasya cāmāvāsyādikāle yaugapadyaṃ pratītaṃ tatraivanayoḥ samānatantratvaṃ na punar mṛtāha ity āha:

	amāvāsyādikāleṣu tad jñeyaṃ na mṛte 'hani | iti |

mṛte 'hani yaugapadyasyāpratīter ity abhiprāyaḥ | kathaṃ punar yaugapadyasyāpratītir mṛtāha ity āśaṅkyāha: amāvāsyādikāleṣv ityādi | tasyāyam arthaḥ: amāvāsyādikāleṣu paitṛkamātāmahaśrāddhayor aviśeṣeṇa prāptayoḥ kālaikatvād ekasminn eva kālabhage kartavyatvāvagamāt samānatantratā yujyate | mṛtāhe tu pratipuruṣam āyuḥpramāṇabhedāt pitṛmātāmahayor bhinnakālatvān mātāmahaśrāddhasya pitṛmṛtāho na kāla iti, tadbhāgarūpakālaikyasya dūrotsāritatvāt tannibandhenānayoḥ samānatantratātyantaṃ na yujyata iti | anenaiva nyāyena mātrādiśrāddhasyāpi pitṛmṛtāho na kāla iti, tatra tasya prāptyabhāvāt | pitṛmṛtāhe kevalapitṛpitāmahaprapitāmahānām eva devatātvam, na punaḥ sapatnīkānām iti mantavyam | yady apy anenaiva nyāyena pitṛmṛtāhaḥ pitāmahaśrāddasyāpi na kālaḥ, mātṛmṛtāhaś ca pitāmahyādiśrāddhasya na kālaḥ, tathāpi pārvaṇavad iti vacanāt pitāmahaprapitāmahayor api pitṛmṛtāhe, pitāmahīprapitāmahyor api mātṛmṛtāhe devatātvaṃ na tu nyāyata iti sarvam anavadyam | yadā pituḥ sāṃvatsarikaśrāddhakālaḥ, mātuḥ sāṃvatsarikaśrāddhakālaś ca daivad eko jātaḥ tadāpi na sapatnīkaṃ pitṛsāṃvatsarikaśrāddham | kiṃ tu mātāpitror maraṇapaurvāparyānusārikrameṇa tayoḥ sāṃvatsarikaśrāddhadvayaṃ vipranimantraṇāditadvisarjanāntaṃ pṛthag eva kāryam | yadā tu mātāpitror yugapanmaraṇe paurvāparyam ajñātam, tadā pūrvaṃ pituḥ sāṃvatsarikaṃ kṛtvā paścān mātuḥ sāmvatsarikaśrāddhaṃ kāryaṃ pitur mukhyatvāt | evaṃbhūtaviṣaye bhrātrādisāṃvatsarikaśrāddhadinaikye śrāddham anekaṃ jyeṣṭhādikrameṇa pṛthag eva kāryam | yat tu pracetasoktam,

	naikaḥ śrāddhadvayaṃ kuryāt samāne 'hani kutracit |

iti, tad ekasminn eva śrāddhe punaḥ punaḥ śrāddhaṃ na kuryād ity evaṃparam | tena nānānimittakānekaśrāddham ekasminn ahani kurvato na pracetaso vacanavirodhaḥ | yat tu lokākṣiṇoktam,

	mṛte 'hani samāsena piṇḍanirvapaṇaṃ pṛthak |

	navaśrāddhaṃ ca dampatyor anvārohaṇa eva tu ||

iti, anenāpi na mṛtāhe sapatnīkaṃ śrāddham uktaṃ yena pūrvoktavirodhaḥ syāt | kiṃ tarhy anenoktam | ucyate: dampatyor mṛtāhaikye samāsena saṃkṣepeṇa piṇḍanirvapaṇaṃ yathā dvaipitṛkaśrāddhe ekasmin piṇḍe dvayoḥ pitror amukanāmne amukanāmne ca ity uddiśyaika eva piṇḍo dīyate tathehāpy ekasmin piṇḍe dvayor mātāpitror amukāyāmukāyai cety uddeśaṃ kṛtvā eka eva piṇḍo deyaḥ | brāhmaṇāś cāyugmāḥ piṇḍadānavad eva dvāv evoddiśya bhojayitavyāḥ | piṇḍanirvapaṇagrahaṇasya śrāddhopalakṣaṇaparatvāt | evaṃ caitac chrāddham anekoddeśyasāhityarūpacodanāliṅgāt pārvaṇadharmakaṃ tantreṇa kāryam | navaśrāddhaṃ tu dampatyoḥ pṛthak kāryam | tataś caikoddiṣṭarūpaṃ śrāddhadvayaṃ prāgdvādaśāhān navaśrāddhadineṣu pitur mātuś ca kāryam | evam uktavidhaṃ sāṃvatsarikaśrāddhaṃ navaśrāddhaṃ caikacityām anvārohaṇe mātrā kṛte kartavyam | nānyatrety avadhārayitum anvārohaṇa evety uktam | yat tu smṛtyantaram,

	ekacityāṃ samāruḍhau dampatī nidhanaṃ gatau |

	pṛthak chrāddhaṃ tayoḥ kuryād odanaṃ ca pṛthak pṛthak ||

iti—odanaṃ odanapiṇḍaḥ—tad etan navaśrāddhamātraviṣaye yojayet | pratyabdaṃ tad yeṣām ekoddiṣṭavidhānenaiva māsikam ābdikaṃ ca śrāddhaṃ mātāpitror mṛtāhe bhedenoditaṃ tadviṣayam iti na pūrvoktasāṃvatsarikaśrāddhaviśeṣeṇa sahāsyāpi virodhaḥ | yat punar bhṛguṇaiva "pratyabdaṃ ca" ity uktvānantaram uktaṃ "navaśrāddhaṃ yugapat tu samāpayet" iti, tasyāyam artha: mātāpitror mṛtāhaikye mātrā caikacityanvārohaṇe kṛte sati pitur navaśrāddhaṃ caikakālam ekapākena (pākābhāvasyaiva?) tantreṇa pradhānāt pūrvāṅgakalāpaṃ kṛtvā prathamaṃ pitre paścānmātre ca śrāddhaṃ kṛtvā pāścātyāṅgakalāpaṃ ca kṛtvā tantreṇa kuryād iti | anekamātṛbhir ekacityām anvārohaṇe kṛte 'py evam eva | pitur anantaraṃ sākṣān mātus tadanantaram upamātṛṣu jyeṣṭhādikrameṇa navaśrāddhaṃ kuryāt tathā ca sa eva |

	ekakāle gatāsūnāṃ bahūnām atha vā dvayoḥ |

	tantreṇa śrapaṇaṃ krtvā kuryāc chrāddhaṃ pṛthak pṛthak ||

	pūrvakasya mṛtasyādau dvitīyasya tataḥ punaḥ |

	tṛtīyasya tataḥ kuryāt saṃnipāteṣv ayaṃ kramaḥ || iti |

śrapaṇaṃ pradeyānnapākaḥ pūrvakasya mukhyasya dvitīyasya mukhyāpekṣā jaghanyasya tṛtīyasya jaghanyatarasyety arthaḥ | bhinnacityām anvārohaṇe tu sarvaṃ pṛthag eva karyam | evam uktavidhiṣv anyatamavidhinā yathoktavyavasthānusāriṇā mṛtāhaśrāddham avaśyaṃ kartavyam | tathā ca kārṣṇājiniḥ |

	ūṣareṣu yathā kṣiptaṃ bījaṃ na pratirohati |

	tathā ca tad bhavet teṣāṃ yan na dattaṃ mṛte 'hani ||

etena mṛtāhe annam avaśyaṃ dātavyam ity abhiprāyaḥ | "tac ca pārvaṇavat smṛtam" iti jātūkarṇādīnāṃ bahutarāṇāṃ pakṣaḥ | "ekoddiṣṭavidhānena" iti yājñavalkyādīnāṃ bahūnām | ata eva sumantuḥ |

	kartavyaṃ parvaṇaṃ rājan naikoddiṣṭaṃ kathaṃcana |

	subahūny atra vākyāni munigītāni cakṣate ||

	alpetarāṇi rājendra ekoddiṣṭaṃ parcakṣate || iti |

atra pārvaṇapakṣe cakṣate pracakṣate dharmaśāstrajñāḥ | alpetarāṇi bahūni katipayāni vākyāny ekoddiṣṭapakṣaṃ pracakṣata ity arthaḥ | tena ekoddiṣṭapakṣaṃ parityajya pārvaṇapakṣa eva parigrāhya ity āha sa eva |

	tasmād vacanasāmarthyāt pārvaṇaṃ syān mṛte 'hani || iti |

vacanasāmarthyād bahutarāṇāṃ vacanānāṃ sāmarthād ity arthaḥ | ayam evārtho jaiminināpy uktaḥ: "vipratiṣiddhadharmasamavāye bhūyasāṃ syāt sadharmatvam" iti | pratyakṣaśrutimūlatvāt jātūkarṇyādivacanāny eva balavanti | pratyakṣaśrutiś ceyam: "māsi māsi ṛtāv ṛtau hemantagrīṣmavarṣāsu pratisaṃvatsare ca daivāś ca pitaraś ca sahāsatām" iti | pratisaṃvatsare mṛtāhe devāś ca pitaraś ca sahāsatāṃ viśvedevāḥ pitṛpitāmahaprapitāmahāś ca śrāddhaṃ bhoktuṃ saha tiṣṭhantv ity arthaḥ | anayā śrutyā sadaivaṃ śrāddhaṃ kāryaṃ mṛtāha ity uktam | tasmāt sarvair eva pārvaṇapakṣo grāhyaḥ | pārvaṇavidhāyakavacanaiḥ ekoddiṣṭavidhāyakavacanānāṃ bādhitatvāt | atha vā katipayair eva parvaṇapakṣaḥ parigrāhyaḥ | tathā ca smṛtyantaram |

	pituḥ pitṛgaṇasthasya kuryātāṃ darśavat sutau |

	pratyabdaṃ pratimāsaṃ ca vidhijñau kṣetrajaurasau ||

ekoddiṣṭavad itare sutāḥ kuryur iti śeṣaḥ | ata eva sumantuḥ |

	pratyabdaṃ pārvaṇenaiva vidhinā kṣetrajaurasau |

	kuryātām itare kuryur ekoddiṣṭaṃ sutā daśa ||

uktā caivaṃ parasparaviruddhānāṃ smṛtīnāṃ viṣayabhedena vyavasthā,

	śrrutidvidhaṃ tu yatra syāt tatra dharmāv ubhau smṛtau |

	smṛtidvaidhe tu viṣayaḥ kalpanīyaḥ pṛthak pṛthak ||

iti jābālasmaraṇāt | evam eva viṣayavyavasthā mātṛmṛtāhe 'pīty āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	pratyabdaṃ yo yathā kuryāt putraḥ pitre sadā dvijaḥ |

	tathaiva mātuḥ kartavyaṃ pārvaṇaṃ vānyad eva vā ||

yat tu tenaivoktam |

	pitṛvyabhrātṛmātṝṇāṃ ekoddiṣṭaṃ sadaiva tu |

iti, tatra mātṛśabdo gauṇamukhyamātṛsapatnīpara iti pitṛvyādisamabhivyāhārād avagamyate | ato na pūrvoktavacanena saha virodhaḥ | etac ca mātṛgrahaṇaṃ mukhyamātṛvyatiriktastrīṇām upalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva viṣṇudharmottaram |

	pratisaṃvatsaraṃ kāryam ekoddiṣṭaṃ naraiḥ striyāḥ |

	mṛte 'hani yathānyāyaṃ nṝṇāṃ yadvad ihoditam ||

yadvat puruṣāṇāṃ samantrakaṃ śrāddhaṃ tadvat dvijātistrīṇāṃ kṛtavivāhānāṃ samantrakam eva śrāddhaṃ kāryam | ity antyapādasyārthaḥ | apariṇītānāṃ tu strīṇāṃ saṃskārahīnatvād amantrakam eva | striyā ity etad aputrāyāḥ striyā ity abhiprāyakam | ata eva gargaḥ |

	aputrā yā mṛtāḥ kāścit striyo vā puruṣāś ca ye |

	teṣām api ca deyaṃ syād ekoddiṣṭaṃ na pārvaṇam || iti |

striyaḥ mātuḥ sapatnyādayaḥ | puruṣāḥ pitṛvyādayaḥ | yad vā,

	yenāsya pitaro yātāḥ yena yātāḥ pitāmahāḥ |

	tena yāyāt satāṃ mārgaṃ. tatra gacchan na riṣyati ||

iti smṛtyantaroktapūrvapuruṣācāreṇaikoddiṣṭapārvaṇapakṣayor uditānuditahomavat anyonyanindārthavādena saha vihitayoḥ mātāpitṛmṛtāhaśrāddhaviṣaye vyavasthā boddhavyā | atra paiṭhīnasiḥ |

	vibhaktais tu pṛthak kāryaṃ pratisāṃvatsarādikam |

	ekenaivāvibhakteṣu kṛte sarvais tu tatkṛtam ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ mṛtahaśrāddhavidhiḥ**

**atha pārvaṇaśrāddhavikṛtibhūtaśrāddheṣu nityādiśrāddhaviṣayāṇi**

atha śrāddhabhedaprakaraṇoktapārvaṇavikṛtibhūtanityaśrāddhaviṣayāṇi kānicid vacanāni likhyante | tatra pāraskaraḥ |

	ahany ahani yac chrāddhaṃ tan nityam iti kīrtitam |

	vaiśvadevavihīnaṃ tu aśaktāv udakena ca ||

vaiśvadevavihīnaṃ tu pārvaṇadharmātideśataḥ prāptasya vaiśvadaivikasya karmaṇonuṣṭhānena (?) rahitam | anena nityaśrāddhaṃ pārvaṇavan na kāryam iti sūcitam | ahany ahanīty etad atyantaśraddhāluviṣayaṃ susamṛddhaviṣayaṃ vā | yathāha devalaḥ |

	etena vidhinā śrāddhaṃ kuryāt saṃvatsaraṃ sakṛt |

	triś catur vā yathāśraddhaṃ māse māse dine dine || iti |

etena vidhinā pārvaṇavidhānena pratisaṃvatsaram ekavāraṃ viśiṣṭe 'hni, pratisaṃvatsaraṃ trivāraṃ vā triṣu maseṣu viśiṣṭe 'hni, pratisaṃvatsaraṃ caturvāraṃ caturṣu māseṣu viśiṣṭe 'hni, māse māse vā viśiṣṭe 'hni, dine dine vā yathāśraddhaṃ śraddhānusāreṇa śrāddhaṃ nityaśrāddhaṃ kuryād ity arthaḥ | yathāśraddham ity etat yathāsāmartham ity asyāpi pradarśanārtham | śaktyapekṣayāpi vyavasthāyā ucitatvāt | asya ca nityaśrāddhasy kalpaḥ asmābhir āhnike samyakprapañcita iti neha prapañcyate |

	naimittikaṃ tu śrāddham ekoddiṣṭātmakaṃ pārvaṇavikṛtibhūtaṃ āśaucakāṇḍe 'smābhir vakṣyate | kāmyaśrāddhaṃ tu śātātapena nirūpitam |

	kāmāya tu hitaṃ kāmyam abhipretārthasiddhaye |
